(kha)/ /shrImAMsadgurubhyassaddharmmAshashrutANAMwarNaNodharmmArthikaphaNIlalitasyadzalanidhirnAmAddwitAeyApustakabidzahAraM/ // /dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i
chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter zhes bya ba las glegs bam gnyis pa bzhugs so/ /

dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter zhes bya ba las/ rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras la rnal 'byor bla na med pa dang rjes su 'brel pa'i snyan
brgyud kyi gdams pa rgya mtsho lta bur bzhugs pa'i nang nas gtso bor gyur pa sa skya'i lcags ri mi 'da' ba'i gser chos bcu gsum du grags pa'i nang nas mchog bsgrubs pas
thun mong zhar las 'byung ba dmar mo skor gsum las/ ji skad du/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos/ rnal 'byor mkha' spyod sgrub pa'i nye ba'i lam/ /sdig can thar par bgrod
pa'i gsang lam mchog / nA ro ta pa'i chig brgyud snying gi gtam/ /sa skya'i bla chen brgyud pa'i gser chos 'di/ /snyan brgyud rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag rdo rje 'chang /
/kun spangs chos rje'i zhal las thos gyur pa/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar grub pa'i dbang phyug rje

btsun nA ro ta pa la/ rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul du gnyis skyes mchog gnyis kyis mtshon pa'i slob ma'i gtso bo paNDi ta bcu gnyis la sogs pa rnams la ming tsam yang ma gsungs
par bal po pham mthing pa 'jigs med grags pa dang ngag dbang grags pa mched kho nar gnang ba'i rje btsun nA ro mkha' spyod mar grags pa'i gdams pa zab mo/ gang zag rab bde
dgyes gang rung gi smin byed sngon du song nas sindhU ra'i byin rlabs nos/ bzlas sgom chag med dang gzhi bsnyen mthar phyin pa tsam gyis lam gzhan la ma ltos par tshegs
chung ngus rdo rje rnal 'byor ma mi mo'i gzugs kyis sgrub pa po'i lag pa'i 'khrig ma nas bzung ste lus ma spangs par mkha' spyod du 'khrid pa/ 'bring langga li ya'i shing
la brten nas sindhU ra'i sgrub pa la brten nas tshul bzhin du legs par brtags pas bud med phal pa'i khrod nas rdo rje rnal 'byor ma ngos zin te des tshe 'dir dngos su
mkha' spyod du 'khrid/ tha ma'ang 'chi ba 'od gsal chos sku las bar dor longs pa'i dus rdo rje rnal 'byor ma dpa' bo mkha' 'gro'i tshogs dang lhan cig pas mkha' spyod du
'khrid par nges pa'i zab pa las kyang ches zab pa/ snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi dang ldan pa'i skor la/ tshogs slob gnyis su grags pa'i nang nas ches cher zab pa gsang chen
slob bshad pa'i lugs bzhin nos pa la/ sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor du sgrub cing mchod pa dang bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba'i cho ga tshar chen rdo rje 'chang blo gsal
rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i mkha' spyod sgrub pa'i nye lam gyi yi ge ltar gyi byin rlabs

dang / yang ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang / thar rtse paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub cing mchod pa dang bdag nyid 'jug
cing dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul du blang ba'i cho ga ste/ yi ge so so'i steng nas sindhU ra'i byin rlabs dang / sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams pas mdzad pa'i
rtsa dbu (dhIH)ma'i khrid kyi chos nyid mngon sum du ston pa de kho na nyi brda chos kyi byin rlabs kyis smin par byas nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags kyis
mdzad pa'i khrid rim gsung sgros ma gzhir mdzad/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i khrid yig chen mo mkha' spyod bgrod pa'i nye lam gyi rgyas 'gebs
dang bcas/ gnyis bral 'chad dus zhal shes gsum zhes pa'i dngos bstan dang shugs bstan gyis thun mong ma yin pa'i zhal shes yig chung gis legs par brgyan/ de yang gang
zag dbang po rtul ba rnams la sems 'dzin gyi dmigs pa kho nas don 'grub na'ang / blos 'chun pa rnams la bsgom bya'i don la thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs dpyad pa bskyed rim rnam
bshad dang / dpyad don nyams su len pa sems 'dzin gyi rim pa gtong lugs sogs kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bzhed pa ma nor ba ltar sngon 'gro'i khrid thun mong ma yin pa bzhi/
rnal 'byor bcu gcig gi bskyed rim sems 'dzin zhar byung rdzogs rim dang bcas pa/ dngos gzhi'i rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma/ bde ba dang 'ja' lus sgrub pa/ 'pho ba/ nang gi mkha'
spyod sgrub pa sogs cha lag tshang ba'i nyams khrid/ rje btsun yab dang thun

mong ba'i rtsa dbu ma che ba'i nyams khrid shin tu rgyas pa/ yang nyin grangs bcad pa med par sgrub thabs kho na'i steng du khrid yig thams cad kyi brjod bya'i snying po bsdus
nas mdzub khrid kyi tshul du mdzad pa'i rgyun bzhugs pa bcas legs par thob nas/ rgyab brten lung gi skor la/ rtsa ba rgya gzhung / gdams skor/ sgrub thabs/ rnam bshad/
byin rlabs/ kha skong gi yi ge khrid yig dang bdun/ dang po ni/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub (edhIH)thabs/  gong ma'i mchan bu dang bcas pa 'di snying po lta bu med du
mi rung ba yin no/ / slob dpon nA ro ta pas mdzad pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ma ti dang dge slong pradznyA kIrtis bsgyur ba'o/ // /gnyis pa (edhIH)gdams skor la/ bskyed
rim phag mo mkha' spyod/ rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma/ thun mong gi dngos grub gnod sbyin mo dbang du byed pa/ lam gyi yan lag dang bzhi/ dang po la/ byin rlabs  bsdus don na
rjes gnang zer/ mjug na mkha' spyod sgrub tshul kyang cung zad yod/ kyi yi ge bu mo (edhIH)gzhon nu ma la ston mo bya ba dam tshig go'i mtha' can/ don 'grel  bskyed rim dngos/
rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub (edhIH)thabs la don bcu gcig gis nges par bya ba de ltar don bcu gcig go'i mtha' can/ spyod lam gyi rnal 'byor las 'phros nas
phyi mchod mdor bsdus (edhIH)bya tshul byang chub sems dpas bkrol ba'o'i mtha' can/  'di zhar byung byin rlabs kyi cho ga zhig yod kyang phyag len du mi mdzad ces brag
phug pa gsung / bskyed pa'i rim pa'i cha bzlas sgom gnyis la brten nas mkha' spyod kyi dngos grub (edhIH)sgrub pa bla ma'i

zhal gyi gdams pa rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ tshogs kyi mchod pa (edhIH)mdor bsdus pa rjes mi mngon par bya'o'i mtha' can/ tshes bcu'i mchod pa (edhIH)yi dam byed tshul nyes
pa thams cad 'dag par gsungs pa'i mtha' can/ rnal 'byor ma'i sbyin sreg rgyas pa (edhIH)bdag nyid la bsdu'o'i mtha' can/ mar me'i sbyin sreg gzhan la phan pa'i blos yi
ge ra bkod pa'i mtha' can rnams so/ /gnyis pa rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma'i zhal shes su kha 'phangs pa/ gsum pa thun mong gi dngos grub gnod sbyin mo dbang du byed pa la gnod
sbyin mo'i rtog pa las tshangs pa'i bu mo 'gugs pa man ngag tu byas pa rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/  'di la rgyud kyi dum bu'ang zer/ gnod sbyin mo padma pa ti'i sgrub thabs
yid du 'ong ba padma'i man ngag rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ de'i zhal shes yid du 'ong ba'i gnod sbyin mo sgrub pa rdzogs so'i mtha' can/  'di brag phug pa'i bsdus don na mi
gsal ba gong gi khongs su gtogs pa'i dbang du btang ba 'dra/ khol po pa ta na'i sgrub thabs zhes brjod do'i mtha' can rnams so/ /bzhi pa lam gyi yan lag la/ pra se na dbab
pa gdams ngag go'i mtha' can/ sman chen po'i bcud len thun mong ma yin pa'i gdams ngag go'i mtha' can rnams bla ma sa chen gyis mdzad pa/  'di rnams la rje btsun chen
po'i gsung mchan dang bcas pa rje grol mchog gi gsan yig na mchan de rnams slob dpon rin po ches mdzad ces bshad/ sa chen gyi yi ge de rnams kyi bsdus don brag phug pa'i
gsung sgros sa (edhIH)bcad bzhir mdzad pa cung zad kyang snang ngo'i mtha' can rnams so/ /gsum pa sgrub thabs la/ brgyud pa'i gsol

'debs rgyas (e)pa bsod nams ye shes ma ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i bsdus pa (dhIH)rdo rje 'chang chen ma/ tshar pa rdo rje 'chang gis stod lung spar
rdzong du mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs (dhIH)mchog gi padmo bzhad pa'i dga' ston nam rgyal ba rgya mtsho mar grags pa kha skong dang bcas pa/ rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i
brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs ngag (ma)dbang blo bzang rgya mtshos mdzad pa/ rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma la kha sbyor yan lag bdun ldan gyi sgo nas bstod pa ye shes chen
po'i mdzod 'dzin ma ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ dpal rdo rje rnal 'byor ma mkha' la spyod pa'i sgrub thabs 'phags pa rin po ches sa sbrul gdu bu'i zla ba la shangs

rang la bsdu'o'i mtha' can/ rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub thabs (dhIH)rgyun du nyams su blang ba'i ngag 'don gyi tshul tshar chen gyi gsung

rgyun gyi nyams len mdor bsdus pa bsnyel byang du bkod pa rnams so/ /bzhi pa rnam bshad la/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi dgongs pa nA ro ta pa'i man ngag gis bskyed pa'i

blang ba'i cho ga 'phags pa rin po ches lcags rta zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bco brgyad la shangs mdor mdzad pa/ 'gor ye shes mkha' 'gro ma lus pa'i/ /zhes yod pa'i byin rlabs
kyi yi ge rje sangs (edhIH)rgyas dpal bzang gis mdzad pa byin gyis brlab tu gsol gyi mtha' can/ byin rlabs (e)kyi cho ga rdo rje 'chang chen po A nanda bha dra'i gsung

ba'i cho ga (dhIH)mkha' spyod sgrub pa'i nye lam rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa/ yang byin rlabs kyi cho

ga sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad pa rnams so/ /drug pa kha skong la/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga go go can gyis bskul nas

rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa/ rje btsun nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i bsnyen pa bya tshul rgyal rtse pa ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa rnams so/

nas bsnyen pas mnyes par bya ba/ zhar

byung gtor ma'i cho ga gzhan don slob ma la phan gdags pa tshogs mchod dang bcas pa/ slob ma rjes gzung byin rlabs kyi yi ge zhar byung sindhU ra'i sgrub pa/ zhi ba'i sbyin
sreg mar me'i sbyin sreg za byed mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg khrus chog 'khor lo'i man ngag tshes bcu'i cho ga dang bcas pa rnams so/ /bdun pa khrid yig skor la dngos dang /
khyad par can rtsa dbu ma che ba'i khrid gnyis/ dang po la rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi phyag chen gces btus nas 'khor lo sdom pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan
gyis bris pa'i rtsa dbu ma'i khrid yig mgor/ bla ma dang rdo rje rnal 'byor ma la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zab yangs rgyud rgyal gsang mtha'i don zhes yod pa/ rgyud sde drug
pa'i rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i yang bcud dpa' mo mkha' spyod dga' ma'i nye lam rje btsun sa skya pa'i gser chos kyi nying khu he ru ka dpal tshar pa chos rje'i gsung bzhin
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses zin bris su mdzad pa'i khrid yig mkha' spyod bgrod pa'i nye lam 'di ni deng sang rnal 'byor bcu gcig gi steng du rtsa dbu ma'i khrid tsam bsnan
nas mkha' spyod ma'i khrid yin no zhes skad gsang mthon por sgrogs pa rnams dang ye mi 'dra ba'i nA ro pa'i gsang chen slob bshad kyi gnad 'gag thams cad tshang ba yin pas/

ma'i gsung gi nying khu yin/ /zhes rang bzo dang 'khrul pa'i dri ma phra mo tsam dang yang

bral ba'o/ /nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i bskyed (dhIH)rdzogs kyi zin bris dpal ldan rgyal po'i dngos slob bzang po dpal gyis brjed byang du mdzad pa/ yang bskyed rdzogs kyi bskyed
rim tshar pa rdo rje 'chang gi gsung rgyun (dhIH)dge slong ring mo pas zin bris su mdzad pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i sbyang gzhi sbyang tshul gyi man ngag shin tu zab pa
rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje'i gsung rgyun/ thun mong ma yin pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor nyams (dhIH)len gyi khrigs rim yongs grags dang cung zad mi mthun pa slob bshad
pa'i bzhed pa thun mong ma yin pa go rim 'khrul med du rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis bkod pa yun ring du gnas par gyur cig gi mtha' can/ sngags 'chang bsod
nams (wA)chos 'phel gyi gsung rgyun rnal 'byor bcu gcig nang bskyed rim lus dkyil sgom tshul/ rdzogs rim shin tu zab pa/ bsam mi khyab kyi zhal shes dang bcas pa mkhas grub
ngag dbang chos grags kyis zin bris su mdzad pa dngos grub myur mgyogs kyi pho nya/ rnal 'byor bcu gcig gi nyams len la sgro 'dogs gcod pa dang sems 'dzin zung 'brel
du gtong tshul mthong grol lde mig (zha)rgyal dbang rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa/ khrid kyi skabs gnyis bral 'chad dus zhal shes gsum gyi dang po thun mong ma yin pa

rig bsre'o'i mtha' can/ yang snga ma dang 'dra min gang (edhIH)gi khyod zhabs ma lo tsA ba'i gser chos/ 'pho ba 'di gnyis dang 'og nas 'byung ba'i mkha' spyod sgrub pa'i

gis 'phen yul au DyAna'i gzhis kar mdzad pa/ 'di'i nyams len la brten nas sa skya pa'i sngags 'chang mang po lus ma spangs par mkha' spyod du byon pa'i lo rgyus ngo mtshar
ba mtha' klas pa snang ngo / /mkha' spyod zhal bzang blta ba'i smon (dhIH)lam tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i bkra shis dge legs kyi dpal (edhIH)ster

zin bris su btab pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i rje btsun yab dang thun mong ba'i (dhIH)rtsa dbu ma che ba'i khrid yig yab dang thun

seng ge rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa skya lo tsA ba/ de gnyis ka las dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ 'jam mgon
dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ de las 'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub dang / kun mkhyen tshul khrims lhun grub/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang
kun dga' bstan 'dzin gsum gyis gsan/ de gsum ka las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis legs par nos so/ /yang na mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mkhan chen bkra
shis lhun

grub dang / mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyi ga las thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong dang / mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang gnyis kyis
gsan/ de las bdag gis legs par thob bo/ /yang na paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang las khri chen pa kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub dang / byams pa kun dga' bkra shis gnyis kyis
gsan/ gnyis char las shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas kyis gsan/ de las rje dam chos bsam grub/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs man 'dra/ yang na rje dkon mchog
lhun grub/ 'jam dbyangs chos 'od zer/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams man 'dra/ yang na rje btsun brang ti pa nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ rin po che dpal ldan don grub/ de
gnyis char las nam mkha' sangs rgyas kyis gsan nam snyam/ de nas rje dpal mchog man 'dra/ yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge 'jam dbyangs sangs
rgyas seng ge brang ti pa man 'dra'o/ /byin rlabs dang yi ge'i rtags med pa'i khrid lung dang bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan
yan chad gong ma ji lta ba bzhin las/ de nas rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug yar klungs pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal ba mchog dbyangs/ yab rje 'jam dbyangs
nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ rje btsun rdo ring kun spangs

pa chen po kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma blo ldan shes rab kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs
mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ sngags 'chang sangs rgyas rin chen/ khyab bdag mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen
rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ de las
bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen du bod pas rmor bsam gtan gling du legs par thob bo/ /tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dkyil chog gi steng nas byin rlabs dang / mkhan
chen ngag dbang chos grags pas mdzad pa'i khrid yig de'i kha 'gengs dang bcas pa'i steng nas bskyed rim rnal 'byor bcu gcig yan lag tu bcas pa dang / rdzogs rim rtsa
dbu ma kha 'byed pa'i man ngag bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i zhal shes/ yab yum gnyis la brten pa dang / yum rkyang la brten pa'i 'pho ba'i zhal shes dang
bcas nyams khrid smin rgyas su thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan yan gong bzhin la/ de nas yar klungs pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod
nams rgyal mchog bdag chen 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rdo ring kun spangs pa chen po/ tshar chen he ru ka dpal
blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rta

ra ba bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhas grub ngag dbang chos grags/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ sa skya pa 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/
grub dbang bsod nams mtha' yas/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug ngag dbang brtan pa rab rgyas/ spro mo lung pa grub dbang bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhas grub chen
po sangs rgyas bstan pa/ mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la dges
bzhin du sa dkar bsam 'grub gling du legs par stsal to/ /yang na ngag dbang chos grags nas/ rgyal rtse ba bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bstan pa rab rgyas man gong bzhin no/ /yang
na dbang phyug rab brtan nas/ de dbon bsod nams mchog ldan/ zhwa lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ de'i mchod dpon manydzu pa/ zhwa lu pa sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/
grub dbang sangs rgyas bstan pa man 'dra'o/ /yang na spro mo lung pa nas/ ngag dbang tshul khrims bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang bsod nams dbang phyug thams cad mkhyen pa
dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang byin rlabs dang a rtags can gyi lung khrid rkyang bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos rje bla ma dam pa yan gong ltar la/ de nas
dpal ldan tshul khrims/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa/ zhwa lu pa sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan rgyal

po/ mkhas pa bzang po dpal ba/ de dbon mus chen nam mkha' dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab
bstan 'dzin bzang po man 'dra/ yang byin rlabs gnyis khrid dhI'i rtags can gyi lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshar chen nas/ 'jam dpal dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang
phyug de las bslab gsum rje dang / bsod nams chos 'phel gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ 'dren mchog
snying rje bzang po/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po man 'dra/ yang byin rlabs dang sa'i rtags can gyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po las/
'jam mgon mkhyen brtse dang / klu sgrub rgya mtsho gnyis kyis gsan/ mkhyen brtse'i zhabs nas rje dbang rab/ khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ byams pa ngag dbang
rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa chen po/ ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ ngag dbang kun dga'
lhun grub man gong bzhin no/ /yang na tshar chen las klu sgrub rgya mtsho dang / sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las mkhan chen ngag dbang
chos grags/ de nas dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras 'jam dpal rdo rje bsod nams dbang phyug man 'dra/ yang bskyed rdzogs kyi
nyams khrid zhal

shes dor ba dang / byin rlabs e g.yung drung can gyi lung bcas kyi brgyud lugs gcig la/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po nas/ mus chen/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge mus chen
sangs rgyas rin chen/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang
po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' lhun grub/ kun mkhyen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen las/ rgyal
tshab kun dga' dbang phyug bsod nams dbang phyug gung ru shes rab bzang po/ mkhyen rab rdo rje 'chang bzhis gsan/ de bzhi ka las rje btsun rdo ring pas gsan pa man 'dra/
yang na gung ru shes rab bzang po dang / rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje gnyis las kun mkhyen shAkya don grub kyis gsan/ de nas 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ she'u
lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ de las ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje dang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po gnyis kyis gsan/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po nas/
byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang byin rlabs rkyang
pa'i brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ mus chen nas/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge byas 'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge rje sgo rum pa/ 'jam mgon

mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ 'khon sa skya pa chen po/ ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams man
'dra/ yang na dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ kun dga' lung rig sa/ sdom brtson sbyin pa grags pa/ dpal sa skya pa man 'dra/ yang na snying rje bzang po nas/ lo pa spyan snga
kun dga' don grub/ sa skya pa chen po man 'dra/ bha'i rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar
rtse pa chen po/ shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje/ khri chen bsod nams bstan 'dzin dbang po/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ rmor chen rdo
rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang byin rlabs rkyang pa'i brgyud lugs gcig la/ thar rtse pa/ shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ de dbon shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal
ldan/ sa skya pa chen po ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po nas/ gu ge paNDi ta grags
pa rgyal mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra'o/ /lcags rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni/
yang na ngor chen nas/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mang mkhar ba rab gsal zla ba mgon po/ rje grol mchog man 'dra/ yang na grol mchog nas/
ngag dbang nyi zla bzang

po/ rje btsun ngag dbang nyi ma/ lcags zam pa chen po kun dga' bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor
chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na rtse gdong khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ lcags zam pa chen po man 'dra/ yang na lo pa spyan snga kun
dga' don grub kyis 'dren mchog snying rje chen po las gsan/ spyan snga nas lcags zam pa chen po man 'dra'o/ /yang na sa paN nas yar sgom se bo/ do pa ston tshul/ de gsum
las rgyal tsha lung mang pos gsan/ de nas mkhas pa yon tan khri/ yar klungs pa seng ge rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na nyan chen pa nas/ dkar po brag pa/ yar klungs pa man
'dra'o/ /!/ /dmar mo skor gsum las rgyal po chen po indra bhU ti'i zhal snga nas kyis legs par bkral ba'i rje btsun ma indra mkha' spyod dam phag mo zhal gnyis mar grags
pa'i chos skor la/ rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i yi ge ltar paN chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs byin rlabs dang bcas pa'i go bde bklag chog tu
bkod pa rnams kyi steng nas sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor du byin rlabs zab mo legs par nos nas/ rgyab brten lung la mi dbang chos gsum du grags pa'i dang po/ rdo rje rnal 'byor
ma zhal gnyis ma'i sgrub pa au DyAn gyi slob dpon chen po mi dbang indra bhU tis mdzad pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal nA wenda pa dang / lo tsA ba pradznyA kIrtis bsgyur
ba/ gnyis pa des mkha' 'gro rgya

mtsho'i rgyud la brten nas mdzad pa'i rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sngags kyi de kho na nyid kyi rang byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa slob ma ye shes rdo rjes bsgyur ba/ gsum pa phag
mo'i las bcu zhes pa/ bsnyen pa'i cho ga gzhan don du slob ma rjes su gzung ba'i cho ga tshes bcu dang 'brel ba'i tshogs mchod/ bdag gzhan gnyis ka dang 'brel ba gzhon
nu ma'i mchod pa/ gnas skabs thams cad dang 'brel ba gtor ma'i cho ga dman pa'i dur khrod dang 'brel pa sbyin sreg gi cho ga bu chung gsar bu la phan 'dogs pa srung ba'i
'khor lo/ rtsub las gdug pa tshar gcod pa sumbha ni'i cho ga bsgom pas phyir bzlog pa dang / bris pas phyir bzlog pa rnams bla ma bha rendra ru tsis mdzad pa bal po ye shes
rdo rje dang bla ma mal lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/ mi dbang chos gsum gyi gsal byed rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma zhal gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs lag tu blang ba'i rim pa tseng
nge gtsang ston pas gsol ba btab pa la brten nas rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa/ sngags kyi de kho na nyid byin gyis brlab pa lag tu blang ba rdzogs pa'i rim pa tseng
nge 'dul 'dzin pas gsol ba btab nas rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa/ phag mo las bcu'i cho ga'i gsal byed tseng nge ston pa dge slong shes rab grags kyis gsol ba btab par
brten nas rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa/ 'gor bla ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal rdo rje rnal 'byor ma zhes yod pa'i gong ma'i gsung rgyun gyi zhal gnyis ma'i sgrub
thabs dngos grub thams cad thob par 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ zhal gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs paN chen grags

pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa ma ti tsi tras brag dkar chos sdings su sbyar ba'i mtha' can/ 'gor phag mo zhal gnyis ma 'di rgyal chen indra bhU tis mdzad pa 'dra yang zhes
yod pa'i byin rlabs kyi yi ge kun mkhyen gung rus mdzad pa rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'o'i mtha' can/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs byin
rlabs dang bcas pa'i cho ga go bde bklag chog tu bkod pa rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ grub chen lwa ba pa/ rgyal chen indra bhU
ti/ lcam lakShmI ka ra/ bram ze birWa pa/ grub chen sha ba ri pa/ mnga' bdag mai tri pa/ rgya gar phyag na rdo rje/ bal po bha rendra ru tsi/  ha ngu dkar po yang zer/
bal po ye shes rdo rje/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ chos
kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bkra shis/
kwanting gu shrI nam mkha' bzang po/ nyi lde ba ngag dbang grags pa/ bdag chen rgya gar ba shes rab rgyal mtshan/ gcung bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje
btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhas grub ngag dbang
chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ bdag chen ngag dbang kun dga' bkra

shis/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhan grub/ mkhas grub chen po 'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen
la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/
/yang na ngor chen nas/ gu ge paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa/ rje btsun sgo rum pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen
brtse'i zhabs man 'dra'o/ /yang na ngor chen nas mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ mkhan chen ratna shI la/ rje sangs rgyas dpal/ sgo rum pa
man 'dra/ yang rtsa ba'i brgyud lugs gcig la/ bram ze birWa pa nas/ a bhi dzukta/ bal po ha ngu dkar po/  bal skad du sngags pa la 'di skad zer zhes chag lo gsung ngo / /
lo tsA ba ye shes rdo rje man 'dra/ yang na sha ba ri pa nas/ a wa dhU tI pa/ a dwa ya badzra/ grub chen badzra pA Ni/ bal po bha rendra ru tsi man 'dra/ yang na a wa dhU
tI nas/ ldeng ngar ba ting nge 'dzin rdo rje/ bsod snyoms pa che ba ma ti badzra/ bsod snyoms pa chung ba ma ti bha dra/ bal po bha rendra ru tsi man 'dra/ nye brgyud ni/
rje btsun rdo rje phag mo nas/ bal po bha rendra ru tsi man 'dra'o/  bal po thugs rje chen po yang zer/ /!/ /sgyu 'phrul drwa ba chen mo ral pa gyen brdzes kyi rgyud la
brten nas slob dpon mai tri pas legs par bkral ba'i rdo rje rnal 'byor ma rig pa 'dzin pa rtsen ma'am mai tri mkha' spyod

du grags pa'i chos skor la/ spro lung pa kun dga' smon lam gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge dang paN chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge la brten nas sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor
du byin rlabs legs par nos nas/ rgyab brten lung la/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo ral pa gyen brdzes kyi rgyud las phyung ba'i rig pa 'dzin ma rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs
rgya gar gyi mkhan po dza ya'i zhabs dang sum pa lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan gyis bsgyur ba/ rdo rje phag mo rig pa 'dzin pa rtsen ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon gnyis med 
rje btsun mai tri pa/ rdo rjes mdzad pa rje btsun dza ya shrI sen dang sum pa lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/ rig pa 'dzin pa rtsen ma rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i rjes su gnang ba'i cho
ga mkhas pa chen po rgyal ba'i sdes mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang btsun pa dar ma yon tan gyis bsgyur ba/ rdo rje 'dzin pa grags pa gzhon nu sogs kyis bskul nas mkha'
spyod sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa spro lung pa kun dga' smon lam gyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i bstod pa yon tan mtha' yas ma/ paN chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis
mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang byin rlabs kyi cho ga go bde bklag chog tu bkod pa rnams legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ dpa' bo spyan ras
gzigs/ byang sems blo gros rin chen/ ri khrod dbang phyug  sha ba ri zer/ grub chen mai tri pa/  gnyis med rdo rje/ rgya gar phyag na rdo rje/ ka ma la badzra/  mtsho skyes
rdo rje/ paNDi ta dza ya se na/ sum pa lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan/ rje btsun chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje

sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ theg chen rin po
che/ kwanting gu shrI nam mkha' bzang po/ nyi lde ba ngag dbang grags pa/ gcen bdag chen rgya gar ba shes rab rgyal mtshan/ gcung bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal
mtshan/ rje btsun rdo ring kun spangs pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po blo gsal rgya mtsho/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/
mkhas grub ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ bdag chen ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin
lhun grub/ bka' drin can 'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis nos so/ /yang na mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub las/ thams cad
mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na brag phug pa nas/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ ngor chen rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa/ de las gung ru shes rab bzang po dang mkhyen rab chos rje gnyis kyis gsan/ rje ratna shI la/ sangs rgyas dpal/
rje sgo rum pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na spyan ras gzigs nas/ ri khrod dbang phyug a wa dhU tI pa/ smr-i ti/ ka la ma badzra/ lI la ya badzra/ lo tsA ba
dar ma yon tan/ rje btsun grags pa man

'dra/ yang nye brgyud ni/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma nas/ mai tri pa/ nam mkha'i paNDi ta/ bla ma a/ shAkya rakShi ta/ ka na ka shrI/ dza ya se na man 'dra/ yang na bla ma a/ dza
ya se na man 'dra/ yang na lo ke shwa ra nas/ ri khrod pa dbang phyug man 'dra/ rgyud nas phyung ba'i sgrub thabs kyi lung brgyud lugs gcig ni/ 'phags pa rin po che nas/
dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bla ma dam pa man 'dra/ yang na bla ma dam pa nas/ ma ti paN chen/ theg chen chos rje man chad gong bzhin no/ /!/ /rmor
chen rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang bsam 'phel nor bu'i steng nas rje btsun sa skya pa'i gser chos kyi nang tshan tshe dpag med sprul
sku'i rjes su gnang ba legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po tshe dpag med/ dze tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med pa/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ ba
ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ brtse chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi
ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ mkhas grub do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug rin chen seng ge bzang po/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug
yar klungs pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog bdag chen 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po/ rje btsun rdo ring kun spangs pa chen po/ rdo rje

'chang tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rje btsun
rin chen rgya mtsho/ dol paN phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rigs kun khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa' ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin
du stsal to/ /rje btsun bsod nams rtse mos mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang bcas kyi lung yang thos so/ /!/ /dpal sa skya pa'i gser chos thun mong ma yin pa 'jam dpal
nag po'i skor la/ tshom bu la brten pa'i sku gsung thugs kyi byin rlabs bzlas lung dang bcas pa khyad par can legs par thob nas/ lung la 'jam dpal nag po'i gnad bcu gcig
dang ldan pa'i gdams ngag nyams su len tshul zhar byung shin tu rtsub cing rnam rtog ches za ba'i tshe bya tshul phan yon dang bcas pa nyams su myong bas kyang grub po'i
mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dang rje btsun 'jam dpal dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'jam dpal nag po sgom par 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge rjes bsngo ba sogs bya'o'i
mtha' can/ gu ge paN chen gyis bdag chen ma dkon mchog rgyal po'i don du mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ tshar pa rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs gnad bcu gcig gi
man ngag dang bcas pa rnams legs par thob pa'i nang nas rgyu 'gul paN chen gyis mdzad pa ma gtogs pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ gsang
ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje/ dze tA ri dgra las rnam

rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med pa/  che ba/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/  chung ba/ lo tsA ba rin chen grags pa/ brtse chen sa skya pa kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po
che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag
phug pa/ lam 'bras pa ye shes dpal/ blo bzang dkar mo/ dkon mchog thugs rje/ gling smad paNDi ta shes rab dpal ldan/  'di rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i slob ma yin/
gong dkar rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ slob dpon rin po che chos mchog mdo khams bla chen yon tan rgya mtsho/ gong dkar ba tshe dbang bkra shis/ mtshungs med rnam
rgyal bkra shis/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang
kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhan po chen po lhun grub dpal ldan/ bstan pa'i sgron me sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ de las bdag
tshul khrims rin chen gyis lan gsum bar du nos so/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ de las bdag gis thos so/ /yang na sangs
rgyas phun tshogs nas/ bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong dang / mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas dpal bzang / de gnyis ka las bdag tshul khrims rin
chen gyis nos so/ /yang na

sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la gnad bcu gcig gi
bsgom lung 'bogs pa dang bcas pa legs par stsal to/ /yang na glo bo mkhan chen nas/ lha mchog seng ge sangs rgyas seng ge thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ yang
na zhang dkon mchog dpal nas/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ 'jam skya nam mkha' dpal ldan/ bla ma mnyam med pa/ bla ma shAkya pa/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge paN  rgyu 'gul paN chen 'di pa'i mtshan gyi rnam grangs yin/ chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa
lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ 'khor lo'i mgon po mkhyen
rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ bka' drin gzhal med ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/
/yang na rgyu 'gul paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs sa paN nas/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ 'jam skya man 'dra/ yang na zhang dkon mchog dpal ba nas/ rgyal
ba bsod nams dpal/ brag phug pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ ye shes dpal man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /yang na dkon mchog rgyal mtshan nas/ sa skya bu ston dbang phyug dar/ theg
chen kun dga' bkra

shis/ spyan snga kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga bsod nams lha dbang / spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan/ she'u lo tsA ba kun dga' chos grags/ mkhyen rab bstan
'dzin bzang po man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ 'phags pa rin po che/ spang sgang pa grags pa seng ge bla ma byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros man 'dra'o/
/!/ /rje btsun sa skya pa'i gser chos mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong pa can gyi skor la/ sindhU ra'am rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor la brten nas seng gdong ma nag mo'i
sku gsung thugs kyi rjes su gnang ba khyad par can/ thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang pas mdzad pa'i yi ge la brten nas legs par thob nas/ rgyab brten lung la/ 'gor rgya
gar skad du/ tsakra saM bha ra ma hA ya na sU tra zhes yod pa'i ba ri bas gter bton nas mu stegs skal ldan rgyal po btul ba'i lo rgyus/  mu stegs bsad pas lo bcu gnyis rdo
rje gdan pas mjal kha ma btang zer ba 'dug bod du byon nas sa chen kun dga' snying po la gnang ngo / /de nas rim bzhin brgyud do'i mtha' can/ gnyis pa las tshogs la nyi
shu rtsa lnga yod pa las/ 'gor sgrub thabs ni skyabs 'gro sems bskyed spyi dang 'dra zhes yod pa'i mngon rtogs gnyis su med par gyur nas bzhugs par bsam mo'i mtha' can/
bzlog pa'i dmigs pa dang dus gnad/ gsod pa'i dmigs gnad/ zhar byung sku smad phur bus bgegs bsgral zhing ngag gnon thabs/ mtshan bcas mtshan med kyi bsrung ba mo'i g.yas
la btags so de ni bsrung ba'o'i mtha'

can/ seng gdong ma dkar mo'i tshe sgrub tshe nyi zla dang mnyam par 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ nor sgrub 'bum tsho gcig bzlas pas 'grub bo'i mtha' can/ seng gdong dmar mo'i dbang
sdud gser srang do'i bka' rgya yod do'i mtha' can/ sri'u gso ba gser 'bul dgos gsungs pa'i mtha' can/ char 'bebs tha ma lnga la mi 'bab mi srid do'i mtha' can/ mtshan med
kyi char gcod ri mgo thams cad me ris khengs par bsgom pa'i char gcod pa'i man ngag go'i mtha' can/ bye ma la brten pa'i 'bu srung / chu la brten pa'i sad srung / mtshan
med kyi ser srung man ngag zhal shes so'i mtha' can/ mtshan bcas mtshan med kyi thog srung thub po'i mtha' can/ dkar gong la brten nas lug nad gcod pa/ bal skud la brten
nas g.yag nad gcod pa/ chu la brten nas lhog pa bsrung ba/ rdzas gnyis kyi dud pas rims bsrung ba/ sran mas 'brum bu bsrung ba/ khyi bal gyis 'khru ba gcod pa/ me btsas
'go yor bsrung ba/ 'dogs pa'i mtshon srung man ngag zhal shes so'i mtha' can/ gu gul gyis gza' nad 'chos pa/ dmigs pas jag pa 'ching ba ste las tshogs nyi shu rtsa gsum
mkha' 'gro'i gdams pa rgya mtsho'i nang nas zab mo chu thigs tsam zhig bkod pa/ 'gor skyabs 'gro sems bskyed ces yod pa'i khyad par gyi bzlog pa dam tshig pa rang la bsdu'o'i
mtha' can/ mngon rtogs shin tu gnyan pas gsang bar bya ba'i mtha' can/ 'gor mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong pa can la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'di'i rjes gnang byed par 'dod
pas zhes yod pa'i rjes gnang gi

yi ge bla ma ba ri lo tsA ba la gdams pa'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor na mo DA ki nI ya mkha' 'gro ma'i man ngag ces yod pa'i yi ge bcu bzhi'i las tshogs dang bcas pa rnams so/ /gnyis
pa gong dkar ba nas brgyud pa la/ 'gor mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong pa can la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'di'i rjes gnang byed par 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i yi ge mi dag las mang
ba la sbyin pa med do zhes dam bcas nas bla ma rdo rje gdan pas ba ri lo tsA bar gdams pa'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma yi dam mkha' 'gro'i tshogs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gdams
pa 'di'i lo rgyus bla ma ba ri lo tsA ba dang mu stegs skal ldan rgyal po zhes yod pa'i lo rgyus dang sdig sbyong du gser gyi gsung rab bris gsungs pa'i mtha' can/ mtshan
bcas kyi srung bas byad kha mkhan po kho rang la bzlog pa/ thal rdab kyis dgra 'chi ba/ ting nge 'dzin gyis ngag gnon pa/ sngags kyis phyogs ngan bdud gcod bsrung ba/ bzlas
pa'i mchil mas mtshon bsrung ba/ rkang 'og gi sas g.yul gyi rang phyogs kun bsrung ba/ sngags kyis jag pa 'ching ba/ mkha' 'gro ma dmar mos nor dang tshe sgrub cing bsod
nams spel ba/ rmi lam ngan pa bzlog par kha gtod pa'i gnad/ dri chus rims nad bsrung ba/ bsnyen tshad dang sham bu'i zhal shes/ seng gdong dmar mo la brten pa'i khyad
par gyi bzlog pa bsam pa'i don rnams thams cad 'grub bo'i mtha' can/ phyir bzlog man ngag tshigs bcad ma zhal gdams bla ma'i man ngag las byung ngo'i mtha' can/ rdo rje
phag mo zhal gsum

phyag drug pa'i mngon rtogs dang / bzlas pas thun mong gi dngos grub mi rtogs pa/ sgrib pa sreg pa/ drod bskyed pa/ gzhan gyi bgegs bzlog pa bcas bstan pa mkha' 'gro ma bdag
gis dbang du sdud do'i mtha' can/ gtor ma gtong ba dang bskul ma mo mkha' 'gro ma zhar byung mo mchod dang bcas pa badzra DA ki nI ye 'grub bo'i mtha' can 'gor/ na mo gu
ru bla ma rdo rje gdan pa zhes yod pa'i kha phyogs/ 'dug stangs/ mngon rtogs/ mtheb mdzub kyi dmigs pa/ ma gcig ye shes ma'i bstod pa dang bcas pa rnams rdzogs par thob
pa las/ rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen dze tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal ba/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba mya ngan med pa/ paNDi ta don yod rdo
rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/
'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa chen po/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rje
kun dga' bkra shis/ rje ngang tshul bzang ba/ 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ rje rong po blo bzang pa/ skyid shod 'bras spungs kyi mkhan thog tu phebs pa gsang
sngags kyi bdag po zhig yin kyang mtshan nyid kyi TI ka ma byung zhes ma gus pa byung zhes gleng / rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ lo chen chos skyong bzang po/ sa lo
'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ mtshungs med dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar

chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ rje btsun kun dga' legs pa/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ de
nyid nas thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis thob bo/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ bsod nams dpal ldan dang
bstan 'dzin lhun grub gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong gis gsan/ de las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis lan mang du thob
bo/ /yang na 'phags pa nas dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/
rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas/ khro phu ba bsod nams
seng ge yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge kun mkhyen bu ston rin po che/ khyung lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ mkhan chen bkra shis rin chen/ skal ldan grags pa/ 'khrul zhig
tshul khrims rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /ngor nas brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa rin po che yan rjes gnang gi brgyud pa dang 'dra zhing / de nas dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ dga'
ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang

po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/
mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dpal rdo rje bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ rmor
chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ kun mkhyen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin stsal to/ /yang na rmor chen pa nas/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang
sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na ngor chen nas/ mkhyen rab rje/ zhwa lu lo chen chos skyong bzang po/ sa lo man gong ltar ro/ /gong
dkar ba nas brgyud pa'i lung gi brgyud pa bcas btsal dgos so/ /!/ /dpal sa skya pa'i gser chos mkha' lding rdo rje khyung khra'i rjes su gnang ba thun mong ma yin pa legs
par thob nas/ lung la 'gor gu ru badzra ga ru TA ya na maH'dir mkha' lding ye shes khyung khra sgrub par 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i sgrub thabs 'dod don gsol ba gdab/ dge
ba bsngo ba'i mtha' can/ mjug tu bstod pa shlau ka gcig yod pa/ gtor ma 'bul na dkar gsum mngar gsum zhes yod pa'i gtor 'bul gyi cho ga khang pa'i sa dgra ngan pa sogs thub
bo'o'i mtha' can/ bong nga za bar 'dod na zhes yod pa'i bong nga bsten thabs mi tshugs par 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ khyi smyon gso thabs tshar gcod pa'i mtha' can/ gnyan
gso ba gsal bar bya'o'i mtha'

can/ srung skud gdags pa/ sman la brten nas mdze gso ba ril bu sbyor thabs sgrub pa sogs rgyas par bstan pa sa skya pa'i gser chos bcu gsum pa'i ya gyal gcig go'i mtha' can/
bstod pa sa yi rang bzhin rnam dag ma rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa/ bzlas lung ster ba'i man ngag rdzogs byang gi mtha' can rnams kyi lung bcas legs par thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / chos rgyal zla ba bzang po/ 'jam dpal grags pa/ padma dkar po/ dus zhabs che chung gnyis/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham mthing sku mched/ mal lo blo
gros grags pa/ brtse chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ chos rgyal blo gros rgyal mtshan/
zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun
dga' bzang po/ paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ rje lha mchog sengge/ sangs rgyas sengge/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / smra ba'i nyi
ma kun dga' bsod nams/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ bka' drin zla bral ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin
chen la'o/ /yang na mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas nas/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ kun mkhyen dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse pa man 'dra/ yang na sa lo nas/ mus chen

nam mkha' dbang phyug she'u lo tsA ba kun dga' chos grags/ ngag dbang chos legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen
bstan pa'i sgron me kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /!/ /dpal sa skya pa'i gser chos lcags ri mi 'da' ba bcu gsum gyi steng du gcig bsnan pa'i klu pa'i gser chos bcu
bzhir grags pa'i ya gyal sengge sgra'i ngag bsrung 'grol gyi man ngag shin tu zab pa'i mthar thug myong bas thon pa'i brgyud pa ni gong gi rje btsun sengge sgra'i skabs
su song ngo / /smras pa/ rnam gsum grub pa'i dbang phyug gis bkral ba'i/ /mkha' spyod gsum gyi byin rlabs tshe dpag med/ /'jam dpal la sogs gser chos gdams pa'i skor/ /thos
pa'i rna lung yangs 'di bla ma'i drin/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ gser chos mkha' spyod skor gsum gyi chos skor thos
pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste nyer gnyis pa'o/ // /bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa'i gser chos bcu gsum gyi nang tshan khyad par gyi gdams pa thun mong bsgrubs
pas mchog zhar la 'grub pa dmar po skor gsum du grags pa la/ rjes 'brangs kyi mkhas pa rnams kyi bzhed tshul mi 'dra ba mang na'ang 'dir rje btsun ma sgrol ma dmar mo
ku ru kulle/ tshogs bdag bgegs kyi rgyal po dmar chen/ khro bo kag chol 'dod pa'i rgyal po gsum las/ dang po ku ru kulle'am rje btsun rigs byed ma'i chos skor rnams kye
rdor rtsa bshad kyi rgyud dang ku ru kulle'i rtog

pa las 'byung zhing / de la'ang sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang rgya mtsho sogs su grags pa'i thun mong ba dang / thun mong ma yin pa gnyis las/ 'dir thun mong ma yin pa zur bka'
dpa' bo rdo rje dang ga ya dha ra'i man ngag 'brog mi lo tsA ba las brgyud pa/ lhan skyes rol pa dang Dombi pa'i man ngag ba ri ba las brgyud pa/ gnyan gyi gdams pa sogs
bka' babs mang du bzhugs pa'i man ngag gi rim pa rnams tshar pa rdo rje 'chang gi dkar chag bzhin tshang bar mnos pa la/ tshom bu la brten nas phyi sgrub sku gsung thugs
kyi rjes su gnang ba tshar lugs thun mong ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi yi ge la brten nas ngor lugs thun
mong ma yin pa'i phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang / dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyi yi ge dang zur 'debs dpal ldan bla ma gzungs kyi dpal bas mdzad pa dang dam pa'i phyag len 'khrul
med la brten nas kha'u pa'i lugs kyi nang sgrub thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang / so 'jigs med grags pa'i yi ge dang mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i byin
rlabs kyi yi ge gsal ba'i sgron ma'i steng nas sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor gsang sgrub ku ru ku lle lha lnga'i byin rlabs dbang bzhi'i tshul du bskur ba rnams legs par nos
nas/ rgyab brten lung gi skor las/ thog mar dpal ldan sa skya pa'i khyad par gyi gser chos dmar po skor gsum zhes grags pa'i chos skor gyi dkar chag dbang sdud padma rA
ga'i za ma tog gi kha 'byed gnad kyi lde mig tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen

pos mdzad pa/ de las byung ba'i ku ru kulle'i chos skor la/ bla chen dang ba ri thun mong nas brgyud pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i dngos grub 'byung ba/ Dombi he ru ka nas brgyud
pa/ bkras rnam pa'i yi ge dkar chag tu ma bzhugs pa'i chos skor dang lnga/ dang po brgyud pa'i lo rgyus rjes gnang dang bcas pa (sgo)(glo)dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis
mdzad pa btsun pa A nandas bris pa brjed byang ngo'i mtha' can/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sgrub thabs 'di'i lo rgyus ni zhes 'gor yod pa'i lo  'di na ma
hA rA dza zer ba dang sa ha dza zhes pa rgyal po ste lhan skyes kyi skad dod las rol pa'i gsal kha med/ rgyus sgrub thabs 'di ma hA rA dzas mdzad do sa ha dza pa'i las so'i
mtha' can/ thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs dbang bzhi'i zur 'debs gzungs kyi dpal ba'i gsung las buddha shrIs zin bris su bkod pa/ ku ru kulle'i sgrub thabs las sbyor
rtsa rgyud brtag gnyis kyi brtag pa dang po'i le'u bcu gcig pa las phyung ba/ sngags btu ba brtag gnyis sngags kyi le'u las phyung ba/ dpal kye rdo rje'i rgyud kyi rim
pa las bdag byin gyis brlabs pa'i ku ru kulle'i sgrub (sgo)(glo)thabs kyi rgya gzhung rgyal po lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang ba ri lo tsA bas
bsgyur ba/ slob dpon chen po lhan skyes sgeg pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs (glo)dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ mang du thos pa'i slob dpon ku mA ra bo dhis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/
rigs ldan ma'am ku ru kulle'i sgrub thabs (sgo)(glo)ma taM gis mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje las byung ba'i man (sgo)(glo)ngag chen po

lnga slob dpon zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ shAkya 'tshos mdzad pa'i man ngag rnam pa lnga dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi gdams (sgo)(glo
)pa rje btsun chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs (sgo)kyi rim pa 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa/  dkar chag na mi gsal yang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen
brtses sgo rum par gsan pa'i yi ge ra bstod pa dang bcas zer ba 'dug pas brtse bas rjes chags ma zhes bya ba shlau ka gcig pu de'o/ / las sbyor gyi man (sgo)(glo)ngag
paNDi ta don yod rdo rjes bla ma ba ri bar gnang ba/ nus pa ma nyams pas khams gsum dbang du byed pa paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/ dbu na yi
ge yaM yongs su gyur pa zhes yod pa'i rdzas sbyor gyi yi ge gla rtsir bcas pa'i du bas mi'i ming rus la bdugs na dbang du 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ gtor ma'i cho ga tshigs bcad
(sgo)(glo)ma nyung ngu yar klungs pas mdzad pa/ las kyi mtha' sdud sbyin sreg (glo)tshigs bcad ma rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ rje btsun ma'i bris sku'i cho ga (sgo)rdzogs
byang gi mtha' can/ gsung rdo rje ma'i lag sgul (sgo)thams cad yid 'phrog par 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ ku ru kulle gzhon nu ma'i sgrub (sgo)thabs/ rje btsun ma'i bka' sdod po
nya (sgo)gnod sbyin mo sku mdog ser mo'i man ngag ku ru kulle sku mdog sngon mo'i char 'bebs kyi yi ge bka' bsgo drag tu bya'o'i mtha' can/ sgrub thabs nag po 'gro shes
('khon)khams gsum dbang du bsdu ba'i gnad yig gadgA'i chu

rgyun/ 'di ni dus gcig la snod ldan gyi slob bu gcig la chig brgyud ma gtogs mang por mi spel ba'i bka' rgya dang phyag len gyi rgyun ma nyams pa yod cing / de'i rgyu mtshan
yang dkar chag tu/ blo chung thun mong gdams pas tshim/ /'byor ldan lung med yig hrul sdud/ /shes 'dod grags pa'i rjes su 'brang / /de dag chu 'dod smig rgyur snyeg/ ces
pa'i ngang tshul dang ye mi 'dra bar slob dpon lhan skyes rol pa nas bzung ste rje btsun kun spangs chen po'i bar du tshad ma bzhi ldan gyi snyan brgyud gdams pa'i ngad
ma yal ba'i zab gnad dang ldan pas/ ji skad du/ kho bos dam pa'i zhabs pad ring du bsten/ /snyan brgyud bdud rtsi'i zhal 'od snying la shar/ /'khrul med gdams pa'i gnad
la nges pa thob/ /grogs dag 'di 'dra'i skal bzang kho bo tsam/ /zhes gsungs pa snying la bcang bar bya'o/ /bdag nyid nus ldan du bya ba dang lingga'i snying gar 'jug pa'i
'khor lo'i zhal shes kyi yig chung bka' rgya shin tu dam pa rnams so/ /!/ /gnyis pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i dngos grub 'byung ba'i skor la/ bsnyen pa/ lha dbang du byas
nas don bsgrub pa/ klu dbang du byas nas char dbab cing nor bsgrub pa/ gnod sbyin dbang du byas nas zang zing bsgrub pa/ mi ma yin dbang du byas te srog 'phrog pa/ rmi
lam ngan pa bzlog pa/ shes rab 'phel ba/ sri'u gso ba rnams ston pa khams gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa ko sa lar
'khrungs pa'i bai ro tsa na'i rang 'gyur/ de'i lag len gyi yig sna la lo rgyus/ zhi

ba'i dkyil 'khor du bsnyen pa/ rgyas pa'i dkyil 'khor du khrol bu/ drag po'i dkyil 'khor du dib ma/ dbang gi dkyil 'khor du ril bu bsgrub pa/ bye brag lha klu gnod sbyin mi
ma yin dbang du bsdu ba/ 'chi bslu/ shes rab 'phel ba/ sri'u bsrung ba rnams ston pa ko sa lar 'khrungs pa'i brtul zhugs spyod pa rnam par snang mdzad rdo rjes yi ge ra
bkod pa/ brgyud pa sgrub pa char dbab pa ste don gsum gyis bstan pa'i klu'i rgyal po wa ru Na'i char 'bebs rgya gar bai ro tsA na'i rang 'gyur du mdzad pa/ char chog gi yig
sna rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ 'gor yang na rang gi dben khang nas zhes yod pa'i gong gi zhal shes dznyA na shrI dharma'o'i mtha' can/ las sbyor gsum pa zhes pa char dbab
pa/ rgyal po/ skyes pa/ bud med/ nor/ mi ma yin pa/ phyag rgya ma/ sngags pa rnams dbang du bya ba/ klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i ku ru kulle'i sa dpyad rdzogs so'i mtha'
can/ 'gor bla ma dam pa la na mo byang chub sems kyi phang la zhes yod pa'i sgrub thabs chung ngu greng greng sha swA hA'i mtha' can no/ /gsum pa Dombhi he ru ka nas brgyud
pa la/ 'gor bla ma'i gsung las byung ba yi zhes yod pa'i slob ma rjes su gzung ba'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga tshigs bcad rdzogs so'i mtha' can  'di dkar chag na mdzad pa
po mi gsal yang rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na sa paN gyis mdzad zer ba snang / 'gor rjes gnang 'di thun mong ba min zhes yod pa'i slob ma rjes su gzung ba'i byin rlabs
kyi lag len shin tu gsal ba yang yig tu grags pa bla ma mnyam med pas mdzad pa sngon chad yi

ger med pa yi ge ra bkod pa bzod par gsol lo'i mtha' can/ sgrub(glo)thabs Dombi he ru kas mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i bstod pa (glo)mi 'gyur ma/ bcom ldan 'das ku ru kulle la
phyag 'tshal lo 'dir rje btsun ma ku ru kulle mos pa zhes 'gor yod pa'i bsnyen pa'i yi ge rdul tshon rgya mtshor 'bab pa'i chu bor dor ba'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dam pa
rnams la phyag 'tshal lo rje btsun ma ku ru kulle dbang du bya ba'i man ngag ces yod pa'i rje btsun ma'i bsgrub pa'i rim pa dang las sbyor gyi rim pa rdzogs so'i mtha' can/
bsnyen sgrub las gsum chig sgril gyi man ngag zab pa sa skya pa chen po shin tu dam par mdzad pa snod ldan gcig brgyud ma gtogs pa shin tu gsang ba/ de'i thun mong ma
yin pa'i zhal shes nyi shu rtsa gcig bar ma chod pa'o'i mtha' can/ zhal shes kyi yig chung snying dang 'dra bas su la yang mi sbyin no'i mtha' can/ yig chung gi yang yig
bzlas pa byed zer ba bde legs so'i mtha' can/ gsang sgrub kyi skor 'dir thor bu tsam ma gtogs cha tshang ba ye med pas dpe su byung la mi ston pa'i bka' rgya yod tshul dkar
chag tu 'dug pa bzhin snying la bcang bar bya'o/ /bzhi pa rje bkra shis rnam rgyal pas mdzad pa'i yi ge ni rje btsun ma ku ru kulle phyi nang gsang gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub
las sbyor dang bcas pa'i yi ge shin tu rgyas pa shar dwags po'i paNDi ta bkra shis rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ lnga pa dkar chag tu ma bzhugs pa'i yi ge la rje btsun rigs
byed ma byon tshul yid 'phrog padma rA ga'i chun po 'a zhwa artha siddhis mdzad pa/ chos tshan gcig tu tshang ba'i dmar po

skor gsum gyi rjes gnang gi gsal byed rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis mdzad pa/ 'phags ma ku ru kulle'i man ngag gi rim pa zhes bskyed rim/ bsam gtan gyi sbyor ba/
sbyin sreg 'khrul 'khor/ las sna tshogs pa ste rim pa lngar phye nas bstan pa'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang ba ri lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ ku ru kulle'i rgyun gyi
rnal 'byor du bya ba'i rim pa ngag 'don gyi sgrub thabs tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs srid gsum dbang mdzad ma/ des mdzad pa'i bstod pa rgyal ba'i
ye shes ma/ sbyin sreg gi yi ge 'phags pa rin po che blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ gnad yig nag po 'gro shes kyi zhal 'phangs sbyin sreg gi yi ge brag dmar mkhan
chen rab brtan dpal bas bskul bar brten nas tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ bsam gtan kho nas las la sbyor ba'i gser chos snying gi yang zhun chig brgyud ma/ gsang sgrub lha
lnga'i byin rlabs kyi yi ge rig pa 'dzin pa gwa chen gyis bskul ba'i ngor so 'jigs med grags pas mdzad pa/ gsang sgrub lha lnga'i byin rlabs kyi sgo dbye ba sbyor dngos
rjes gsum pa zhal shes zab mo yi ge ra bkod pa'i mtha' can/ lha lnga'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga gsal ba'i sgron me mkhan chen 'jam dpal dbyangs ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad
pa rnams dang / dpe'u ris la/ sgrub pa'i maNDal sgrub rdzas dang bcas pa/ rang nyid nus ldan du bya ba'i 'khor lo/ lingga'i snying gar 'jug pa'i 'khor lo/ de dang 'dra
min gcig sbyin sreg gi thab/ klu sgrub kyi rgya gzhung

dngos sgrub 'byung gnas kyis don kun sgrub pa/ lha klu sogs dbang sdud spyir dril gyi 'khor lo/ char dbab pa'i dkyil 'khor/ sbrul dang sbal bar 'jug pa'i phyed mtha'i tsakra/
ril bu 'khor lo can/ rlung gnon 'khor lo/ nor sgrub 'khor lo/ sri'u gso ba'i 'khor lo dang bcas pa rnams phyag len dmar khrid du legs par thob pa las sa dpyad lnga pa'i
thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge dang / sindhU ra'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga gsum dor ba'i thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang sa bcad dang po dang lnga
pa'i lung klu rtags can dang man ngag tshang bar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma ku ru kulle/ rgyal po lhan skyes rol pa/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med pa/ paNDi ta
a mo gha badzra/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags pa/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa
rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ glo bo lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ rgyal tsha chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan
khri/ mkhan chen sengge bzang po/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal ba mchog dbyangs/ yab rje 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'
rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ rdo rje 'chang tshar chen chos kyi
rgyal po/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mthu stobs dbang phyug bsod nams chos 'phel/ khyab bdag

dbang phyug rab brtan/ de gnyis char las mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ rje btsun ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po dpal sa skya pa
chen po thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ snyan brgyud rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag
ngag gi dbang po tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po nas/ rje btsun bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga mi pham chos
kyi rgya mtsho/ khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra/ yang na mkhyen brtse'i zhabs nas rje btsun gzhon nu stobs ldan/ rje dbang rab man 'dra/ yang rjes gnang gnyis
kyi brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po nas/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse/ yab sras gnyis ka las rje dbang rab kyis gsan pa man 'dra/ yang na mkhyen brtse'i
zhabs nas/ bslab gsum rje/ rdo rje 'chang dbang rab man 'dra'o/ /yang ngor lugs kyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa skya paNDi
ta yan gong ltar las/ de nas 'u yug  rgyal dbang dang rmor chen pa'i gsan yig tu 'u yug pa bsod nams sengge zhes byung ba brtag pa kun dga' bsod nams/ nyi thog pa kun smon/
bla ma yon tan dpal/ pu lung pa kun dga' rdo rje/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ chos rje brag phug pa/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/
shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun

dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rje lha mchog seng ge des rje buddha singha dang shar khang pa gnyis la gnang / de gnyis char
las paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / de nas dbon nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin
lhun grub/ bka' drin rmad byung 'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la dges bzhin du stsal to/ /yang na mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs
nas/ rje bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ kun mkhyen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen can la'o/ /yang na dga' ldan pa kun bsod nas/ bag ston gzhon
tshul/ bla ma tshul rgyal ba/ ngag dbang grags pa/ mkhan chen byang chub sengge/ shar pa man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /thun mong ba e rtags can gyi lung gi brgyud pa lugs
gcig ni/ kun dga' bzang po yan chad bshad ma thag pa'i ngor lugs kyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa dang 'dra la/ de nas mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ gu ge paNDi ta
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug gsum gyis gsan/ phyi ma gnyis nas mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba/ thams cad mkhyen
pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / brtse chen smra ba'i nyi ma kun dga' bsod nams/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje
'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag

dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na mus chen nas rdo rje
'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen
rab bstan 'dzin bzang po man 'dra/ yang bshad ma thag pa'i lugs srol dang 'brog mi nas brgyud pa'i lugs srol gnyis man ngag phra mo re gnyis min pa rjes gnang dang
chos skor gcig pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal ldan birWa pa/ nag po pa/ DA ma ru pa/ gnyis spangs zhabs/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog
mi shAkya ye shes/ thugs sras se ston kun rig bla ma zhang dgon pa ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po man 'dra'o/ /yang rjes gnang thun mong ba'i brgyud tshul gcig la/ 'phags
pa rin po che nas/ 'u yug pa bsod nams sengge/ nyi thog pa kun smon/ kha'u pa 'od ldan dpal/  yon tan dpal zhes rgyal dbang lnga pa'i gsan yig tu byung / pu lung pa
kun dga' rdo rje/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen
rdo rje 'chang / gzhi thog bdag chen kun dga' dbang phyug bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na brag phug pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/
mkhan chen byang chub

sengge/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang rjes gnang gnyis dang sgo'i rtags yod pa'i lung brgyud ni/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yan gong ltar las/ de nas sgo rum
pa kun dga' legs pa/ rje mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra/ thun mong ba'i rjes gnang dang / glo'i rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po yan gong
ltar las/ de nas gzhi thog bdag chen kun dga' dbang phyug rgyal tshab rje/ glo bo mkhan chen/ rje grol mchog 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen nas/
chu mig bdag chen blo gros dbang phyug paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ brag dkar ba sems dpa' chen po/ mkhan chen bkra shis rnam rgyal/ rje grol mchog man 'dra'o/ /sa bcad gnyis
pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i dngos grub 'byung ba'i skor gyi lung brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon klu'i byang chub/ dga' rab rdo
rje/ bla ma rdo rje gdan pa/ bla ma ArYa pA la/ bla ma bai ro tsa na badzra/ rje btsun gnas nang pa/  khams pa dbu se yin/ de la gsan yig nges pa zhig med 'dra bas bla ma
bdun tsam chad/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/  'di ku rab pa'i zhal ngo paN chen bkras rnam pa'i dbon po sa skya pa'i dge bshes yin kyang rjes su karma pa brgyad pa'i bla
mar gyur cing gnyug la legs bshad gling gi 'chad nyan du bskos pa sogs nas karma phrin las zhes grags pas brgyud 'debs su thams cad mkhyen pa rje btsun phrin las zhabs zhes
gsung / rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra/ Dombi he ru ka lugs kyi sindhU ra'i lha lnga'i byin rlabs dang de'i chos skor
sa bcad gsum yongs

rdzogs dang lnga pa'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga le tshan gnyis kyi lung dang bcas pa las byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje snying po/ DA ki ni su bha giDAombi
he ru katsa Na pa/ tai lo pa/ nA ro paN chen/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med pa/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob
dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ khang ston 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod
nams/ bla ma mnyam med chen po/ mkhas grub gzungs kyi dpal ba/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ de dbon bsod nams rgyal mchog brag thog pa bsod
nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ bla ma blo gros rnam rgyal/ rje btsun phrin las zhabs/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang
phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa bsod nams mtha' yas/ mkhan chen thams
cad mkhyen pa bzang po rgyal mtshan/ bka' drin zla bral rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /'di skor lung  rtags yod med la ma
ltos pa'i/ yongs rdzogs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags yan gong bzhin las/ de nas byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags
'chang ngag dbang kun dga'

bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /sa bcad
bzhi pa kun mkhyen bkra shis rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ kun mkhyen bkra shis rnam rgyal/ spyan snga bsod nams lha dbang / chos rje kun dga'
bkra shis/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ sngags 'chang bsod nams chos
'phel/ khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa bsod nams mtha' yas/ dpal sa skya pa chen po/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa/ rdo rje
'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /dkar chag tu ku ru kulle'i chos skor du gsungs shing mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig sogs phal che ba zur du phyung nas gser chos
bcu gsum gyi grangs su'ang 'dren pa bla ma gnyan lo tsA ba'i dbang gi lha gsum du grags pa'i skor la/ so so'i yig snying la gzhi byas/ brgyud pa'i phyag len gyis brgyan
pa'i rjes gnang spyi dang mi 'dra ba'i dpal mo gser gyi snying thag can gyi sku gsung thugs kyi rjes gnang khyad par can/ nor rgyun ma dmar mo'i sku sgom pa dang bzlas pa'i
lung gi rjes gnang / lha mo ti nu'i rjes gnang bdud rtsi/ sindhU ra/ dril bu la brten pa'i sku gsung thugs kyi rjes gnang rnams legs par thob nas/ lung la dpal mo gser
gyi snying thag can gyi skor ni/ gnyan los paN chen 'bum phrag

gsum pa dbang du bsdus pa'i lo rgyus/ bsnyen pa srog gi 'khor lo zhes pa bsnyen sgrub las gsum du yod pa'i bsnyen pa la sngon 'gro dngos gzhi rjes gsum/ sgrub pa la sbyor dngos
rjes gsum/ las sbyor dbang du bsdu ba/ bsgral ba/ las la gzhol ba gsum gyis bsdus pa/ longs spyod rdzas kyi 'khor lo zhes pa sbyor dngos rjes gsum gyis bstan pa/ dbang
sdud yid bzhin gyi 'khor los phyag rgya mtshan ldan ma 'gugs pa sbyor dngos mjug gsum gyis bstan pa/ lung blang ba'i yi ge dkar chag tu mi gsal ba/ gnyan los gnyan lha
khang gi khro bo dme brtsegs kyi zhabs 'og tu gter du sbas tshul gyi lo rgyus rnams/ nor rgyun ma dmar mo'i chos skor la/ na mo ba su dha rA yai/ gnas yid dang mthun pa
zhes 'gor yod pa'i sgrub thabs/ kha zas la sogs pa med par bya'o'i mtha' can/ A tsarYa'i zhal la rag lus pas zhal shes/ rjes gnang gi yi ge mjug na a na ya sogs kyi sngags
byang yod pa/ lha mo ti nu'i chos skor la/ 'gor dwang ba'i lha la phyag 'tshal lo zhes yod pa'i sgrub thabs thun mong ma yin pa'o'i mtha' can/ lung blang ba'i yi ge sa
skyar yar sgom gyis zhus pa/ rjes gnang gi phyag len/ dmar chung skor gsum gyi rjes gnang bya tshul shin tu gsal ba/ chos tshan gcig tu dril ba kun  bkras rnam pa'i dbon
po rje phrin las pas mdzad/ mkhyen bkra shis rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i bstod pa padma rA ga'i lcags kyu rnams dang bcas pa rdzogs par thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol

ma/ gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po
che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ khams pa rdo rje dpal/ bla ma grags pa dpal/ bla
ma 'phags pa/ bla ma dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rin chen dpal/ bla ma sengge dpal/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ thugs sras kun
dga' rgyal po/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag
mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa chen po ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' lhun grub/
e waM pa rigs brgya'i khyab bdag dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na/ rje rdo rje gdan pa nas/ bla ma blo gros rnam rgyal/ rje phyogs las
rnam rgyal/ tshar chen man 'dra/ yang na rje btsun grags pa nas/ bla chen yar sgom/ rgyal tsha chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen sengge bzang po/
yar lung pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rgyal mchog brag thog pa man 'dra'o/ /yang na sa paN nas/ tshogs sgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ brag phug pa/ bka' bcu pa gzhon nu sengge/
gung pa bkra shis bzang

po/  rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na/ bar 'dir lung mang po zer ba zhig 'dug kyang / rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na mi 'dug pas brtag mkhan chen sengge dpal/ brag thog pa man
'dra'o/ /yang na gnyan lo tsA ba nas/ dpyil ston rdo rje thog 'bebs/ yol thogs med/ bla ma grwa zhig pa/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma 'phags pa/ bla ma dkon mchog rgyal
mtshan/ bla ma rin chen dpal/ mkhan chen sengge dpal/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ 'bras spungs pa tshe
dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/ yang na mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags nas/ 'dren mchog snying rje bzang po/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ drin
can rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /zhar byung du dzambha la tshogs bdag a pa ra tsitta gsum la brten
pa'i gnyan lo'i gser chos dzambha la sum sgril gyi gdams pa las sbyor kho nas lag tu lon pa'i man ngag zab mo'i sgom lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang dbang
phyug rab brtan yan gong du bshad ma thag pa ltar las/ de nas rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ drin can mkhyen rab bla ma/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen kun dga' lhun grub/
des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /dkar chag tu/ dA na shI la las brgyud pa la gtso bor mi mdzad gsung ba gtso mi che ba ma gtogs don dkar chag gi tshig gis zin pa yin
pas thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad

pa'i mngon dkyil la brten nas/ rje btsun ma ku ru kulle lha lnga'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa mngon dkyil gnyis kyi lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ kha che'i paNDi ta shAkya shrI bha dra/ paN chen dA na shI la/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ 'u yug
pa bsod nams sengge/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ nyi thog pa kun smon/ rje yon tan dpal/ kun dga' rdo rje/ kun dga' bsod nams/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ ri khrod
pa blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo
bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse mkhas grub nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa ngag dbang mchog
legs rdo rje/ 'khor lo'i mgon po mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ bka' drin gzhal med ngag dbang kun dga' lhun
grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na badzra pA Ni/ dze tA ri/ a sho kaa mo gha badzra/ ba ri lo tsA ba/
mchims brtson seng / mkhan chen chos rin/ chos rje dge sdings pa/ bla ma sgom pa/ bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ khyung po lhas pa gzhon nu bsod
nams/ shar chen ye shes rgyal

mtshan/ ngor chen man gong ltar ro/ /gnyis pa bde mchog rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud las bshad pa'i lha chen tshogs kyi bdag po khams gsum dbang du byed pa'i gdams ngag gi chos
skor rnams sa skya'i rje btsun brtse ba chen po la bka' babs par brten/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi tas hor dang rgya gar gyi rgyal po sogs 'gro ba mang po dbang du bsdus
pa ni rgyud sde rin po che'i dgongs pa ltar 'phags yul gyi grub chen du mas bstan pa la mi dad pa'i rgyal po dregs pa can dbang du bsdus nas bstan pa la bcug pa'i tshul
dang mtshungs shing / zangs tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis tshogs bdag gzir ba'i mthus/ des bskul nas sa ston ri pa bsams bzhin 'phags pa rin po cher skye ba bzhes nas
hor rgyal po'i ti shrI gyur te bod chol kha gsum gyi bdag por dbang bskur ba/ khams su dge slong bzhi sde zhig gis lha chen 'di bsgrubs pas gser lug gi mchin pa tsam rnyed
pa sogs thun mong gi dngos grub bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' ba'i gser chos zab mo'i skor la/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge'i dgongs pa ngor
chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi yi ge la brten nas ngor lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang / paN chen  'di sngon ma thos kyang
slar thos rgyur bris/ ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i phyag len khrigs chags 'dod dgu'i dpag bsam gyi steng nas dmar chen phyag bcu gnyis pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i
rjes gnang / rje dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i ma nor

don tshang gsal ba'i sgron me'i steng nas dmar chen phyag bcu gnyis pa'i khyad par gyi rjes gnang / rje ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i ma nor gsal ba'i sgron me'i steng
nas jo bo chen po lugs kyi tshogs bdag dkar po chags pa'i rdo rje'i rjes gnang / she'u lo tsA ba'i yi ge'i steng nas jo bo chen po'i lugs kyi tshogs bdag glang gdong
dkar po phyag bzhi pa'i rjes gnang rnams legs par nos nas/ rgyab brten lung gi skor la/ rtsa 1ba'i yi ge gsal 2byed kyi lhan thabs/ gsang 3sgrub kyi yi ge zhar 4byung jo
bo chen po nas brgyud pa'i dkar po/ gser 5chos kyi gsang sgrub dmar po phyag bzhi pa'i yi ge dkar 6chag tu ma bzhugs pa'i skor dang drug dang po la/ 'gor 'jig rten dbang
phyug la (glo)phyag 'tshal lo tshogs kyi bdag po'i lo rgyus ni zhes yod pa'i lo rgyus/ mngon brjod kyi bstan bcos las dbang phyug gi chung ma phag mo'i bur tshogs bdag skyes
pa'i gtam rgyud/ 'gor dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bgegs kyi rgyal po'i rjes gnang gi cho ga ni zhes yod pa'i rjes (glo)gnang gi yig rnying mal los mdzad
pa rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi phyag len rgyas bsdus yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan gyis zin bris su mdzad pa/ 'gor dpal rdo rje mkha'
'gro la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bgegs kyi rgyal po'i rjes gnang byed par 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i khyad par gyi rjes gnang gi yi ge dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis mdzad pa khyad par
gyi gdams pa brjed thor bkod pa'i mtha' can/ yar klungs pa'i thun mong ma yin

pa'i rjes gnang gi gsal byed bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa bla ma gong ma'i yi ge dang mi mthun pas spang bar bya'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag
'tshal lo/ /dpal tshogs kyi bdag po zhes yod pa'i thun mong gi rjes (glo)gnang ngor chen gyis mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag gi rjes gnang bya tshul i thi'i mtha' can/ tshogs bdag
gi rgyud rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i le'u bcu dgu pa las phyung ba'i 'phags pa bgegs kyi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs/ 'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po'i snying po'i gzungs (glo)lo tsA
ba dge slong puNye shrI bha dras dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba/ grub chen nag po spyod pas mdzad pa'i dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sgrub thabs zhes pa 'byung po
'dul byed kyi sgom bzlas paN chen ga ya dha ra dang bla chen 'brog mis bsgyur ba/ yang des mdzad pa'i bgegs kyi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs (glo)ga ya dha ra dang gyi jo zla
ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba/ des mdzad pa'i 'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po'i bstod pa 'jig rten mgon mdzad ma/ 'di'i gsham du bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa rgyal ba'i
phrin las ma dang de nas mu mthud pa'i bzlas pa bya tshul sogs yar klungs pa'i mdzad byang yod pa zhig chos tshan gcig gi tshul du 'dug pa dkar chag na mi gsal yig rgyun
ma dag pa 'byams pa las 'og gi yar klungs pa'i gtor chog na mdzad byang sogs mi 'dug pas de'i zhabs yin nam snyam pa slar yang dpe rnyed na dpyad dgos 'dug go/ des mdzad
pa'i bgegs kyi rgyal po'i bris sku'i man ngag

ga ya dha ra dang gyi jo'i 'gyur/ des mdzad pa'i 'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po'i gtor ma'i cho ga 'gyur bshad ma thag pa dang 'dra ba/ des mdzad pa'i bgegs bdag gi sbyin sreg
gi cho ga 'gyur gong 'dra/  dkar chag dang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di ltar 'dug sbyin sreg gi yi ge ra 'brog mi'i 'gyur zer ba 'dug pas dpyad/ shin tu
myur ba'i lha bgegs chen po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dI paM ka ras mdzad pa/ dpal tshogs kyi bdag po'i las bzhi'i 'khor lo'i gsal byed Dombi he ru kas mdzad pa/ slob dpon
nag po spyod pas mdzad pa'i bgegs kyi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs kyi rnam par (glo)bshad pa rje btsun rin po che grags pas mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i bsnyen sgrub las sbyor gyi
sbyin sreg dang bcas pa mjug na zhar byung gi zhal gdams mang po yod kyang ma bris so'i mtha' can/ 'gor rdo rje mkha' 'gro la phyag 'tshal lo ga Na pa ti sgrub par byed
par 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i gsang sgrub lha dgu'i sgrub (glo)yig rnying pa dngos grub kyi rgya mtsho brtol nas 'ong ngo'i mtha' can/ 'gor dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro la phyag
'tshal lo/ /ga Na pa ti sgrub par 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i gsang sgrub lha dgu'i sgrub thabs sa skya paNDi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so'i mtha' can zhar byung dam tshig dang 'phags
pa rin po che sum cu rtsa gsum du khyer ba'i lo rgyus zur tsam dang bcas pa/ de dang 'dra min 'gor dpal rdo rje 'dzin pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /yod pa gsang sgrub drag po'i
lag len sa skya paNDi tas sbyar ba rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ zhar byung sgrub pa'i sngon 'gro dang sngags byang bstan pa/ tshogs bdag gi

mngon rtogs/ gtor 'bul/ bstod pa/ rmi ltas/ sku'i dbang sdud/ 'khor lo'i las sbyor 'dre mthong dang bcas pa rnams zangs tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ dpal ga Na
pa ti'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum spogs chog dang bcas pa gsal bar ston pa'i sgrub yig chen mo gzhan las ches khyad par 'phags pa stong gsum nor bus bkang ba las kyang dga'
ba 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa/ 'di dus gcig la slob ma gcig las mi ston pa'i gser chos bka' rgya can yin no/ /des mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs khrigs kyi sdom tshig shin tu
gsal ba/ 'gor bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo zhes yod pa'i tshogs bdag gi gtor chog (glo)rnal 'byor dbang phyug yar klungs pas mdzad pa/ 'di'i mjug rgyal ba'i
sku gsung ma zer ba'i bstod pa slob dpon nag po'i zhabs kyis mdzad zer ba zhig gis rdzogs pa las yar klungs pa'i mdzad byang ma byung bas gong du dogs slong bris pa'i nag
po pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa 'jig rten mgon mdzad ma'i gsham du drung chos rje pas mdzad zer ba'i bstod pa dang gtor chog sogs kyi mthar yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan
gyis dam pa mang po'i bzhugs gnas bsam gling bde chen du sbyar zer ba 'dug pa/ dpe gong 'og gnyis po'i mjug pa'i yig mkhan gyis nor nas bris sam snyam pa slar yang ma dpe
rnying pa rnyed na zhu dag gtugs dgos par snang ngo / /gnyis pa gsal byed lhan thabs la/ bris sku bri zhing sgrub pa'i yi ge de phyir sngags la nan tan bya sa mApta mi
thi'i mtha' can/ bris sku

bri ba'i man ngag rab tu gnas pa dang bcas pa bris sku'i cho ga rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ gnod sbyin chen po bse gdong gi gzugs mnan pa'i yig rnying tshigs bcad ma/ gnod sbyin
bse gdong can mnan pa'i lag len chos rje bla ma dam pa'i gsung bzhin yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan gyis bsam yas su zin bris mdzad pa/ sku rten bri ba/ dngos grub
kyi rten gtor bca' ba/ gsang rten lus la bcang ba/ rgyun gtor gter du sba ba/ thun mong ma yin pa'i gnad dbab kyi yig chung bka' rgya can gser chos chig brgyud ma/ sgrub
pa'i sgab 'dre gnon pa/ gsang rten bca' ba/ bla rdo 'chang ba/ dngos grub blang thabs rnams ston pa'i gsang ba gnad kyi yig chung sgrub yig chen mo'i lhan thabs bdag chen
rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i gser chos chig brgyud ma/ gsang ba snying gi 'khor lo'i las bzhi sgrub tshul spogs chog gsang ba thugs kyi man ngag nor bu bsam gtan/ tshogs
