bdag dang tsartsi zhal sbyor gyi thab gter/ bang mdzod kyi cho ga rnams ston pa'i yi ge rin chen ljon shing gser chos chig brgyud gras/ 'gor dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro la
phyag 'tshal lo/ /gsang sngags ma bzlas mi 'grub cing zhes yod pa'i sbyin sreg gi lag len me ma shi bar gzhan reg tu mi 'jug go'i mtha' can/ bi na ya'i rgyud nas gsungs
pa'i phyag mtshan bcu gnyis kyi las tshogs (glo)zhes pa dgra stwas dgra bo gzhom pa/ gtun shing gis bgegs tshar gcod pa/ mda' gzhus dgra bo dbang du byed pa/ kha TwAM gas
'byung po dga' bar byed pa/ lcags kyus 'gro ba dbang

du bsdu ba/ thod pas gdul bya 'gugs pa/ rdo rjes gdon bgegs tshar gcod pa/ ral gris gza' bsrung ba/ thod pa sha chen gyis nor bsgrub pa/ phub la brten nas gnod pa gang 'dod
bsrung ba/ ba dan gyis grags pa spel ba/ mdung gis bsam pa sgrub pa rnams ston pa/ 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i (glo)bstod pa tshig rkang bcu bdun ma/ des mdzad pa'i
spyan 'dren mchod phreng shapta pra tItstsha hU~M gi mtha' can/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa paM pad raM nyi ma/ des mdzad pa'i rgyal ba'i phrin las ma/
ngor chen gyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa (glo)gdug pa kun 'dul ma rnams so/ /gsum pa gsang sgrub kyi yi ge la/ tshogs bdag dmar po gsang sgrub zhal gcig phyag drug pa'i sgrub (glo)pa
dpal nA ro pas mdzad pa'i paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/ de'i lag len tshogs kyi bdag po'i gsang sgrub kyi lag len rdzogs so'i mtha' can/
Dombi he ru ka nas brgyud pa'i tshogs bdag dmar chung zhal gcig phyag gnyis nor rgyun ma dang yab yum du sgrub pa'i yi ge mchod pa'i las so'i mtha' can/ rgyal blon btsun
mo 'bangs sogs dbang du bsdu ba'i yi ge rten phyi nang gsang gsum bca' ba'i yi ge rdzogs so'i mtha' can zhar byung dbang du ma 'dus na dmigs pa bya tshul dang bcas rnams
so/ /bzhi pa zhar byung jo bo chen po nas brgyud pa'i dkar po'i skor la/ tshogs bdag rigs lnga ston pa'i rgyud rin chen gter mdzod le'u dgu pa paNDi ta dI paM kA ra dang
nag tsho lo tsA bas bsgyur

ba/ 'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po'i 'gyur ge gas sel ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon indra bhU tis mdzad pa paNDi ta dI paM kA ra dang lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng gis yam bu mkhar
du bsgyur ba/ de'i lag len 'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po'i ge gas sel gyi sgrub thabs jo bo a ti shas mdzad pa gu gul gyis bdug cing gtor ma btang ngo'i mtha' can/ des mdzad
pa'i bstod pa phyag 'tshal dpal ldan ma/ tshogs bdag gi sku la rab gnas bya ba mchod thabs rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ gnad la dbab pa rgya brtson 'grus sengge'i man ngag
shin tu zab pa/ gnad la bor ba/ bzlas pa'i zhal gdams sbyin sreg gi las med thabs med pa'i mtha' can/ bsad pa'i las rta phru ma/ spogs pa'i yig chung / rjes gnang lo
rgyus dang bcas pa'i yi ge yang jo bo rje'i gdams pa tshogs bdag dkar po phyag bzhi pa a mo gha nas brgyud pa'i skor la/ tshogs bdag sgrub pa'i rten gyi gang zag gis zhes
'gor yod pa'i tshogs bdag dkar po glang gdong phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs ma mthong bar du'o'i mtha' can paNDi ta a dkar dri la dur khrod phung lung nag por skye ba sngon
ma'i yon bdag dang phrad pa'i lung bstan byung tshul sogs kyi lo rgyus/ dkar chag na bar 'dir tshogs bdag dkar po sha ba'i gdong can gyi sgrub thabs zer ba zhig 'dug kyang
dpe ma 'byor pas lung ma thob/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i gsang sgrub a mo gha badzra gyis mdzad pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM kA ra shrI dznyA na dang lo tsA ba nag tsho
tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba/ tshogs kyi bdag po sgrub pa'i man ngag nges par dbang du 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ sku la

rab gnas bya thabs rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ mnyes par bya ba'i phyir gtor ma 'bul ba rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ bstod pa sum cu rtsa gsum ma a mo gha badzra gyis mdzad pa rnams so/
/lnga pa gser chos kyi gsang sgrub phyag bzhi pa'i yig rnying la/ dpal tshogs kyi bdag po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /tshe 'di la bsod nams che ba zhes 'gor yod pa'i gsang sgrub
dmar po phyag bzhi pa'i yig rnying stong grogs gyis shig gi mtha' can/ de'i rten bca' ba sogs kyi zhal gdams dam pa kun dga' grags kyis yi ge ra bkod pa/ bstod cing gsol
ba gdab pa nor gyi rgyur 'gyur ma 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag yang gsang drag po btsan thabs su sgrub pa'i nying khu zab mo phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs
sbyin sreg spogs chog dang bcas pa bla ma sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag glang po'i gzugs sgrub thabs kyi sgo nas nor sbyin pa'i zhal gdams zhes pa glang po
che'i gzugs la brten nas sgrub pa rje bsam gtan gling pa'i phyag dpe dngos las bshus pa rnams so/ /sa bcad lnga pa 'di thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na gsum
pa'i mjug na mthud pa'i rje btsun sa skya pa'i khyad par gyi gdams pa gser chos thun mong ma yin pa'o zhes yar bcad nas sa bcad bzhi pa 'di logs su mdzad pa don la gnas
na'ang / 'dir dkar chag chen mo'i bzhugs tshul ltar bkod pa chos sde'i brgyud babs kyi dbye ba ma 'dres par byed dgos shing / dpa' bo rdo rje/ ga ya dha ra/ ha ngu dkar
po/ paNDi ta 'jam dbyangs te brgyud pa

bzhi'i gdams pa thun mong ma yin pa'i khyad par gyi dbye ba'ang kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bstan 'dzin zhig gi zhal lung las len dgos kyi shes rlom kun gyi spyod yul ma yin no/
/drug pa dkar chag tu ma bzhugs pa'i skor la dpal tshogs kyi bdag po dmar chen phyag bcu gnyis pa'i rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa'i phyag len khrigs chags 'dod dgu'i dpag
(ngag )bsam paN chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i tshogs kyi bdag po'i khyad par gyi rjes gnang (ngag )ma nor don tshang gsal ba'i sgron me/ tshogs
bdag dmar chen phyag bcu gnyis pa'i bsnyen pa/ sgrub pa/ sdogs pa/ sbyin sreg dang bcas pa'i tshigs bcad ma bla ma gnyan phul byung bas (chen)mdzad pa sba zhing gsang
la sgrub pa'i mtha' can/ des mdzad pa'i bstod pa dpal (chen)chen spyan snga ma/ dbang du byed na zla (chen)gam dmar po zhes sogs kyi zhal shes/ 'gor gdams pa 'di'i don la
gsum ste zhes dang (chen)a kA ro bdun gyis dbul lo'i mtha' can/ gnod sbyin bse gdong mnan pa'i gdams (chen)pa sems can kho na'i don du dam tshig go'i mtha' can/ yang 'gor
bzlog pa rem du bya zhes yod pa'i bse gdong mnan pa (chen)lus nag sna dmar gzugs su 'dri'i mtha' can/ dang po tshogs bdag gi phyi nas 'brangs zhes 'gor yod pa'i bse gdong
mnan (chen)pa smon lam 'debs su 'jug go'i mtha' can/ dpal tshogs kyi bdag po'i sgrub thabs rin chen spungs (klong)pa zhes pa snyan ngag mkhan dpal ldan bsam

yas pa'am klong chen rab 'byams kyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i bstod (klong)pa sdeb sbyor rgya mtsho'i sprin/ mgon po tshogs kyi bdag po mchod cing sgrub pa'i thabs dngos grub
kyi 'byung (mi)gnas paN chen bkra shis rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ mchod gtor 'bul zhing phrin las 'chol (chen)ba tshar gyis mdzad pa phun tshogs dngos grub ma/ tshogs kyi
bdag po sgrub thabs (nA)slob dpon nA ro pas mdzad pa gsang ba'i man ngag chags pa rdo rje'i skor nas rgyud kyi bsdus don rnam par bshad pa'o'i mtha' can/ tshogs bdag khro
bo spre'u ltar sgrub pa bla ma gser gling pas mdzad pa/ spre'u ltar sgrub pa'i tshogs kyi bdag po'i gsang sgrub dpal a ti sha nas brgyud pa'i zab pa/ tshogs bdag gi gtor
ma sa mApta'i mtha' can/ gsol gdab mi 'gyur bkod pa zhar byung spyan 'dren ri rab ma dang bcas pa/ chags pa rdo rje'i zhal gdams tshigs gnyis ma/ sngags 'bum gyi gdams
pa ga Na pa ti spre'u'i sgrub thabs rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ tshogs bdag gsang sgrub ces pa bsnyen pa bla rdo gnad dbab dang bcas pa ga lnga mar grags pa bla ma'i zhal
las rnyed pa'i gdams pa/ 'gor sngags gzhan gnyis po 'di gong ma gtsigs che zhes yod pa'i spre'u'i zhal gdams bsam gtan gling pas mdzad pa thugs dam ma nyams pa'o'i mtha'
can/ a mo ghas mdzad pa'i skor la/ la du 'chos thabs/  rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di'i 'og tu gcun sngags zer ba logs su ma rnyed/ zan nam chan la gtor ma bre gang
yan chad bzang bar byas te zhes pa

'gor yod pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ tshogs kyi bdag po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de la 'di sgrub par 'dod pas zhes 'gor yod pa'i sgrub thabs dbu shar du blta ba yin
gsungs pa'i mtha' can/ dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po'i snying po'i gzungs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'gor yod pa'i bstod pa zhes su gsol gyi
mtha' can/ dpal phyag na rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rnal 'byor longs spyod brtag dka' ba zhes 'gor yod pa'i sgrub thabs thob par 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ mig mthong gi gdams
pa rnams so/ /dpe ris skor la/ sgrub pa'i maNDal/ dmar chen dang dmar chung gi gtor dpe/ bse gdong can gyi ling gag brgyad 'khor lo/ 'di la 'phags pa'i sku srung dang
gong ma'i yig rnying gi lugs srol gnyis tsam yod/ gsang ba snying gi 'khor lo las bzhi sgrub pa'i gnam sa bar gsum gyi 'khor lo bcu gnyis/ tshar chen gyi sku srung la rgyas
pa'i steng 'khor gyi yi ge ma log pa dang 'jam dbyangs chen po'i sku srung la drag po'i steng 'khor yi ge log pa sogs gong ma'i gsung rgyun sku srung sogs kyi zab gnad
mang bar snang ngo / /rgyas pa'i bar 'khor gyi lte bar 'dri rgyu'i nor bu mig gsum/ thab gter gyi dngos grub myur du blang 'khor/ tshogs bdag dang tsartsi ka zhal sbyor
gyi thab dang mdzod kyi 'khor lo rnams kyi dbang lung phyag len man ngag legs par nos pa las/ thog mar ngor lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang legs par thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ dpal rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo rje phag mo/ grub chen sa ra ha/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ grub

chen sha wa ri pa/ ha ngu dkar po/  gsan yig gong ma rnams na hU~M ka ra zhes snang / mal lo blo gros grags pa/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon dpal
ldan bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/  rdo rje gdan pa dang thar rtse ba dang sangs rgyas
phun tshogs pa rnams kyi gsan yig na 'di ltar yod kyi/ mkhyen brtse dang rgyal dbang lnga pa rmor pa rnams kyi gsan yig na sa paN dang 'di'i bar na 'gro mgon 'phags
pa yod pa'ang byung / rin po che skyob pa dpal bzang po/ rong pa shes rab sengge/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas
phun tshogs kyi gsan yig na bar 'dir bla ma ngag dbang zhes pa zhig byung ngo / /mkhan chen byang chub sengge/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun
dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rje lha mchog sengge/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas sengge/ paNDi ta nam mkha' dpal bzang / brang
ti nam mkha' rin chen/ se chen gan nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'dren mchog shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ shar pa blo gros grags
pa/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang ba chen po bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la lan gnyis su bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs
nas/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ bstan

'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la lan mang du stsal to/ /yang na 'dren mchog ratna wardha nas/ thams
cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ bka' drin gzhal med rdo rje 'chang mkhyen
rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang ba chen po dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na ngor
chen nas/ gung ru shes rab bzang po/ mkhyen rab chos kyi rgyal po/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba byang chub rab tshes zla
ba/ ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ de dbon mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ de dbon ngag dbang bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun
grub man 'dra/ e rtags can gyi brgyud tshul yang 'di nyid do/ /rjes gnang thun mong ba'i brgyud pa ni/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ nyi lde ba ngag dbang grags pa/ bdag
chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ de gnyis ka las sgo rum pa/ de gnyis ka las tshar chen rdo rje 'chang / 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug yab sras gnyis ka las rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ grub mchog bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ grub dbang ngag dbang rnam rgyal/
dpal sa skya pa chen po ngag dbang kun dga' bkra

shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ bstan pa'i mnga' bdag ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje
'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ shar phyogs nag po pa/ DA ma ru pa/ a wa dhU tI pa/ ga ya dhA ra/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ brtse ba chen po kun
dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bla chen yar sgom se bo/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon
tan khri/ mkhan chen sengge bzang po/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rgyal mchog bdag chen 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'
rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rje gzhon
nu stobs ldan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan man gong dang 'dra/ yang na tshar chen yab sras las/ mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan dang / sngags 'chang bsod
nams chos 'phel gnyis kas gsan/ gnyis ka nas rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra/ tshogs bdag gi khyad par ba'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang dbang
phyug rab brtan yan gong ltar las/ de nas mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/
tshogs

sgom kun dga' dpal/ rin po che skyob pa dpal/ rgyal tsha lung mang po man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ khams sgom byang chub dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ ti shrI kun dga' blo
gros/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ de gnyis ka las bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ de nas yar klungs pa man 'dra/ yang na dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ gan pa rin rgyal/
'bri phyug pa rin chen 'bum/ yar klungs pa man 'dra/ yang rtsa ba'i yi ge dang / gsal byed lhan thabs kyi yi ge dang / gsang sgrub skor nas Do'i rtags can rnams kyi brgyud
pa ni thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa dang 'dra/ yang na mkhyen brtse'i zhabs nas sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/
khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis man sngar dang 'dra/ ngag rtags
can gyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan nas/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ 'khon sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras 'jam pa'i rdo
rje bsod nams dbang phyug de sras ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ rmor chen pa man 'dra/ klong rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni/ kun mkhyen klong chen rab 'byams/ pha rgod rtogs
ldan rgyal po/ drin chen thugs sras chos rje/ sprul sku rdo rje sengge/ bka' bcu pa puNya singha/ rje blo gros sengge/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po man 'dra'o/ /maM gyi
rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ kun mkhyen bkra shis rnam

rgyal/ bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ dpal ldan rgyal mtshan rje phrin las pa/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje man 'dra/ glo'i rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ gong ngor lugs rjes
gnang gi thun mong ma yin pa dang 'dra/ nA ro pa'i gsang sgrub dang nA'i rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa/ mal lo/ sa skya pa chen po man 'dra/ sa
dpyad gsum pa Dombi lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ Dombi pa/ dznyA na panydza/ kr-iShNa pa/ bhi na su kadharma sidha/ su kha pa ti/ rdo rje gdan pa/ khro phu lo chen/ sangs rgyas
zhig po/ sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma 'ban ston/ bla ma rdo rje sengge/ bka' bcu pa bsod nams sengge/ bla ma blo gros sengge/ rdo ring pa chen po man 'dra/ tshogs bdag chags
pa rdo rje'i rjes gnang dang / sa bcad bzhi pa dang drug pa'i chos skor gyi lung brgyud ni/ rgyal po indra bhU ti/ rgyal po grags pa/ bo dhi a ka ra/ rin chen 'od zer/ yang
dag sbyin pa/ ratna a ka ra shAnti/ jo bo chen po a ti shalo tsA ba rgya brtson 'grus sengge/ grub thob shol po ba/ sangs rgyas dbon ston/ sangs rgyas ston tshul/ khyung
tshang pa tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ snar thang mkhan chen nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ dbu ma pa grub pa brtson 'grus/ bka' bcu pa gzhon nu sengge/ gung chen pa bkra shis bzang
po/ gnyags phu ba bsod nams bzang po/  rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na tshal min chos rje zer/ sengge dbal ba/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga'
rnam rgyal/ 'di rmor chen pa'i gsan yig na ma byung yang / lnga pa chen po'i gsan

yig na chos rje klu dbang gling pa zhes byung / tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po man 'dra/ sa bcad bzhi pa dang / sa bcad drug pa'i a mo gha nas brgyud
pa gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ a mo gha badzra/ paN chen nA ro pa/  lam yig sogs su jo bos nA ro par phyag mi mdzad pas chos 'brel med pa 'dra zhes zer yang bka' gdams glegs
bam du brgyud pa'i khrod du bgrang yod pa 'di dang mthun no/ / jo bo dI paM ka ra/ 'brom rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ po to ba rin chen gsal/ sha ra ba yon tan grags/ bya 'chang
kha ba/ khra phu ba/ khyi lo yo gshI la pra bha wa/ dol ku mA ra/ lcan bande/ gsal ba sgang pa/ slob dpon dpal mgon/ slob dpon bde ba/  rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na
slob dpon 'od ma zhes snang ngo / /gnyags dbon rin chen man 'dra/ yang na a mo gha badzra/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams
rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ khang ston 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ bla ma byang chen pa/ bka' bcu pa gzhon seng man 'dra/ tshogs bdag
phyag bzhi pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ gzhon nu sengge yan gong ltar las/ de nas srib ri ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ lhang phug pa rin chen 'od zer/ bla ma dpal ldan
grub pa/ rin po che sangs rgyas 'od zer/ gtsang pa blo bzang pa/ bka' 'gyur ba shAkya rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga bsod nams chos grags rgyal mtshan/ she'u lo tsA ba/ mkhyen
rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun

grub/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /sa bcad lnga pa gsang sgrub gser chos kyi lung brgyud ni yar klungs pa khu dbon
nas/ bla ma dge bzang pa/ dung gzims khang dbon po/ rje ratna bha dra/ tshar pa rdo rje 'chang man 'dra'o/ /rtags yod med la ma ltos pa tshogs bdag gi chos skor yongs rdzogs
kyi lung ni/ mkhyen brtse yan gong tshar chen brgyud par bzhugs so cog ltar las/ de nas bar bar/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ ngag dbang kun
dga' bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /!/ /dpal kye rdo rje'i rgyud 'bum phrag lnga pa/ bde mchog
rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud/ padma he ru ka'i dbang du bsdu ba'i le'u sogs nas bstan pa'i khro bo kag chol 'dod pa'i rgyal po'i chos skor ni/ dkar chag las/ gsang ba'i
snying po A li kA li'i bcud/ /gsang sngags 'dzin pa gzhan la ma grags pa'i/ /gsang chen chos kyi bdag po sa skya pa'i/ /gsang ba'i gdams pa zab mo 'di ltar snang / /zhes
dang / 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis/ gdams pa 'di dag thub pa'i bstan pa dang / /khyad par sa skya'i rje btsun bstan pa'i ched/ /nyams su blangs na yid ches 'phel
du 'byung / /zhes bsngags par mdzad pa don dang mthun pas bla ma ba ri bas mnga' bdag rtse lde sogs rgya bod mang po dbang du bsdus/ bal por bod thang zhes bya'i sa gzhi

chen po gser dpag med kyi rin gyis nyos/ brtse ba chen po la 'phrang brag dmar gyi sde mgon gyis sku dgra byas pa 'di'i sgo nas dbang du bsdus/ gshen rdor seng gis dpal phag
mo grub pa dbang du mdzad/ do pa ston tshul ngom shod rje btsad kun gyi bla mar gyur/ rgyal tsha lung mang po hor rgyal po'i ti shrIr bskur ba sogs ngo mtshar lo rgyus
nges shes can gyi man ngag skor la/ sa paN gyi yi ge dang dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas ngor lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang / mkhan chen ngag
dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas thun mong ma yin pa gsang sngags sgra'i rjes gnang legs par nos nas/ rgyab brten lung la/ thun mong ba/ thun mong ma
yin pa/ dkar chag tu ma bzhugs pa'i skor dang gsum/ dang po la 'gor bla ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gdams ngag 'di'i brgyud pa ni zhes yod pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i
lo rgyus mdor bsdus rong pa dge ring gis zhus pa'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor padma dbang gi lha la phyag 'tshal lo/ /mkha' 'gro ma'i sgrub thabs zhes yod pa'i dbang sdud las
kyi 'khor lo yang sdud thugs kyi 'khor lo byung tshul sogs kyi lo rgyus cung zad rgyas par phye ba thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa chos kyi rjes
gsungs pa'o'i mtha' can/ dbang sdud kag chol ma'i lung gi rjes gnang gi cho ga (glo)dpal ldan sa skya paNDi tas rgyas par bkod pa/ byin rlabs kyi lung blang ba'i zhal shes
sa skya paNDi ta chen po'i man ngag zab mo/ bla ma sa skya pa'i gdams pa (glo)nam

mkha' mdzod kyi rjes gnang rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ gro ge ma'i sgrub ka kha ma'i sgrub thabs kyang zer thabs kyi rjes gnang bla ma'i phyag bzhes bzhin sngags 'chang rgyal ba
dpal gyis sa skya'i sku 'bum gyi gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa/ sngags kyi rgyal po'i dam tshig gi dngos grub mchog sgrub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba 'dod rgyal gyi sgrub (glo)thabs
slob dpon rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po de bzhin gshegs pa bsrungs pa'i dpal gyi zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rin chen grags kyis bsgyur
ba/ gsal byed nyi ma'i 'khor lo snod bcud dbang du bya ba paNDi ta rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa rgya gar gyi paNDi ta stha bI ra'i zhal snga nas dang ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur
ba/ dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma'i sgrub thabs (glo)dbang sdud las kyi 'khor lo'i man ngag ba ri bas bsgyur ba/ khams gsum dbang du bsdu ba'i man ngag rdo rje gdan pas mdzad
pa/ phrin las bzhi'i sgrub thabs kyi don yang dag par bsdus pa rgya sgom tshul khrims grags kyis mdzad pa/ slob dpon rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs gsal bar
byed pa'i 'grel (glo)pa rin po che'i myu gu rje btsun sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa/ 'gor zhi ba la kha dog dkar po zhes yod pa'i phrin las bzhi'i man ngag zhi rgyas dbang
drag thams cad de dang 'dra bar go bar bya'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor 'dir 'khor lo rab tu gnas pa byed par 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i las bzhi 'khor lo'i rab gnas so so'i skabs
dang sbyar bar bya'o'i mtha' can/ bsnyen pa/ 'khor lo/ dngos gzhi/ tsakra sgrub pa/ rjes spogs pa/ gnad kyi man ngag dngos grub dam tshig ste spyi don rnam pa dgus bstan
pa'i spyi'i man ngag mdor bstan zhes bya ba dbang gi phrin las kyi lag len mngon rtogs smar khrid du dge slong shI la kIrtis bkod pa/  rgya sgom tshul khrims grags/ 'gor
khro bo 'dod pa'i rgyal po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /oM wa shaM ku ru ho yod pa'i dbang sdud kag chol gyi sgrub thabs rje sa paN gyis mdzad pa 'dzam gling gser gyis bkang ba bas
kyang 'di mi dga' ri shi'i mtha' can/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge ba ri lo tsA ba'i gser chos rje sa skya pa'i zhal gdams thun mong ma yin pa/ gor rnal 'byor pa sgrub
pa la 'jug pa'i dus su zhes pa'i bzlas pa'i zhal gdams bla ma sa skya pa'i gsung me spel gsang ba'i bka' rgyas btab pa'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor gsang sngags kyi rtsa ba dbyangs
yig dang zhes pa'i dbang gi gtor ma'i man ngag (glo)dpal ldan sa skya paNDi ta'i phyag bzhes so'i mtha' can/ dbang gi 'khor lo'i rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga sngon 'gro
dngos gzhi rjes gsum gyis bstan pa bla ma ba ri lo tsA ba'i gdams pa/ 'gor thun bzhi la nyer spyod kyi mchod pa byed na zhes yod pa'i mchod pa 'bul ba'i rim pa'o'i mtha'
can/ sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa rab dga' zla rgyas ma/ 'gor sangs rgyas don yod grub pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'khor lo dpe'u chung ltar bris la zhes yod pa'i ting nge
'dzin gyi rim pa dang 'khor lo'i nang tshan bstan pa bla ma ba ri ba'i gdams ngag gnad khyad par du 'phags pa/ sgom pa'i dus kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi zhal gdams bla ma sa
skya pa'i

gdams ngag shin tu zab pa gzhan la gsang bar zhu'i mtha' can/ sngags byang 'byin 'jug dang bzlas thabs bla ma'i zhal shes so'i mtha' can/ gnad kyi sgrub thabs snying dang 'dra
ba/ 'gor oM shIntaM ka ra Ni bhrU~M yod pa'i sngags dang 'khor lo'i gnad lung 'bogs pa rA dza la sogs pa dbang du bya ba'i yig chung gzhan rnams gong dang mthun no'i
mtha' can/ bri gzhi sogs lnga/ maNDal sogs lnga/ snod sogs brgyad de man ngag gi bsdus don nyung ngu mchan bu dang bcas pa/ 'gor bsnyen pa 'dod rgyal la 'bum phrag nyer bzhi
bskyal la zhes yod pa'i ka kha 'khor lo brtsegs rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba la mi phyed pa/ dbang du 'gyur ba/ 'ong ba bcings pa bzhin 'gyur ba/ 'gugs pa/ nor rgyas
pa/ gnod sbyin mo sgrub pa/ rig byed mas 'gugs pa/ bu mo dbang du byed pa/ gnod sbyin mo'i nor 'gugs pa/ thams cad dbang du byed pa/ bran du 'gyur ba/ 'bru 'phel ba/ bang
mdzod mi zad pa/ sngar ma mthong ba'i bud med dang / rgyal po'i btsun mo 'gugs pa/ bltas pa/ byin pa/ brgyab pa/ reg pas dbang du 'gyur ba/ mi 'bral ba/ rgyal po dbang
du bya ba/ DA ki thams cad 'ong ba la sogs las phran tshegs bstan pa'i skor/ dbang gi sbyin sreg gi lag len bla ma chen po sa skya pa'i phyag bzhes/ sku gsung thugs kyi
rab gnas kyi zhal gdams zin bris/ tsakra'i rab gnas bya thabs ba ri lo tsA ba'i man ngag bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge bsdus pa bar gcod mi 'byung zhing las myur ba yin

gsungs pa'i mtha' can/ DA ki ma'i 'gro ba dbang sdud kyi gdams pa zhes pa dbang drag gi man ngag zhal gdams dang bcas pa gnang ngo'i mtha' can/ 'gor na mo buddhA a mo gha siddhi
zhes yod pa'i 'khor los bsgrub bya dgug pa sogs ba ri lo tsA ba'i gdams pa dpal ldan sa skya pa'i zhal gdams bod du thon pa'i man ngag la 'di las zab pa med do'i mtha'
can/ 'khor lo'i yi ge la gtor ma 'bul ba'i zhal gdams bla ma (glo)sa skya pa chen po'i phyag bzhes/ gnod sbyin rin chen sgrub pa'i u pa de sha'agor wa shaM ku ru ho gro
ga mdzub gang pa gcig la zhes pa'i 'khor lo'i man ngag gsung tshad ma gru bzhir bya'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor gro ga mdzub gang la nang du sor bdun tsam zhes pa'i 'khor lo bri
thabs sba ba'i man ngag bzla tshe sbrel nas bzla zhes pa'i mtha' can/ dbang gi tsakra'i zhal gdams nam mkha' mdzod kyi gdams pa nyung ngu la 'dus pa khyad par du 'phags
so'i mtha' can/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi gnad bod du 'gyur ba'i gdams pa zab pa nus pa chung ngu mi 'gro ba'i gnad yin no'i mtha' can/ 'gor yar gyi tshes brgyad la rjes
gnang zhu'o zhes yod pa'i zhal gdams zin bris ji lta ba bzhin du 'grub bo rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ DA ki ma'i gdams pa rdzun mi smra'o'i mtha' can/ DA ki ma'i srog snying
khong nas phyung ba ba ri lo tsA ba'i gdams pa chig brgyud/ bla ma ba ri bas sag thang pa dang dol po bsod nams 'phel la gnang ba'i DA ki ma sgrub pa'i lag len zhes pa 'khor
lo/ bzlas sgom mchod gtor/ lag len ga'u gzhung dang mthun zhes pa

rnams bstan pa/ rtags kyi yi ge (glo)ba ri lo tsA ba bod du 'byon khar bla ma rdo rje gdan pas gnang ba/ gzhan dbang du byed pa'i gdams pa rin po che'i zhal gdams mthar thug
pa/ tshe bsring ba'i thabs/ de'i zhal shes padma kha sbyor gyi ting 'dzin/ rgyas pa'i gtor ma'i phyag bzhes dpal ldan sa skya paNDi ta'i khyad par gyi man ngag drag po'i
phrin las sgrub par 'dod pas 'grub nas dben par sba'o'i mtha' can/ bla ma la phyag dang maNDal phul nas lung 'bogs pa'i gdams pa/ chu dang phyag rgya'i nyin srung mtshan
srung gi man ngag de'i yi ge mchan bu dang bcas pa bar du gcod pa rnams srungs shig gi mtha' can rnams te/ man ngag 'di'i mjug tu bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos/ grub
pa'i dbang phyug sa skya pa'i/ /dbang sdud man ngag khyad par can/ /snyan brgyud zhal gdams ma gtogs pa/ /thun mong chos skor tshang bar bzhugs/ /snod ldan slob ma 'ga'
tsam las/ /gzhan la rgya cher spel mi bya/ /rdo rje lta bur rtogs dka' zhing / /rtogs na yid bzhin nor 'dra'i chos/ /des na 'di lta'i zab don la/ /mkhas pas gces spras bya
bar rig sa/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar shin tu zab cing dkon pa'i chos 'di snying gi thig ler 'chang ba'i 'os so/ /!/ /gnyis pa thun mong ma yin pa la/ khams gsum 'gro ba dbang
byed kag chol gyi bla ma brgyud pa'i lo rgyus (glo)mkhas pa yon tan khris mdzad pa/ dbang sdud kag chol ma'i A li kA li'i sngags ring 'dri bzlas kyi (glo)man ngag sa
skya paNDi tas dag cing

gsal bar mdzad pa/ kag chol chen mo'i rtsa ba'i tho yig brjed byang tsam du shryA nanda garbhas  dpal kun dga' snying po/ mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i de'i 'grel TIka sbas pa'i
mig 'byed gser gyi thur ma/ 'khor lo'i rab gnas bya ba'i man (glo)ngag zhal gdams dang bcas pa sa skya paNDi tas rgyas par bkod pa/ des bkod pa'i bde ba rgyas byed ma'i
sku (glo)la brten pa'i dbang gi nang sgrub zab mo/ gsang sgrub tha chen gyi tsakra'i man (glo)ngag rje btsun rin po che grags pas mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i gnad 'bebs (glo)nyi
zla'i 'khor lo'i gdams pa/ mkha' 'gro ma'i spogs chog gis gnad la dbab (glo)pa'i man ngag sa skya paNDi tas rgyas par bkod pa/ des mdzad pa'i sbyin sreg bya ba'i man
ngag (glo)bla ma'i zhal las byung ba'i bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun/ yul bdag dbang du bsdu ba'i zhal gdams ba ri'i man ngan rje sa skya pa'i gdams pa/ 'gor bzlas pa'i sngags kyi
man ngag ni zhes yod pa'i sngags kyi 'byin 'jug gi yi ge las de bzhin du 'gyur ba'i phyir ro'i mtha' can/ gsal byed nyi ma'i 'khor lo'i bsdus don rang bsrung ngo'i mtha'
can/ ma grub na spogs pa'i cho ga mnyam par bzhed do'i mtha' can/ 'khor lo bltab tshigs kyi zhal gdams smin mtshams su reg pa'o'i mtha' can/ ma grub na gnad 'bebs kyi
'khor lo gces par zung gi mtha' can/ 'gor kho bo'i bla ma 'di skad gsung zhes pa yod pa'i pho mo gnad 'bebs kyi 'khor lo/ 'gor phyi sgrub 'khor lo chen mo zhes pa'i gnad
'bebs nyi zla'i gdams pa/ 'gor bla ma'i zhal

gdams 'dri bar bya zhes pa yod pa'i pho mo gnad 'bebs kyi 'khor lo'i zhal gdams sa skya pa chen po'i zhal gyi gdams pa ma bu 'di rnams bris pa legs kyi mtha' can/ 'gor dngos
grub kyi mkha' 'gro ma la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes yod pa'i tha chen 'khor lo'i gsang ba'i sgrub thabs the tshom med do'i mtha' can/ de'i zhal gdams bla ma sa skya pa'i gdams
ngag nor bu rin po che phag mo grub pa la gnang ba/ tha chen 'khor lo'i yi ge dbang sdud dam pa/ 'gor bla ma bde chen lhag pa'i lha zhes yod pa'i mkha' 'gro ma'i rdzas
sgrub gshen bde ba'i rdo rjes bla ma sa skya pa chen por zhus pa khyad par gnad kyi gdams pa'o'i mtha' can/ de'i gsal byed 'gor mkha' 'gro bde ba rgyas byed kyi sku zhes
yod pa'i zhang btsun sag thang ba'i zhal gdams/ phrin las myur du sgrub pa dbang gi rlung 'khor zab mo (glo)dang rlung lha las la gzhug pa sogs gab pa'i man ngag sa skya
pa'i zhal gdams/ 'gor dpal 'khor lo bde mchog dang zhes yod pa'i a'i gdams pa zur gcig 'dri ba A li gnad kyi gdams pa rin chen yid bzhin nor bu bla ma'i bka' rgya can/
de'i zhal shes 'gor spyir ni khams gsum sems can thams cad la zhes yod pa dbang gi gdams pa'i mtha' can/ A li'i sbyin sreg gshen gyi lugs/ rje sa chen dang 'gro mgon phag
mo grub pa gnyis kyis zhu ba (glo)zhus lan A li kA li las sna tshogs la 'jug pa zhes pa'i gdams pa le'u nyi shu rtsa brgyad pa/ 'dod rgyal yab yum sbags te sgrub pa'i man
ngag lag len du

dril ba'i nag po 'gro shes bshes gnyen gra bo rin chen phan gyi don du sngags 'chang rgyal po dpal gyis mdzad pa/ de'i zhal shes de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i sa skya pa'i gdams
pa khyad par 'phags pa 'dzam gling gser gyis bkang ba las ches cher dga' ba/ thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi zur 'debs 'jam dbyangs mgon pos mdzad pa/ dbang sdud las
kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel (glo)pa 'gro ba'i srog snying 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ khyad par gyi sgrub thabs nor bu gsal 'bar snying gi thig le'i dwangs ma
drung nam mkha' bzang pos bskul nas rin po che bsod nams rgyal ba mchog dbyangs kyi gsung las skyes pa'i rig pa 'dzin pa ri khro dbang pos bsam gtan gling du mdzad pa/
mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags pa'i gsan yig na bsam gtan gling pa dpal ldan bzang pos mdzad ces snang / 'di gser chos shin tu zab pa'i chig brgyud dus gcig la slob ma
gcig las mi ston pa'i bka' rgya can yin te/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi gsung las/ snying dang 'dra ba'i gdams pa 'di/ /snod ldan slob ma gcig la ni/ /bstan par bya yis
gzhan du min/ /gsang ste nyams su blang bar rig sa/ /zhes pa ltar sa bcad gnyis pa 'di bka' dog par mdzad pa'i rgyun ma nyams par yid kyi dran gsor bstan par rigs so/ /gsum
pa dkar chag tu ma bzhugs pa la/ dbang sdud 'dod pa'i rgyal po'i man ngag thun mong ma yin pa'i brgyud 'debs padma rA ga'i chun po tshar pa rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/
'gor rtsa ba'i 'khor lo 'di la zhes pa'i 'khor lo'i bri yig zin bris

gsang ba ni gcig la yin na'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor 'dod pa'i rgyal po'i bsnyen pa byed par 'dod pas zhes pa'i 'dod rgyal gyi sgrub thabs thun mong ma yin pa gtor ma bya khyi dang
mi gzhan la mi sbyin no'i mtha' can/ byin rlabs kyi lung blang ba'i gsal byed tsha rong pa rin chen rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ 'dod rgyal yab yum gyi rjes gnang gces spras
su mdzad pa rje (ngag )dbang phyug rab brtan gyi gsung las mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis zin thor btab pa/ des mdzad pa'i gsang sngags sgra'i rjes gnang bklag
chog tu bkod pa (ngag )zhar byung thun mong gi rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ nyi zla 'khor lo'i rig pa bande bsam gtan gling pas gzhan la phan pa'i sems kyis mdzad pa rnams so/
thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na bsam gtan gling pa phyi ma zhes snang ba nor bu gsal 'bar mdzad mkhan dang gcig gam snyam/ / dpe ris skor la/ sgrub pa'i
maNDal mi 'dra ba gsum/ rab gnas kyi maNDal mi 'dra ba gsum/ gtor ma'i maNDal zhi rgyas dbang drag gi phyi sgrub kyi 'khor lo bzhi/ drag po'i 'khor lo 'dra min gnyis/ yang
sa chen gyi bzhed pa dang mthun pa gcig las bzhi sgrub pa'i 'khor lo kha sbyor bzhi/ sbas pa mig 'byed nas gsungs pa'i rgyas pa'i 'khor lo/ pho mo gnad kyi 'khor lo bzhi
yod pa'i rje btsun rin po che'i gsung dang mthun pa dang po/ phag gru'i bzhed pa dang mthun pa gnyis pa/ dpe ris rnying pa kho na la thugs gtsigs su mdzad pa gsum pa/
gsum pa'i mu khyud kyi sngags dum bu gsum du byas pa bzhi pa/ gnad 'bebs nyi zla'i

'khor lo rigs mi gcig pa gsum/ dril sgrub la dgos pa'i tha chen 'khor lo/ gsang sgrub tha chen 'khor lo/ nang sgrub yab rkyang dang yum rkyang gi 'khor lo re/ rlung 'khor dang
bcas pa'i rjes gnang lung man ngag phyag len dmar khrid du thob pa las/ ngor lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang
ngam/ dpal mchog rdo rje chos/ DA ki bde ba rgyas byed ma/ grub chen dze tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal ba/ grub chen la li ta badzra/ paNDi ta chen po ta thA ga ta rakShi
ta/ bla ma rdo rje gdan pa che ba/ thar rtse ba sogs ngor pa'i gsan yig rnams su rdo rje gdan pa/ stha bI ra zhes pa las che chung gnyis ma bshad do/ rdo rje gdan pa
chung ba/ stha bI ra/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ lcags thang pa/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ rgyal dbang dang rmor chen pa sogs kyi gsan yig tu 'dir slob dpon
rin po che dpal ldan bsod nams rtse mo zhes byung zhing ngor pa'i gsan yig rnams su ma byung ba brtag byar bzhagarje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs
sa skya paNDi ta/ khang ston bsod nams 'bum/ bla ma gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag dbang grags pa/ bla ma byang chub sengge/ shar
chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rje lha mchog sengge/ rdo rje 'chang
sangs rgyas sengge/ ma hA paNDi ta nam mkha' dpal bzang / brang ti nam mkha' rin chen/ se chen gan nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'dren mchog pradznyA sA ga ra/ mkhas grub

chen po sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang ba chen po bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la lan zung gi bar du bka'
drin du stsal to/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la lan mang
du stsal to/ /yang na sa skya paNDi ta nas/ 'phags pa rin po che/ khang ston bsod nams 'bum/ gzhon nu tshul khrims/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar
chen ye shes rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ rtags yod med la ma ltos pa'i lung yongs rdzogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa rin po che nas/ mkhas grub do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tsha
lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ rin chen sengge bzang po/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ dpon mkhan chen bsod nams
rgyal ba mchog dbyangs/ yab rje 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar
pa chos rje/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug yab sras gnyis ka nas rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang
rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa chen po ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' pa bsod nams dbang phyug thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos
skyong bkra shis

grags pa'i rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na rdo ring pa chen po nas/ rje btsun sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ tshar pa rdo rje 'chang man 'dra/ yang na tshar chen yab sras
gnyis nas/ mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra/ yang na mkhyen brtse'i zhabs nas/ drang srong ka bzhi pa'i sras gzhon nu
stobs ldan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra/ yang thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rje mkhyen brtse nas/ mkhas pa gzhon nu stobs ldan/ rdo
rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun
dga' lhun grub man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /ba ri bas sag thang par gsan pa'i chos skor ni/ jo btsun sag thang pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ rje btsun lcags thang pa/   gsan yig gadgA'i
chu rgyun du bar 'dir se chung ba zhes pa dang 'ga' zhig tu lcags thang pa med par de'i tshab tu se chung ba zhes pa byung ngo / /sa skya pa chen po man 'dra/ ngag rtags
can gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang bsod nams chos 'phel dang rje dbang rab gnyis nas mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ 'khon ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams/ de sras 'khon ston bsod nams dbang phyug 'khon ston ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /yang rjes gnang thun mong ba dang glo'i
rtags can rnams kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ kun spangs rje nas/ rje btsun kun dga' grol

mchog 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas bla ma gzhon nu 'bum/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla
ma ngag gi dbang phyug mkhan chen byang chub sengge/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ bdag chen gzhi thog pa kun dga' dbang phyug
bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ khang ston bsod nams 'bum/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ shar pa shes rab
'byung gnas/ de'i gcung rdo rje 'od zer/ 'dul 'dzin bsod nams ye shes/ bla ma bsod nams dar/ bag ston man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen nas/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug glo
bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen nas/ chu mig bdag chen blo gros dbang phyug paN chen shAka mchog brag dkar
sems dpa' chen po/ mkhan chen bkras rnam pa/ rje grol mchog man 'dra'o/ /!/ /dpal sa skya pa'i gser chos dzam dmar srog sgrub kyi skor la/ yig rnying rnal 'byor dbang phyug
yar klungs pa'i mchan ma dang / thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'i lhan thabs ltar sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor du gnod sbyin dmar po yab yum gyi sku gsung thugs kyi rjes
gnang bzlas pa dam bca'i lung dang gtor dbang dod kyi chu sbyin dang bcas pa nos nas/ lung la gsang sgrub thun mong ma yin pa'i yi ge la nang gses kyi rten bca'

ba/ bsnyen sgrub/ las la bskul ba dang bcas pa bla ma chen pos ma sbas par dpal kha gdangs su yi ge ra bkod pa sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ lung blang ba'i man ngag bla ma'i
gsung bzhin dpal sa skyar sbyar ba/  'di yan gyi mchan rnams rnal 'byor dbang phyug yar klungs pas mdzad la/ dam bca' ba'i mchan bu rdo rje gdan pas mdzad do/ / rdo rje
gdan pas mdzad pa'i sku gsung thugs kyi rjes gnang gi gsal byed/ grwa pa dang gser chos kyi dzam dmar gnyis kyi rjes gnang lhan cig pa'i phyag len gzhan rnams dkyus kyi
yi ge bzhin no'i mtha' can dang bcas pa'i lung legs par thob nas/ rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug birWa pa/ grub dbang shar
phyogs nag po pa/ rgyal rigs DA ma ru pa/ gnyis spangs a wa dhU tI pa/ paN chen ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu
ba dgra lha 'bar/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che dpal ldan bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bla chen
yar sgom se bo/ mkhas grub do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen sengge bzang po/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug yar
klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bsod nams dar/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ dpal kun bzang rtse pa/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ shes
rab rgyal mtshan/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ thar rtse paN chen/ ngag dbang mchog legs rdo

rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhan chen bsod nams bzang po/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na rmor chen pa nas/
mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / brag thog
pa dpal 'dzin bzang po/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa/ rje blo gros rnam rgyal/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ tshar pa rdo rje 'chang / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse/ yab sras gnyis
ka nas rdo rje 'chang dbang rab pa/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na rje shar khang pa nas/
rje shAkya 'od zer/ she'u lo tsA ba man 'dra/ yang na shAkya 'od zer nas thar rtse paN chen man 'dra'o/ /rmor chen pas mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge'i steng nas bdag
gis nos so/ /smras pa/ padma rA ga'i lhun por nyi gzhon gyis/ /lan brgyar dkris lta'i 'od 'bar rigs byed ma/ /tshogs bdag 'dod pa'i rgyal po rmugs 'dzin bcas/ /khams gsum
dbang sdud gdams pa mnos tshul lo/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ gser chos dmar po skor gsum dang rmugs 'dzin dmar po srog
sgrub bcas pa'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste nyer gsum pa'o/ /!/ /phyi rol yul du snang ba'i dregs pa gsum/ /nang du rdo rje'i

lus kyi rtsa khams gsum/ /gsang bar sems nyid gsal stong zung 'jug gsum/ /dbyer med srid zhi'i mgon po'i chos kyi skor/ /de'ang 'dzam gling bstan pa'i mnga' bdag lha mchog
'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi sgyu 'phrul rol pa rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras la bstan pa bsrung ba'i mtshon char chos skyong ba'i srung ma grangs med pa zhig bka' babs pa'i nang
nas rgya gar ma ga dhA'i rdo rje gdan gyi sgo skyong 'phags yul paN grub rnams kyi srung ma'i gtso bo rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po ni/ mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur
gyi rgyud las/ de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa chen pos nag po chen po 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo zhes 'byung ba ltar/ bcom ldan
'das rdo rje 'chang chen po'i sku gsung thugs dbyer mi phyed pa'i sprul par bstan pas phyogs re tsam gyi sprul pa'i bstan srung gzhan las ches khyad par du 'phags pa'i
phyir bstan srung kun gyi gtso bo ste/ tshul de la dgongs nas kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis/ bgrang yas bstan srung kun gyi sde dpon che/ /dran pas snying gi
mun sel rdo rje gur/ /zhes ched du brjod pa'ang sgro skur gyis dben pa'i rang bzhin brjod pa'i rgyan kho na ste/ de'ang dpal kye rdo rje'i bshad pa'i rgyud rdo rje gur/
mgon po mngon par 'byung ba/ lha mo'i khungs 'phags yul na bzhugs pa'i gdan bzhi'i rgyud rgyas pa la sogs pa rnams las gsal bar bstan/ bka' lung gi 'grel byed dam pa 'phags
pa'i yul du grub pa mchog gi sa la bzhugs pa'i slob dpon bram ze mchog sred la sogs pas dar zhing

rgyas par mdzad/ bsil ldan kha ba'i ljongs 'dir ma hA paNDi ta gha ya dha ra dang don yod rdo rje dang shraddhA ka ra warma dang shAkya shrI rnams las brgyud de byon pa 'jam
dpal rdo rje rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras rnams kyis ches cher gsal bar mdzad de/ ma hA kA la'i chos skor gyi brjed byang bsam 'phel nor bu'i phreng ba las/ khyab bdag
gur gyi mgon po'i chos skor ni/ /'phags pa'i yul du paN grub rnams kyis phye/ /rgyud rgyal ma dros chu gter las byung ba'i/ /bka' babs rnam bzhi'i gdams pa'i chu rgyun ni/
/lo tsA rnam bzhi'i gsung gi 'bab stegs las/ /legs 'ongs sa skya'i bla chen thugs mtshor 'khyil/ /gang de'i gsung gi bdud rtsi'i zegs ma ni/ /phyogs brgyar 'phros pas
kha ba'i sman ljongs 'dir/ /zab ston lbu phreng bye bas phyug pa yi/ /rjes 'brangs chu klung rnam bzhi ring du babs/ /zhes pa ltar rgyud rgyal rnams kyi gdams pa'i snying
po 'phags yul paN grub rnams kyis srol rgyas bsdus sna tshogs su btod pa'i nang nas rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa las brgyud pa'i lam 'bras pa'i gur gyi mgon po'i gdams
pa lo chen 'brog mis bsgyur ba dang / bla ma rdo rje gdan pa las brgyud pa sgrub thabs kun las btus pa lugs kyi mgon po'i gdams pa ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba dang / paNDi
ta dad byed go cha las brgyud pa'i mgon po'i gdams pa lo chen rin bzang gis bsgyur ba mal lo tsA ba'i lugs su grags pa dang / kaShmi ra'i bsod snyoms pa chen po paN chen
shAkya shrI las brgyud pa'i mgon po'i gdams pa sa lo tsA ba

kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba ste lo paN chen po bzhi las brgyud pa'i bka' ma chad pa chu bo chen po bzhi'i rgyun ltar babs pa'o/ /gyi ljang lugs ni lo chen rin bzang
nas mal lor brgyud pa yin na'ang / stod lugs smad lugs gnyis su byung ba'i stod lugs rnams mal lo nas brgyud pa yin pas bka' babs phyi ma'i khongs su don gyis 'du zhing
/ lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang lo chen nas brgyud pa dang gyi ljang smad lugs kyi gdams skor rnams rje btsun gong ma rnams las ma brgyud na'ang / gzhi thog pa sngags 'chang kun
dga' zla ba nas sa lugs su bka' babs pas deng sang man ngag rnams phyogs gcig tu mdzad pa yin no/ /de la bka' babs bzhi'i gdams pa rjes 'brang gi mkhas grub ngor pa dang
rdzong pa dang gong dkar ba las brgyud pa dang / kha'u brag rdzong pa las brgyud pa'i lugs srol gnyis las/ phyi ma'i nang du gong ma gsum yang 'dus par bzhed pa'ang lugs
srol 'di nyid kyi phyogs la sku drin gzhal du ma mchis pa'i snyan brgyud bstan pa'i srog zung sa chen por gyur pa tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po blo gsal rgya mtsho'i
zhal snga nas/ khyad par nag po chen po'i man ngag ni/ /brgyud ldan bla ma bcu phrag gcig la zhus/ /'gran zla kun bral drin can rdo ring pa'i/ /snyan brgyud zab mo bum
pa gang byor thob/ /e waM pa ni bsdus la spros pa chung / /mus srad pa ni dkar chag khrigs chags can/ /rdo rje gdan pa 'cham dang nus pa'i bdag/ kho bos thob pa'i thun mong
brgyud pa gsum/ /zhes snga ma gsum po thun

mong bar bzhed cing de dag kyang thun mong ma yin pa rin chen sgang pa sgos kyi zhal ngo nang brgyud snyan brgyud 'dir 'dus pa yin no zhes bzhed do/ /gang ltar yang 'di nyid
ji ltar 'chad par byed pa la snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi ldan gyi tshul du 'chad de/ spyir gsang chen gdams pa'i chos skor snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi dang sbyar ba'i lugs
ltar na khog 'bubs lo rgyus rnams ni bla ma tshad ma/ nyams khrid dang mngon spyod drag po'i las sbyor sogs phyag len dmar khrid du bstar pa ni nyams myong tshad ma/ rgyab
brten gyi man ngag be bum rnams ni bstan bcos tshad ma/ bshad khungs kyi rgyud dang rgya gzhung rnams ni lung tshad mar yang 'gyur la/ gtso bor snyan brgyud bzhi dang
sbyor dgos pas/ de ni byin rlabs chu bo'i rgyun dang 'dra ba'i bka' ma nub pa/ gdams ngag gser 'gyur gyi rtsi lta bu'i sarga ma log pa/ mos gus gzhon nu'i dga' ba lta bu'i
bsam pa tshim pa/ bsnyen bkur lha 'dod yon la longs spyod pa lta bu'i dpal 'byor gyi rgyun ma nyams pa ste bzhi'am/ 'ga' zhig tu byin rlabs kyi sgo dbye ba'i rten 'brel
dang por bsgrigs pa'i ched du snyan brgyud bzhi pa dang por byas pa'i go rim yod pa dang / yang na bla ma snga phyi mang po'i gsung sgros su snyan brgyud gsum pa dang bzhi
pa gnyis go rim log par bshad pa'i tshul yang yod de/ 'di ltar snyan brgyud dang  rdo rje slob dpon la ltos pa'i sngon 'gro'i snyan brgyud/ po dbang dang rjes gnang byin
rlabs kyi bka' chu bo'i rgyun ma nub par bskur ba thob pa'o/ /snyan brgyud gnyis  rdo rje slob dpon la ltos pa'i dngos gzhi'i snyan brgyud/ pa man ngag gser

'gyur gyi rtsi dang 'dra ba gdams pa'i sarga ma log par thob pa'o/ /snyan brgyud gsum pa  snyan brgyud kyi rgyu la snyan brgyud kyi ming btags/ rdo rje'i slob dpon chen po'i
lus dang longs spyod thams cad kyi sgo nas mnyes par byas pa las snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa zab mo thob par 'gyur ba ste/ rje sa skya pa chen pos bla ma mal lo tsA ba la
gser srang bcu bdun dus gcig tu phul bas gdams pa ma lus pa thob pa lta bu'o/ /snyan brgyud bzhi  snyan brgyud kyi 'bras bu la ming btags/ pa mos gus gzhon nu'i bde ba lta
bu shugs las 'byung ba'i go rim mi 'dra bar snang na'ang 'chad tshul gyi khyad par cung zad las don gyi cha la khyad par med pa yin la/ de ltar snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi
ldan gyi sgo nas 'chad dgos pa/ thog mar byin rlabs chu bo'i rgyun dang 'dra ba'i bka' ma nub pa la dbang dang rjes gnang gnyis/ dang po dbang gi bka' ma nub pa la/ 'jam
dbyangs grags rdzong chung ba'ang zer/ pa'am chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i nag po chen po'i dkyil 'khor gyi mngon par rtogs pa bdud las rnam rgyal dang
dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga mgon po rnam rol/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i zin bris rnams la brten nas ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du bram ze chen po nas nye
bar brgyud pa'i mgon po gri gug lha lnga'i rig pa'i dbang lnga/ sku gsung thugs yon tan phrin las kyi rjes gnang / brtan byed du chu'i dbang / sngags kyi bzlas lung dang
bcas pa/ mngon dkyil bshad ma thag pa'i steng nas/ bla ma mal lo'i bzhed pa'i gur mgon lha brgyad kyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor

du rig pa'i dbang lnga/ rjes gnang bzlas lung dang bcas pa/ mngon dkyil de dag la brten nas bla ma brag steng pa'i bzhed pa gur mgon lha bcu gnyis ma'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor
du rig pa'i dbang lnga/ sku gsung thugs yon tan phrin las kyi rjes gnang bzlas lung dang bcas pa/ mngon dkyil de khar brten nas rgyud dur khrod nag po'i rjes su 'brangs
pa'i gyi ljang lugs kyi mgon po lha bcu bdun ma'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du/ chu cod paN rdo rje dril bu ming dbang bzlas lung dang bcas pa rnams dkyil chog tu lugs
gnyis gsungs pa'i rgya gzhung lugs sor gnas/ yang mngon dkyil de dag la brten nas sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor du gri gug lha lnga'i dbang snyan brgyud lugs ltar bzlas lung yan
rgya gzhung sor bzhag la/ sku gsung thugs kyi rjes gnang / gsang dbang sher dbang dbang bzhi pa dang bcas pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa rjes gnang gi bka' ma nub pa'i skor la/
rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge dang / paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas lo chen gyi bzhed pa gtso bor gyur pa'i lcam
dral lha gsum sbags te bsgrub pa'i sku gsung thugs kyi rjes gnang / dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i phyag len la gzhi byas rgyal tsha lung mang po dang bla ma zhang ston khu dbon
gyi phyag bzhes zin bris kyis brgyan te yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge dang bsham sogs mthong brgyud kyi bka' srol ltar lha brgyad mkha' 'gro
sbags sgrub thun mong ba'i rjes gnang / mgon po rnam rol gyi mngon rtogs dang dam pa gong ma'i phyag len ltar mgon po lha bcu gnyis pa thun mong ba'i rjes gnang / ngor chen
rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge dang / paN chen brang ti pas mdzad pa'i lha bcu gnyis ma'i rjes gnang gi yi ge ra 'dor len bgyid
pa la brten nas lha brgyad mkha' 'gro sbags sgrub thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang / gtor chog pho nya myur mgyogs dang thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i tho yig bzhin
dus gcig la chig brgyud las mi gnang ba'i lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang / paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge'i steng nas gur
gyi mgon po lha brgyad kyi steng sgo ma bzhi bsnan pa'i lha bcu gnyis kyi rjes gnang / mgon po rnam rol gyi

mngon rtogs dang kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyi tho yig ltar dus gcig la chig brgyud kho nar gnang ba'i mgon po lha bcu gnyis thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang / rje byams
pa rab brtan pas mdzad pa dang / mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags pas mdzad pa/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge so so'i steng nas mgon po khro
bo bcu'i rjes gnang bka' rgya shin tu dam pa/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan  kha byang legs sbyar gyi skad du byas pa yod/ gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge la brten nas gsang
khrid kyi smin byed lha brgyad kyi steng du las mkhan zangs gri can gyi mngon rtogs bsnan pa'i mgon po lha dgu'i rjes gnang bka' rgya shin tu dam pa/ mus chen sangs rgyas
rin chen pa'i yi ge ltar dpal ldan lha mo dud sol ma'i phyi sgrub thun

mong ba'i rjes gnang / rngog ston bsod nams bstan 'dzin gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge ltar dpal ldan lha mo dud pa'i sol ba can gyi gsang sgrub thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang nan
chags mar grags pa/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gi zin tho dang brgyud pa'i gsung sgros ltar nang gi 'di slar thob rgyus bris/ las mkhan ber nag zangs gri can gyi rjes gnang
bka' rgya ma/ yang bshad ma thag pa'i yi ge gnyis dang / mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i zangs gri skor gsum gyi rjes gnang gi zin bris la brten nas gcer
bu zangs gri can gyi  'di sngon ma thob kyang slar thob rgyu'i dbang gis bris/ rjes gnang / sa skya'i sngags 'chang chen po kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge dang
gsung rgyun phyag bzhes ltar gsang ba'i las mkhan pu Ta ming sring gi rjes gnang / pu Ta'i rjes gnang gi chings la gzhi mdzad cung zad mi mthun pa brgyud pa'i gsung sgros
kyi brgyan te ru mtshon gyi las mkhan bran bdud gshin rje nag po'i rjes gnang thun mong ba/ sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge ltar bran bdud gshin
rje nag po'i rjes gnang rnams legs par nos nas/ snyan brgyud gnyis pa gdams ngag gser 'gyur gyi rtsi dang 'dra ba'i sarga ma log pa'i skor la/ gdams pa'i dngos gzhi dang
rgyab brten lung dang 'brel ba'i sgo nas sgro 'dogs dpyod pa gnyis/ dang po la/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen pos mdzad pa'i phyi khrid rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i yi ge dang
/ de'i lhan thabs kyi tshul du thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa'i yi

ge gnyis la gzhi byas/ yig chung zur 'debs dang brgyud pa'i zhal shes kyis brgyan te/ sngon 'gro thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ dngos gzhi zab pa'i gnad lnga dang khyad
par gyi man ngag mde kha gdags pa'i sgo nas bsrung ba/ spyi dang bye brag khyad par gsum gyi sgo nas bzlog pa/ bstan pa'i spyi dgra dang rnal 'byor sgos dgra bsgral ba'i
sgo nas gsad pa/ rdzas dang dmigs pa la brten pa'i mnan pa'i dmigs khrid rnams dngos bstan nyams su len dgos pa'i nyams khrid/ mtshan bcas rdzas dang 'khor lo la bstan
pa sogs la ngo sprod phyag bzhes/ khyad par thun mong ma yin pa'i man ngag gi mde kha gdags pa la gsum gyi nang dam tshig gi 'khor lo sems nyid ye shes kyi rtsal 'don zhes
pa rnam rtog bdud bzhi bcom nas tshe 'di nyid la mchog gi dngos grub sgrub pa'i gsang ba'i yang snying skal ldan gyi slob bu gcig la chig brgyud du ston pa/ gong gi sa
bcad kyis ma zin pa'i drag po sngags rgod kyi man ngag gi khrid/ 'di la brten nas bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis rgya 'dre tshar gcad pa'i lo rgyus ngo mtshar ba yang yod/
'di dag la phyi nang gsang gsum du dbye na gdams pa dngos gzhi spyi'i brag rdzong / drag po sngags rgod nang gi brag rdzong / ye shes kyi 'khor lo gsang ba'i brag rdzong
ste zab khrid kha lag tshang ba 'di ni rjes 'brang gi mkhas grub phal cher la ma grags shing gdung brgyud rim par chig brgyud du byon pa'i slob bshad kho na yin pas/ 'jam
dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis/ rjes 'brang mkhas dang grub par grags rnams la/ /thun mong gdams pa'i

dpal 'byor mtha' yas mod/ /gsang chen slob bshad bdud rtsi'i thigs pa 'di/ /mkhas rlom phal gyi rna ba'i spyod yul min/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu'i nyams khrid smin rgyas dang
/ rdo rje nag po chen po'i nang khrid dam gsang khrid du grags pa ni nang rtsa gsum 'khor lo lnga la brten nas bsgrubs pas nang sgrub/ gsang ba sems kyi gnad la brten nas
bsgrubs pas gsang sgrub tu grags shing 'di la thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa gnyis yod pa la gnyis ka'i rtsa bar gyur pa gong mas mdzad pa'i man ngag mdor bsdus/ de
nyid cung zad rgyas su btang ba dam pas mdzad pa dang / gsang rten lus la sba ba'i yig chung rnams dang / zhal shes la brten nas nang khrid thun mong ba rnal 'byor dbang
phyug chen po yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i bsnyen sgrub thun mong ma yin pa'i man ngag la sogs pa rgya cher bzhugs shing / 'di skabs su rgyal dbang
thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtshos/ yar klungs pas mdzad pa'i man ngag 'di yi ge nag 'gros lta bur bkod pa'i thog ma yin 'dug pas/ gsung las/ gzhan gyis
bskul phyir gzhan phan bsam pas bris/ /snyigs dus nub par dogs pas 'dir brjod bya/ /zhes dang / dpe mkhyud med par ma bris na snyigs dus su song bas brjed pa dang nub kyis
dogs nas/ yi ge ra gsal por 'dri bar srung ma rnams la lo gsum gyi bar gsol ba btab/ ces sogs ltar/ de yan chad du yi ge gsal po med par shes nus/ mal lo'i rjes gnang
gi thor/ man ngag

phyi sgrub dang nang lus la brten pa rnams sbyin zhes dang / sa chen gyi 'byung lugs gtor mar rang nang gi rnal 'byor pa yin na bdag nyid kyi lte ba chos 'byung gru gsum nang
du bsdus la bzhag ces gsang rten lus la sba ba'i gnad zab mo zur tsam bstan pa sogs cung zad ma dgongs pa khrid brgya'i nang du/ skyed cing gsed nas phyag bzhi'i srog
thig phyung / /gur la'ang 'dra cog yar klungs pa yis sbyar/ /zhes zur za mdzad pa ni rje btsun grol mchog mkhas grub chen po yin yang phyogs 'di la gzigs pa'i spyan dkyus
thung bas thugs su ma shong ba'i gsung tsam mo zhes zur za ba mdzad do/ /de yang nang khrid kyi khrid tshul la phyi'i brag rdzong gis bskyed rim dang / nang gsang gis rdzogs
rim byas pa'i lugs dang / bskyed rim gong ltar la/ rdzogs rim yar klungs pa lugs kyi nang khrid thun mong bas byas pa'i lugs dang / rdzogs rim thun mong ma yin pa gsang
khrid kyis byas pa sogs lugs gsum tsam las dang po ni gong du song zin zin pa dang / da lta'i phyag len la gsum pa song na gnyis pa'ang zhar las 'byung bas rje btsun
rdo ring pas sam mkhas grub ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i khrid yig dang thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i khrid yig yid bzhin nor bu la gzhi byas/ yig
chung zhal shes sogs kyis legs par brgyan te/ sngon 'gro skyabs 'gro sems bskyed/ yi ge brgya pa/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ dngos gzhi rten bskyed pa'i rim pa khrid gzhung du'ang
bshad kyang brag rdzong mar rgyas par song bas yang skyor ma dgos/ brten pa

rdzogs pa'i rim pa rdo rje'i lus kyi gnad shes pa la brten nas rang sems gsal stong zung 'jug gi mgon po mngon du bya ba'i nye lam rtsa gsum 'khor lo lnga la brten nas bsnyen
pa'i dmigs rim/ 'khor lo lnga ldan dang rdo rje'i bzlas pa'i sgo nas bsgrub pa'am rbad pa/ las sbyor thun mong ba bstan pa'i spyi dgra dang rnal 'byor sgos dgra bsgral
ba/ thun mong ma yin pa'i 'khor lo lnga ldan gyi khrid dang bcas pa nyams myong yid ches su legs par nos so/ /de yang zab lam 'di la brten nas gnas skabs kyi dngos grub
tu ma zad mchog gi dngos grub kyang bde blag tu bsgrub nus pas/ mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis/ zab las ches zab gsang chen snying po'i bcud/ /dkon las ches dkon yid bzhin rin
chen dbang / /mchog las ches mchog snyan brgyud gdams pa 'di/ /sa skya'i rje btsun thugs kyi nying khu yin/ /'di 'dra rtse gcig bsgoms na lta ci smos/ /thos pa tsam gyis
snang srid 'khor 'das chos/ /kun gyi rang mtshang rjen par ston pa'i phyir/ /zab par rlom pa gzhan gyis do zla min/ /zhes bsngags brjod mdzad pa ni bla ma dang gdams ngag
la sngon med pa'i mos gus gzhon nu'i dga' bas thugs gting nas tshim zhing shin tu rangs pa'i gsung du mngon zhing / dpe 'di rang gi bstan pa 'dzin nges las/ /gzhan gyi
rna bar ming tsam mi bsgrag cing / /snying nas dad kyang bstan pa mi zin na/ /chos rgyun shod la dpe rgyun sba bar byos/ /zhes gsungs pa shin tu snying la bcang bya'i bslab
par snang ste deng gi dus 'dir la la dag

gis mchog dang thun mong gi dngos grub bsgrub pa'i sgo nas rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa dang sems can gyi khams la phan par bsgrub pa'i bsam pa dang / bla ma dang chos la ci
yang mi bsam par/ chos skyong gnyan pa dang gdams pa zab pa'i grags pa tsam la brten nas chos ci thob tu byed kyin 'ongs pa'i slob ma chu shing gi rnam par thar pa 'chang
ba'i rigs can la mi smra ba'i brtul zhugs 'chang ba'i zhal gdams su gda'o/ /!/ /gnyis pa rgyab brten lung dang 'brel pa'i sgo nas sgro 'dogs gcod pa la/ rtsa ba'i yi ge
bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos dkar chag bsgrigs par mdzad pa'i mgon pod me 'bar ma'i skor/ der ma 'dus pa'i yan lag gi yi ge'i skor dang gnyis/ dang po ni/ bdag chen
rdo rje 'chang gis lcam dral gyi chos skor gsan pa'i yi ge phal cher glegs bam du bsgrigs par mdzad pa dus re zhig na nyang stod rgyal mkhar rtse nas sa skyar spyan drangs
tshe chom pos khyer bar glo bur du me 'bar zhing sgra chen po sgrog pa dang 'phar ba la sogs byung bas de nas bzung ste bu yig rnams la'ang me 'bar mar grags pa'i chos
sde 'di la/ phyi nang gsang ba thun mong ma yin pa'i skor dang gsum/ dang po la/ yid ches bskyed pa lo rgyus/ snod ldan du bsgrub pa rjes gnang / gang las byung ba'i gzhi'i
rgyud/ rtsa ba'i sgrub yig de dag la mkho ba'i las tshogs lhan thabs dang lnga/ dang po la/ rdo rje gdan gyi ka ba nas rgyal rigs padma badzra zhes bya bas spyan (mchod
rten)(e)(mu)drangs pa'i mgon po 'di nyid gter nas 'byung ba'i lo rgyus/ bka' ma'i lo

rgyus zhes pa chos skyong gi brgyud pa'i lo rgyus (mchod rten)tho tsam bla ma'i gsung bzhin rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug gis sa skya dang yar klungs phyogs
su bris pa/ gnyis pa snod ldan du bsgrub pa rjes gnang la/ 'gor dpal nag po chen po bsten pa'i gang zag des zhes yod pa'i lcam dral gyi rjes gnang (mchod rten)gi tho bla
ma mal gyis mdzad pa las mkhan gyi khyad par ni gud na mchis so sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ lcam dral gyi rjes gnang gi cho (mchod rten)(e)(mu)ga nyi mas bskul nas 'phags
pa rin po che blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis me yos smin drug zla ba'i tshes bcu dgu'i nyin byang 'dam gyi sa'i char mdzad pa/  ngor rdzong gnyis kyi be bum du 'di dang tshig
mi 'dra ba 'ga' re 'dug pa zhus dag ma song ba zhig nas mched dam snyam/ nag po chen po lcam dral gyi rjes gnang (mchod rten)bla ma chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po
che'i gsung zhang dkon mchog dpal gyis zin bris su byas pa 'di rnams mi la mi spel ba'i bka' rgya can/  gser pod kyi de lha brgyad dang sbyar ba'i 'di dang zhus dag ye mi
pher zhing brjed tho lta bu'i 'dra min gnyis 'dug pa zur pa zhig yin par snang ngo / / dpal rdo rje nag po chen po lcam dral gyi rjes gnang gi zur 'debs kyi man (mchod rten)ngag
snyan nas snyan du brgyud pa zur khang pa slob dpon dkon mchog 'od kyis yi ge ra bkod pa/ rdo rje nag po chen po lcam dral gyi rjes gnang gi chings (mchod rten)bla
ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis phyag len dus dang mthun par rgyas bsdus ci rigs mdzad kyang lan mang du mdzad par bltas shing drung gi gsung

las zin bris su yar klungs pa ldong ston sengge rgyal mtshan gyis dpal bsam yas lhun gyis grub par sug bris mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i 'gor bla ma dam pa la phyag 'tshal lo dpal
ma hA kA la'i rjes gnang gi zhes yod pa'i rjes gnang (mchod rten)gi yi ge 'chams sku mi g.yo bar gda'o'i mtha' can/  dngos gzhi lcam dral gyi rjes gnang yin 'dug cing
deng sang lha brgyad thun mong ma yin par mdzad pa'i phyag len dang phyogs tsam mthun par tshogs sgom pa nas brgyud pa'ang bris 'dug go/ lcam dral gyi rjes su gnang ba'i
rim pa bla ma (mchod rten)rnams kyis phyag len ji ltar mdzad pa bzhin du dpon shes rab bzang pos bskul nas dam pa kun dga' grags kyis tre stod 'bom dgon par yi ge ra bkod
pa/  mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags lha brgyad ma'i rjes gnang gi yi ge ra ngos 'dzin mdzad pa mdun du bka' sdod rnams sam zhes pa la dgongs pa 'dra/ 'gor khyed rnams
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i sgor zhugs nas zhes yod pa'i dpal mgon lcam dral gyi rjes (mchod rten)(e)gnang gi brjed byang  gser pod na lo rgyus 'dra min dang go rim cung
zad mi mthun pa snang ba yig skyon du mngon/ btsun pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos sbyar ba/ thun mong ma yin pa lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang bya (mchod rten)thabs
rgyas pa bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi phyag len mang du mthong ba la gzhi byas zhang dang brag phug pa'i zin bris dang rgyal tsha lung mang po'i phyag len gyis
cung zad brgyan nas bdag cag gi bla ma'i gsung gis rjes su gnang zhing bkas bskul ba dang / bshes gnyen grogs mched dam pas nan gyis bskul nas yar klungs pa sengge rgyal
mtshan gyis

klu'i dgon pa bde chen du sug bris su mdzad pa rnams so/ /gsum pa gang las byung ba'i gzhi'i rgyud ni/ 'phags pa mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po
chen po'i dkyil 'khor bsdus (mchod rten)(e)pa'i rtog pa'i le'u  glegs bam du 'di tsam las mgon po mngon byung nas rigs drug gi rnam gzhag bstan pa yig tshogs dang / khros
rgyud kyi le'u bcu par bshad pa sogs rgyud gzhan rnams dpyad gzhir dgongs nas ma bkod dam snyam/ bco lnga pa las khol du phyung ba  'di gyi ljang po ti na yang yod/ paNDi
ta ga ya dha ra dang lo tsA ba 'brog mi'i 'gyur las bris pa/ bzhi pa rtsa ba'i sgrub yig la/ 'phags yul gyi paN grub kyis rgyud la brten pa'i sgrub skor/ gangs khrod kyi
skyes chen rnams kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub skor te gnyis/ dang po la 'gor skad shan sbyar dang / bla ma la gus snying rjer ldan/ /tshul khrims sogs ldan bsdu dngos bzhis/ /zhes
yod pa'i sgrub (mchod rten)(rdo rje)thabs rgyas  sgyur byed kyi lo paN mi gcig tsam ma gtogs gyi ljang po ti na yang yod cing birWa pa'i slob ma nag po par bka' sdod/
tshogs bdagagashin rje/ gnod sbyin ltar gyi pho rkyang gi sgrub lugs bzhi bram ze chen pos gsan pa yin/ pa bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po shraddhA
ka ra warma dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba/ yang mdzad pa po dang sgyur byed kyi lo paN gong ma ltar gyi sgrub thabs (mchod rten)(e)bsdus pa 'gor skad shan
sbyar dang rdo rje nag po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo sngar gsungs pa'i cho gas zhes yod pa/  dkar chag na chung ngu zer ba 'dug cing gser pod kyi de yig skyon yin nam dbu
nas cung zad ma mthun/ 'gor skad

shan sbyar dang rdo rje 'chang chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /ji ltar sngon gsungs pa'i rim pas stong pa nyid du bsgoms pa'i rjes la zhes (mchod rten)yod pa'i nag po chen po'i
sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa lo tsA ba ga rod kyis bsgyur ba/ 'gor skad shan sbyar dang dpal nag po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /tho rengs mal nas langs
nas zhes yod pa'i nag po chen po'i sgrub (mchod rten)thabs byin gyis brlab pa dang bcas pa slob dpon bsod snyoms pas mdzad pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ma ti kIrti dang
lo tsA ba dge slong pradznyA kIrtis bsgyur ba/ 'gor skad shan sbyar dang dpal mgon po nag po la phyag 'tshal lo de kho na bzhin du sngon du bstan pa'i cho gas zhes yod pa'i
sgrub (mchod rten)(mu)thabs bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/  'di dang lo chen gyis bsgyur ba'i sgrub thabs chung ba dang klu sgrub kyis mdzad
pa'i sgrub thabs gsum 'gyur khyad tsam ma gtogs don gcig ces bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gsung / kha skong po ti na'ang bzhugs so/ / 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i dpal mgon
po nag po'i sgrub thabs dregs pa zil (mchod rten)(rgya)gnon zhes pa slob dpon chen po padma 'byung gnas kyis bsam yas mchims phur mdzad pa/ 'di rgya padma dbang phyug
gis gter nas spyan drangs pa rgyal tsha lung mang po nas brgyud pa ma gtogs rje btsun gong ma nas ma brgyud pas bka' gter gnyis med do/ /bram ze chen pos mdzad pa'i mgon
po lha lnga'i dkyil (mchod rten)(rdo rje)(pra)chog paNDi ta ga ya dha ra dang 'gos lo tsA bas bsgyur ba/ 'gor skad shan sbyar dang slob dpon sku

la sdo byed dang zhes yod pa'i dpal nag po chen po srog gi spu gri'i sgrub (mchod rten)thabs bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa mal gyo lo tsA ba blo gros grags kyis bsgyur ba
rnams so/  'gyur byang tsam ma gtogs gyi ljang na'ang yod/ / gnyis pa gangs can gyi ljongs su byon pa'i skyes chen rnams kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub skor la/ rkyang sgrub dang
sbags sgrub gnyis/  ma hA kA las bram ze chen por gnang ba'i sgrub thabs gsum zhes pa rang lugs la pho rkyang mo rkyang sbags sgrub gsum du bzhed/ dang po la pho rkyang
du bsgrub pa/  bka' sdod/ tshogs bdagagashin rje/ gnod sbyin ltar grub pa bzhi yod pa lha'i rnams mi 'dra ba bzhi dang bdag mdun sogs kyi sgo nas dbye ba rang lugs su bzhed
cing / rdzong chung ba gshin rje dang gnod sbyin ltar sgrub pa'i yi ge logs su ma mthong gsung ba brag steng pa'i sgrub lugs bzhi dang bla chen bsod blo'i man ngag tshigs
bcad ma dam pa'i gshin rje ltar sgrub pa sogs ma gzigs pa'i skyon no/ / mo rkyang du bsgrub pa/ 'khor rkyang du bsgrub pa dang gsum/ dang po la 'gor bla ma dam pa rnams
la phyag 'tshal lo spyir bram ze mchog sred kyi mgon po lcam dral sgrub lugs 'di la zhes yod pa'i pho rkyang (mchod rten)(e)(mu)gi sgrub thabs bod yig mar grags pa/ 
rdzong chung bas dgra dang bgegs la bya ba zhes pa las mdzad pa po ngos ma zin par snang ngo / /mal lo chen pos mdzad pa phyis sa chen gyis zhus dag ma dam tshig bsrung ba
dang 'bad pa shin tu gal che'o pho rkyang du bsgrub pa'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo brgyud pa bzang ldan mal gyi bu thu bo zhes yod pa'i
pho rkyang gi bsnyen bsgrub sbags (mchod rten)(e)(mu)te bsgrub pa  'di'i sbyar byang

na puNya badzra gyis sbyar zer ba 'dug cing mkhan chen ngag chos pa'i gsan yig na'ang de ltar snang la/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse/ lo pa spyan snga/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba
gsum gyi gsan yig na dkar chag sor gnas bzhin mdzad 'dug pa don la gcig ser pod na kha skong nang gi pho rkyang gi sgrub thabs shog sngon can gnyan phul byung bas mdzad
par ngos bzung nas 'di la rkyang sgrub kyi bsnyen sgrub sbrags ma zhes pa las gnyan phul byung bas mdzad pa'i 'phros mi 'dug la/ rdzong chung ba'i der bgegs la bya ba man
chad ma tshang zhing slob dpon rtse mos mdzad ces snang ngo / / sa chen gyi slob ma gnyan phul byung bas mdzad pa/ 'gor oM swa sti bla ma dang nag po chen po la phyag 'tshal
lo kA la'i man ngag la  yig rnying snga ma'i 'phros zhes pa dkar chag dang dpe'i zhal byang gnyis kar snang / zhes dang mjug (mchod rten)tu sa skya jo sras kyi yi ge
man ngag rnying pa snga ma'i 'phros sa mApta'i mtha' can/ 'gor oM swa sti dpal nag po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rten gyi gang zag dbang bzhi'i snod du rung ba zhes yod
pa'i nag po chen po'i 'byung lugs bstan (mchod rten)cing gtor ma dang po'i 'phros kyi yi ge rnying pa'i cha lag gong mas mdzad pa rje btsun gyi bla dpe las bris pa/ 'gor
bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la spyi bos gus pas phyag 'tshal lo bhe dan gyi yul na bram ze mchog sred ces yod pa'i tshogs kyi bdag (mchod rten)(mu)po'i tshul du sgrub pa'i u
pa de sha sa chen gyis mdzad pa/ mgon po khro bcu tshogs bdag ltar sgrub par ngos 'dzin yang / de'i rjes gnang gis mal lo'i lugs kyi pho rkyang la rjes gnang med par bzhed
pa la mi gnod pa 'dra ste/ de ni gtso rkyang la dgongs kyi 'di ni pho rkyang gtso 'khor sbags sgrub yin pas so snyam

zhing / mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyi lhag bsam rab dkar gyi dri lan du sbags sgrub yin pas so rje tshar pa gsung ba'i ngag rgyun de legs po snang zhes pa 'dug kyang
/ sa bcad du rkyang sgrub sbags sgrub ces so sor dbye ba'i dbang du song na 'di lugs gnyis gang du'ang ngos 'dzin dka' ba'i dogs gnas che ba zhig 'dug go/ 'gor bla ma dang
dpal kye rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo tshogs kyi bdag po'i tshul du sgrub pa'i bsnyen sgrub gnyis sngon du song nas las (mchod rten)(mu)(rdo rje)la sbyar ba zhes yod pa'i
man ngag gi yig rnying  rdzong chung ba ser ba dbab pa gzhung gi yig sna'i zhabs na yod ces logs su ngos bzung ba de 'di'i nang gi de'o/ ser ba bcad pa'i las rnams sgrub
thabs nyid las btsal  rdzong chub ba gsal zhes sgra bshad dang bcas gsung / lo'i mtha' can/ de'i bsad las 'gor dpal (mchod rten)(rdo rje)nag po chen po sgrub par 'dod pas
zhes yod pa'i slob dpon bram ze mchog sred kyi man ngag bsad pa'i las sbyor ro'i mtha' can/ 'gor ma hA kA la'i bsnyen pa (mchod rten)(mu)(rdo rje)yang dang po lhag pa'i
lha gang yang rung ba'i bsnyen pa sngon du 'gro bar bya ste zhes yod pa'i bka' bsgo'i tshul du sgrub pa bla ma gong mas mdzad pa sgra snyan gyi rdzas rdzogs so'i mtha'
can/  rdzong chung pa 'di'i nang gi sreg rdzas la ba la ta ka'i rdzas dang bcas bsad smyo dbye gsum so sor kha bsgyur chog pa sgrub thabs nyid nas gsal zhes zhal 'phangs
pa 'dir ngos bzung 'dug yang des mdzad pa'i 'gor dang por bdag nyid kyis bsnyen sngags dang sngags ring gnyis ka la bsnyen pa (mchod

pa'i phyag dper rang

rdzi phyogs su mi sdod zer ba yan las mi 'dug cing 'di'i mjug na yod pa'i me'i gdung ba zhes pa ser pod na chos tshan logs su ngos bzung yod do/ / 'gor skad shan sbyar dang

pa/  'di la dkar chag tu phyi pa mu stegs pa ltar sgrub pa zhes gsung ba rdzong chung bas phyi sgrub dang nang sgrub kyi khyad par yin zhes zur za dang gyi ljang ma gtogs

/ yang nang pa la/ 'jam pa/ cung zad 'jam pa/ shin tu 'jam pa'i rnam gzhag kyang yod cing lha mo bdag bskyed du byed pa lo ka shrI'i yi ge 'di ma gtogs med pa'i tshogs

pa bzhin gzhan

'di dam pa'i gsung dngos min par bskang mdos chen mo las sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal bas zur du phyung ba yin zhes bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gsung zhing / gong dkar rdo
rje gdan pa yang don gyis bzhed la rdzong chung pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan dam pa'i bskang gso 'bring po'i tha snyad mdzad do/ /'gor bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo/
/'di'i shom la g.yang gzhi'i steng du zhes yod pa'i (mu)chos nyid ma dam pa'i bskang gso chung bar rdzong chung ba bzhed pa/ 'gor na mo gu ru/ gzungs gsar pa'am rnying
pa gso bar 'dod na (mchod rten)(mu)zhes yod pa'i nag po chen po'i gzungs 'dzugs  me 'bar mar yang yod/ lugs dam pas mdzad pa/  glegs bam na 'di'i 'gor 'phags pa rin po ches
chu byi mi nyag gi yul du mdzad pa'i gzugs (mchod rten)(mu)'dzugs bstan pa dri med ma zer ba zhig snang ba dkar chag tu mi 'dug pa chad dam snyam/ bka' bsgo dpal ldan
ma hA kA la ma 'phags pas mdzad pa (mchod rten)(mu)bcol pa'i phrin las mdzod kyi mtha' can/  me 'bar ma'i nang sa paN gyis mdzad pa de 'di las nyung ba 'dug nag po chen po'i
(mchod rten)(mu)mnga' gsol kye rdo rje ma dam pa kun dga'

grags kyis shing kun du rang gi brjed byang du bris pa/ brag tsitta dmar po'i gter nas bton pa'i tho yig la brten nas dam pa'i gcung kun dga' dpal gyis (mchod rten)mdzad pa'i
bskang gso he ru ka dpal zhes pa'i shlau ka gcig 'gor yod pa'i dpal ldan ma hA kA la ma/  la la skye ba sngon ma bskang gso'i tho brtsams nas gter du sbas pa skye ba 'dir
dran nas mdzad zer ba rig dpyad tsam ste/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis rtsom pa po'i thugs kyi dkyil las bton par ngos 'dzin mdzad pa ni shin tu legs par mngon no/ /
bskang gso dpal ldan ma hA kA la ma bla chen (mchod rten)grags 'od pas mdzad pa/  dkar chag las 'di ltar byung bas yi ge na yar klungs pas mdzad zer ba nor ram snyam/ bskang
bshags 'byung ba rnam bzhi ma bshes gnyen rdo rje 'dzin pas mdzad pa shes rab dpal sogs kyis bskul ba'i ngor chos rje bla ma dam pas bsam yas su mdzad pa/ dpal rdo rje
nag po chen po lcam dral mnyes par byed pa'i mdos bskang chen mo'i cho ga (mchod rten)rab myos kyi lo snron gyi zla ba'i dkar phyogs la bla ma chen po bsod nams blo gros
kyis mdzad pa/  pu Nya ma ti dhwa dza shrI bha dras sbyar zer ba snang / nag po chen po lcam dral 'khor dang bcas pa'i mdos byang rin po che'i phreng mdzes zhes bya ba
(mchod rten)sngags 'chang kun dga' zla bas dpal ldan sa skya'i dben gnas nyi thog tu rang gi dran pa gso ba dang skal ldan gcig gnyis la phan pa'i phyir du mdzad pa/ mdos
kyi cho ga (mu)bla ma rta nag pa A nandas bskul ba'i don du sa skya'i gzims khang rdzong chung du chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/  'di gnyis rdzong chung glegs
bam du med kyang brgyud pa gcig pas mu'i rtags

thob/ bskul ba po dang mdzad pa po gong ltar gyi (mchod rten)(mu)ma hA kA la'i mdos kyi bsham yig gsang rgyud thugs rgyud bshan pa nag mo'i rgyud la brten nas (mchod rten)dpal
ldan lha mo'i gsang mdos slob dpon chen po padmas mdzad pa/  'di bka' ma yin nam snyam mtha' ma chod/ mgon po'i mnga' gsol gtor chen ru mtshon 'dzugs pa rnams la nye
bar mkho ba'i cho ga (mchod rten)mthu stobs gter mdzod me khyi'i lo sa ga zla ba la bdag chen grags pa blo gros kyis mdzad pa/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis mgon po'i bskang
ba rnying pa rnams las zur du phyung nas rgyas bsdus 'tsham par (mchod rten)(sgo)bsgrigs pa'i gtor bskang dad pa dam tshig ma gnyis med bde chen rol par shog gi mtha'
can/ des yab 'jam dbyangs chos rje'i phyag len bzhin kha'u brag rdzong du (mchod rten)(sgo)sbyar ba'i bla ma spyan chen po'i mdos bskang gi gsal byed/ de nyid la dpal ldan
lha mo zhal gzigs nas 'di ltar rtsoms zhes lung bstan (mchod rten)(sgo)pa ltar mdzad pa'i dud sol ma'i bskang gso/ des thob rgyal gyi rdzong rir rdzong mi rgyag pa dang
dmag sgar mi 'cha' ba'i rdo rje'i chos skyong rnams la (mchod rten)(sgo)bka' bsgos pa'i yi ge nag po chen po'i gtor mdos kyi bskang gso  rdzong chung glegs bam na med kyang
brgyud pa gcig pas mu'i rtags thob/ (mu)rgyas bsdus 'tsham zhing lag len bde bar btsun pa 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i dpal gyis mdzad pa rnams so/ /bdun pa bstod 'bum la/
bram ze blo ldan mchog sred kyis

nag po chen por rtags kyi sgo nas bstod pa dpal ldan mgon po (mchod rten)(mu)ma paNDi ta shraddhA ka ra warma dang gu rub yon tan shI las gu ge tho ling du bsgyur ba/  'di
gyi ljang glegs bam du dngos su med kyang don gyis thob pa 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na gsal/ yang des nag po chen po zhal gzigs dus mdzad pa'i bstod pa'i phreng
ba (mchod rten)(mu)nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ma paNDi ta la li ta badzra dang lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba/  gyi ljang po ti dang bstod 'bum zhabs btags mar
yang yod/ slob dpon bha wi lhas mdzad pa'i bstod pa (mchod rten)(mu)las rnams kun byed ma gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba/ mai tri pas mgon po zhal gzigs dus mdzad pa'i
bstod pa chos dbyings (mchod rten)(mu)rnam dag ma la li ta badzra dang gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba/ slob dpon a bha yas mgon po zhal gzigs dus mdzad pa'i bstod pa
(mchod rten)(mu)phyogs bcu dus gsum ma dad byed go cha dang gu rub yon tan tshul khrims kyis gu ge tho ling du bsgyur ba/ paNDi ta spyan chen pos dur khrod bsil ba'i tshal
du mdzad pa'i (mchod rten)(mu)bstod pa bde dga' rgya mtsho ma gyi ljang gis bsgyur ba/ yar klungs pas bskul ba ltar bde ba chen po'i shlau ka gcig sngon du btang ba'i bstod
pa rgyal kun (mchod rten)(mu)phrin las ma bla ma dam pas bsam yas su mdzad pa/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i bstod pa (mchod rten)nag po rngams pa ma/  zhabs
btags mar yang yod/ dpal ldan sengge mdzad pa'i bstod pa (mchod rten)(mu)rang

bzhin dag pa ma/ bdud re lde 'gong yag gis lha mo la bstod pa 'gor spyan (mchod rten)'dren thod pa dgu brtsegs ma/  spyan 'dren 'di zhabs btags mar yod/ yang de dang dkyus
gcig tu skad shan sbyar ba'i lha la dbang sgyur ma (mchod rten)mkha' 'gro Dombi ka ma la dang lo tsA ba cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba/ lha ma srin gyis bstod pa
ma bcos chos sku ma (mchod rten)(mu)la li ta badzra dang gyi ljang gis bsgyur ba/ yang lo paN de nyid kyis bsgyur ba'i drang srong ke'u trir mas (mchod rten)(mu)bstod pa'i
srid gsum zil gnon ma/ yang lo paN de gnyis kyis (mchod rten)(mu)bsgyur ba'i bla ma mai tri pas lha mo zhal gzigs dus bstod pa bskal pa me 'bar ma/ a bha yA ka ras lha
mo zhal gzigs dus bstod pa'i sangs rgyas bstan pa ma (mchod rten)(mu)paNDi ta shraddhA ka ra warma dang gu rub yon tan tshul khrims kyis gu ge tho ling du bsgyur ba/ nam

ba/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug yar klungs pas bskul nas bstod pa bde ba chen po ma shlau ka (mchod rten)(mu)gcig sngon du 'gro ba'i 'dod khams dbang phyug ma chos rje bsod
rnams rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ dpal ldan sengges mdzad pa'i bstod pa (mchod rten)(mu)nam mkha'i mdog can ma rnams so/ /brgyad pa bskul la/ gnod sbyin yab yum dang pu
tra ming sring ru

'dren bcas pa'i drag bskul (mchod rten)(mu)gyi yig rnying gnod sbyin nag 'jigs ma/  yig mchan bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad zer ba 'dug kyang rnal 'byor dbang phyug sa skya
pa zhes sogs kyi dam bsgrags la dpags na min pa 'dra zhing dkar chag dang gsan yig tshor yang mi gsal lo/ / 'od ldan dpal gyis mdzad pa'i drag bskul (mchod rten)(mu)dur

rten)(mu)zhe sdang me 'bar ma/  rdzong kha ba'i dkar chag na 'di la mal gyi mngon rtogs las byung ba'i sprul pa ru 'dren gyi bskul zhes pa dang sa skya'i phyag dper
dam pa'i shog dril bcu'i dang po shom sgos stab tu ngos bzung ba 'dra zhig 'dug pa yig skyon yin nam som nyir snang ngo / / thun mong gi 'khor brgyad brgyad drug cu rtsa
bzhi'i bskul (mchod rten)(mu)bcom ldan mi bskyod dpal chen ma/ phyogs skyong bcu sprul pa dang bcas pa'i bskul (mchod rten)(mu)bcom ldan dpal chen he ru ka ma/ sprul pa'i
