gyi dkar

chag (mu)rdzong chung pa byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis chu sprul rgyal zla'i tshes bcu gnyis la sa skya'i zhe dgon du bris pa/ des stag tshang lo tsA ba manydzu shrI'i
gsung bzhin sa skyar bris (mu)pa'i gyi ljang lugs kyi chos skor gyi dkar chagades mdzad pa'i rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas pa'i gsal byed las le'u gnyis pa bskang gso rgyas
'bring bsdus gsum (mu)gyi thems yig khol du phyung ba/ bskang gso nag po mchod rten gyi sa bcad (mu)sngags 'chang gzungs pa'i slob ma bo dong dge legs bzang pos mdzad
pa rnams so/ /bcu pa gong dkar ba'i lugs la/ rong pa rgwa lo'i dpon brgyud bla ma dpal ldan grags pa la bla dgas su chos rje bla ma dam pas ngag dbang grags par 'bod cing
/ phyis gsang phu brag nag tu bzhugs pas brag nag pa ngag dbang grags par 'bod pa des mdzad pa'i dpal ldan sa skya pa'i chos skyong gur zhal rnam gnyis kyi mngon rtogs
mchod bstod bzlas pa rjes gnang bskul sogs tshang ba'i sgrub thabs chen mo'i mjug tu/ ji skad du/ ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa gzhir bzhag la/ /brgyud pa'i phyag len rim
dang lung yod pa'i/ /rigs rnams zhabs su btags pa'i bstod 'bum 'di/ /rdo rje gdan du bkod nas rnal 'byor la/ /brtson rnams dga' phyir par du'ang bgyis te spel/ /zhes pa
ltar bstod pa rnams mjug tu btags pas gnyis ka sbrel bar bstod 'bum zhabs btags mar grags pa la/ brag nag pa rang gis mdzad pa'i mchod (brag)(rdo rje)gtor sgrub bstod

phyag len rgyun chags gcig tu bsdus pa bdud rtsi'i dpal 'byung /  'di'i nang gi dur khrod nag po'i rgyud las phyung ba'i mgon po'i bstod pa (mu)'das dang ma 'ongs ma/ bram
ze chen pos mdzad pa'i bstod pa (mu)ma skyes mkha' klong ma/ rgyud las phyung bar grags pa'i dpal ldan (mu)mgon po sa'i dam tshig can gyi dgra lha nag po che yin/ dus gsum
rgyal ba'i spyan snga ma (mu)rnams rdzong lugs bstod 'bum na'ang yod/ bstod 'bum la/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal gyis mdzad pa'i (rdo rje)bshags pa tshigs bcad bla ma rnams

siddhaM dpal nag po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /nag po chen po'i srung 'khor bsgom par 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i mgon po khro bcu'i (e)srung 'khor mkhas grub gung ru'i zin
bris kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i go 'phang thob par shog gi mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dang lhag pa'i lha dbyer ma mchis pa kye rdo rje'i zhabs la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /rgyal ba'i

'dzin pa'i gsung sgros/ bdag (4)chen rdo rje 'chang gi

gsung / rje btsun (5)rdo ring pa chen pos mdzad pa'i yi ge rdo rje 'chang (6)tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa'i yi ge dkar (7)chag tu ma 'khod pa'i yi ge de dag (8)kun la thun mong
du nye bar mkho ba'i skor dang brgyad/ dang po la/ 'gor oM swa sti/ dha ma sang kri ma tang bi ra zhes yod pa'i nag po chen po'i lo rgyus lha bkod las sbyor gsum dang
bcas pa las sbyor bde ba'i rnam dag bzhugs so'i mtha' can/ 'gor nag po chen po'i lo rgyus ni ma rgyud mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur nas zhes yod pa'i mgon po'i bla ma brgyud
pa'i lo rgyus zhes bya ba'i yig chung deng sang gi bar na kun la gsal te lo rgyus so'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'khor lo mu khyud lnga
bskor/ lte ba la gri gug gi zhes yod pa'i rang srung 'khor lo rab gnas dang bcas pa A tsArYa kr-iShNa pA da'i man ngag thun mong ma yin pa badzra kha tham gyi mtha' can/
'gor 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed la na mo/ gshin rje pra khong nag gi rgyud las zhes yod pa'i dam can la (rgya)ru mtshon 'dzugs pa'i yi ge au DyAn chen pos gud du bkol ba rdzogs
byang gi mtha' can/ de'i zhar byung du srog mdung ru mtshon 'dzugs pa'i tshigs bcad  dkar chag na mi gsal ba gong gi khongs su gtogs sam snyam/ bcol ba'i phrin las
grub par mdzod kyi mtha' can/ 'gor lha mo chen mo la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de'i sgrub pa la bzhi ste zhes yod pa'i lha mo phyi pa mu stegs pa ltar sgrub pa'i rgya gzhung gsal
byed kyi yig chung yid bzhin nor bu  rngog pa'i lha mo phyi sgrub kyi rgya gzhung gi 'grel pa lag len ma

dang zhus dag pher zhes tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po gsung ngo / /zhes bya ba lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po la gdams pa/ 'gor dpal mgon po zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ dpal he
ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bla ma la gus snying rjer ldan/ /zhes yod pa'i ye shes kyi mgon po dang las kyi mgon po ber nag zangs gri can sbags ma'i gsang sgrub kyi yig rnying
rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ las mgon gyi yum 'jigs byed khrag 'thung ma rnam 'phrul gyi gaNDi la brten nas sgrub pa dang / las kyi mgon po gsod byed gdug pa'i gri gug can
tsandan gyi bing dang mtshon cha gri gug 'bar ba la brten nas sgrub pa 'khor lo dang las sbyor la brten nas dgra bo myur du sgrol ba'i thabs bal po pham mthing pa nas mal
lo la brgyud pa'i yi ge 'bum phrag gsum bzlas na 'di thams cad 'grub pa yin gsung ba'i mtha' can/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i mu stegs kyi ngan sngags rkyal 'bud ces
pa mon chung pu tra'i rkyal 'bud kyi rtsa ba'i yi ge gnyal pa rong ling lo tsA bas bal yul du bram ze ha ra ri ma la gser srang gsum phul nas zhus pa/  'di gsang ba'i las
mkhan pu tra dang tha dad yin pas bsre bar mi bya zhes snyan brgyud rol mtsho dang lhag bsam rab dkar gyi dri lan sogs su snang ngo / /'gor mon chung pu tra'i rkyal 'bud
thun mong ma yin pa/ nag po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /thebs bzlog brtsi mi dgos zhes yod pa'i de'i lag len gyi yi ge rnal 'byor smyon pa'i mtshon char gnang ba'i mtha'
can/ 'gor oM swa sti/ mon chung rkyal 'bud la gsum ste zhes yod pa'i rkyal 'bud kyi zhal gdams yi ge gnas dben par mis mi mthong ba bya'o'i mtha'

can/ 'gor na mo ma hA kA la/ mu stegs shrI ral pa can gyi rkyal 'bud 'di byung tshul ji ltar brgyud pa'i rim pa ni zhes yod pa'i lo rgyus (zha)dang bcas pa'i yi ge bstan pa
la phan pa rgya chen po 'byung bar gyur cig gi mtha' can/ nor phyir gtang ba'i mon bu pu tra nag po rnam gsum gyi yi ge mal lo'i lugs slob dpon snye ston gyis jo sras rgyal
mtshan la gnang ba/ bdud pu tra'i sgrub thabs gtsang rong gi rwa nag lo tsA ba'i gdams pa khyad par can rgya ston gyis gsal bar bris pa/ phyi pa'i lha bshan pa ro khur
'di la yang bdud pu trar lhag bsam rab dkar gyi dri lan du ngos 'dzin no/ /gyi man ngag bshan pa'i cho 'phrul mgo brnyan mar grags pa yar klungs pas klu'i dgon pa shug
ra bde chen du dag par bgyis pa/ sbags sgrub kyi skabs su ma hA kA la'i sgrub thabs kyi rigs bsdus pa zhes pa dpal ldan mgon po ma hA kA la la mgon po chen po bcu gnyis
kyis bskor zhes sogs brgyad brgyad drug cu rtsa bzhi ston pa'i yig chung tshigs  'di dang kha skong po tir yod pa 'dra min snang / bcad ma dgra bgegs ma lus thal ba'i rdul
du rlog gi mtha' can/ las sbyor gyi skabs su nye bar mkho ba'i slob dpon chen po padmas mdzad pa'i srung ma spyi'i dmod bcol  me 'bar mar yang bzhugs/ (rgya)mi brjed gzungs
thob jo mo mkhar chen bzla'i bla dpe/ yang des mdzad pa'i chos skyong spyi'i snying chu (rgya)bsre ba yon tan rab rgyas ma/ des mdzad pa'i chos skyong gi srog 'phrog
pa/ bcing ba/ khyi bzhin khrid pa/ snga ma la phyi ma mi 'khrid pa/ rtsal 'gran pa ste zab pa'i gnad

(rgya)(rdo rje)lnga'i man ngag 'khon nag zas su za ba'i gdams pa slob dpon klu sgrub nas ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma dang gnyan lo nas brgyud pa/ bya rog gi dbang po lnga sogs
la brten pa'i nag (mu)(zha)po chen po'i cho 'phrul ston pa'i man ngag rnams so/ /gnyis pa rgwa A nanda dam pas mdzad pa'i yig cha la/ nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs 'di la
mang du gsung yang don gsum du 'du tshul sogs spyi'i khog bsgrigs A nanda kIrti'i zhal gyi bdud rtsi'o'i mtha' can/ sngon 'gro rten dang mchod gtor gyi skabs nye bar mkho
ba'i shog dril bcu par grags pa'i nang tshan/ 'gor rtsa brgyud dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams zhes yod pa'i sngon 'gro shom gyi shog dril dam pa kun dga' grags kyis 'phags
pa rin po cher lus longs spyod thams cad phul nas sku gsung thugs mnyes pa'i bka' 'bangs dang zhabs tog mdzad par brten/ pha phogs kyi tshul du gnang ba 'khon dharmA rakShi
ta dang zhang dkon mchog dpal sogs kyi ched du mdzad pa'i rin chen nor 'dra'i man ngag zab mo 'di su zhig rnyed nas srog ltar gces par zung gi mtha' can/ sku gzugs
bzheng tshul yid bzhin nor bu zhes pa dgos 'dod thams cad kyi 'byung khungs bris sku sgrub pa'i shog dril/ phyag mtshan gri gug gis gsod pa'i las sgrub pa'i shog dril/ phyag
mtshan thod pa la brten nas dngos grub rnam gnyis sgrub pa'i shog dril/ dgra bgegs tshar gcod gaNDi sgrub pa'i shog dril/ dmag thog ser rlung gnon pa ral gri sgrub pa'i
shog dril/ dgra bgegs zil gyis gnon cing cho 'phrul sna tshogs ston pa

thugs chen sgrub pa'i shog dril/ khro tshogs pho nya sdud cing dgra bgegs tshar gcod pa rnga chen sgrub pa'i shog dril/ nyams chag thams cad skong zhing bar gcod kyis mi tshugs
pa kha TwAM sgrub pa'i shog dril/ gtum drag mi bzad pho nya'i las rim sgrub pa'i shog dril te bcu/ gzungs 'bul ba'i tshigs bcad lus kyi mun nag zil gnon ma/ 'gor de
nas rta nag po sogs rten rnams la tshon dmar po bskus zhes yod pa'i gzungs bskyed chog rgyas pa dang bsdus pa hU~M las byung ba'i rta mchog ma dang bcas pa bla ma la gus
pas zhu bar bya'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor na mo ma hA kA lA ya dang / mgon po'i man ngag tsitta brtag pa'i rim pa ni zhes yod pa'i gsang rten gyi skabs su gri snying brtag pa'i
yi ge nag po'i rgyud las gsungs pa'o'i mtha' can/ dus gcig la chig brgyud kyi gras/ 'gor bla ma dang dpal he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bca' ba rten gyi skabs su gri snying
'khor lo zhes yod pa'i gri snying 'khor lo thun mong ma yin pa'i bca' tshul rab gnas zhag bdun ma dang bcas pa'i yig chung yid bzhin gyi nor bu ci bsam 'grub par 'gyur
ba dus gcig la chig brgyud ma/ sbags sgrub kyi skabs su 'khor lo dang ling ga'i bri yig (mu)ces pa mgon po'i 'khor lo pad 'dab bzhi pa/ lha mo'i brgyad pa/ gnod sbyin pho
mo'i lto 'khor/ 'jam lugs kyi pho mo'i 'khor lo/ rtsub lugs kyi pho mo'i 'khor lo/ bzlog 'khor/ dgra bo'i snying gar 'jug pa'i 'khor lo/  rdzong chung pa rnams 'di ling
ga'i bri yig tu bzhed/ ming sring gsum gyi gzungs 'dri

lugs/ ling ga 'khor lo can  'di rdzong chung par med/ gyi bri yig rnams ston pa/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi zhal gdams (khra)yig brgyas nyams chag kha skong ngo'i mtha' can/
'gor bsnyen sgrub las gsum la bsnyen pa'i dus su mgon po'i sngags thung zhes yod pa'i sngags kyi bzla (khra)thabs de nas brgya pa bzla'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor hU~M la sngags
kyis bskor ba la zhes yod pa'i las bzhi'i dmigs (mu)(khra)pa tshar gcad par bsam mo gu hya sa ma ya'i mtha' can/ srog gta' mar 'dzin pa/ snying rten du 'dzin pa/ 'khor lo'i
dbye ba/ rang gshed dbab pa/ yi dam gyi bsnyen grub/ gtor ma'i gnad de chings chen drug gi zhal gdams snod min dam tshig med pa la sbyin na nag po chen pos snying khrag
'thung zhig gi mtha' can/ bsgom pa lha'i gnad kyi man ngag sbyor dngos rjes rnam pa gsum sgrub pa'i man ngag dam pa yin no zhes bla ma gsung ngo sa mApta mi thi'i mtha'
can/ zhar byung bsnyen sgrub las gsum gtor ma dang bris sku tsam la brten pa/ glo bur las bcol gsum gyi tho tsam bstan pa/  dkar chag na mi gsal/ zhi rgyas dbang drag gi
gtor ma/ nyams chag skong ba/ 'chi ltas dang rmi lam ngan pa bzlog pa/ lo zla dus tshod dang rdzas gnad/ rjes gnang gi khyad bcos/  'di dkar chag na mi gsal/ gtor ma phul
bas rtags ma byung na nyes pa bsgrag pa gsang 'dus lugs bzhin bya ba'i zhal 'phang / byad sha sbags pa dang bcas pa rnams gcig tu dril bar gtor ma'i man ngag pha rol gyi
rbod gtong drag po rlung sbyor gyi sgo nas bzlog pa/ 'di las

'phros pa'i man ngag  'di dkar chag na mi gsal/ shin tu zab pa'i gnad dang bcas pa/ sprul pa'i khyung chen gyi man ngag sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/  'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i
gsan yig na pho nya'i las sbyor zhes snang / 'gor dpal ma hA kA la la na maH'dir gtor ma'i bsad las rab dur khrod kyi rdul tshon zhes yod pa'i shin tu drag po'i gtor
chen gyi yig chung gdams pa zab mo sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ de ltar gtor bsgrub byas nas zhes yod pa'i gtor ma'i sgo nas dgra bgegs kyi stobs srog gzhom pa'i zhal shes
bsad mnan gnyis ka tshang ba phyi mig mi lta bar 'ong bar bya'o'i mtha' can/ mdun gang 'phags pa'i srung 'khor gyi yi ge bla (mu)ma'i zhal las thos pa nyid do'i mtha'
can/ zhar byung yul phyogs tsam du yang nad rims mi 'byung ba'i srung ba (mu)dang ser ba srung  rdzong pod na 'di ma gtogs zhar byung gzhan gnyis po med/ ba myong grub ma
yin no'i mtha' can/  zhar byung gsum po 'di gong gi khongs su bgrangs pa las dkar chag na mi gsal/ 'gor yul phyogs kyi nad rims srung ba'am gcod pa zhes yod pa'i mdun gang
'phags pa'i srung 'khor gyi zhal shes gzhung bzhin bya'o'i mtha' can/ byad ma srung 'khor can gsod pa'i gdams pa sngags nus can la lhag par 'gro gsung ba'i mtha' can/
rmi ltas ngan pa bzlog pa'i za ba rlung sbyor gyi gdams pa snying dang 'dra ba la sbyin gyi gzhan la ma yin no'i mtha' can/ drag po'i sbyin sreg tshigs bcad (mu)(zha)()ma
gzhan phan dge ba byang chub tu bsngo ba'i mtha' can/ las bzhi'i bro brdung gi yi ge bcom

ldan dpal chen mi bskyod ma rnams so/ /gsum pa bar skabs kyi snyan brgyud 'dzin pa'i gsung sgros kyi yi ge la/ zab pa'i gnad kyi man ngag gi rtsa ba'i bsnyen pa'i yi ge'i chos
skyong gi zab (sdings)gnad thams cad gcig tu dril nas bsnyen pa'i man ngag sbas pa'i rnal 'byor bar sdings pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa dus gcig la chig brgyud
gras/ las mgon zangs gri can gyi sngags dang bskyed chog gi yi ge zhabs gnyis brkyang bskum gyis bzhugs par bskyed do gu hya sa ma ya kha tham gyi mtha' can/ sngags 'chang
kun dga' zla bas mdzad pa'i dbang phyug chen po'i sras po drag po chen po'i bsnyen sgrub las la 'jug pa don gsum ma zhes pa thun mong ma yin pa'i bsnyen pa'i yi ge chig
brgyud ma'i gras/ des mdzad pa'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi dus su rmi lam gtan la dbab pa'i man ngag rtags yig tu grags pa/ pu tra'i gtor chog theg chen chos kyi rgyal
pos dpal nyan po'i gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa/ gur zhal rnam gnyis kyi bla brgyud bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yan gyi mtshan byang skad gnyis sbyar ba/ nag po chen po 'khor
dang bcas pa'i spyan 'dren sngags byang dang bcas pa dad pa dam tshig ma 'byug rdzas kyi ngos 'dzin dang bcas pa rje btsun gyi phyag bris dngos las zhal bshus pa/ shA
sa na'i sngags don (e) gser pod na i daM duShTAM yan rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos 'grol bar mdzad/ de man zhabs tog tu bris zar ba 'dug dkyus su bkral pa gcig  dkar
chag na gur zhal las mkhan dang bcas pa'i sngags byang zer ba las ngor pa dang sa bzang pa sogs nang gses kyi dbye gsal mi 'dug yang sa bzang

ma tis rgya dpe bdun la gtugs nas mchan bus (e)(mu)bkral ba gcig  lha mo'i sngags kyang bkral 'dug des shA sa (e)(mu)na bod  'di glegs bam du bzhugs kyang dkar chag tu mi gsal/
skad kyi tshigs bcad du bsdebs pa gcig gur zhal las mgon dang bcas pa'i sngags byang rgyas pa mchan bus bkrol ba/  gong gsal gyi sngags byang gsum po dpe tshan gcig
tu yod/ mgon chen las mgon dang bcas pa'i 'grol med pa'i sngags byang (mu)bsdus par grags pa bla ma dam pa ngag dbang grags pa'i dpal gyis gong ma'i phyag dpe la gtugs te
mdzad pa/ yang sngags byang mjug na kun la ngag 'dzin byed pa phyag len yin zhes yod pa'i chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis zhus dag mdzad pa ltar yar klungs
pa sengge rgyal mtshan dpal gyis klu'i dgon par bris pa'i phyag bris dngos las bshus pa/ gtsang rigs kyi dpal mgon bdun cu dang bstan ma bcu gnyis kyi srog sngags dang
bum rdzas lnga tshan lnga'i ngos 'dzin phan yon dang bcas pa rnams so/ /bzhi pa bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi gsung la/ de nyid kyis mdzad pa dngos dang de'i gsung sgros
zin bris su byas pa gnyis/ dang po la/ 'gor bla ma dang rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i tshogs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'dir rdo rje nag po chen po'i man ngag gi tho bla ma'i zhal las
byung ba cung zad brjod na zhes yod pa'i sgrub skor gyi khog phub kyi yi ge phyogs thams cad las rgyal bar gyur cig gi mtha' can/ me 'bar ma'i dkar chag yid bzhin nor bu'i
bang mdzod/ mgon po lha brgyad kyi sgrub thabs thun

mong ma yin pa gsang ba yid bzhin nor bu/ deng sang gsang ba'i mgon khang la gsang ba yid bzhin nor bu'i mgon khang zhes pa'ang sgrub yig 'di la brten nas thogs shing / thog
mar slob dpon sangs rgyas dpal bar zin bris tsam zhig gnang ba khong gi grogs dam pa zhig nas 'phel ba'i phyag tu 'byor bas man ngag shes par 'dod na med kha med cig byung
'dug par dgongs nas chos kyi bu dang rigs kyi tsha bo rnams kyi don du zhus dag dang mjug gi chags bcad sogs gnang ba yin la/ de yang / gangs kyi chu dang 'o ma 'dres
pa de/ /ngang pa'i rgyal pos 'byed shes gzhan min ltar/ /ma nor gnad kyi bcud rnams len shes pa/ /da lta'i dus na bdag las gzhan su zhig / de lta'i blo gros gang gis mthus
byung ba/ /mkhyen brtse nus mthu mchog gi 'byor pa can/ /dpal ldan bla ma nam mkha'i mtshan can zhabs/ /'dren mchog de yi drin las rnyed par gyur/ /zhes zab pa las kyang
ches zab pa snying nang gi khrag lta bu snyan nas snyan zhal nas zhal du brgyud pa'i gdams pa rnams ni yab 'jam dbyangs chos rje nam mkha' rgyal mtshan kho na las gsan
zhing / de yan du gdams pa kha 'thor nas shes rlom phal cher gyis zing zing por gyur nas rtogs dka' ba dag bstan pa rin po che'i lcags rir nag po 'gro shes kyi tshul du
bkod pa gnang ba yin pas/ spyir snyan brgyud kyi glegs bam yongs rdzogs bka' dam par ma zad/ gsang ba yid bzhin nor bu'i yi ge 'di dus gcig la snod ldan gyi slob ma gcig
la chig brgyud du spel ba'i phyag len nyams pa med cing / de'i

rgyu mtshan yang ji skad du/ mthu chen dregs pa'i dbang phyug gdong bzhi la/ /gnyer du gtad do dam nyams snod min la/ /spel na de yi snying khrag gsol bar mdzod/ /bla ma la
gus dam tshig snying rjer ldan/ /bstan la sems pa'i snod ldan byung gyur na/ /thog mar dam btags chig brgyud tshul du sbyin/ /de mthar bka' rgyas gdab pa shin tu gces/ /zhes
gsungs pa brgyud 'dzin mtha' dag gis snying gi dpal be'ur bcangs shing 'chang bar 'gyur ba sha stag go/ // 'gor na mo gu ra we/ 'di ltar phyi nang gis bsdus pa'i da
ltar gyi 'char sgo rtog rigs bag chags dang bcas pa 'di dag ces yod pa'i nang sgrub dang gsang sgrub kyi gnad kyi zin bris skye ba'i cho 'phrul sna tshogs 'byung ba mtshon
pa'o'i mtha' can/ nang gsang gi khrid ma thob par lung mi mdzad pa phyag len no/ /mgon po khro bcu'i srung 'khor la nye bar mkho ba'i khro bcu'i man ngag zhal (zha)()gdams
dang bcas pa bya 'gyur rdo rje'i pho brang du kun dgas yi ge'i rkyen sbyar ba la brten nas mdzad pa rnams so/ /gnyis pa gsung sgros zin bris kyi skor la/ bka' babs bzhi'i
rnam gzhagasku gsung thugs phyi nang gsang ba'i rten bsham tshul/ bsnyen sgrub las sbyor/ gtor ma dang mchod pa'i rim pa/ dam pa'i shog dril drug gi lag len rnams gsal
bar ston pa'i zin bris chen (zha)mor grags pa/ mjug na ji skad du/ 'di las phun tshogs dge ba gang thob des/ /blo gros khang bzang snyan brgyud nor gyis gtams/ /rgyal
mtshan 'phyar bas gzi brjid

khams gsum 'gengs/ /dpal 'byor bzang pos dbul phongs zhi bar shog/ ces pa'i mtha' can/ 'di yang dus gcig la chig brgyud las mi gnang / yang mgon mkhan chen dpal ldan bkra shis
pas zin bris su btab pa'i skor la/ 'gor oM swa sti siddhaM/ bla ma dang dam can srung ma'i tshogs la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /sems can thams cad kyi don du sku bzhi'i
dbang phyug ces yod pa'i rgyud sde bzhi'i dbye ba/ brgyud nas chos skyong bsten tshul/ brgyud pa'i lo rgyus/ rkyang sgrub sbags sgrub/ phyi rten phyi ru bca' ba/ nang rten
nang du bca' ba bsnyen sgrub las sbyor/ gsang rten gsang bar bca' ba 'khu ldog spong ba/ phyi sgrub shog dril drug gi lag len sogs ston pa'i zin bris rgyas pa gzhan gyi
rkyen bzlog tu song ba'i nyen yod/ sa skya pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i man ngag go'i mtha' can/ dus gcig la chig brgyud ma'i gras/ 'gor sa skya pa'i mgon po'i ru mtshon
bca' thabs la zhes yod pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i ru mtshon gyi zin bris bstod pa byed tshul rnams gzhan dang 'dra'o'i mtha' can/ mgon po'i gtor chen byed tshul la rnal
'byor pa kha lho la bltas pa'i mdun du zhes yod pa'i gtor chen gyi zin bris rkang rjes rnams rdo rje rgya gram du bsam mo'i mtha' can/ 'gor mdos la rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum
yod pa la/ dang po ni zhes gnyis sogs yod pa'i mdos kyi zin bris mkha' 'gro rnams kyi 'khu ldog mi 'byung zhing bzod par gsol gyi mtha' can/ de'i cha lag mdos byin gyis
brlab pa  'di dkar chag na mi gsal yang gong gi 'phros yin nam

snyam/ bdag gi bsam pa'i stobs dang ni zhes sogs brjod do'i mtha' can/ yang mgon mkhan chen pa'i zin bris 'di rnams ngo mtshar ba'i legs bshad dang nor 'khrul cung zad kyang
yod ces rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes gsungs pas slad mar yang yi ge man ngag gzhan dag dang bstun pa'i dpyad dgos par snang ngo / /lnga pa rje btsun rdo ring pa chen
pos mdzad pa'i yi ge la/ nag po chen po'i 'khu ldog spang ba/ bzlas pa spyi'i sngon du 'gro ba brgyad dang so so'i khyad par gsum bstan pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i bsnyen
pa/ srog phur gyi man ngag rnams bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis yig ris so sor bkod pa slob ma'i don du mkha' 'gro chos skyong la gtor ma phul nas mi dgag pa'i mtshan ma
byung bar brten/ bcos bslad med par gcig tu bsdoms nas kha'u skyed lhas nas mgo brtsams dpal e waM chos ldan du rdzogs par grub pa'i yi ge mjug tu/ 'phags pa/ dam pa kun
dga' grags/ badzra shrI mangga la siddhi/ bar sdings pa/ 'jam dbyangs chos rje rnams las rim par brgyud pa bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis bka' rgyas btab nas gnang tshul bcas
yod pa dus gcig la chig brgyud las mi gnang ba/ mnga' ris pa dge slong chos skyong grags dang dmar khams pa grags pa dkon mchog sengges lo drug bdun gyi bar du bskul
ba la brten nas chos skyong la gsol ba btab pas mi dgag pa'i gnang (zha)(khra)ba byung bar brten lcags bya snron zla ba'i nyer lnga la dpal e waM chos ldan du mdzad pa'i
kha sbyor dbye ba brgyad kyi man

ngag gi yi ge dus gcig la chig brgyud ma'i gras/ de'i mjug tu lha dbye'i ngag 'don gyi rim pa/  'di dkar chag na mi gsal ba gong gi 'phros su gtogs sam snyam/ nag po chen po'i
nang sgrub thun mong ma yin pa'i gsang sgrub kyi khrid yig ('a)rab 'byams pa blo gros rab gsal gyis bskul ba la brten/ dpal mgon por gsol ba btab pas gnang ba'i skabs
thob nas kha'u brag rdzong du mdzad pa/ srung 'khor rdo rje brag rdzong gi nyams len gyi yi ge rgyas pa tshar chen gyis yun ring nas bskul zhing yi ge'i rkyen sbyar ba la
brten nas nag po chen pos gnang ba'i skabs thob ste kha'u brag rdzong gi gnas mchog tu sbyar ba/ 'gor na mo gu ra we/ dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i srung 'khor brag rdzong
gi nang gi nyams len zhes yod pa'i drag po sngags rgod kyi man ngag gsung gi bdud rtsi i thi'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma nag po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bsgom pa'i man
ngag la gsum gyi dang po zhes yod pa'i nang dam tshig gi 'khor lo zhes bya ba gsang ba'i brag rdzong ma'i yi ge snod dang ldan pa la sbyin gyi gzhan la ni ma yin no'i
mtha' can/ phyi nang gi khrid yig 'di rnams nyams khrid ma thob par gnang srol mi 'dug go/ ser ba srung ba'i yi ge 'jug tu/ 'di 'dra'i man ngag gdams pas ni/ /ser ba thub
pa the tshom med/ /rang gi slob mas bskul nas ni/ /snyan brgyud gdams pa bris pa la/ /bla ma mkha' 'gros bzod par mdzod/ /ces sogs kyi tshigs bcad yod pa/ sngags pa nang
rgyas kyi man ngag shin tu gsang zhing sba bar bya zhes pa'i mtha' can dus gcig tu chig brgyud kyi gras/ las

mgon bran bdud gshin rje nag po'i gtor chog tshar chen gyis bskul ba la brten nas kha'u brag rdzong du mdzad pa rnams so/ /drug pa rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa'i
yi ge la/ me 'bar ma'i dkar chag snying po gnad kyi sgron me tshigs bcad ma/ mgon po'i man ngag zab bsdus kha skong rnams kyi dkar chag zab don gsal ba'i sgron me/ snyan
brgyud zhal shes yi ge ra bkod pa'i dkar chag gsang chen gnad kyi za ma tog gyi ljang lugs kyi khog phub dkar chag zab don gnad kyi lde miga'adod khams dbang phyug dud
sol ma'i dkar chag snyan brgyud gsal ba'i me long / dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i lha dang chos skor byung tshul gyi lo rgyus man ngag gi khog phub snyan
brgyud rin po che'i lde miga'agor na maHshrI gu ru badzra ma hA kA la ya/ gur gyi mgon po khro bcu'i zhes yod (zha)pa'i mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang gi yi ge bkra shis
sengge des bdag blo gsal la'o'i mtha' can/ las mgon zangs gri can rnam gnyis kyi rjes gnang gi yi ge chos rje tshul khrims pa des bdag la'o'i mtha' can/ dpal sa skya pa'i
bstan srung dbang po rnams la gtor ma 'bul ba'i cho ga snyan brgyud zab mo'i man ngag gis rnam par brgyan pa'i phrin las myur mgyogs kyi pho nya/ 'gor bla ma mchog dang
dpal he ru ka dbyer med pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po zhes yod pa'i mgon po lcam dral gyi gtor chog mi dbang gzhon nu'i gsung gis bskul ba'i ngor gtsang
stod zhwa lu'i chos grwar sbyar ba/ 'gor bla ma dang dpal

he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po zhes yod pa'i lcam dral gyi gtor chog shin tu bsdus pa/ sngon tshe bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan snga ru sogs brjod kyi
mtha' can/ 'gor na maHshrI ma hA kA lA ya/ dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i sgo nas tshe'i dngos grub sgrub pa zhes yod pa'i gur mgon dkar po'i tshe sgrub kyi
yi ge dgyes pas bskyang du gsol gyi mtha' can/ mgon po'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi sgo nas bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga (zha)dngos grub rin chen bang mdzod/ brgyud 'debs rnam
kun mchog ldan ma/ srung 'khor ('a)gsang khrid  ljags lung dngos gzhi'i skabs gsang khrid man gyi dpe ma 'byor/ dang bcas pa rgyun du nyams su len tshul kha'u brag rdzong
pa'i bzhed pa ma nor ba'i snyan brgyud yid bzhin nor bu rdo rje'i mched zla artha siddhi shrI maM gyi nyams len du zho lung mtsho kha'i ri khrod du mdzad pa/ dpal gur
gyi mgon po lha brgyad sbags te bsgrub pa'i srung 'khor mdun khang 'phags pa'i yi ge'i gsal (zha)byed rje bla ma ma hA kA la'i gsung gi bdud rtsi myangs te tho tsam bkod
pa/ 'di'i nyams len yod na nad yams sogs yul phyogs tsam du yang mi 'byung zhes rgwa A nan dam pas che ba dpag tu med pa mdzad pas zab gnad ma'o/ /'gor gu ru badzra nha ra
na mo/ gsang sgrub kyi skabs su rje bla ma'i gsung nas zhes yod pa'i gsang sgrub kyi skabs su nye bar mkho ba'i gsung sgros snying gi dkyil las gzhan du ma yin no'i mtha'
can chig brgyud kyi gras/ rdo rje gur gyi rgyud kyi le'u bco lnga pa dkyil 'khor chen po bsdus pa'i rtog pa las nang sgrub dang

gsang sgrub bstan tshul pha rgod rdo ring pa kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma'i gsung ji lta ba bzhin de ma thag tu zin bris bgyis pa/ gsang rten bla rdo bcang thabs/ 'di'i sbyar
byang du/ dam can 'khu ldog spong ba'i gdams pa'i bcud/ /rtsa brgyud bla mas cung zad yig ris su/ /mdzad kyang nam mkha'i mdzub ris ji bzhin du/ /snyan brgyud zhal shes bral
bas rtogs mi nus/ /'dir ni ma sbas lag len lhug par bris/ /bka' drin dran no rje btsun kha'u pa/ /gsang chen bstan pa gtad do snying gi bu/ /zhes mdo khams rdo rje bkra
shis la gnang ba yin pas bka' rgya shin tu dam par 'dug cing chig brgyud kyi gras kyang yin/ nang sgrub kyi 'khor lo lnga'i las sbyor thun mong ma yin pa spu gri so 'debs
kyi gdams pa rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po'i phyag bris dngos zin bris thor bu 'khrugs can du bzhugs pa las bka'i gnang ba zhus te dkyus su bris pa chig brgyud ma'i gras/
'gor na mo badzra A tsArYa/ dam can rgya mtsho'i yum chen ma/ /zhes yod pa'i e ka dza TI la brten nas rims nad bsrung ba'i gdams pa rje btsun rdo ring pa'i gsung gi
nying khu sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ nag po chen po la klu brgyad kyis bskor ba'i sgo nas char 'bebs pa'i yi ge zhag gsum tshun la 'bab par 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ 'gor na
mo gu ru/ bla ma dang ma hA kA la'i tshogs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'dir mgon po dbyer med du bsre ba zhes yod pa'i chos skyong gi snying chu bsre ba'i zhal shes kyi yi ge
mkhas grub rin po che'i gsung brjed byang du bkod pa'o'i mtha' can/ srung 'khor

rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i zab gnad kyi bsdus don nam thun mong ma yin pa'i snyan brgyud kyi sa bcad mthong smin dge legs kun 'byung du grags pa/ brag rdzong ma'i mde kha gdags
pa'i man ngag phyi rol rdzas kyi sbyor ba'i man ngag zhal shes mal phur gyi yi ge dbon chen chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyis bskul nas mdzad pa bka' rgya dam pa'i gras/ 'gor
oM swa sti/ dam pa kun dga' grags kyis mdzad pa'i srung 'khor rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i yig chung las zhes yod pa'i gtor ma la brten nas dgra bgegs rang gshed rang la dbab
pa'i man ngag gi yi ge lta ba'i ngang du bzhagarjes spyi ltar bya'o'i mtha' can/ ser ba srung 'bebs kyi man ngag dug gi rlung chen nag po zhar 'byung thog srung shwa bzlog
dang bcas pa dpal brag mig chos rdzong gi yang dben du mdzad pa/ dam can srung ma rnams la phyi rten 'dzugs pa'i lag len gyi yi ge nag po 'gro shes kyi tshul du gtsang
rong mtsho la'i mgul gyi ri khrod bsam gtan rtser sbyar ba/ gnas de nyid du mdzad pa'i dam can srung ma rnams kyi thun mong gi ru mtshon 'dzugs pa'i yi ge zab gnad 'di
dag la brten nas chos srung rnams mtsho la ngang pa dang sha rul la sbrang ma ltar 'dus pas kha'u skyed lhas/ rtses thang bsam gtan gling / phan yul dpal ldan rtse sogs srung
ma rang bzhin gyis 'du ba'i gnas yin zhes pa'ang gnad 'gag zab mo la brten pa yin gyis/ snang shas dbang gis khang pa'i yang thog rtser/ /rnga thug 'dzugs pa'i skye
bo mang na yang / /brgyud pa'i man ngag lag len dang ldan pa/ /'di 'dra shes pa'i sngags 'chang nyin skar

tsam/ /zhes gsungs pa don la gnas pas zab gnad mi shes pa'i lder bzo gog po tsam la yid gtod par mi bya'o/ /nag po chen po'i dmar chen gtor bzlog gi cho ga dgra bgegs kyi stobs
'phrog rol pa/ 'di ni mgon po la brten pa'i gtor bzlog gi cho ga 'khrul pa med pa yin la/ deng sang dmar nag 'jigs gsum gyi tshab la mgon po dang las gshin gyi tshab
tu pu tras byas pa'i mgon po drug cu par grags pa sogs ni zur za ba'i yul du byed pa'ang yod do/ /bstod bskul 'og min bde chen ma/ dam can pu tra'i bskang gso phrin las
lhun grub/ de'i bskang rdzas byin rlabs rlung ltar 'tshub ste byon par gyur/ badzra sa mA dza'i mtha' can/ chos skyong gi dri ba lhag bsam rab dkar rnams so/ /bdun pa dkar
chag tu mi bzhugs pa'i yig cha'i skor la/ mthu chen A nan dam pas mdzad pa/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen pos mdzad pa/ rdo rje 'chang
tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis mdzad pa/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags
kyis mdzad pa/ lo pa spyan snga kun dga' don grub kyis mdzad pa/ rdo rje 'chang mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan gyis mdzad pa/ khyab bdag mkhan chen zhwa lu pas mdzad pa/ kha'u
brag rdzong pa'i phyag len du mdzad pa'i bstod 'bum dang bcu gnyis/ dang po ni/ nang sgrub la brten pa'i bsnyen pa/ mi 'khu mi ldog srog tig blang ba'i gnad 'jam par
bsgrub pa/ las sbyor/ myur

ba'i gnad/ gtor ma'i man ngag dang bcas pa/ ma hA kA la'i spu gri so 'debs kyi man ngag shin tu rno myur du bsgrub par grags pa/ dus gcig tu chig brgyud kyi gras/ gnyis pa
bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ mkha' 'gro 'khu ldog spong bar (zha)rgyu rtags nyes dmigs/ mi ldog pa'i man ngag gi phyi rol lha sogs gnad drug  'di gnyis gzhan du
zhal 'phangs/ nang sngags sogs gnad drug gi man ngag gsang ba yang tig sems kyi gnad lnga la brten nas bran bzhin bkol ba'i zab pa'i gnad kyi man ngag spogs chog  'di gzhan
du kha 'phangs/ dang bcas pa snying nang gi khrag lta bu gzhan la phan pa'i blos mkha' 'gro chos skyong rnams la gsol ba btab ste mdo smad gnyan tshe'i sa'i char sbyar
ba/ mjug na/ bla ma la gus snying rjer ldan/ /bstan la sems pa'i bu yi mchog / snying dang 'dra ba cig la sbyin/ /gzhan la mang du spel gyur na/ /las mkhan pu tra 'khor
bcas kyis/ /mgo chod snying khrag zhal du gsol/ /zhes bka' rgya dam par snang ngo / /'khu ldog spong ba'i sa bcad bzhi pa'i zhal 'phangs pa spogs chog gi gsal byed srog
phur gyis gnad du bsdigs pas las myur du 'grub pa snying nang gi khrag lta bu'i yi ge rang gi dran pa gso phyir bris pa/  rje btsun rdo ring pas mdzad pa'i yig cha 'di rnams
'khrugs sdebs su gong du'ang bzhugs/ 'gor na mo gu ru/ mgon po'i gtor chen bya bar 'dod pas rnal 'byor pa kha lhor bltas zhes yod pa'i mgon po lha brgyad (zha)kyi gtor
bzlog gi phyag len dben gnas kha'u brag rdzong du sbyar ba rnams/ bzlas pa spyi'i sngon 'gro

brgyad/ so so'i khyad par bstan pa gsum gyi zhal shes skal bar (zha)ldan pa rnams kyi don du legs par sbyar ba/ mjug na/ snying dang 'dra ba'i man ngag dam pa 'di/ /kun la
mi sbyin gsang ba'i bka' rgya yod/ /snod ldan dag la chig brgyud tshul du sbyin/ /gzhan la rgya cher mang du spel gyur na/ /las kyi mgon pos zangs gri rnon po yis/ /de yi
mgo chod yan lag rgyan du gyis/ /man ngag rin chen snying gi dkyil du chongs/ /zhes snang ngo / /chos tshan bzhi po dus gcig la chig brgyud du gnang ba'i bka' rgya can yin
cing / las sbyor gyi sngon 'gro zhes pa kha sbyor dbye ba brgyad kyi man ngag lung yang snang ngo'i mtha' can/ rig sngags go ldog yig chung / nag po chen po'i sgo nas
phrin las gang sgrub kyang gtor ma bca' shes dgos sogs zhi rgyas dbang drag gi gtor ma'i rnam (zha)gzhag bzod par gsol ba'i mtha' can/ lcam dral gyi gtor ma (zha)bsham thabs
don gsum pa dam pa kun dga' grags las brgyud pa man ngag i thi'i mtha' can/ gsum pa rje btsun rdo ring pas mdzad pa ni/ spyi don gsum pa dgra bo rang gshed rang la dbab

la/ nag po chen po'i chos skor gyi khog phub man ngag gi rnam par bshad (zha)pa zab don snyan brgyud kyi rol mtsho legs bshad kyi rba rlabs rnam par g.yo ba mchod pa bsham
pa man 'phror lus pa/ khro bcu'i rjes

gnang gi skabs nye bar mkho ba'i sku gsung thugs mi 'gyur ba'i man ngag rakSha rakSha hU~M bhrU~M hU~M phaT swA hA'i mtha' can/ ru mtshon gyi las mkhan bran bdud gshin rje

lo/ /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i srung ba'i 'khor lo'i zhal shes ni zhes yod pa'i brag rdzong ma'i srung 'khor thun mong ma yin pa'i zhal shes zin bris rdo rje'i
go khrab khyad par gyi man ngag mde kha gdags pa dang bcas pa bkra shis bde bas khyab pa deng 'dir stsol gyi mtha' can chig brgyud ma'i gras/ nang sgrub kyi thun mong ma

tu/ snyan brgyud nying khu yin gyi bslus pa med/ /snying dkyil sbos la bsnyen sgrub tshad du skyol/ /khas zhan skyabs dang bral ba'i dus byung na/ /mtshon 'di phyung la

bris zor lam dbye ba sogs lhan thabs ji lta ba bzhin mdzad do'i mtha' can/ sku rten bris 'bur bzheng tshul/ rab gnas zhag bdun ma/ gsung rten glegs bam/ thod rnga/ rnga

phreng ba rnams so/ /drug pa rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis mdzad pa la/ 'gor nang rtsa gsum 'khor lo lnga la brten pa la thog mar gzhi skye med dngos po'i

dbyangs chos skyong dbang phyug gis bskul ba la brten nas bla ma mgon po dang bcas pa la gsol ba btab nas mdzad pa 'di'i rjes gnang dang lung ma thob pa la rna ba'i lam tsam
du yang mi bsgrag pa'i bka' rgya can/ dri chu la brten pa'i rims bsrung (zha)mi 'dra ba rnams kyi nang nas pha bla ma bslab gsum bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i
zhal snga nas kyis thugs gtsigs su gnang ba zin bris su bkod pa/ mgon po khro bcu'i brgyud 'debs bdud las rnam par rgyal (zha)ba rigs brgya'i mkhyen brtse ma mi dbang
tshe dbang don grub kyis bskul nas zhwa lu ri sbug tu mdzad pa/ yang rje bslab gsum pa'i gsung la zin bris su mdzad pa'i rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i bsdus (zha)don gyi yi ge
rje nyid kyi spyan sngar zhus dag pa nyams khrid 'di nyid mkhan chen bslab gsum pa kho

na'i bka' drin las byung bas/ sbyar byang du/ blo 'das gdod ma'i mgon po rdo rje 'chang / /gang 'dul dag pa'i zlos gar drin chen rje/ /bka' drin dran no pha rgod bslab gsum
zhabs/ /snying nas 'du 'bral med do thugs rjes skyong / /zhes drin bzo'i tshul du bstod pa ni brgyud pa dang bla ma la ci yang mi sems pa'i chos 'dod mkhan po rnams la dgongs
pa 'dra'o/ /brag rdzong ma'i gtor ma la brten nas rang gshed 'bebs pa'i man ngag rgwa A nan dam pa sogs gong ma mang po'i yi ge ra tho tsam las mi gsal ba'i gsal byed
nag 'gros su mgon po khro bcu'i gtor bzlog gi cho ga (zha)bdud las rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba/ skyed tshal mkhan po thar pa bzang po'i gsung gis bskul ba la brten nas
chos sde de kha'i mgon khang du mdzad pa rnams so/ /bdun pa mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa la/ mgon po lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang thun mong ma (ngag )yin
pa bla ma gong ma'i rjes gnang (sha)gi yi ge rnying pa las tshig sna bsrings te rgyas su btang ba/ zangs gri can skor gsum gyi rjes gnang gi zur (ngag )'debs rje bla ma
dbang phyug rab brtan gyi phyag bzhes rang gi yid la gang zin tsam zhig phyag len zin bris su bkod pa/ 'di gnyis rjes gnang ma thob par mi gnang ba'i bka' rgya can/ mthu
stobs kyi dbang phyug bsod nams chos 'phel gyi gsung rgyun/ phyi srung ba'i 'khor lo la brten nas sgrub pa'i brag rdzong gi khrid kyi yi ge 'dod (ngag )dgu'i dpal ster tsha
lung dgon par shing rta'i lor zin bris su mdzad

pa/ rin po che rta rwa bas nang gi brag rdzong ma'i khrid rgya (ngag )'dre tshar bcad pa'i lo rgyus kyang snang bas shin tu zab gsung ngo'i mtha' can/ gsang ba'i brag rdzong
sems nyid ye shes kyi rtsal 'don gyi khrid (ngag )rig sngags 'chang ba'i gtsug rgyan bsod nams chos 'phel gyi gsung la tsha lung dgon par zin bris su mdzad pa/ nag po chen
po'i gsang khrid kyi yi ge rin po che rta rwa ba'i gsung sgros yid bzhin nor bu (ngag )de bla ma'i bzhugs gnas tsha lung dgon par zin bris su zla ba dgu pa'i nyer gsum
gyi nyin rdzogs par grub pa rnams nyams khrid ma thob par mi gnang ba phyag len gyi rgyun bzhin no/ /brgyad pa lo pa spyan snga kun dga' don grub kyis mdzad pa la/ nang
gi brag rdzong drag po sngags rgod kyi (lo)nyams len rje bla ma mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho'i gsung bzhin dpal ldan sa skya'i lha chen gsang ba'i mgon khang du sbyar ba/
brag rdzong ma'i sngags pa nang rgyas kyi man ngag gi zhal shes lus dbral ba/ stobs gzhom pa/ rnam shes spor ba gsum gyi gdams pa (lo)khyad par can spyan snga mi pham chos
kyi rgya mtsho'i gsung bzhin 'jam dbyangs gdung brgyud la yab chos phul ba'i tshe lha chen gsang ba'i mgon khang du sbyar ba/  'di dang dbyibs 'dra ba zhig tshar chen
dang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses mdzad pa deng sang lung rgyun chad 'dug pas 'di nyid mkho bar snang ngo / /yi ge gnyis ka chig brgyud kyi gras/ dgu pa rdo rje 'chang mgon
po bsod nams mchog ldan gyis mdzad pa ni/ rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i sku rten bzheng tshul ('a)dang khyad par gyi rab gnas bya tshul gsal ba'i me long chig

brgyud ma/ bcu pa khyab bdag zhwa lu (zha)pas mdzad pa ni/ brag rdzong ma'i rdzas bzlog las kyi mtshon cha/ tshad med bzhi/ lce byin brlab/ bzlas pa/ skyabs yul/ dgra bgegs
kyi sa bon/ thal rdeb/ 'khor lo 'khor lugs/ thun bsdu ba/ bzlog pa'i sku'i tshad rnams kyi zhal shes rnams kyang chig brgyud ma'o/ /bcu gcig pa kha'u brag rdzong pa'i phyag
len du mdzad pa'i bstod 'bum la/ srin gzugs ma'i shlau ka gsum/  'di yan me 'bar mar yang yod/ 'gor yod pa'i dpal ldan mgon po ma (mu)'phags pas mdzad pa/  rdzong kha
bas rgyud nas phyung gsung yang lhag bsam rab dkar gyi dri lan du pod mar bzhed pas dpyad do/ /e ka dza TI'i bstod pa kun bzang ma/ lha mo'i bstod pa (mu)til mar ma/ de'i
bstod pa rgya (mu)mtsho'i klong gnas ma/ zhal gyi bstod pa sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i dpal ldan dbang ldan ma/ mchog sred kyis mdzad pa'i gur gyi bstod pa (mu)sngon tshe bde
gshegs ma/  me 'bar ma dang gyi ljang po tir yang yod/ mal los lha mor bstod pa (mu)gang gi sku gsung ma/  rdzong chung pa 'phags pa rin po ches mi nyag tu mdzad par bzhed/
'phags pas mdzad pa'i phrin bcol khyod kyi phrin las ma/ gnam kha'u pas mgon po gdong bzhi pa zhal gzigs dus bstod pa'i rdo rje 'chang dbang ma/  zhabs btags mar yang
yod/ 'phags pas mgon por bstod pa gang (mu)thugs ma/  'di me 'bar mar yang yod/ paNDi ta lo ka shrI'i sgrub thabs las byung ba'i mchog sred kyis lha (mu)mo la bstod pa
mi pham srid gsum ma/  dud sol phyi sgrub kyi rgya gzhung na'ang

yod/ gnyan los zhal la bstod pa paM pad raM nyi ma/ las mgon rnams kyi bstod pa mgon po'i bka' (mu)nyan ma/ bstod pa nag po rngams pa ma/  dpal ldan dbang ldan ma'i shlau ka
gcig bcug 'dug pa ma gtogs kha skong bstod 'bum dang zhabs btags mar yang yod/ bskul mgon po ma hA kA la ma rnams/ gzhan yang khro bcu'i phrin las bskul ba mkha' dbyings
dag klong ma sa rta rgyal zla la pho brang du 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa/ khro bo bcu gcig gi gtor 'bul dang bstod pa ser sna rnam dag ma mkhan chen gnas drug pas rgyud
las phyung ba/ yang des rgyud las phyung ba'i bskul byang chub sems bskyed ma/ des mdzad pa'i bstod pa me stag thim 'gyur ma rnams kyang thob bo/ /rtsa ba'i gsum pa
bla ma gyi ljang lo tsA ba nas brgyud pa'i gyi ljang po ti'i skor ni/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i khog phub yi ge'i dkar chag zab don gnad kyi lde migade las
byung ba'i chos skor la/ sngon du 'gro ba lo rgyus kyi yi ge snod rung du bya ba dbang dang rjes gnang gi yi ge rtsa bar gyur pa rgyud kyi yi ge nyams su len pa sgrub thabs
kyi yi ge dkar chag tu ma 'khod pa'i yi ge dang lnga/ dang po la/ 'gor bla ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rdo rje nag po chen po'i skye rgyud ni zhes yod pa'i yig
rnying (mchod rten)gur mgon gyi skye rgyud rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ 'gor dpal nag po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de la sngon gyi dus na rgyal bu gcig dang blon po'i bu
gcig gis zhes yod pa'i (rdo rje)lha dngos kyi lo rgyus dang bram ze mchog sred sogs brgyud pa'i bla ma rnams ston pa'i

yi ge dge slong dharmA gzi brjid la gnang ba lags so'i mtha' can/  rdzong chung pa dam pas mdzad pa'i lcam dral gnyis ka'i lo rgyus 'dren pas mtshon te/ rgyud sgrub thabs bstod
pa thams cad du lha mo'i rnam gzhag mdzad kyang lugs 'di la lha mo'i sgros med pas 'thad par ma mngon zhing kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa dang rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos
rje gnyis kyang mi bzhed do/ /'di dharma gzi brjid kyis mdzad ces dkar chag na 'dug go/ gnyis pa snod rung du bya ba dbang dang rjes gnang gi yi ge la/ dpal nag po chen
po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bram (rdo rje)(mu)ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po la li ta badzra dang bod kyi lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba/
rdo rje gdan pa gcig lha lnga dang gcig bcu bdun pa'i dbang chog yin par bzhed pa gsan yig dang phyag dpe gnyis kar 'dug pa brjod don lhag po mi 'dug pas dpyad dgos par
snang ngo / / 'di dang tshig sna ring thung cung zad yod pa'i mchan bu dang bcas pa nag po ro 'dzin dang gyi ljang gis bsgyur ba dang dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyis mdzad
pa'i dbang chog la li ta badzra 'di phal cher dur khrod rnams su bzhugs pas mtshan dur khrod nag po ro 'dzin du grags zhes khog phub dang rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig tu snang
na'ang 'dir dbang chog 'dra min gnyis byung ba'i sngon mar la li ta dang / phyi ma la nag po ro 'dzin zhes so sor byung ba dang 'byung khungs bsdus don na mi gcig par
bshad cing 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na'ang so sor snang ba brtag dgos 'dug go/ 'gor dpal nag po chen po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga 'di la spyi don gsum ste zhes
yod pa'i dbang chog rgya gzhung gi sa (rdo

rje)bcad dkyil 'khor gshegs su gsol ba'o rdzogs so'i mtha' can dharma gzi brjid kyis mdzad pa/ 'gor ye shes mgon po'i dbang bskur ba'i rjes la zhes yod pa'i bran bdud rjes
gnang gi zur (mu)'debs kyi yi ge las mgon gyi rjes gnang rdzogs so'i mtha' can rnams so/  yig cha dang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na rjes gnang gi yi ge rnying
pa zhes snang ngo / /gsum pa rtsa bar gyur pa rgyud kyi yi ge la/ 'gor bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mkha' 'gro la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'phags pa mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur zhes yod
pa'i gtso rkyang ston (mchod rten)pa'i rgyud rdo rje gur gyi le'u bco lnga pa las phyung ba/  'di me 'bar mar yang bzhugs/ lha bcu bdun dngos ston pa dur khrod nag po'i
rgyud brtag pa bcu gnyis (rdo rje)(mu)pa bla ma nag po ro 'dzin dang gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis zhus te gtan la phab pa/  'di'i sngags btu'i le'u'i 'gyur khyad tshigs bcad ma
lo paN gnyis kyi g.yar dam brgyud pa zhes dkar chag tu gsungs pa le'u bcu gcig pa 'di kha las logs su ma rnyed cing rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na'ang mi snang ngo / /nag
po chen po 'di'i rgyud la dur khrod chen po sku'i rgyud/ dur khrod nag po gsung gi rgyud/ gri gug brtsegs pa thugs kyi rgyud ces gsum yod pa las glegs bam du yang dur
khrod nag po'i rgyud las mi bzhugs shing nyams len man ngag rnams kyang 'di kho na la brten pa'o/ /rdzong chung pa'i dkar chag na lha mo srog gi 'khor lo'i rgyud drangs shing
gter ma yin pas gyi ljang du 'thad mi 'thad the tshom mdzad 'dug kyang rang lugs la dogs pa tsam yang ma dgos so/ /rgyud kyi don 'grel bzhi sdom bcu (mu)pa slob dpon
chen po

bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/  dkar chag dang rje mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'di ltar snang yang yig cha na la li tas mdzad zer ba 'gyur byang dang nor ram brtag dur khrod
nag po'i 'byung khungs stong thun (mu)gyi khog don bsdus pa rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/  rdzong chung pa'i dkar chag na phyis kyi bla ma dag gis mdzad ces snang ngo /
/ rgyud dur khrod nag po'i bsdus (rdo rje)don sa bcad dge slong dharma gzi brjid kyis sbyar ba/ des mdzad pa'i dur khrod nag po'i rgyud kyi rnam (rdo rje)par bshad pa rdo
rje'i tshig don gsal byed rnams so/  gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na rgyud rtog pa bcu gnyis pa'i 'grel pa zhes snang / / bzhi pa nyams su len pa sgrub thabs kyi yi ge la/ mgon
po'i sgrub thabs/ las mgon gyi sgrub thabs/ las sbyor thor bu'i yi ge dang gsum/ dang po la gang zag dbang po rab spros pa la mi dga' ba'i don du rdo rje gur dang dur

paNDi ta nag po ro 'dzin  yig cha na paNDi ta a thu la badzra zhes snang ba brtag dang lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba/ 'gor dpal nag po chen po me 'bar
mar yang yod/ dpa' bo gcig pa sras kyi tshul du zhes yod (rdo rje)pa'i gong gi bsdus don bsam gyis mi khyab pa yod pa bstan pa'o'i mtha' can/ sgrub thabs 'bring po

'gor skad shan sbyar dang dpal he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /mi bsad mtshon nam seng ldeng la/  khog phub na phur bu'i sgrub skor rnams la gzhan yang zhes sgrub thabs che 'bring

ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bstan pa gnas par bya ba'i phyir/ /nag po chen po'i phur bu sgrub/ /ces yod pa'i nag (mchod rten)(rdo rje)(mu)po chen po'i srog phur gyi yi ge 'am
phur bu gdab pa srog phur dang bcas pa'i sgrub thabs su grags pa bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/  me 'bar mar 'di dang phal cher zhus dag pher ba la/ 'gor skad shan sbyar
med pa sogs mi mthun pa kha shas yod cing / de yang dkar chag tu phur bu sgrub pa'i khongs su 'dren pa las logs su mi snang / thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'i phyag
dper 'og nas yig phreng gnyis tsam mi gcig de phyin me 'bar ma'i de dang zhus dag pher ba zhig 'dug 'gor bla ma dang dpal he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /nag po chen po'i
phur bu'i sgrub thabs kyi rim pa gza' skar drag po la zhes yod (mchod rten)(mu)pa'i mgon po phur bu'i sgrub thabs kyi gsal byed  me 'bar mar yang bzhugs/ sa chen gyis

ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /slob dpon sku la sdo byed dang / /dkon mchog gsum la gnod byed dang / /zhes yod (mchod rten)(mu)pa'i nag po chen po srog gi spu gri'i sgrub thabs
bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/  'di gnyis me 'bar mar yod kyang sgrub thabs dngos gzhi rgya gzhung gi sdebs su sku smad phur bu'i gsal kha yang mi 'dug pas de dang mi

gong gi gsal (mchod rten)(mu)byed brtse ba chen pos mdzad pa'i nag po chen po phur bu'i sgrub thabs sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/  'di la rdzong chung ba dge slong shrI bha
dras mdzad pa la sa chen gyis mdzad kyang sbyang gsung yang shrI bha dra zhes pa'i gang zag su yin 'chad rgyu rang gzhan gnyis kar ngos 'dzin rgyu ma byung zhes rdo rje

drug lus la bkod de bsgoms pa'i sgrub thabs (mu)gsang ba zhes bya ba gsang sgrub bam phrin las gsang ba'i sgrub thabs su grags pa bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa A tsArYa

pa'i dbang po tha ma spros pa la

dga' ba'i ched du lha bcu bdun gyi dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs par bsgom pa dur khrod nag po dngos bstan gyi sgrub (rdo rje)(mu)thabs rgyas pa  'di la bsnyen pa'i tshul du
sgrub pa/ bod pa'i man ngag sgrub pa'i tshul du nyams su blang ba/ rbad pa'i man ngag las sbyor gyi tshul du nyams su blang ba yod ces dkar chag tu gsungs pa ltar don la
tshang zhing gsal ba 'og gi bla ma'i zhal snga nas kyis gdams par 'dug go/ nang sgrub tu grags pa nag po chen po'i khyad par gyi cho ga bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa la
li ta badzra dang gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba/ 'gor slob dpon chen po bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa'i dpal mgon po chen po'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo drag byed

po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dbang bskur dam tshig sdom la gnas/ /zhes yod pa'i dpal (rdo rje)(mu)nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs bla ma'i zhal snga nas kyi gdams pa lag
tu blang ba'i rim pa/ 'gor bla ma dang ni yi dam lha/ /chos skyong mgon la gus btud de/ /zhes yod pa'i dpal nag po chen po lha bcu bdun ma'i bsnyen sgrub las (mu)gsum gyi

dpa' mor bcas/ /mchod 'os kun la btud byas te/ /zhes yod pa'i mgon po lha bcu bdun ma'i bod rbad bsad gsum gyi mngon rtogs rgyas

(mu)pa sgrub thabs lag tu blang ba'i rim pa yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che zhes bya ba/ gyi ljang lo tsA ba chen po'i gsung las ji ltar byung ba bzhin mdo smad kyi slob ma'i
gtso bo tshar dgu ston pa dang gru gu ston pa gnyis kyis bka' bgros nas yi ge ra bkod pa mngon par rtogs pa nye bar mkho ba rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ lugs srol 'di'i nyams
len la sgrub thabs 'di med kha med snying ltar gces pa'i gdams pa yin pas 'chol bar mi ston pa'i bka' rgya dam po dkar chag tu gsal bar 'dug go/ lugs srol 'di nyid kyi

dam pa kun dga' grags kyis mdzad pa/ de dag la nye bar mkho ba'i cha laga'agor bla ma rnams la na mo/ dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyis/ /bstan pa bsrung zhing mnga'

ma thams cad byang chub tu bsngo'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor/ 'thung zhig 'thung zhig rdo rje'i chu/ /zhes yod pa'i nag (mu)po chen po'i mchod phreng las kyi 'bras bu mchis
par mdzod kyi mtha' can/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i nag po chen po'i gtor ma'i cho ga (rdo rje)slob dpon bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa dpal sgeg pa'i rdo rje dang
gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur

ba/ 'gor gtor ma'i cho ga 'di la gsum ste zhes yod pa'i gong gi bsdus (rdo rje)don dharma gzi brjid kyis mdzad pa/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i dpal ldan nag po chen po'i
sbyin sreg gi cho ga bram ze (mu)mchog sred kyis mdzad pa zhar byung me lha'i bstod pa gsang gsum ma dang bcas pa/ 'gor sbyin sreg gi cho ga 'di la gsum ste zhes yod pa'i
gong gi bsdus (rdo rje)don dharma gzi brjid kyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i dpal nag po chen po'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga lag tu blang ba'i rim pa rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/
dpal nag po chen po'i bstod pa'i phreng ba (mchod rten)(rdo rje)(mu)bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa la li ta dang lo tsA ba gyi ljang gis bsgyur ba/  kha skong bstod 'bum
dang zhabs btags mar yang yod/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na zhal gzigs ma'i bstod pa rnams gsung 'dug pa/ paNDi ta snying phreng can dang gyi ljang gis bsgyur
ba'i mgon po'i bstod pa rnams la dgongs 'dra ba brgyud pa so sor bgrangs phyin sgyur byed kyi stabs nas bgrangs kyang mi 'gal lo/ /yang lo paN de gnyis kyis bsgyur ba'i
dpal nag po chen po la bstod cing phrin las 'chol ba (mchod rten)(rdo rje)sngon tshe bde gshegs ma bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/  me 'bar po ti dang tshar lugs bstod
'bum na'ang yod/ 'di'i rjes su nag po chen po'i bsnyen sgrub rbad bsad kyi yi ge rnying pa/ bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa'i rab gnas kyi cho ga 'am bkra shis kyi cho
ga ra grags pa sna tshogs rdo rje ma gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba rnams so/ /gnyis pa las mgon gyi sgrub thabs la/ 'gor rgya skad yod pa'i mgon po gcer bu'i ngan sngags
sam dur khrod kyi mgon po

gcer bu'i sgrub thabs (rdo rje)(mu)bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba/ 'di la nang gses sgrub pa las sbyor ser 'bebs dang bcas pa yod cing rang
'dra'i 'khor bzhis bskor ba'i lha lnga dang kShe tra pA la dang pi tA pA la gnyis bsnan pa'i gtso 'khor bdun du 'gyur bas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na lha
bdun ma zhes yod/ kha cig gur mgon dpa' gcig dang rdzong chung pa gur mgon nyid du bzhed pa ni sgrub yig rnying par mdun du mgon po'i bka' nyan gyi tshul du bskyed par bshad
pa dang sgrub lugs dang sngags sogs gang la'ang the tshom ma zhugs pa'i skyon yin zhing / gnod sbyin klu bdag nag po zhes bya ba las mkhan shin tu gnyan pa zhig yin tshul
bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras gsung ba sogs dkar chag tu gsal bar yod pa zhib mor dpyod pa gnad du che'o/ /'gor bla ma dam pa rnams dang dpal nag po chen po la phyag
'tshal lo/ /dur khrod na gnas pa'i mgon po gcer bu zangs gri can zhes yod pa'i (mchod rten)sgrub thabs gong ma'i yi ge lhag chad dang bral bar bris pa rdzogs so'i mtha'
can/  me 'bar mar yang bzhugs/ 'gor skad shan sbyar dang dpal mgon po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gtso bo'i nga rgyal sngon song bas zhes yod pa'i bran bdud (mu)(rdo
rje)gshin rje nag po'i sgrub thabs rgya gar gyi mkhan po bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa gzhan la mi spel bar bka' rgyas btab pa gyi ljang gis bsgyur ba/ 'gor 'di'i lung
sbyin pa'i tshul 'dri ste zhes yod pa'i rje sa chen gyis do

pa ston tshul la gnang ba'i (mchod rten)(rdo rje)(dung)bran bdud kyi lung sbyin pa zhes bya ba'i rjes gnang gi yi ge ngag 'dzin yi ge la zin bris byas pa'o'i mtha' can/  me
'bar du yang bzhugs/ 'gor bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal nag po chen po'i drag sgrub spyi'i las la zhes yod pa'i (mchod rten)(rdo rje)(dung)bran bdud kyi
sgrub thabs dpal brtse ba chen po chos kyi rje'i zhal snga nas kyi rjes su bzung ste rgyal khams pa do pa ston tshul la gtsigs su mdzad de gnang ba/ 'gor bla ma dang dpal
ma hA kA la la phyag 'tshal lo/ /nag po lcam dral mchod dang bsten/ /zhes yod pa'i ru mtshon bca' (mchod rten)(rdo rje)thabs kyi yig rnying yar klungs pa sengge rgyal
mtshan gyis zhus dag mdzad pa/  me 'bar mar yang yod/ la la dag bran bdud 'di lugs gzhan zhig tu ngos 'dzin pa dang 'phags pa rin po ches gzigs snang gi mgon po rta nag mar
'dod pa sogs rnam par ma brtags pa kho na ste 'di'i sgrub skor bla ma mal la brtse ba chen pos gser srang gang gis bslus pa'i gtsigs chen yin tshul sogs yig rnying du
yod pas kyang shes nus so/ /bran bdud 'di shin tu bka' gnyan pas gser gyi maNDal dang bcas chig brgyud du gnang ba yang phyag len ma'o/ /gsum pa las sbyor thor bu'i yi ge
la/ dpal nag po chen po dang las byed rdo rje mong spu can gyi sgo nas ser ba dbab pa'i yi ge mgon po'i ser ba rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ 'gor gzhan yang ser ba dbab pa
dang / zhes pa ni dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo bsgom zer ba yod pa'i gong gi gsal byed

kyi yi ge gzhan rnams gzhung na gsal lo'i mtha' can/ 'gor gzhan yang man ngag 'di lta ste zhes yod pa'i rbod gtong bzlog pa'i man ngag mthar ni byang shar mtshams su mnan zhes
pa'i mtha' can/ nag po chen po'i rgyud las rdo rje'i tshig tu sbas nas gsungs pa'i man ngag (rdo rje)(mu)brgyad ces pa dregs byed thams cad gnon par byed pa/ bgegs thams
cad rlag par byed pa/ char dbab pa/ char gcad pa/ yi dwags bskrad pa/ phyag rgya ma 'gugs pa/ rgyal po la sogs pa dbang du bya ba/ rig sngags rbod gtong gcod pa rnams
so/ /lnga pa dkar chag tu ma 'khod pa'i yi ge la/ rdzong chung pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i (mu)dkar chaga'ajam dbyangs mkhyen brtses dpal bde gsal gyi mgon khang
du (zha)mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs khyab bdag sku bzhi ma/ 'gor bla ma la na mo/ nag po chen po'i dbang bskur ba la rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor dang zhes yod pa'i mgon po
lha bcu bdun (mchod rten)ma'i dbang gi tho yig rnal 'byor dbang phyug yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan gyis bla ma'i phyag bzhes bzhin bris so'i mtha' can/ des mdzad pa'i
'gor dpal rdo rje 'chang dbang chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal nag po chen po'i dkyil 'khor du zhes yod pa'i gyi ljang (mchod rten)lugs kyi dbang gi lag len nyi shu
dgu'i dgongs mo bka' gnang ba shin tu gal che gsung ba'i mtha' can/ mgon po lha bcu bdun ma'i sgrub yig paN chen byams pa gling pas mdzad pa rnams legs par thob bo/ /bdun
pa

'dod khams dbang phyug khrag 'thung dud pa'i sol ba can gyi skor la/ de yang dpal ldan lha mo 'dod khams kyi dbang phyug ma la rje khol gnyis su grags pa'i dud pa'i sol ba
can 'di rje mo re ma tI yin zhing / gur mgon gyi skabs mgon po lcam dral gnyis su grags na'ang sa skya pa'i lugs la rjes gnang zur pa med cing sgrub thabs la tshogs bdagabaka'
sdod/ phyi pa/ nang pa ltar sgrub tshul yod kyang man ngag yongs su rdzogs pa med par brten/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes yum bka'i skor gyi rjes gnang man ngag
tshang ba zhig thugs la bzhed nas/ tshul de sa lugs dwags brgyud pa sogs gang du'ang ma rnyed par rim gyis rtsad gcod gnang bas chu mgo gangs dkar gyi dpe bzhin/ rje mar
pas/ dud sol lha mo ma gtogs pa'i/ /bstan srung brgya dang rtsa brgyad zhus/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar shin tu gces spras su mdzad pa'i lha mo'i skor 'di spyir dpal nA ro pa
la bstan srung brgya rtsa brgyad yod pa'i khrod nas gtor ma dngos su len pa'i chos skyong gsum yod pa'i nang nas gdam nga 'di la mdzad pas rten 'brel gyi sgo 'grigalo gsum
bal po'i mthil du bsdad/ /rje byin rlabs can gyi bal po la/ /rgyud gnyan por grags pa'i gdan bzhi zhus/ /chos skyong dud sol lha mo zhus/ /zhes bal po pham mthing pa spyi
ther ba las kyang gsan cing rje mar pa la slob ma'i gtso bo ka chen bzhi'i nang gi rngog chos kyi rdo rjes lo tsA ba'i chos skyong gi gtso bor dud sol ma/ kaM ka rtsal/
thod phreng can gsum zhus pas gsum ga mi yong 'dam btang bar kye rdor dang

gdan bzhi sogs rgyud mang po'i bka' srung du 'dug pa dang bla ma yang thugs gtsigs che bar 'dug pa sogs nas 'dod khams ma 'dams te rdzogs par gsan/ de nas rngog tshang 'og
mar grags pa'i rngog ston chen po bsod nams bstan 'dzin gyi bar du rigs dang chos kyi brgyud pa zam ma chad pa'i nges shes kyi gnas chen por gyur te rjes gnang sgrub skor
dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs par gsan/ phyogs der bla ma'i sku srog la bsdo ba'i bsgral bya'i zhing zhig 'dug pa chos bka' rnams rdzogs par gnang ba'i bka' drin gsob ched
du chos skyong 'di'i sgo nas gtor ma la brten pa'i las sbyor mdzad pas ring por ma lon par rjes med du gyur pa sogs ngo mtshar yid ches dang ldan pa'i chos skor la/ dpal
ldan lha mo 'dod khams kyi dbang phyug ma 'jigs byed dud pa'i sol ba can gyi chos skor gyi dkar chag snyan brgyud gsal ba'i me long zhes bya ba rdo rje 'chang tshar pa
chos rjes mdzad pa/ de las bstan pa'i gdams pa la/ 'gor bla ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal ldan lha mo'i sgo nas gtor ma'i rjes gnang byed par 'dod pas zhes yod
pa'i lha mo phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang gi yi ge rngog zhe sdang rdo rjes mdzad pa/  'di nyid kyi lag len gsal byed rngog bsod nams don grub kyis gzhung ri bo khyung lding
gi chos grwar mdzad pa ni dpe ma 'byor pas ma thob/ 'gor lha mo chen mo la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dang po rten rdzas thams cad tshogs par byas la zhes yod pa'i lha mo gsang
sgrub kyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa nan chags mar grags pa'i rtsa ba'i yi ge rngog zhe sdang rdo rjes mdzad

pa/ de'i gsal byed mar rngog gi phyag len zhes pa'i gsang sgrub rjes gnang gi yi ge mkhas pa'i dbang po blo gsal rgya mtshos bskul ba la brten nas rngog bsod nams bstan 'dzin
gyis stod lung mtshur phu'i gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa/ ma mo spyi'i rgyud dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma me lce 'bar ma'i rgyud le'u nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa au DyAn gyi gnas
chen por mkha' 'gro ma Dombi ka ma la'i zhal snga nas dang sgyur byed kyi lo tsA ba cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis zhus te gtan la phab pa/ dud sol ma'i sgos rgyud dpal
lha mo nag mo dngos grub thams cad 'byung ba'i rgyud le'u bco lnga pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po nA ro pa dang bod kyi lo tsA ba bande lo ka shrIs bsgyur ba/ yang lo paN de
gnyis kyis bsgyur ba'i 'dod khams dbang phyug ma phyi sgrub kyi rgya gzhung zhes pa bsnyen pa/ smyo zhing bsad pa/ bsam gtan gyis gsod pa rnams ston pa'i mkha' 'gro dud sol
ma'i sgrub thabs mkhas pa chen po bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/  'di dang me 'bar ma'i phyi pa ltar sgrub pa gnyis khyad par med ces dkar chag tu gsung pa ltar zhus
dag kyang pher ba 'dug go/ de'i bsdus don sa bcad 'gor/ dpal ldan lha mo nag mo la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /'di sgrub pa la don bzhi ste zhes yod pa rdzogs byang gi mtha'
can/ bsnyen pa la don bco lnga/ sgrub pa/ las sbyor/ smyo zhing bsad pa la don lnga/  don lnga zer yang rdzas bsags pa nas sbyin sreg gi bar brgyad 'dug go/ bskyar ba'i
cho ga dang bcas pa'i lag len shin tu zab cing gsal ba rgya gzhung gi 'grel pa zhal gdams mar grags pa zhag bdun du ci yang mi za bar byed do des nges par 'grub bo'i mtha'

can/  snyan brgyud po tir bzhugs pa'i yig chung yid bzhin nor bu dang zhus dag pher zhes dkar chag na snang ngo / /'gor dpa' bo chu skyes sngon po'i mdog ces yod pa'i 'dod
khams dbang phyug ma'i bsnyen pa'i yi ge rje mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyi gsung las byung ba bla ma'i zhal nas gsung ba rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ 'gor dpal he ru ka la phyag
'tshal lo/ /dam tshig ldan pa'i sngags pa yis/ /zhes yod pa'i sgrub pa dang las sbyor gyi zhal gdams shin tu zab pas gsang bar bya zhes pa'i mtha' can/ mar pas nA ro pa
la chos skyong zhus pa'i lo rgyus yod pa'i lha bskyed/ bzlas pa/ rmi ltas/ srog thun sum cu'i rno tshad/ bzlas pa'i skyon yon/ sgrub pa/ las sbyor/ sbyin sreg gsum gyi dkyil
'khor la brten tshul/ bod rbad bsad gsum gyi sngags byang / gtor ma dang ling ga bltab tshul rnams chos sde gcig tu bzhugs pa'i 'dod khams dbang phyug ma'i zhal gdams
rngog gzhung pa yab sras la gnang ba/  'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'dod khams dbang phyug ma'i zhal gdams bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge zhes pa 'dug 'gor ma
hA de wI na mo/ gzhan yang bdag gi rmi ltas su zhes yod pa'i sgrub pa las sbyor gyi yi ge zhal gdams rmi ltas mar grags pa dpal ldan lha mo'i rmi ltas rdzogs so'i mtha'
can/ 'dod khams dbang phyug dud sol ma'i gsang sgrub kyi rgya gzhung rgya gar gyi mkhas pa chen po nA ro pas mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi blo
gros kyis bsgyur ba/  yig cha'i kha yig na birWa pas mdzad zer ba 'dug pa 'khrul gzhi byung ba ste 'di dur khrod dga' ba'i tshal du rnal 'byor

dbang phyug birWa pa la lha mos dngos su gnang nas shar phyogs nag po las brgyud pa yin gyi yig cha 'di ga mdzad pa ni min no/ /de'i 'grel pa'i lag len ma 'dod khams dbang
phyug drag mo rkang thang ma rno ba'i mde'u ha la reg chod ces bya ba zhe sdang rdo rjes yi ge ra bris pa/ 'gor dpal he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /lha mo sgrub pa'i thabs
la gru gsum steng du zhes yod pa'i drag mo rkang thang gi sgrub thabs thun mong ma yin pa rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ drag mo rkang thang yang snying bkol ba'i sgrub thabs dud
sol ma mngon sum du bkol ba'i man ngag tu grags pa rngog zhe sdang rdo rjes mdzad pa/ 'gor dpal khrag 'thung gi rgyal mo la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dur khrod sol ba can gyi sgrub
thabs ni zhes yod pa'i 'dod khams dbang phyug yang gsang rkang thang du sgrub pa'i yi ge rngog zhe sdang rdo rje'i zhal gdams ji lta ba bzhin du bkod pa'i mtha' can/
tshe dang bsod nams rgyas par byed pa'i las sbyor gyi yi ge longs spyod thams cad lha'i dbang po dang mnyam mo'i mtha' can/ la cha'i sdig par brten nas ma mo rang gi lus
dang grib ma bzhin 'grogs pa'i rten gyi yi ge dpal ldan lha mo'i sgo nas dgra la ltas ngan dbab pa'i thabs bstan pa'i yi ge rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ dpal ldan lha mo'i
mngon par shes pa sgrub pa'i lag len gnad dbab dang bcas pa slob dpon chen po zhe sdang rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so'i mtha' can/  gong ma 'di la pra rten gyi khye'u sogs
'dug pa dang 'og ma 'dir khye'u med pa'i me long sogs la brten pa'i mo yin pa'i brjod bya 'dug pa nas gong 'og gi ming nor ba yin min som nyir snang ngo / / dpal ldan lha
mo'i sgo nas pra dbab pa spyan 'dren ma gcig

lha mo ma dang bcas pa/ gri snying sogs la brten nas mngon shes bsgrub pa/  dkar chag na 'di logs su med la zhal gdams dang bcas zer ba'i zhal gdams yin nam snyam/ spyan 'dren
thod pa dgu brtsegs 'phrul gzhal ma rgyal tsha rdo rje sems dpas mdzad pa/ mchod 'bul/ khyed la gtsang dme'i rtog pa mi mnga' ma/ gzhan yang mchod 'bum ma/ gtor bskang
bandha lcang lo ma/ thugs dam bskang zhing phrin las bskul ba/ bdag ni rig 'dzin ma rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ gtor gshegs dpal ldan ma/ gtor gshegs bzlog bsgyur dang bcas
pa rdo rje gar dbang ma/ bstan ma skyong ba/ bka' yi tshogs bcas ma rnams dud sol gtor chog gi lhan thabs skabs nye bar mkho ba/ bstod snying / sems nyid phrin las ma/
zhabs btags mar yang yod/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis dge ba bcu'i sgo nas bstod pa/ sngon 'das bskal pa ma/  tshig zur tsam ma gtogs rags rim zhus dag pher ba me 'bar
mar yang bzhugs/ phyogs bcu'i lha mo 'khor dang bcas pa'i sgo nas bskul ba/ ma mo'i gtso bo ma/ 'dod khams dbang phyug khrag 'thung dud sol ma'i phrin las kyi las byang
rgyas pa DA ki ma'i thugs kyi ze'u 'bru dbye bar byed pa'i man ngag rgya mtsho gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba sngags 'chang A nanda dhwa dza dang btsun pa kye rdo rje
shrI badzra gnyis kyis ngan rtog spangs nas rgyud sgrub thabs rnams dang mthun par bsgrigs pa dang bcas pa rnams kyi smin grol rjes gnang nyams khrid lung man ngag phyag
bzhes dang bcas pa'i sgo nas legs par thob pa'i dang po rnal 'byor dbang phyug

birWa pa nas brgyud pa'i nag po chen po dpa' bo gcig pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa
pa/ grub dbang shar phyogs nag po pa/ rgyal rigs DA ma ru pa/ gnyis spangs a wa dhU tI pa/ paN chen ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ thugs sras se mkhar chung pa/
bla ma zhang ston chos 'bar/ brtse chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po
'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor
chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams sengge/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ rgyal ba lha mchog sengge/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog
rgyal mtshan/ zhabs drung a mi lags yab sras/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ mkhan po rin po
che sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na ngor chen la mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug paN chen grags
pa rgyal mtshan/ gung ru shes rab bzang po bzhis gsan/ de bzhi char las kun mkhyen bsod nams sengge/ de las yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba dang / mus chen sangs rgyas rin
chen gnyis kyis

gsan/ de gnyis ka las thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis gsan pa man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs gnyis pa ba ri lo tsA ba nas brgyud pa'i mgon po dpa' gcig gi rjes gnang
gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ dze tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa a shwa ka shrI/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/
rje btsun sa skya pa kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen
bsod nams brtan pa/ bla ma bsod nams skyabs/ mkhas pa gzungs kyi dpal ba/ rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje btsun lha mchog sengge/ rje sangs rgyas sengge/ brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas
grub dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med shes bya bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa bkra shis lhun grub/
de las bdag tshul khrims rin chen gyis thob bo/ /yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ mkhas grub dpal rdor ba/ dkon mchog 'phel ba man snga ma dang 'dra'o/ /yang na ngor
chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams sengge/ rje ratna wardha man 'dra/ 'di'i sgrub skor kha skong po ti'i mchod rten dang
e

rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni ngor chen nas/ mus chen/ mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba/ mkhyen rab
bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande
tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /mchod rten dang buddha'i rtags can gyi lung ni/ ngor chen nas/ mus chen/ rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros
rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun kun spangs chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ khyab bdag dbang
phyug rab brtan/ bka' 'gyur ba chen po mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub man gong dang
'dra'o/ /bka' babs bzhi pa kha che paN chen nas brgyud pa'i spu gri skor gsum ga dang lhan cig pa'i mchod rten gyi rtags can gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bram
ze mchog sred nas rim par kha che'i paNDi ta shAkya shrI/ sa paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ dge slong zla ba rgyal kye rdor zhal lan gsum gzigs par grags/ mtshan/ bla
ma khams pa/ ri pa dge tshul/ 'di rnams kyis chos skyong lan lnga re gzigs skad/ dar ma dpal/ rim bzhin yab chos rje 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan man zhal ngo nang
brgyud ltar ro/ /e rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ dar ma dpal nas rim

bzhin/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang man gong ngor lugs bzhin no/ /bka' babs gsum pa'i gri gug lha lnga/ lha brgyad/ lha bcu gnyis pa rnams kyi rgya gzhung lugs kyi dbang rdo rje
dang g.yung drung can gyi lung bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur/ slob dpon bram ze mchog sred/ nor bu gling pa/ shraddhA ka ra warma/
lo chen rin chen bzang po/ bla ma brag steng pa/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ bkras lung pa nam mkha' bsod nams/ dge sdings pa chen po/ rje sangs rgyas dpal
ba/ rin chen gling pa/ dkar shongs pa rin chen rdo rje/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rdzong chung pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/  'jam dbyangs grags pa'ang zer dbang lnga po'i
dkyil chog mdzad po de yin/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang /  jo gdan khrom yon yang zer/ brag thog pa dpal 'dzin bzang po/ rje rdo rje gdan pa/ de las klu dbang gling
pa  gnas kyi ming yin zhing yongs grags la thugs sras zer/ kun dga' rgyal po dang / lcang lo can pa bsod nams mchog ldan gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis las rig 'dzin tshe dbang
bkra shis/ tshar pa rdo rje 'chang chen po/ bod mkhar ba byams pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras sngags 'chang bsod nams dbang phyug de

yi sras sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan po mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ thams cad mkhyen pa chen po bkra shis lhun

bsod nams dpal ldan/ kun mkhyen dpal ldan chos skyong bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas/ shar pa ye shes
chen po/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon po/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/ dol po kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byang chub sengge/ theg chen chos rje man 'dra/
lha brgyad rgya gzhung lugs kyi dbang brgyud gcig la/ rdo rje gdan pa nas/ yangs pa can pa byang chub dbang rgyal/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis man gong dang
'dra/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon/ skyi ston grags rgyal/ kun mkhyen dol bu/ mkhan chen byang sems pa/ theg
chen pa man 'dra/ gri gug lha lnga rgya gzhung lugs kho na'i dbang brgyud gcig la/ 'phags pa rin po che nas/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ bag
ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rje kun dga' rnam rgyal man 'dra'o/ /yang gri gug

lha lnga'i dbang dang lha bcu gnyis ma bcu bdun ma rnams thun mong gi dbang brgyud lugs gcig la/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa/ bla brang
pa nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ rje ye shes dpal bzang / rgyal sras blo bzang dpal 'byor/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/
rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje man 'dra/ yang lha bcu gnyis ma'i brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ shraddhA ka ra nas/ jo bo rje/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ dge tshul pUrNa ba/
rgya lcags ri gong pa/ rdzing bu kha pa shAkya grags/ spen phug pa dar ma shAkya/ zhang ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ze ba don grub ye shes/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ bar thang
chos grags/ bla ma dar ma shAkya bsod nams dbang phyug gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa ta dben chen po/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims brtan pa/ byams pa gling pa bsod nams rnam
rgyal/ thams cad mkhyen pa tshar pa chos rje man 'dra/ yang na bsod nams dbang phyug bla ma mchog ldan/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rin chen rdo rje/ mkhan chen dbang

lha lnga sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor du snyan brgyud lugs kyi dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ a nangga badzra/
padma badzra/ indra bhU ti/ phun tshogs

bde ba/ nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ ga ya dha ra/ bla chen 'brog mi/ se mkhar chung ba/ zhang ston  rol pa'i rdo rje zhes lakShmI'i gsan yig tu byung / chos 'bar/
rje brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon rin po che dpal ldan rtse mo'i zhabs/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/

khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag dbang pa/ mkhan chen byang chub sengge/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang
/ brag thog pa dpal 'dzin bzang po/ rje btsun kun dga' rnam rgyal/  'jigs med dpa' bo yang zer/ klu dbang gling pa kun dga' rgyal po/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis/

skyong / des bdag la'o/ /gyi ljang lugs kyi mgon po

gshin rje ltar sgrub pa lha bcu bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa mtha' brten sku gsung thugs kyi rjes gnang bzlas lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i dbang
gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ slob dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rje/ grub chen nag po ro 'dzin/ lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar ba/ tshar dgu ston pa/ grub
thob bsod  'di rmor gyi la ma byung nams grags/ mon mig dmar ston pa/ bla chen ra lam pa/ bla ma zhang ston pa/ long gro byang chub dar/ de las lce mdo sde dang / dpal chen
skye med/ jo gdan gsum gyis zhus/ de gsum ka las grub ston shAkya 'bum/ dge bshes dbugs/ sa skya pa dharma gzi brjid/ nyi thog pa sngags 'chang kun dga' zla ba/ 'dar
yar 'dren mkhan po blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen sengge dpal bzang / brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rje kun dga' rnam rgyal/ thugs sras klu dbang gling pa man 'dra/
yang na grub ston shAkya 'bum/ de la dkar gshongs pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan dang bdag po bsod nams yon tan pas gsan/ de gnyis las bla chen chos dpal bzang pos gsan/ de nas
lo tsA ba manydzu shrI dznyA na/ rje mus chen rnam rgyal bzang po/ rje klu dbang gling pa man 'dra'o/ /yang na tshar chen nas/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug sngags

rkyang pa'i

brgyud lugs gcig la/ rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ dad byed go cha/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti shalo chen rin chen bzang po/ dge tshul pUrNa/ rgya lcags
ri gong kha ba/ rdzing bu kha ba shAkya grags/ spen phug pa dar ma shAkya/ zhang ye shes rgyal mtshan/ gze pa don grub ye shes/ khams pa sa phug pa shAkya rdo rje/  'di
gnyis la bar thang pa yab sras zer/ bar thang pa chos grags/ slob dpon dar ma shAkya/ spur ston bsod nams dbang phyug bla ma mchog ldan pa/ skyi ston pa grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ bla ma rin chen rdo rje/ mkhan chen byang chub sengge/ mkhan chen nam mkha' ye shes/ de gsum ga las theg chen chos kyi rgyal pos gsan/ de nas rje 'jam dbyangs grags
pa/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / mus srad pa man sindhU ra'i dbang dang 'dra/ yang na skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/ dol po kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ mkhan
chen byang chub sengge/ theg chen pa man 'dra/ yang na spur bsod nams dbang phyug nas/ gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa/ ta dben chen po/ lo tsA
ba tshul khrims brtan pa/ byams pa gling pa bsod nams rnam rgyal/ rje kun dga' rnam rgyal man 'dra'o/ /rjes gnang skor la/ gur gyi mgon po lcam dral lha gsum gyi rjes gnang

shraddhA ka ra warma/ jo bo rin chen bzang po/ gu rub  lo rgyus na go rub pa

rin chen bsod nams zhes pa 'di sku tshe'i stod rab byung gi mtshan dang sku tshe'i smad la dkar chas su gyur pa'i mtshan brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims zhes grags pas tha
dad du mi bzhed do/ /rin chen bsod nams/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos
rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro mgon 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos

mkha' dpal bzang gi gsan yig las de ltar 'byung la/  zhabs drung rgyal rtse bas shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas la'ang gsan 'dug ces gsan yig dbang gi rgyal por 'byung / 'dir
ni 'gro mgon 'phags pa'i rjes su dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen
kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo

gros rgyal mtshan/ rje rdo ring pa/ rje blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug yab sras gnyis ka las mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan dang / sngags
'chang bsod nams chos 'phel gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka las rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan dang / mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags gnyis kyis gsan/ phyi ma las sa
skya bdag chen kun dga' bsod nams/ rgyal mkhar rtse pa ngag dbang bsod nams/ rje ri khrod pa kun dga' rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang

mtshan/ sa skya pa a mi'i drung ngo / /rje thar rtse nas/ sngags 'chang blo gros/ de la'ang a mi'i drung gis so/ /yig cha ni thog mar mal los tho tsam mdzad/ de rjes 'phags
pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa sogs kyis mdzad pa'i yig cha yod la/ 'dir paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i gur gyi mgon po lha bcu gnyis ma sbags te sgrub pa'i

khrims/ shar pa

ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ rgyal ba lha mchog sengge/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas sengge/

rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA/ rje btsun dkon mchog grags pa/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / grub mchog rdo rje'i
mtshan can/ bla ma nam mkha' chos dar/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ byams pa bkra shis lhun

grub/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ 'phags pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ mkhas mchog bkra shis dbang phyug bka' drin can bkra shis bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin
chen la bka' drin stsal to/ /yang na rje shes rab rgyal mtshan nas/ brang ti pa paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'di'i bar nas bla ma kha cig btsal dgos so/ /de nas chos
rje bkra shis dpal ldan/ rje ri khrod pa buddha sA ga ra/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang bkra shis lhun
grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /lha bcu gnyis ma'i
rjes gnang gi brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ dam pa kun dga' grags yan gong ltar las/ de nas dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bdag
chen gzhi thog pa/ bdag chen kun dga' rin chen/ bdag chen grags pa blo gros/ bdag chen blo gros dbang phyug drung btsun rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin
chen/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje man gong dang 'dra'o/ /lcam dral lha gsum thun mong ma yin pa dang / lha brgyad thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa dang / lha bcu gnyis thun

mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur/ bram ze

man

'dra/ gur gyi mgon po gsang sgrub lha dgu'i rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa gsang ba'i yang gsang rje tshar chen yan snyan brgyud 'ba' zhig tu bzhugs pa la/ tshar chen gyis
tho tsam mdzad pa dbang phyug rab brtan gyis tshig sna cung zad bsrings ba kha byang rgya skad yod pa'i steng ngam mkhan chen ngag chos pas mdzad pa gang rung gi steng nas

yongs 'dzin ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen kun dga' tshul khrims/ chos rje buddha shrI bha dra/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun
grub/ rdo rje 'chang chen po bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /srung 'khor rdo rje brag rdzong ma bsrung zlog bsad gsum gyi phyi khrid/ nang khrid drag po sngags rgod
