chen ngag dbang chos grags/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ khams ston bkra shis dpal ldan/ khams ston sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun
tshogs/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la nyams khrid zab mo smin rgyas
su 'khor lo mdo'i pho brang gi ba gam gsum par legs par stsal to/ /yang kun gyi spyod yul ma yin pa gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi
mgon po lcam dral lha dgu rtsa gsum 'khor lo lnga la brten nas bsgrub pa'i gsang khrid thun mong ma yin pa snying nang gi khrag lta bu zhal shes snyan brgyud kyi khrid thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje yan gong ltar las/ de nas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang
dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ he ru ka dpal ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /tshar
chen gyis mdzad pa'i rgyun gyi nyams len

dang / nang 'khor lo lnga la brten pa'i las sbyor/ khrid rje mkhyen brtse pas mdzad pa'i steng nas mdzad cing lung yang thos so/ /tshe sgrub kyi brgyud pa ni/ chos rje bla
ma dam pa nas/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / rje bsod nams dbang phyug rje btsun rdo ring pa/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje man 'dra'o/ /yang
khrid yongs rdzogs kyi brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ tshar chen yab sras gnyis nas sngags 'chang sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen
rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /brgyud pa 'di las 'ongs pa'i lcam dral lha gsum/ lha brgyad/ lha bcu gnyis
ma rnams kyi thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang so sor thob bo/ /de dag gi rgyab brten lung gi skor la/ lha/ rgya/ sdings/ yar gyi rtags yod pa rnams ma gtogs
pa'i me 'bar ma dang kha skong gnyis kyi mchod rten gyi rtags can rnams dang / gya/ ngag sa/ lo'i rtags can rnams ma gtogs pa'i snyan brgyud po ti'i rtags yod med yongs
rdzogs kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/  pho rkyang gi thog ma'i brgyud rim du/ rdo rje 'chang / klu sgrub/ ArYa de wa/ birWa pa/ nag po pa/ mchog sred ces sgo rum dpe khang
gi sa chen gyi phyag bris ngo ma bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis rnyed pa las byung ngo / /rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje nas/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mthu stobs
kyi dbang phyug bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag mkhan

chen zhwa lu pa/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub man 'dra/ yang me 'bar ma'i phyi'i chos skor nang sgrub kyi yi ge lnga/ gsang ba thun mong ma yin pa'i
yi ge bdun dang bcas pa'i lung gi brgyud pa lugs gcig la tshar chen dang / kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zhabs gnyis ka las/ sngags 'chang sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhyen rab
bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub man gong bzhin no/ /rdo rje'i rtags can rnams kyi lung brgyud ni/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rgyal mchog brag thog pa bsod
nams bzang po/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa man gong bzhin no/ /rdo rje dpal be'u can gyi lung brgyud ni/ yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan blo gros/ dmar
chos kyi rgya mtsho/ paN chen byams pa gling pa/ rje btsun kun dga' rnam rgyal man 'dra'o/ /ru rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / grub chen bram ze mchog
sred/ la li ta badzra/ nag po ro 'dzin/ gyi ljang dbu dkar ba/ gshen rdo rje sengge/ 'brom rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ sgom rin chen sengge/ sengge dpal/ chos kyi rin chen/ dmar
bsod nams 'phel/ sangs rgyas 'bum/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ bag ston/ thog ston shes rab rdo rje/ rin chen 'phel/ rgya ma ba yon tan
'od/ mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/ rgya ston tsandra de ba/ ri khrod pa bsod nams rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ byas 'gyur
ba bsod nams sengge/ 'gos ston rdo rje

sengge/ bla chen nam mkha' gzi brjid/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug drung kun dga' legs pa/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ drin
chen rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ de man chad snga ma dang 'dra ba nyid do/ /sa rtags can gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug
rab brtan nas/ sa skya pa chen po ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras 'jam dpal rdo rje bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub man 'dra/ yang ngag gi
rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni/ sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel nas/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ khri chen ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras ngag dbang bsod nams
dbang phyug mkhan chen zhwa lu pa man 'dra/ lo rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje yan gong ltar las/ de nas bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal
mtshan/ spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ lo pa spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams man 'dra'o/ /yang gyi ljang lugs kyi mgon
po'i chos skor yongs rdzogs kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur/ slob dpon bram ze mchog sred/ la li ta badzra/ grub thob nag po ro 'dzin/
lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar ba/ tshar dgu ston pa/ gru gu ston pa/ dge bshes dbugs/ sa skya pa dge slong dharmA gzi brjid/ nyi thog pa sngags 'chang kun dga' zla ba/
mdar mkhan po blo

gsal rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen sengge dpal/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ thugs sras klu dbang gling pa/ drin chen tshe dbang bkra shis/
rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen ngag dbang
chos grags/ rje ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ sa skya pa chen po ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub man gong dang 'dra'o/ /yang na bram ze mchog
sred nas/ badzra pA Ni/ ku ku ri pa/ la li ta badzra/ gyi ljang dbu dkar ba/ gru gu ston pa/ mon mig dmar ston pa/ ra lam ston pa/ mgon po jo zhang / lang 'gro byang
chub dar/ lce ston mdo sde sengge/ gru ston shAka 'bum/ dkar gshongs pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ mnga' ris bla chen chos dpal bzang po/ stag tshang lo tsA ba manydzu shrI/
rtsang byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ mus chen rnam rgyal dpal bzang / thugs sras klu dbang gling pa man 'dra'o/ /yang na gru ston shAka 'bum nas/ bdag po bsod nams yon tan/
mnga' ris bla chen man 'dra/ yang na bram ze chen po nas/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ shraddhA ka ra/ jo bo dI paM ka ra/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po/ dge tshul purNa/ rgya lcags
ri gong kha ba/ rdzing bu kha pa shAkya grags/ spen phug pa dar ma shAkya/ zhang ston ye shes/ bze pa don grub/ bar thang pa yab sras/ slob dpon dar shAkaspur bsod nams
dbang phyug bla ma mchog ldan/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal

mtshan/ bla ma rin chen rdo rje/ mkhan chen nam mkha' ye shes/ mkhan chen byang chub sengge/ phyi ma gsum char las theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rdzong chung pa kun dga' rgyal
mtshan/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / rtsang byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /yang na skyi ston/ dol bu kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byang
chub sengge/ theg chen pa man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ nag po ro 'dzin/ gyi ljang dbu dkar ba/ mal lo blo gros grags pa/ sa skya pa chen po/ bla
chen yar sgom se bo/ rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin chen sengge bzang po/ yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam
dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen 'bum phrag gsum pa/ rje tshul khrims pa/ tshar pa rdo rje 'chang man 'dra'o/ /kha skong
po ti'i mu g.yung drung can gyi brgyud pa'ang 'di nyid do/ /me 'bar/ kha skong / snyan brgyud gsum gyi chos skor gter byon gyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa
klu sgrub/ 'dis rdo rje gdan gyi ka ba la gter du sbas/ de nas dpal au DyAn chen po padma badzra gyis spyan drangs nas rgya gar shar phyogs dharma pA lar gnang / des ti
se dang mtsho ma dros pa gzigs pa'i ched du byon pas lo tsA ba chen po mjal bar gdams pa rnams gnang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po man gong bzhin no/ /me 'bar po ti'i phyi
sgrub yig sna brgya dang nyi shu'i brgyud pa lugs gcig

ni/ yab 'jam dbyangs chen po nas/ gcen rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ yab sras gnyis ka las gcung bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / de las rdo ring rin po che dang mkhan chen ratna
shI las gsan/ gsum ka las rje btsun sgo rum pa/ de nas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na tshar pa rdo rje 'chang chen po nas/ rje bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub
rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ rab 'byams chos rje kun dga' lhun grub/  chos sku rdo rje yang zer/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba/ mkhan chen rin chen
bsod nams mchog grub man 'dra'o/ /rgya rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / klu sgrub/ au DyAn chen po/ mkha' 'gro ye shes 'tsho rgyal/ mnga' bdag khri srong lde'u
btsan/ gter ston rgya padma dbang phyug lho pa ston nyi/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen sengge bzang po/ yar klungs pa
sengge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal ba/ brag phug pa bsod
nams dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang phyi khrid nang khrid/ de las 'phros pa'i yi ge me 'bar dkar chag gi
gsang ba thun mong ma yin pa'i yi ge mchod rten gyi rtags can rnams kyi lung brgyud ni/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan nas/ do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tsha lung
mang po man 'dra/ bran bdud kyi chos tshan gsum gyi lung ni/ sa chen

nas/ zhang mnga' ris pa/ dge gnyan sras mchog mgon po/ dol po 'byung gnas pa/ bla ma mgon pa rgya/ do pa ston tshul man 'dra'o/ /yar gyi rtags yod pa'i lung brgyud ni/ rje
btsun sa skya pa chen po nas/ bla chen yar sgom se bo/ rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen sengge bzang po/ yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan
chen bsod nams rgyal mchog yab rje 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon dpal ldan rgyal po/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ bdag chen
ngag gi dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje man mchod rten gyi rtags can dang 'dra/ sdings rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni/ dam pa kun dga' grags nas/ bla ma rdo rje
dpal/ mtshungs med bkra shis dngos grub/ sbas pa'i rnal 'byor bar sdings pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ yab chos rje 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan man zhal ngo nang brgyud
bzhin no/ /dkar chag tu ma 'khod pa'i yi ge sa bcad bcu gsum po'i lung brgyud ni mchod rten gyi rtags can rnams dang mthun no/ /dud sol ma phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang gi
brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ lus med ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa lo tsA ba/ rngog chos sku rdo rje/ zhu
chos sdings pa/ sha sgang pa/ gnyags ston chen po/ gnyags dge bshes mus pa/ mdo sde grags/ slob dpon jo ye/ gnyags gnas gsar ba/ gle lung jo sras ma gcig dgon chung

ma/ mus chen rgyal mtshan bzang po/ gug shrI rin po che/ smon lam rdo rje/ bsod nams blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ sngags 'chang mchog rgyal ba/ mus chen sangs rgyas
rin chen/ lo pa ngag dbang chos grags/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' legs grub/ byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag
dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngag dbang chos grags nas/ sangs rgyas sengge/ mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / mchog legs rdo rje man
'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang / bram ze sa ra ha/ mgon po klu sgrub/ DA ki ma bskal pa bzang mo/ slob dpon lwa ba pa/ de bzhi ka las tai lo pas gsan pa man 'dra/ gsang sgrub
rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa nan chags mar grags pa dang chos skor gyi lung yongs rdzogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rngog chos sku rdo rje nas/ rngog zhe sdang rdo rje/ rngog
thogs med grags/ rgyal tsha ra mo/ rngog kun dga' rdo rje/ rngog gzi brjid grags/ rngog rin chen bzang po/ rngog chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rngog don grub dpal/ rngog byang
chub dpal/ rngog khra tshang pa bsod nams don grub/ rngog shAkya don grub/ rngog thar gling pa bsod nams lhun po/ de sras rngog bsod nams bstan 'dzin/ rdo rje 'chang tshar
pa chos rje/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag
dbang lhun

grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa chen po ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /phyi'i las mkhan gcer bu zangs gri can gyi rjes gnang gi
brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa rin po che yan zhal ngo nang brgyud ltar las/ de nas do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin chen sengge bzang po/
yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ gcen rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen 'bum phrag gsum  'bum
byams pa chos kyi don grub/ pa/ mkhas pa ratna  chos rje tshul khrims pa'ang zer/ shI la/ rje sgo rum pa/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras gnyis ka nas 'jam dbyangs
mkhyen brtse/ de las rje bslab gsum dang rta rwa ba gnyis kas gsan/ yab sras bzhi ka las rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag mkhan chen zhwa lu pa/ mkhyen rab
byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /yang na rje sa chen nas/ yar sgom se bo/ do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tsha lung mang
po man 'dra/ yang na rje btsun sa chen nas/ 'gos ston tshar sgang pa/ dge bshes mi g.yo ba/ gshen sgom bla ma dpal/ slob dpon shes rab bla ma/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga'
ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa/ yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na rje btsun sa paN nas/ mdo khams kyi rta rge bla ma/ slob
dpon shes rab bla ma man

'dra/ lugs gcig la/ rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ badzra pA Ni/ ku ku ri pa/ nag po ro 'dzin/ gyi ljang dbu dkar ba/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa chen man 'dra/ nang gi las mkhan
ber nag zangs gri can gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ 'gos ston tshar sgang pa dang / rta rge bla ma yod pa sor gnas kyi/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen
rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang man chad sngar dang 'dra'o/ /gsang ba'i las mkhan pu tra ming sring
phyi nor srung gnod sbyin pho mo'i tshul dang / nang bsad pa gshin rje pho mo'i tshul du sgrub pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa klu sgrub/ au DyAn
chen po/ paN grub dharma pA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ de las mal lo tsA ba dang / 'brom jo sras zhang dge gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis
ka las bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/
'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rgwa A nan dam pa/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/
grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel
ba/ sa lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun

dga' bsod nams/ grub chen sbas pa'i rnal 'byor dpal ldan bkra shis/ sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po/ sngags 'chang ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ rdo rje 'chang bzang po rgyal mtshan/ 'phags pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun bsod nams dbang
phyug bka' drin can rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na 'phags pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan nas/ mkhas mchog bkra shis
dbang phyug  sde dge lhun grub steng pa/ khams sde dge lhun grub steng pa/ ston rdo rje 'chang nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag tshul rin la'o/ /yang rjes gnang dang lha'i
rtags yod pa'i lung brgyud la rgya gar gyi gter ma dang / bod kyi gter ma gnyis las dang po ni/ bla ma dam pa yan rjes gnang dang 'dra zhing / de nas bla chen kun dga'
rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun rdo ring pa kun spangs pa chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos
rje/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rdo
rje 'chang rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /yang rjes gnang rkyang pa'i brgyud lugs gcig la/ bla ma dam pa yan sngar ltar las/ de nas bla ma dpal ldan
tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal

mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon
mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas sengge/ mkhas grub nam mkha' dpal bzang / ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ drin chen mkhyen rab bla ma
man 'dra'o/ /yang na ngor chen nas/ rgyal tshab rje/ ratna wardha/ dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /bod kyi gter ma'i brgyud pa ltar na/ dpal au DyAn gyi slob dpon chen
po nas/ jo mo mkhar chen bza'/ mnga' bdag khri srong lde'u btsan/ lha btsun byang chub 'od/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po man sngar ltar ro/ /ru mtshon gyi las mkhan bran bdud
gshin rje nag po'i rjes gnang thun mong ba'i brgyud pa ni/ sa paN yan gong zhal ngo nang brgyud ltar las/ de nas do pa ston tshul/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang
phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen sengge bzang po/ yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ tshem bu pa dpal ldan blo gros/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ dpal kun bzang
rtse pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ti'u ra pa chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ gcung 'jam dbyangs ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sngags
'chang ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po/ sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams/ dpon slob kun dga' dpal 'byor/ 'di nas bla ma gnyis tsam btsal dgos/
thams cad mkhyen

pa bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ ku ku ri pa/ dur khrod nag po ro 'dzin/
gyi ljang lo tsA ba dbu dkar/ mal lo tsA ba blo gros grags pa/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po/ bla chen yar sgom se bo/ rgyal khams pa do pa ston tshul man 'dra/ yang na sa
chen nas zhang mnga' ris pa/ dge bsnyen sras mchog mgon po/ dol po 'byung gnas pa/ rgya sgom tshul khrims grags/ do pa ston tshul man 'dra'o/ /de yang gong gi rtsa ba'i
rtags bzhi rgyag pa'i dgos pa ni/ ji skad du/ de dag las 'ongs so so'i ngos 'dzin ni/ /ngor lugs yi ge e yi rtags kyis mtshan/ /rdo rje gdan pa las byung rdo rje'i rgya/
/mus srad pa ni yi ge mu yi rgya/ /bdag chen rdo rje 'chang dbang las brgyud pa'i/ /rtsa ba'i yi ge mchod rten rgya yis mdzes/ /thor bu gzhan dag mchan bu btab pas shes/
/zhes gsungs pa ltar rtogs par bya zhing gong du ngos ma zin pa'i me 'bar kha skong gi ljang gsum la rtags med pa 'ga' zhig byung ba rnams mchan bu 'grol rgyu yi ge ngos
ma ma mthong bas re zhig dpyad par bya'o/ /smras pa/ phyi rol snang ba'i dregs pa rgyud gsum po/ /rang sems gdod ma'i mgon por ngo sprod pa/ /bka' babs rnam bzhi'i dbang
dang byin rlabs khrid/ /rgyab brten glegs bam phal cher lung du mnos/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ gser chos rdo rje nag
po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i chos skor

thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste nyer bzhi pa'o/ // /rnal 'byor dam tshig ldan par rtag 'go zhing / /rgyal gsung gsang mdzod bsrung ba'i g.yar dam mdud/ /mi shigs dam can
yongs kyi sde dpon che/ /zhing skyong gdong bzhi ldan pa'i chos skor la/ /de yang dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rtsa brgyud le'u bcu bdun pa las/ drag po mi sdug khros pa ni/
/utpal sngon po'i kha dog 'dra/ /phyag bzhi pa ni cho ga yis/ /phyag na thod pa bsnams par bsgom/ /zhes dngos su bstan cing / dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bshad rgyud las kyang
gsal bar bstan pa'i stobs 'phrog nag po chen po gdong bzhi pa'am drag po gzi ldan dbang phyug tu grags pa 'di nyid ni/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes/ de ltar rgyal
ba'i dri med rgyud sde las/ /gsungs pa'i bstan srung kun gyi mchog gyur pa/ /drag shul mthu ldan stobs 'phrog nag po zhes/ /rgya bod mkhas grub kun la rlung ltar grags/ /zhes
gsungs pa ltar 'phags pa'i yul du sangs rgyas gnyis pa dpal mgon klu sgrub zhabs/ bsod snyoms pa chen po ta thA ga ta rakShi ta/ ma hA paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa/ ri
sul gyi rnal 'byor ma ku sa li chen mo sogs paN grub du mas chos skyong gi gtso bor mdzad cing / bsil ldan kha ba'i ljongs 'dir skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang po gnyan lo tsA
ba dar ma grags kyis gdan drangs pa'i bstan srung brgya rtsa tsam gyi nang nas gtso bor gyur pa bzung / bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras la bka' babs
bstan pa srung ba'i mtshon char mgon po che chung gnyis su dbye ba'i chung bar

grags shing shin tu rtsub 'gyur che zhing gnyan pas bka' dam par mdzad/ khyad par sbas pa'i mgon po la rigs mang du yod pa'i nang nas sbas pa'i mgon po'am dam tshig gi mgon
po yin pas zhal bzhi yongs rdzogs kyi sku gzugs bris 'bur sogs kyang mi bzhed zhing / re gnyis byung ba dag kyang khyab gdal du ye mi ston pa gnad kyi gdams pa yin gyi/
deng sang 'di'i sku 'dri ba dang ston pa sogs bag med du byed pa rnams ni 'di dag rna bas ma thos shing 'tshub 'gyur mi 'byung ba sogs kyang chos skyong ye ma 'khor ba'i
rtags so/ /des na dam tshig che phra kun la gces par mdzad pa smin grol gdams pa'i gnad mtha' dag ma nyams pa snyan brgyud mkha' 'gro'i kha rlangs thul le ba/ thos bsam gyis
gtan la dbab byar snyan brgyud dang po byin rlabs dang rjes gnang / gnyis pa gdams pa dngos/ gsum pa bla ma dang mkha' 'gro chos skyong longs spyod kyis mnyes par byas
pa la brten nas snyan brgyud bzhi pa'i rten 'brel shugs las 'grig pa'am/ yang na tshar pa rdo rje 'chang gis/ de yang thog mar tshogs kyi 'khor lo dang / /rin chen gser
gyi maNDal la sogs pa/ /snyan brgyud dang po'i rten 'brel kun bsgrigs nas/ /snyan brgyud gnyis pa byin rlabs rjes gnang sbyin/ /snyan brgyud gsum pa gdams pa'i dngos gzhi
'di/ /bklag lung min par lag len dmar khrid du/ /byin pas snyan brgyud bzhi pa shugs las 'byung / /zhes pa ltar rdo rje slob dpon mnyes pa dngos grub kyi rtsa ba dang /
shin tu bka' gnyan pa'i zab

chos rnams la dpon slob gnyis kas tshogs dang bskang bshags sogs kyi sgo nas mkha' 'gro srung ma rnams kyi nyams chag skong zhing bka' rgya bkrol te gnang ba zhu ba ma byas
na 'phral du 'tshub cing mthar mi shis pa la sogs pa 'byung bas lha 'dod yon la longs spyod pa lta bu'i snyan brgyud dang por byas te/ gnyis pa chu bo ganggA'i rgyun lta
bu/ gsum pa gser 'gyur gyi rtsi lta bu/ bzhi pa chos la yid ches kyi mos gus rnyed pa gzhon nu'i dga' ba lta bu'i go rim ste/ de yang bshad tshul gnyis po gang byas kyang
go rims tsam las don la khyad med na'ang phyi ma'i rjes su 'brangs te snyan brgyud dang po'i rten 'brel bsgrig pa sngon du 'gro ba byas nas/ snyan brgyud gnyis pa rjes
gnang dang gsum pa gdams pa'i dngos gzhi gnyis/ dang po la/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang pas mdzad pa'i gnyan mgon chen po zhal bzhi pa yum chen sring mo bzhi dang bcas
pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge'i steng nas sam/ gnyan lo'i gnad yig dang dga' ldan pa kun bsod kyi yi ge dang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge dngos
grub rgya mtsho dang brgyud pa'i phyag len la brten nas bsnyen dus kyi mgon po'i rjes 1gnang / pho nya myur mgyogs dang rjes gnang gi yi ge gong ma rnams la brten nas sgrub
dus thun mong ba'i rjes 2gnang / yi ge de gnyis dang rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa'i bka' rgya ma la sogs pa la brten nas sgrub dus kyi rjes 3gnang thun
mong ma yin pa/ rjes gnang gi yi ge gong ma dang mthong brgyud kyi phyag len dbri snon ltar las sbyor gyi mgon

po'am paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa lugs kyi dpal mgon gdong brnyan can du grags pa'i rjes 4gnang / dngos grub rgya mtsho dang gsang ba thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi yi
ge dang phyag len gsung rgyun ltar gsang khrid kyi rjes 5gnang / las bzhi'i rjes gnang la mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'am 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses mdzad
pa'i yi ge la brten nas dkar po tshe 'phel thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes 6gnang / dkar chag na bzhugs pa'i las bzhi'i mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi yig chung dngos grub rgya
mtsho/ gsung rgyun phyag len ltar g.yas zhal dkar po las byung ba'i dkar po tshe 'phel thun mong ba'i rjes 7gnang / steng zhal dud kha las byung ba'i ser po rgyas byed lha
dgu'i rjes 8gnang / ser po rgyas byed lha lnga'i rjes 9gnang / g.yon zhal dmar po las byung ba'i dmar po dbang sdud kyi rjes 10gnang / rtsa zhal mthing nag las byung ba'i
nag po dgra bgegs sgrol ba'i rjes 11gnang / dngos sgrub rgya mtsho'i yi ge dang mthong brgyud kyi phyag len dbri snon la brten nas shi sa bstan pa'i rjes 12gnang /  'di
la gdong gsum dang brtsegs zhal mar grags/ yig cha dngos gzhi dang tshar chen gyi zin tho la brten nas gnad dbab kyi mgon po nang gshin rje ltar sgrub pa'i rjes 13gnang
/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i zin tho ltar khyung zhal can nam dmag dpon mgon po'i rjes 14gnang / rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje'i zin tho la brten nas gsung ngag
gser chos bcu gsum/ mgon po che chung sogs slob bshad gdams pa phal cher rdzogs mthar

bstan pa gtad pa'i tshul gyis bram ze nag po'i sngags gtad kyi rjes 15gnang dang bcas pa rnams legs par nos so/ /gnyis pa snyan brgyud gsum pa gdams pa dngos la/ man ngag gser
'gyur gyi rtsi lta bu'i nyams khrid/ rgyab brten lung dang phyag bzhes man ngag bcas pa gnyis/ dang po la/ thog mar rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa'i tshe
sgrub srung 'khor rgyun gyi nyams len mar grags pa'i yi ge dang zhal shes la brten cing sngon 'gro gsang khrid nas kha bskangs te phyi nang gi srung 'khor 'chi med sgrub
pa zhar byung bzlog pa dang bcas pa'i phyi'i nyams khrid zab mo/ 'di byin rlabs kyi tshan kha shin tu che bas bla ma gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyis dgung lo brgya dang
lnga bcu bzhugs pa'ang man ngag 'di nyid kyi che ba yin par snang ngo / /rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa'i khrid yig zung 'jug rnam par rol pa bdud sde 'joms
pa'i bshan pa chen po la gzhi byas/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan pas mdzad pa'i lhan thabs yig chung zin bris zhal shes dang bcas pas brgyan nas/ sngon 'gro skyabs
sems/ yig brgya/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ maNDal dang bcas pa'i khrid/ dngos gzhi 'khor lo bzhi la brten pa'i bsnyen pa/ 'khor lo bzhi ldan gyi sgrub pa/ thun mong dang thun
mong ma yin pa'i las sbyor/ zhar byung ma 'grub na spogs chog gi ngo sprod dang bcas te sngon 'gro dngos gzhi rjes gsum tshang ba'i nyams khrid la brten nas rdo rje'i lus
la gnad du bsnun pa'i gnad kyi gzung 'dzin gyi rtsa mdud rnams grol nas cir snang bde ba chen po'i rol par shar

te/ tshe 'di nyid la zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang chen po'i go 'phang mngon du byed nus pa'i gsang khrid kyi nyams khrid zab mo dang zhing skyong dbang po 'khor bcas byang chub
ma thob kyi bar du rang gi snying dbus su 'bral med du bzhugs nas mchog dang thun mong gi dngos grub ma lus pa stsol ba'i dmar khrid dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud
kho na la chig brgyud du bzhugs pa'i nyams khrid zab mo smin rgyas su legs par nos so/ /gnyis pa rgyab brten lung dang phyag bzhes man ngag bcas pa la/ dkar chag gis zin
pa'i skor dang / ma zin pa'i skor te gnyis las/ dang po ni/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gdong bzhi pa'i chos skor gyi dkar chag gsung
rgyun padma'i srad bur brgyus pa'i zab don nor bu'i do shal/ de las gsungs pa'i chos sde'i rnam grangs paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa nas brgyud pa/ shrI paNDi ta ta thA
ga ta rakShi ta nas brgyud pa/ kha sarpA Ni'i ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma ku sa li chen mo nas brgyud pa dang gsum/ dang po la/ 'gor skad shan sbyar dang dpal mgon po nag
po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'jigs pa'i tshogs rnams 'jigs byed pa'i/ /nag po de la phyag 'tshal nas/ /zhes yod pa'i mgon po gdong brnyan can nam las sbyor gyi mgon por grags
pa glang gdong phyag drug pa'i sgrub (glo)(nyi)()thabs kyi rtsa ba'i rgya gzhung slob dpon klu sgrub snying pos mdzad pa paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa dang lo tsA ba gnyan
dar ma grags kyis bsgyur ba/ rgya gzhung gi 'grel pa dri med don

gsal dge bshes dge ba rgyal mtshan gyis bskul nas mdo stod pa 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan gyis nyang brag dga' ldan dgon du mdzad pa/ 'gor tA ra na mo/ dpal gdong bzhi pa'i mngon
rtogs kyi man ngag (glo)paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa'i zhal gdams mthar thug pa ni zhes yod pa'i gtso 'khor lnga'i mngon rtogs chung ngu bla ma gong mas mdzad pa der
rtogs par bya'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rang skad cig gis hU~M mthing nag tu gyur pa las 'od zer 'phros/ zhes yod pa'i gtor chog gi yi ge gong
mas mdzad pa de wI siddhi zhes nyer gcig gam gsum la sogs pas dbul lo'i mtha' can/ 'gor tshangs pa ser po ngang pa zhon zhes yod pa'i 'khor mang gi mngon rtogs tshigs
bcad ma gong mas mdzad pa bka' nyan gsung bstod las byed tshul du bsam gyi mtha' can/ las sbyor gyi gsal byed las kyi sham bu brgyad (glo)(nyi)()pa zhes pa bsad pa'i las/
mdze gtong ba/ rabs gcod pa/ zhing la lo mi skye ba/ rims nad gtong ba/ grong khyer dkrugs pa/ grong bshig pa/ bskrad pa/ smyo bar byed pa/  'di gnyis lhag pa 'dra zhig
byung kyang gong gi khongs su bsdus sam snyam/ dbang du byed pa rnams gnyan los mdzad pa/ 'di yan gyis glang gdong ma'i skor rdzogs nas/ zhar byung 'gor dpal phyag na rdo
rje la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa bsrung ba'i phyir/ /dpal ldan mgon po zhal bzhi pa'i/ /gser gyi spu gri'i lag len 'dri/ /zhes yod pa'i dpal mgon khyung zhal
can nam dmag dpon mgon po'i sgrub

thabs lag len gzhung nas dril nas btus/ sngags 'chang bstan pa bsrung bar shog gi mtha' can rnams so/ /gnyis pa shrI paNDi ta ta thA ga ta rakShi ta nas brgyud pa la/ 'gor
rgya skad dang zhal bzhi pa'i dam tshig dngos grub sgrub pa'i thabs zhes yod pa'i rtsa ba'i sgrub (e)(sgau)(glo)(nyi)thabs  rdzong pod na'ang yod/ ta thA ga ta rakShi tas
mdzad pa'i  bdag mdun mgon po zhal khra can nam sgrub dus kyi mgon por grags shing / deng sang yongs grags sgrub dus kyi mgon po zhal g.yas g.yon mthing nag tu byed pa'i
yi ge 'ga' zhig 'dug kyang tshar lugs la sgrub dus kyang zhal khra can du mdzad pa gzhung 'di'i gnad 'gag gtso bor ston par snang / rgya gzhung rtsom pa po rang nyid dang
gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyis bsgyur ba/ gzhung chung 'di la phrin las rnam bzhi bye brag tu sgrub tshul gyi gnad 'gag kyang zur tsam bstan 'dug cing / rdo rje 'chang
tshar pa chos rjes gsang sgrub gsal byed snying thig gi skabs rgya gzhung las bshad tshul gyi rtsa ba'ang gzhung 'di la brten pa yin no/ /'gor rgya gar gyi yul du chu
bo ganggA dang nyi ma phyed dang gnyis tsam yod pa'i grong chung ngu'i 'gram zhig na zhes yod pa'i gnyan los mdzad pa'i paNDi ta mjal tshul gyi lo rgyus nyung ngu dang sbrel
ba'i (glo)sgrub thabs  rdzong pod na'ang yod/ kyi rim pa bsnyen pa dang las sbyor ston pa zla ba gcig gis las rnams 'grub bo ta thA ga ta rakShi tas gnyan la'o'i mtha'
can rnams so/  phal cher snyan brgyud kyi zhal shes la rag las zhes dkar chag na snang bas yi ge 'di las mang ba zhig thog ma nas med tshod du 'dug gsum pa kha sarpA Ni'i
ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma ku sa li chen mo las

brgyud pa la/ zab cing rgya che ba phyi'i sgrub skor/ rdo rje'i lus la gnad du bsnun pa gsang ba'am nang gi man ngag snying nang gi khrag lta bu khyad par gyi man ngag dang
gsum/ dang po la/ yid ches shing khungs btsun pa lo rgyus kyi yi ge nus ldan du bya ba rjes gnang gi yi ge rtsa bar gyur pa bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge gsal byed du
gyur pa lhan thabs sam yan lag gi yi ge 'phral du nye bar mkho ba gtor chog dang bskang ba bstod bskul gyi yi ge dang lnga/ dang po la/ 'gor na mo gu ru/ man ngag 'di'i brgyud
pa'i lo rgyus ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang zhes yod pa'i lo rgyus kyi yi ge sa chen gyis mdzad pa bon po pho mo 'dres pa lnga bcu tsam chos
skyong gi nus pas bsad zer ro'i mtha' can/  'di'i nang du kha'u par rje btsun sa skya pas zhus zer ba ltar na tshig gcig gnyis slar bsnan pa 'dra'o/ /'gor brgyud pa'i
bla ma rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bka' srung 'di'i lo rgyus ni bla ma rdo rje gdan pa la zhes yod pa'i lo rgyus (nyi)kyi yi ge rgyas pa 'phags pas mdzad pa mnga' bdag kyang
de'u grong blon po la la yang shi skad kyi mtha' can zhar byung bla brgyud dang bcas pa/ gnyis pa nus ldan du bya ba rjes gnang gi yi ge la/ 'gor oM swa sti siddhaM/ nag
po chen po'i lung sbyin pa ni 'byor na tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i rting la bya (sgo)zhes yod pa'i nag po chen po'i rjes gnang gnyan lo tsA bas mdzad pa gdams pa'o'i mtha' can/
rdzong pod na'ang yod/ 'gor bla ma dang tA ra la na mo/ nag po chen po zhal bzhi pa'i rjes gnang la gsum ste zhes yod pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge kha'u pas mdzad pa

smon lam gdab bo zhal bzhi pa'i rjes gnang rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ 'gor na mo gu ru/ dbang thob cing dam tshig ma nyams pas 'di'i rjes gnang dang bka' lung thob cing zhes yod
pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge sa chen gyis mdzad pa smon lam gdab bkra shis bya'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor tA ra la na mo/ 'di'i rjes gnang la don gsum ste sbyor ba dngos gzhi rjes
so zhes yod pa'i rjes gnang (e)(sgo)(glo)gsal  rdzong pod na mchan mi 'dug ba don du gnyer ba 'gas yang yang gsol ba btab pa'i ngor rnal 'byor pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis
bris pa/ 'gor oM swa sti/ srid gsum dbang sgyur dpal ldan nag po che/ /zhes yod pa'i rjes gnang shin tu rgyas pa nag po 'gro shes (nyi)zhes pa dpang por nag po chen po
bzhugs pa 'di rang gi bla mas rjes su gnang nas bkas bskul zhing grogs mched dam pa'i gsung gi ngor rje btsun pa'i yi ge'i steng du 'phags pa'i phyag len dang zhang khu
dbon las brgyud de bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi phyag bzhes ltar yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan gyis klu'i dgon par mdzad pa/ des slob mas bskul ba'i ngor
mdzad pa'i 'gor/ dpal zhal bzhi pa'i rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa la zhes yod pa'i gri snying bla rdo srog 'khor phyag mtshan rnams kyi rjes gnang gi yi ge rnams so/ /gsum
pa rtsa bar gyur pa bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi yi ge la/ kun gyi rtsa ba ri sul gyi rnal 'byor mas mdzad pa'i sgrub (sgo)(glo)(nyi)thabs mchan bshad du grags pa'i yi
ge  rdzong chung pa'i der 'gro ba'i lam du an dha mu shar bcug la sba'o yan las mi 'dug cing gong dkar ba'i glegs bam na de'i 'jug tu grong khyer bskyod pa dang sngags thung
bris pa cig dang yang dngos gzhi dkyus dang mthun pa la ta thA ga ta rakShi ta'i lugs kyi lo rgyus sgrub thabs gnyan gyis mdzad pa de'i lo rgyus chu bo ganggA zhes sogs
yod pa mjug na btags nas bsres pa zhig kyang snang ngo / /gzhung de la brten nas bsnyen sgrub zhar byung mnan pa dang bcas pa 'gor ma hA kA (sgo)(glo)la'i man ngag la
bsnyen sgrub gnyis las zhes yod  rdzong pod na'ang yod/ pa gnyan lo'i u pa de sha'o'i mtha' can/ gnyan los mdzad pa'i chos skyong gi gnad kyi yig chung (sgo)(glo)zhes pa
bsnyen pa/ sgrub pa/ bsad pa/ las sbyor dang bcas pa zhal gyi gdams  rdzong pod na'ang yod/ pa 'di mi la ma spel rnam smin che'o gsung ba'i mtha' can/ mgon po sgrub dus kyi
las rdzong pod na'ang yod/ khrigs (sgo)bla ma kha'u pa chen pos mdzad pa snying phyung rigs brgyud rtsad nas chod ces brjod do'i mtha' can/ 'gor ma hA kA la tsa turmu
kha u pa de sha zhes yod pa'i mgon po sgrub (e)(sgo)(glo)dus kyi las khrigs gsal  rdzong pod na'ang yod/ byed sa chen gyis mdzad pa de'i snying ga bsnun par bya'o'i mtha'
can/ kha'u pas mdzad pa'i las khrigs kyi gsal (e)(sgo)(pha)byed 'gor bla ma mgon po nag po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /mgon po sgrub dus kyi las khrigs la gsum zhes yod
pa'i yi  rdzong pod na las khrigs chen po zhes pa las mdzad pa mi gsal/ ge sngags 'chang gzungs pas mdzad pa dgra na ba dang 'chi ba la sogs pa'i nges par 'grub bo sa mApta
mi thi'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag

'tshal lo/ /dpal ldan nag po chen po gdong bzhi pa bsnyen cing sgrub par 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i bsnyen sgrub (e)(nyi)las gsum gyi sgrub thabs nag po 'gro shes dga' ldan pa
kun bsod kyis mdzad pa sgrub pa dang las sbyor gyi yig chung mi spel gsang bar bya'o'i mtha' can/  rdzong pod na 'di gzungs pa'i nag 'gros su ngos bzung / rnam gsum lag leg
gsal byed zhal nas snyan du brgyud pa'i lag len dmar khrid mthong chog bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi gsung bzhin bsod nams grags pa dpal bzang pos yon tan du
mas mngon par mtho ba'i blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis bskul ba la brten nas zin bris su bkod pa/ bsnyen pa'i go rim gnad don snyan brgyud bdud rtsi'i skyes phreng rnal 'byor
dbang phyug yar klungs pas dad ldan slob ma'i zhal ngor sbyar ba/ des mdzad pa'i 'gor tA ra na maHdpal mgon tsa turmu kha'i bsnyen pa bya bar 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i bzlas
pa dang ge gas sel gyi man ngag snyan brgyud gser chos mthar thugades mdzad pa'i 'gor/ bla ma mchog dang chos skyong la/ /lus ngag yid gsum gus btud nas zhes yod pa'i
bsnyen sgrub las gsum spogs chog shi sa bstan pa dang bcas pa'i mngon rtogs gsal byed gnad kyi zhal gdams mthar thug snyan nas snyan du brgyud pa'i gser chos mchog tu gyur
pa'i mkha' 'gro'i snying khragades mdzad pa'i dpal gdong bzhi pa'i gtor ma bca' thabs kyi snyan brgyud snying gi khrag thigs lta bu/ des mdzad pa'i 'gor/ bla ma yi dam
bstan skyong la/ /sgo gsum gus

pas phyag 'tshal nas/ /zhes yod pa'i las rab 'byams dang bsad bskrad kyi 'khor lo'i zhal gdams chig brgyud ma snying nang gi khrag lta bu/ des mdzad pa'i 'gor/ sangs rgyas
kun dngos bla ma dang / /zhes yod pa'i bye brag tu bsad las kyi 'khor lo'i man ngag mkha' 'gro'i kha rlangs can du grags pa rno myur spu gri reg chod dang 'dra ba'i man ngag
snyan brgyud mthar thugades mdzad pa'i 'gor/ bla ma mchog dang lha mchog la/ /zhes yod pa'i 'khrul 'khor bltab cing sba ba sogs mnan pa'i man ngag mthar 'don thabs dang
bcas pa snyan brgyud sbas don gsal ba/ yar klungs pa'i gsung 'di rnams phyi sgrub la ltos pa'i bka' brgya dam pas mang ba la mi ston pa'i gras/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi

ba nor bar 'dug go/ de'i gsal byed (nyi)'gor tsa turmu kha la na mo/ de'i bka' sdod ma hA bA la zhes yod pa sngags bzla zhing sa bcag go'i mtha' can rnams so/  'di dkar

cing ma/ chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan par chos skyong gis rmi lam du bskul nas kha'u skyed lhas su mdzad pa'i bstod pa ha ha dgod pa ma/ shrI mAn bha dras rtsa sngags

srog mthu  'di phyi bram ze ltar sgrub pa'i man ngag yin nam snyam/ dgra bo'i srog gi bshan pa dmar po snying khrag thang la 'pho zhig sa ma ya na ra skan gyi mtha' can/

can/ 'gor tA ra na mo/ mgon po'i nor sgrub ni zhes yod pa'i gnyan mgon lha dgu'i sgrub (rdo rje)thabs thun mong ma yin pa snyan brgyud kun la ma grags pa'i snying nang

ba'i man ngag (ldong)(nyi)ltas kyi le'u 'o'i mtha' can/ mngal bsrung ba'i gdams (ldong)(nyi)pa dbang phyug dang padma la brten pa gnyan gyi u pa de sha'i mtha' can/
ma hA kA la'i sku gzugs (nyi࿊)la brten nas sri'u gso ba/ 'gor tA ra na mo/ zhal bzhi pa'i sgo nas srid med pa srid dang phrad pa 'di la gsum ste zhes yod pa'i srid med pa
'tshol ba lung skam chu 'bebs/ klung log bu mor 'ong bas srid pa lte ba bsgyur ba/ yod pa gso ba'i gdams pa rnams kyi yi ge bla ma gnyan gyis mdzad pa bka' rgya ma/ 'gor
tA ra na mo/ nag po chen po'i sgo nas chung sri zhes yod pa'i chung sri 'dul (nyi࿊)ba gnyan lo'i man ngag i thi'i mtha' can/  dkar chag na 'di gong ma'i khongs su bsdus
pa las zur du med/ zhal gdams snying gi dum bur grags pa'i nang tshan la

'gor tA ra na mo/ tsa turmu kha'i zhal gdams snying gi dum bu zhes yod pa'i spu gri so 'debs kyi gdams (ldong)pa rnal 'byor dbang phyug yar klungs pa'i zab chos gzhan la mi
ston pa'i bka' rgya dam po yod do'i mtha' can/ 'gor tA ra na mo/ tsa turmu kha'i rang srung gnad kyi 'khor lo zhes yod pa'i rang srung phra mo yid bzhin 'khor lo'i zhal
gdams gcig las mang ba la mi spel gsung ngo'i mtha' can/ 'gor na mo/ bla ma'i zhal nas spyir 'di la zhes yod pa'i rten gyi zhal gdams phyi nang gnyis ka la rtsub gsung ngo'i
mtha' can/ 'gor na maHgtor ma bzhi zhes yod pa'i gtor ma'i zhal gdams mtha' yas pa bya'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor bla ma dang ma hA kA la la na moHsnying dang 'dra ba'i slob
ma gcig ces yod pa'i sngags kyi zhal gdams sngags sgrigs sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ 'gor shrI ma hA kA la pu dze ta zhes yod pa'i sngags kyi zhal gdams rnam 'gyur 'di
tshe bag thung ba yin no'i mtha' can/  dkar chag na 'di gong gi khongs su bsdus pa las zur na mi gsal/ dgra bgegs bsad pa/ gzhan srung ba/ rang srung ba'i 'khor lo'i zhal
gdams rdo rje 'dzin pa shrI wAn ma tis bsam gling dgon par bris pa/ de'i zhar byung 'gor bla ma'i zhal nas bod rbad bsad gsum zhes yod pa'i rang srung gi yi ge man ngag
dngos su bkod pa'o'i mtha' can rnams so/  'di dkar chag na mi gsal ba gong ma'i khongs su bsdus sam snyam/ de yang dkar chag tu/ sngon chad gangs ri'i ljongs 'dir ma grags
pa/ /sngon gyi mkhas grub gnyan lo'i thugs bcud

'di/ /bdag gi 'dren mchog kun spangs chos rje las/ /gzhan na yod med gzu bo'i blos ltos shig/ 'di lta'i man ngag snying khrag zhun ma 'di/ /spel ba'i gnas med bse brag dmar
por sbos/ /cis kyang spel na snod ldan gcig nyid la/ /bka' rgyas thob la mgon po dpang du tshugs/ /zhes 'byung ba ltar sa bcad gsum pa'i skor 'di kha'u brag rdzong pa'i
brgyud 'dzin rnams las kun la ma grags pa'i zab cing gnyan pas snod dang ldan nges la chos skyong dpang du btsugs nas ston dgos pa'i tshul 'di snying gi dpal be'ur bcang
bar bya'o/ /zhar byung dpe ris kyi skor la/ gtum po rang srung gi 'khor lo rtsibs drug pa/ chung ba gri gug ma/  'og gi 'khor bsrung ba'i dpe ris kyang dbyibs 'di kha la
'dri tshul gyi khyad par cung zad yod/ rang srung phra mo yid bzhin 'khor lo'i dpe ris rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/  'di gsum gyi dbye ba zhal las shes dgos/ dkar chag na/ rang
srung 'khor lo che chung gsum gsungs pa'i chung ba shog dril nyer gcig gi 'khu ldog bsrung ba'i rang srung 'khor lo gri thod ma'am sku gsung thugs 'khor du grags pa/ 
zhal bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa'i rang srung yang zer/ gtum po'i sgo nas mi ma yin drag po srung ba'i 'khor lo/ 'khor srung ba'i gri gug can/ shog dril nyer gcig gi gsang ba
rang srog rten gyi 'khor lo rtsibs drug kha sbyor lus dang grib ma bzhin 'grogs pa/ yi ge rnying pa las byung ba'i bsad pa'i 'khor lo ling tshe nyi shu pa dang / bco lnga
pa/ dmar gyi bzhed pa gcig ling tshe rkyang pa bco lnga pa dang / nyi shu pa/ ling ga 'khor lo can/ ling ga ling tshe can 'khor

lo yod med gnyis/ chos rje sa paN la mgon po nyid kyis gdams pa'i ling tshe nyi shu pa dang bco lnga pa/ de'i bzhed pa'i rang srung 'khor lo ling tshe nyi shu pa dang bco lnga
pa/ de'i bzhed pa'i ling ga 'khor lo can gnyis/ de'i bzhed pa'i ling tshe rkyang pa gnyis/ de'i bzhed pa'i ling ga ling tshe can gnyis/ gzhan yang gong dang cung zad
mi 'dra ba'i ling tshe nyi shu pa gtor ma la 'dzugs rgyu'i 'khor lo rtsibs drug pa/ ling ga sngags bkod lugs mi 'dra ba gnyis dang sngags med gcig rdo nag maNDal mchod gtor
dang bcas pa'i shom/ phyag mtshan/ las khung / rdo zor/ rwa zor/ mda' zor/ thun khung / rlon thun/ sbyin sreg gi thab khung mi 'dra ba gnyis/ rdza'i an dha mu shal cha'i
an dha mu sha'abru nag gi sdig pa/ sgab 'dre 'brug mgo can gyi mnan 'khor mal 'og bsrung ba'i ngag mnan 'khor lo/ ma hA ba la/ de'i rgyab yig ling gargya gram/ glang dmar
gyi rwa/ tshe sgrub kyi bca' gzhi'i mchod rten/ nor sgrub kyi bum pa/ dbang sdud gri lagalam srung gi rde'u dang rdo rje rgya gram rtse mor phyag mtshan dang bcas pa/
shwa bzlog phur thod/ bya rog bskrad 'khor gyi 'khor lo ling ga dang / bya rog gi gzugs/ ma chun spre'u'i 'khor lo/ lha mo nag mo'i dpe/ mngal srung padma'i pho 'khor mo
'khor dbang phyug gi gzugs/ nA ga stobs 'phrog gi ling gsAtstsha/ bum pa/ rgya gram/ yang ling ga 'khor lo can lugs gcig klu sgrub rgya gzhung gi sham bu brgyad pa'i dkyil
'khor ling ga thun

snod dang bcas pa/ nam mkha'/ rgyang bu/ mda' 'phang / pho gdong mo gdong / ri rab gling bzhi/ gdugs sogs mdos kyi cha lag rnams dang / gzhan yang dpe ris rnying pa na med
pa'i mgon po che chung gi dam rdzas rgyan gyi gtor ma/ dpal gyi zhal zas/ dzambuu ti ba/ bshos bu dmar nagagur gyi bsnyen sgrub rjes gnang gi gtor dpe/ dud sol ma'i gtor
ma/ zhal gyi dam tshig bskang gso dang rtag gtor/ pu tra'i gtor ma/ beg tse'i gtor ma/ gzhi bdag gtor ma/ dmar chen gtor ma/ mgon po che chung gi gtor ma'i dar gur/ zangs
gri can gyi zor gtor/ zhal gyi gtor chen gyi dpe rnams rdo rje 'chang mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan gyi zhal bkod ma rnams so/ /gnyis pa dkar chag gis ma zin pa'i skor la/
phyi sgrub dang khyad par gyi man ngag la mkho ba'i skor/ gsang sgrub kyi skor/ phyi sgrub kyi snying por gyur pa zab pa las kyang ches zab pa'i snying thig ha la nag po'i
skor dang gsum/ dang po la/ 'gor gdong brnyan can la gtor ma 'bul na/ paM las padma raM las nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gyi steng du bzas pa bsgyel zhes yod pa'i glang ('bum)gdong
phyag drug pa'i gtor 'bul e ka dza TI hU~M phaT ces pa'o i thi'i mtha' can/ 'gor oM swa sti/ bla ma dang ma hA kA la la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'jigs pa'i tshogs rnams 'joms
mdzad pa/ /zhes sogs kyi mchod brjod shlau ka gnyis mdo stod pa 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i 'grel pa dri med don gsal ji lta ba la de nas slob dpon klu
sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i rgya

gzhung la dpang po byas zhes yod pa'i gdong ('bum)brnyan gyi bsnyen pa'i yi ge 'phags pa klu sgrub snying po'i rgya gzhung ltar bsnyen pa'i cho ga 'o'i mtha' can/ thams cad
mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtshos bskul nas tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i zhing skyong stobs 'phrog gdong bzhi pa las sbyor gyi mgon po gdong brnyan can 'khor mang
dang bcas pa la bstod cing (dbang)'phrin las gsol ba bdud dgra'i srog 'phrog dam nyams kyi tsitta dmar 'byin/ 'gor bla ma dam can srung ma'i tshogs la phyag 'tshal lo/
/shes bya kun la blo gros rab rgyas shing / /zhes yod pa'i gdong bzhi pa'i lo rgyus dkar chag bskyed chog mi 'dra ba'i khyad par mkha' 'gro 'khu ldog spong ba dang bcas
ston pa'i yi ge bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa mngon sum nyid du grub pa'i las mdzod cig gi mtha' can/  'di'i 'go'i mchod brjod la bdag chen
rje'i mtshan spel yod pa de rdo ring rin po che'i gsung yin pa 'dra zhes yig char snang ngo / /'gor rdo rje 'chang dbang rtsa ba'i bla ma dang zhes yod pa'i brgyud 'debs
(glang)kyi lo rgyus zung ldan gyi rgyan dang bcas pa bdud rtsi'i 'od can zhes bya ba rdo rje 'chang tshar pa blo gsal rgya mtshos kha'u brag rdzong nag por mdzad pa/ des
mdo khams pa dbon po dpal grub dang bsod nams mchog grub gnyis kyis bskul ba ltar na landar (ldong)mdzad pa'i rdo rje nag po chen po stobs 'phrog dbang po gdong bzhi pa
'khor bcas kyi rjes gnang dngos grub rgya mtsho/ bskul ba po dang mdzad po gong ltar gyi dpal stobs 'phrog dbang po

gdong bzhi pa sgrub (ta)dus kyi thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang chig brgyud gser chos kyi yig chung / sgrub dus kyi mgon po zhal khra can gyi rjes gnang gi khog phub bsnyen
dus sgrub dus thun mong ma yin la/ dkar po tshe 'phel thun mong ma yin pa/ dmar po dbang sdud/ ser po rgyas byed lha dgu/ sngon po bgegs 'joms dang bcas pa rnams kyi tho
yig (ngag )mun sel sgron me zhes bya ba thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa/ des rtse gdong phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba'i chos grwar mdzad pa'i dpal
mgon gdong brnyan ('bum)(ngag )can gyi rjes gnang go bde bklag chog tu bkod pa/ 'gor tA ra na mo/ 'di chig brgyud ma gtogs ye mi byed do zhes yod pa'i gnad dbab (A)kyi
mgon po nang gshin rje ltar sgrub pa'i mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi yi ge dkyus dang 'dra'o'i mtha' can tshar chen gyi gsung / de'i gsung 'gor tA ra na maHbram ze mngags pa'am
bran du gtad pa zhes yod pa'i bram ze nag po mngags gtad kyi rjes (braM)gnang 'chol bar spyad na dam tshig nyes pa chen por 'gyur/ de bas gsang zhing sba bar bya'o'i mtha'
can/ 'gor oM swa sti/ rdo nag po mi gcig gis theg mi theg cig ces yod pa'i sgrub dus kyi las khrigs gsal byed kyi yi ge rnying pa zhes spel ba ni man ngag dam pa'o'i
mtha' can/ dpal mgon gdong bzhi pa'i gtor ma zhi ba dam tshig bskang ba'i gtor skyong dang gtor ma'i las tsam gyis dgra bgegs 'dul ba'i tshe bya ba drag po gtor chen gyi
tshul lhan cig tu gsal bar ston pa'i cho ga gnam

lcags (rdo rje)'bar ba zhes bya ba mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug dpal rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ 'gor oM swa sti/ dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin thams
cad kyi gtsug rgyan zhes yod pa'i zhal bzhi pa'i dam tshig bskang gso/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje'i gsung (ku)rgyun phyag len ltar mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros
kyis zin bris su mdzad pa nag po chen po mche ba can sogs kyi bskul bya'i mtha' can/ 'gor a mr-i tas bsang / swa bhA was sbyangs zhes yod pa'i rdo rje nag po chen po stobs
'phrog dbang po'i gtor ma drag po'i cho ga (rdo rje)bsgrigs tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa gnod byed tshar bcad par bsam mo'i mtha' can/ dpal
mgon gdong bzhi pa'i gtor chen gyi (rdo rje)'chams yig thu btsun thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i gtor chen gyi rnga brdung bstan pa
ni zhes yod pa'i gtor chen 'chams (rdo rje)yig gi zhal shes mthar dgu brdung 'ba' zhig gis sdud do'i mtha' can/ dpal mgon khyung zhal can gyi rjes gnang (shI)gi yi ge las
sbyor gyi mgon por gtags gsung ngo'i mtha' can/ dpal mgon sengge nag po'i gtor chog (badzra)las dang po pa 'ga' dang rang gi rgyun gtor gyi phyir phun tshogs gling du
bris pa/ de'i rjes gnang 'gor (badzra)mkhyen brtse'i 'od zer stong 'phros pas zhes yod pa ga ga na dharma shrIs bris pa/ 'gor dpal mgon gdong bzhi pa'i srung (dbang)(sa)(glang)'khor
tshe sgrub ces yod pa'i yi ge

rin po che rta rwa ba'i gsung la rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis reg zig mdzad pa de tsam ma gtogs rgyun khyer ji lta bas khrid mdzad kyi 'dug go'i mtha' can/ sa
skya khri chen ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad pa'i srung (mus)'khor tshe sgrub kyi yi ge bdud rtsi 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu/ gnyis pa gsung gi mgon po dmar po'i nyams
len snyan brgyud zab mo'i bdud rtsi rnal 'byor (ldong)(dbang)(sa)(glang)dbang phyug yar klungs pas mdzad pa chos bdag zhing skyong mkha' 'gror gtad pa'i mtha' can/ des
mdzad pa'i rgyas pa gtso 'khor dgu'i khrid gzhan la med pa'i khyad chos bla ma dam pa'i bka' (ldong)(dbang)(sa)(glang)dang bshes gnyen dam pa 'ga'i ngor bkod pa chos bdag
zhing skyong mkha' 'gror gtad pa'i mtha' can/ des mdzad pa'i gsum pa rgyas pa'i las sgrub na yon tan gyi mgon po ser po lha lnga'i nyams len brgyud pa bzang (ldong)(dbang)(sa)(glang)sa
skya pa'i snyan brgyud zab mo'i gdams pa chos bdag zhing skyong mkha' 'gror gtad pa'i mtha' can/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa'i bla rdo bca'
ba'i thabs (ldong)man ngag gis rnam par brgyan pa/ des mdzad pa'i chu bo ganggA yang gyen la nges par ldog nus pa'i shwa bzlog gi man ngag rje btsun kun spangs (ldong)(sa)(glang)chen
po'i gsung gi nying khu 'gro don dpag yas sa steng khyab par shog gi mtha' can/ bla ma gser gling pa'i man ngag rgya gar khrag 'thung nag po la zhus pa srog
me khab (sa)ma gser srang

bdun ma'i yon can yar klungs pa'i phyag dpe las bshus pa/ dpal mgon gdong bzhi pa'i thebs bzlog brtsi ba'i man ngag (sa)rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis mdzad pa/
'gor na ma tsa turmu kha/ 'gab chad dang gzhogs drud dang zhes yod pa'i dpal 'bar gyi me bkra brtag pa kha'u pas gnang ba'i mtha' can/ 'gor skyabs med skyob pa rnams la phyag
'tshal lo/ /sgrub pa'i khang pa dben pa ru/ /zhes yod pa'i me bkra dang du ba brtag pa zhal las shes par bya'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor tA ra na mo/ me bkra 'di la bzang po'i
rtags bzhi zhes yod pa'i me bkra brtag pa mngon shes su 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ dpal 'bar (dbang)bkra rtags/ ba len bkra (dbang)rtags rnams so/ /gnyis pa gsang sgrub kyi
skor la/ dpal ma hA kA la zhal bzhi pa'i gsang sgrub kyi rnam gzhag gsal bar byed pa snying gi yang thig ces (sa)(glang)bya ba rdo rje 'chang tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtshos
kha'u brag rdzong nag po'i ru 'dren gyi pho brang sum cu rtsa gsum du mdzad pa/ des mdo khams pa lcags sgom chos rje'i gsung ji lta ba bzhin (glang)mdzad pa'i 'gor bla
ma mchog dang yi dam lha zhes yod pa'i gsang ba thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi tho/ des mdzad pa'i zhing skyong gdong bzhi pa'i gsang khrid kyi sngon 'gro rnam pa
bzhi'i khrid nyams len gyi snying po dril ba yin no'i mtha' can/ lcags sgom chos rje'i gsung bzhin des dam pa'i gsung ngor bris (glang)pa'i zhing skyong dbang po'i gsang
khrid kyi skabs su 'khor lo bzhi la brten pa'i

las sbyor gyi gdams pa snyan brgyud ma/ gong gi 'phros 'gor gsum pa tsitta dharma tsakra zhes yod pa'i ches zab (glang)(sa)yang gsang snying ga chos kyi 'khor lo'i las sbyor
gyi yi ge rtags myur du 'byung ba ni nges pa'o'i mtha' can/ 'gor gsum pa las sbyor la thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa zhes yod pa'i snying ga (glang)(sa)chos kyi 'khor
lo'i las sbyor snyan brgyud zhal shes kho na yin gyi mtha' can/ bsnyen sgrub las gsum (glang)gyi phyi ma'i yang yig 'gor lha mo nag mo'i gdams pa ni rang nyid sgrub pa'i
dus kyi mgon po zhes yod pa'i las sbyor spogs chog gi dus su nye bar mkho ba'i lha mo nag mo'i gnad 'bebs shog dril gyi gnad 'bebs las khyad par du gyur pa'i zab khyad
can tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung rgyun gzhan du ma 'khyar ba mdzod ces bka' bsgo yod do'i mtha' can/ zab chos 'di nyid 'chad pa la med du mi rung ba'i snying nang
gi khrag lta bu'i khrid yig (glang)rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis zin bris su mdzad pa/ 'di nyid mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug dgon gsar ba bsod nams chos 'phel
gyi bka' drin la brten pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis/ mjug tu/ rgyal ba kun dngos khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / /rigs brgya'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i zlos gar gyis/ /deng 'dir skye dgu'i
don slad bshes gnyen sku/ /pha rgod sku drin dbang po dgon gsar ba/ /mgon de'i gsung gi gsang ba mi zad pa/ /zab rgyas snyan brgyud bdud rtsi'i rgya mtsho las/ /dad
gus snyim pa'i bcud kyis bsdus pa 'di/ /skal bzang snying la grub pa'i dga' ston

spel/ /zhes pa'ang snang ngo / /'gor bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpa' zhes yod pa'i gsang khrid kyi zin bris (zha)mkhan chen zhwa lu pa rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams
mchog sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i yig chung ltar gsung gin 'dug go'i mtha' can rnams so/ /gsum pa phyi sgrub kun gyi snying por gyur pa zab pa las kyang ches zab pa'i snying
thig ha la nag po'i skor ni/ phyi bram ze ltar sgrub pa/ nang zhing skyong gzi ldan dbang phyug gi sgrub pa/ gsang ba stobs 'phrog nag por sgrub pa gsum las phyi ma ste/
gong gi phyi sgrub dang khyad par gyi man ngag rnams su gab sbas thor bu bzhugs pas shes rlom can dag man ngag gi khog sgrig mi shes pas dpe mthong bas phyogs tsam yang
mi rtogs pa'i phyir snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa zab mo dang ldan pa'i rdo rje slob dpon gyi gsung rgyun zhal shes phyag khrid kho na la bltos dgos pas/ rje btsun kun spangs
rdo ring pa chen po yan chad du yi ge gsal bar bkod pa med 'dug na'ang / snyigs ma lnga ches cher bdo zhing bdud rigs snying la zhugs pa'i skye bo mi srun pa dag gis rnam
par 'tshe ba bsrung ba la ji skad du/ 'phags pa'i yul dang gangs ri'i ljongs 'di na/ /bstan pa srung ba'i chos skyong bgrang yas kyang / /khro zhing 'khrug la gnyan zhing
myur ba ni/ /yongs su grags pa stobs 'phrog dbang po yin/ /zhes ches khyad par du 'phags pa'i gdams skor rnams med du mi rung ba lta bu yin na'ang / kwa ye da ni lang
tsho mthon por song / /kha ba'i khrod na 'di 'dra shes pa med/ /ga le spel kyang

nub par gyur dogs nas/ /nga yis 'di ni yi ge ra gsal bar bris/ /zhes bstan pa rin po che'i btsas su 'khrugs bsdebs su mdzad pa shin tu rno ba reg thabs med pa lta bu nas/ de
ltar 'di ni srog 'phrog ha la'i dug/ bstan dgra'i klad 'gems gshin rje'i dbyug pa ste/ /rnal 'byor sgos dgra'i snying 'byin bshan pa che/ /gang la'ang thogs med gnam lcags
'bar ba'i mtshon/ /sa skya'i rje btsun thugs kyi gces pa'i nor/ /kun spangs chos rje'i zhal gyi bdud rtsi'i bcud/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa bsrung ba'i mtshon cha'i mchog
/ rnal 'byor g.yul las rgyal ba'i dpa' bo'i chas/ /zhes dga' rab dbang phyug sde dang bcas pa las rnam par rgyal ba'i go mtshon yin la/ de yang dgos pa'i gtso bo/ gang 'di
thub bstan 'jig la thug pa'am/ /rnal 'byor kha zhan skyabs dang bral gyur nas/ /kha drag dpung gis bsdigs shing gnod pa'i tshe/ /mtshon 'di phyung la sdig can chos dbyings
skyol/ /zhes bstan pa'i spyi dgra dang rnal 'byor byang chub sgrub pa'i sgos dgra bsgral ba la dgongs nas mdzad pa yin pa las/ de la ma yig dang bu yig gnyis/ dang po
ni/ dpal mgon zhing skyong nag po chen po dgra bo'i stobs 'phrog gdong bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs thun mong ma yin pa gsang ba las kyang ches gsang snying thig ha la nag po'i
be bum zhes bya ba/ 'di nyid kyi lung gnang ba'i dus mgon po'i bris 'bur gyi sku byin rlabs can gyi drung du mchod gtor dang bcas te spyir las 'bras la 'dzem zhing bstan
pa rin po che gces spras dang / khyad par dpal ldan sa skya pa'i

bstan pa dri ma med pa spyi dang / yang sgos gsang chen slob bshad pa'i ring lugs la gces par 'dzin zhing / snod ldan la chig brgyud las mang por mi spel ba sogs mgon po dpang
du btsugs pa'i dam bsgrag cing / 'chol bar spyod pa rnams gnod sbyin beg tse lcam dral gyis snying khrag 'thung ba'i bka' rgya shin tu dam pa/ dus der chos kyi yon la
gser srang gang ngam yang na de ri ba'i dngos po 'bul ba sogs kyi phyag len deng sang gi bar du'ang ma nub par yod pas dpe tsam mthong bas nyams su len pa/ rku thabs su
byed pa/ sa skya pa'i bstan pa spyi sger la gces par 'dzin pa lta zhogaganod pa lhur len bzhin du tshul 'di don du gnyer ba rnams ni sa bon mes tshig pa la so nam 'bad pa
lhur len pa dang / btsan dug la rjen zas byed pa dang mtshungs pas bag yod par bya ba ni gnad dam pa'o/ /gnyis pa bu yig ni/ gong gi ma yig gi be'u bum mi'i lus kyi phyi'i
dbyibs lta bu la stod smad bar gsum gyi zab gnad don snod dang dbang po lta bu rnams logs su gab pa yin la/ de'i rgyu mtshan ni/ tshe 'di'i 'dod pa phra mo tsam gyi phyir/
/drag po'i las sbyor byung rgyal rtsom byed cing / /chos la brten nas sdig chen gsog pa yi/ /blun po zhe sdang can de'ang 'di'i snod min/ /sdig can mi dpon stobs ldan
khyim nang du/ /las sbyor drag pos lto gos 'tshol byed cing / /las 'bras rgyab bskyur mthu stobs chen por rlom/ /dmyal ba'i bud shing chos 'di'i snod ma yin/ /zhes pa'i
gang zag gi lag tu son tshe spre'u la sgron me bskur ba

bzhin thams cad phung la sbyor ba'i dgag bya dang dgos pa la dgongs pa yin pas bu yig gi skor la/ mA ri'i 1lag len de 'khor gsal byed dang / 2/ mal srung bzlog 3zab tsakra'i
bri 4yig bcas/ /gta' ru srog 5bzung kha sbyor de'i gsal 6byed/ /yid bzhin 7'khor lo lo tsA'i sgros rnying gi/ tsakra 8(glang)mkha' 9mig (glang)mda' gzugs 10(glang)ling
tshe rnying / /'khor 11(glang)can ling can 12sngags (glang)can 13rkyang (glang)gzugs 14(glang)bzhi/ /paNDu ra yi mkhas pa'i bzhed tshul 15gcig (glang)/ tsaNDa'i tsakra 16de
yi lag 17len bcas/ /rdo rje gri gug 18dngos sku'i bsrung 19ba dang / /mi min 20rakShi ta dwang ba 21liM gzungs/ /spu gri so 'debs 22mantra lugs 23ldog dang / /ral gri
rtags can las bshus rnam dag 24sngags/ /nyi zla can 25dang de wI kA 26li ma/ /mnan 27pa dur rdo mantra'i 28ri mo can/ /bri yig lag 29len (glang)(sa)gsal phyed zhal 30shes
(glang)(sa)dang / /drag 31gtad (glang)(sa)gzugs 32bsnun (glang)(sa)rten 33brab (glang)(sa)spre'u 34(glang)(sa)dang / /gcun 35(glang)(sa)'khor ka 36pA (glang)(sa)la dang
gnad 'khor 37(glang)(sa)lo/ /gnad dbab shi sa'i tshod 38'dzin 'tshams sbyor 39(glang)(sa)dang / /'jam mgon sa skya'i chos kyi khrir bzhugs pa'i/ /ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams grags pa yis/ /khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan zhabs brtan nas/ /yab chos gsan tshe 'di dang gsang sgrub zung / /dkar 40(sa)chag zhing skyong dgyes pa'i mchod

rdzas kyis/ /mtha' rten kho bo'i snying dbus bum par bltams/ /zhes grangs tsam 'god pa las gsal bar mi 'dri ba ni/ 'di ni lho bal gser gyis gnongs pa ltar/ /yod ces mi smra
shin tu gsang zhing sba/ /sbas kyang shes na khyi dang glo ba ni/ /phrad ltar mi bya rim gyis brtags byas te/ /skal bzang snod dang ldan pa'i bu mchog la/ /chig brgyud kho
nar byin la rgyas gdab bya/ /zhes pa'i don snying gi dpal be'ur bcang dgos pas zhib cha mtha' dag yid la ri mor 'dri ba dang / gal te brjed ngas kyis 'jigs na tho gsal
po bris nas gud du bcang ba las tho yig yongs grags su'ang rgyas par mi 'dri ba phyag len no/ /de ltar chos skor rnams yongs su rdzogs par nos pa las/ thog mar thar rtse
paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge ltar bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang rkyang pa ngor lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / 'phags mchog klu
sgrub zhabs/ grub chen ba linta pa/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal bde ba'i zhabs/ bi ma la gupta/ ratna badzra/ ratna kIrti/ ri sul gyi
rnal 'byor ma/ gnyen lo tsA ba dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ grub chen brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ thams cad mkhyen
pa bsod

nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ de sras shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan dang grub chen buddha shrI gnyis kas rjes su bzung ba/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga'
bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug kun mkhyen bsod nams sengge/ 'dren mchog ratna wardha/ rgyal ba lha mchog sengge/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas sengge/ paN chen
nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ gzar chen pa/ rje dam chos bsam 'grub/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ drin chen
rdo rje 'chang bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos
skyong / des bdag la lan mang du stsal to/ /yang na shug rwa ba grub mchog he ru ka dpal kun dga' dpal 'byor/ de pa'i gsan yul gyi bla ma shug ra gong ma kun dga' rgyal
mtshan yin nam gang yin ma nges/ de nyid las bdag bande tshul rin gyis so/ /yang na byams pa bsod nams bzang po las thob pa'i gsan yul gyi bla ma slar rnyed na bri dgos/
yang na ngor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab kun dbang man 'dra/ yang na 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel nas/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/
sa lo tsA ba/ sangs rgyas sengge man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal
mtshan/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal

mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba/ 'jam dbyangs ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ paN chen man 'dra/ yang
na rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ byas 'gyur ba bsod nams sengge/ bla ma rdo rje sengge/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen man 'dra/
yang na sa lo/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ gzar chen man 'dra/ yang na paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ zhabs drung
nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rgyal rtse ba ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs man 'dra/ yang na sa lo nas/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga'
rin chen/ de sras sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ de sras sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ rgyal rtse pa man 'dra/ yang na zhabs drung
a mi lags/ de sras bdag chen bsod nams dbang phyug zhabs drung rgyal rtse pa man 'dra'o/ /yang bsnyen  tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa'i pho nya myur mgyogs dang rjes gnang gi
yi ge'i steng nas/ dus kyi mgon po'i rjes gnang dang / ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma nas brgyud pa'i sa bcad dang phyi sgrub skor dang / sa bcad gsum pa snying nang gi khrag
lta bu khyad par gyi man ngag rnams las shog dril dang po'i gsal byed rje btsun rdo ring pa chen pos mdzad pa ma gtogs pa yongs rdzogs dkar chag gis ma zin pa'i sa bcad
dang po'i ldong g.yung drung lhan

cig pa'i rtags can/ rtags gang yang med pa'i lung rnams dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa klu sgrub/ ba linta pa/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/
mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal bde ba'i zhabs/ dri med sbas pa/ rin chen grags pa/ rin chen rdo rje/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ gnyan lo tsA dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u pa dar
ma rgyal mtshan/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che dpal ldan bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon sa
skya paNDi ta/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa chen po/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun dga'
rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ rje btsun kun spangs rdo ring pa/ rdo rje 'chang tshar chen
blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mthu stobs dbang phyug bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod
nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong bstan pa'i rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /rjes gnang ni dngos grub rgya mtsho la sogs pa ltar/ sgrub dus kyi rjes gnang / dkar chag gi
sa bcad dang po yongs rdzogs/ gsum

pa'i nang gi ldong gi rtags can/ dkar chag gis ma zin pa'i sa bcad dang po'i ldong g.yung drung can dang bcas pa'i lung gi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ grub chen brag phug pa yan
gong gi bsnyen dus dang 'dra ba las/ de nas/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams
rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun rdo ring pa kun spangs chen po/ thams cad mkhyen pa blo gsal rgya
mtsho/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mthu stobs dbang phyug bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab
byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang
na rmor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang kun dga' rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o/ /'di dag la spyir rjes gnang so so'i brgyud pa
ni/ rang gi rtsa ba'i bla ma'i bar tha dad du bkod pa ji lta ba bzhin yin la/ lung gi brgyud pa rnams ni dang po rtags so so ba ltar brgyud pa kho na yin yang / phyis su
glegs bam phyogs gcig tu bsdebs zin pa tshun chad nas lung gi brgyud pa tha dad bgrang du med par bsdoms nas glegs bam dang be'u bum gyi lung thob yul gang yin ltar rgyun
chags su sbrel shes

dgos so/ /yang rjes gnang dang sa bcad dang po'i lung brgyud lugs gcig ni/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan nas/ bdag chen zhwa lu pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ paN chen shAkya
mchog ldan/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po man 'dra/ e'i rtags can gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ bla ma dam pa nas/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/
ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gzhi thog pa bdag chen kun dga' dbang phyug bdag chen rdo rje 'chang man gong ltar ro/ /yang rjes gnang dang sgo rtags can
gyi lung brgyud ni/ rje btsun rdo ring pa yan gong ltar las/ de nas rje btsun sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra'o/ /rdo rje
rkyang pa'i rtags yod pa'i lung brgyud ni/ 'phags pa rin po che nas/ bla chen rong pa/ bla ma shes rab sengge/ bla ma bsod nams lhun grub/ bla ma ngag gi dbang phyug bla
ma dpal ldan legs dbang / brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rje rdo rje gdan pa/ thugs sras klu dbang gling pa/ rig 'dzin tshe dbang bkra shis/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos
rje man 'dra'o/ /rdo rje g.yung drung gi rtags can gyi lung brgyud lugs gcig ni/ gnyan lo nas gshongs ma'i sngags ban ga rod/ rtogs ldan 'tsho dkar ba/  'dis dgung lo phyed
nyis brgya tsam bzhugs sku tshe'i stod la sngags ban dang mjal sku tshe'i smad la spyan snga dang mjal zhes rdo rje gdan pa dang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig
na snang / thel spyan snga bsod nams grags pa/ rin po che tshal min pa/ rje sengge dpal ba/ pha brag thog pa man 'dra/ 'di skor la

brgyud tshul zur pa 'di 'dra zhig kyang mchis na'ang / de rgyu mtshan du byas nas rje btsun gong ma nas ma brgyud par 'dod pa ni log rtog go zhes rgyal dbang lnga pa chen pos
gsungs/ rdo rje dga' 'khyil bcas pa'i rtags can gyi lung brgyud lugs gcig ni/ kha'u pa nas/ slob dpon go cha/ dam pa de skyes/ gru rdo rje sengge/ bcom ldan ral gri/ skyi
ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/ jo nang kun mkhyen chen po/ nya dbon kun dga' dpal/ rje lung rig pa/ mkhan chen sengge dpal ba/ brag thog pa man 'dra/ glo'i rtags yod do
cog gi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo ring pa chen po/ rje grol mchog mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra/ ku'i rtags can gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po nas/
gnyan ston sprul ba'i zlos gar rdo rje 'chang gzhon nu blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen zhwa lu pa/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo
rje 'chang kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' ba mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug bstan pa'i snang byed mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin
chen la stsal to/ /dbang gi rtags can gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen zhwa lu pa man 'dra'o/ /ngag gi rtags
can gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ rje dbang rab yan gong ltar las/ de nas mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras bsod nams dbang
phyug khyab bdag mkhan chen zhwa lu

pa/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /mus kyi rtags can gyi brgyud pa ni/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/
mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams man 'dra'o/ /nyi g.yung drung bcas pa'i rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal
mchog nas/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa/ rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal/ yangs pa can pa shAkya kun dga'/ dam chos gling pa ye shes dbang
po/ bla ma badzra ma ti/ nyi ma gling pa tshul khrims bkra shis/ de gnyis ka las paN chen kun bzang rtse pas gsan/ de las zhwa lu mkhan chen/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/
rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang ba chen po dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul rin la'o/ /shin
tu zab pa'i gdams pa dkar chag gis ma zin pa'i sa bcad gsum pa snying thig ha la nag po ma yig bu yig rtags med rnams kyi lung man ngag phyag khrid dang bcas pa thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po nas/ drung yig byams pa don grub/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ ngag dbang
rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ rmor chen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ skyor mda' ba bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong
/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang

na rmor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po nas/ grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang kun dga' rgya mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na/ mgon
po bsod nams/ rin chen rgya mtsho/ bka' bcu rnam rgyal/ rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub man gong bzhin no/ /rjes gnang bsnyen dus dang / sgrub dus khe rkyang gi brgyud pa
ni/ rje sa paN nas/ nub pa rigs 'dzin grags/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ gu ru dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bag ston
gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma rdo rje sengge/ mkhan chen bka' bcu pa/ chos rje paNDi ta/ rtses dang dge 'phel ba bsod nams blo gros/ rje rdo ring pa/ de las rje btsun sgo
rum pa dang tshar chen gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses gsan pa man sngar ltar ro/ /yang na zhang dkon mchog dpal nas/ dgon pa ba bsod nams 'bum/
bag ston gzhon tshul man 'dra/ yang na chos rje bla ma dam pa nas/ bdag chen kun dga' rin chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ bdag po bla ma/ chos rje paNDi ta man 'dra/ yang
na bla ma dam pa nas/ gung thang pa sengge dpal ldan 'od mdzes bzang po/ bla ma paNDi ta man 'dra/ yang na gzhi thog pa kun dga' rin chen nas/ gzhi thog pa blo gros rgyal
mtshan/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ grwa thang ba shes rab zla ba'i dbang po/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na bdag chen zhwa lu pa nas/
chos rje rgyal mtshan

dpal bzang / byas 'gyur ba bsod nams sengge/ rje rdo ring pa man 'dra/ yang na chos rje bla ma dam pa yan gong ltar las/ de nas ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ de gnyis ka las
chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ byas 'gyur ba bsod nams sengge man 'dra/
yang na ngor chen las/ rje bsod nams dbang phyug rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug rje bsod nams sangs rgyas/ mkhas grub gung ru shes rab bzang po bzhi kas gsan/ de bzhi
ka las rje btsun rdo ring chen pos gsan pa man 'dra/ yang na rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje nas/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug yab sras gnyis ka las mkhan chen
bslab gsum rgyal mtshan dang / sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel gnyis kyis gsan/ yab sras de bzhi char las rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyis gsan pa man 'dra'o/
/sgrub dus kyi mgon po'i rjes gnang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa dang / ta thA ga ta rakShi ta nas brgyud pa'i sgrub skor dang / dkar chag gis ma zin pa'i sa bcad
dang po'i ta'i rtags can gyi lung dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa klu sgrub/ ba linta pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad/ dpal bde ba/ bi

pa gnyis sngags 'chang

bsod nams chos 'phel bzhugs pa dang 'dra'o/ /sgrub dus kyi mgon po'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud lugs gcig ni/ 'phags pa rin po che/ brgyud lugs 'di lo pa spyan
snga'i der yod par grags/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ chos rje bla ma dam pa man 'dra/ yang na bla ma dam pa nas gzhi thog bdag chen kun dga' rin
chen/ gzhi thog pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rig pa'i dbang phyug dge ba rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med grwa thang pa shes rab zla ba/ rje btsun rdo ring pa man 'dra'o/ /yang sgrub
dus kyi mgon po'i rjes gnang thun mong ba'i brgyud lugs gcig ni/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan nas/ mkhan chen zhwa lu pa chen po man 'dra'o/ /yang na tshar chen
nas/ rje btsun bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ skyed tshal mkhan chen thar pa bzang po/ zhwa lu pa chen po man 'dra'o/
/sgrub dus dam can rgya mtshos bskor ba'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa rin po che nas/ tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ rje brag phug
pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ gzhi thog pa kun dga' rin chen/ bdag chen grags pa blo gros/ mkhan chen sengge dpal ba/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rje kun dga' rnam rgyal/

mkhan chen man 'dra'o/ /tshar chen gyis mdzad

pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge bka' rgya ma la brten nas mthong brgyud kyi phyag bzhes dbri bsnan dang bcas pa'i sgo nas las sbyor gyi mgon po gdong brnyan can gyi rjes gnang gi
