grags pa/ ma hA paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa/ gnyan lo tsA ba/ gnam kha'u pa/ dpal sa skya'i rje btsun gong ma lnga/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ grub chen brag phug pa/ chos
rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rgyal mchog bdag chen 'jam dbyangs chos rje nam
mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun rdo ring pa kun spangs chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ bod mkhar ba mai
tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ zhwa lu pa chen po man 'dra'o/ /yang na 'phags pa rin po che yan
gong ltar las/ de nas lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan sengge/ chos rje dharma kIrti/ chos rje blo bzang pa/ nya dbon kun dga' dpal/ bla ma lung rigs rgya mtsho/
mkhan chen sengge dpal/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ mthu chen 'jigs med dpa' bo/ mus chen rnam rgyal dpal bzang / thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ 'bras spungs pa tshe
dbang bkra shis/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje man

gong bzhin no/ /yang na kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa nas/  'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na 'khor zhal gyi rjes gnang zhes logs su bgrangs 'dug pa gdong brnyan can las
zur pa med kyang lo mchog pa yod pa'i brgyud pa'i skabs gdong brnyan can dang las bzhi lhan du bgrangs pa'i dbang gis so sor phye bar snang ngo / / mdo khams pa yon tan
rgya mtsho/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis man 'dra/ yang na sa paN nas/ tshogs sgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ na bza' pa/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa/ gzhi thog pa kun dga' rin
chen/ gcung grags pa blo gros/ mkhan chen sengge dpal man 'dra/ yang na bdag po kun rin pa nas/ bdag chen blo gros pa/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ rje zla ba shes rab/
rdo ring pa man 'dra/ yang rje rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig ltar na/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ gnyan lo tsA ba man 'dra/ 'di nye brgyud yin pa 'dra zhing
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig gi tshar lugs nas brgyud pa'i skabs ring brgyud dang gong dkar ba lugs kyi gsan yig skabs gsan yig rgya mtsho sor bzhag bgrangs 'dug
pa rgyas bsdus su mngon/ paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa nas brgyud pa'i chos skor dang dkar chag gis ma zin pa'i 'bum gyi rtags yod pa'i lung brgyud ni/ tshar chen yan zhal
ngo nang brgyud dang yar klungs pa nas brgyud pa rta rwa ba bzhugs pa nas/ mkhyen brtse'i zhabs/ rta rwa ba/ rje dbang rab man 'dra/ dngos grub rgya mtsho dang gsang ba
thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge gsung rgyun phyag len ltar nang zhing skyong ltar sgrub pa'am gsang

sgrub kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa rin po che yan bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang tshar lugs ltar las/ de nas dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ chos rje
bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba/ chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub dge ba rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sangs rgyas mchog pa/
mtshungs med skyes mchog rgyal mtshan/ mdo khams pa lcags mo bkra shis sengge/  'dis stan thog gcig tu zhal gyi sngags thung 'bum phrag brgya song zhing zhal dngos su gzigs
pa yin no/ /rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen
rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des
bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la gsang khrid kyi sngon du 'gro bar stsal to/ /yang na rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub yan gong ltar las/ de nas skyor mda' ba bsod nams
dbang phyug mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag la'o/ /phyi nang gi srung 'khor 'chi med sgrub pa zhar byung
bzlog pa dang bcas pa'i phyi'i nyams khrid dang / gsang khrid kyi nyams khrid zab mo smin rgyas su thob pa/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma nas brgyud pa'i sa bcad gnyis pa'i
skor/ dkar chag gis ma zin pa'i sa bcad gnyis pa'i rtags gang yang med pa rnams kyi lung rnams dang

bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan yan bshad ma thag pa'i gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang ltar las/ de nas khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba chen po/ de gnyis ka
nas rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab bla ma byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen du bod pa la'o/ /gsang khrid yig rnying dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa lugs gcig la/ chos rje bla ma dam pa nas/ yar klungs pa sengge
rgyal mtshan/ g.yag phrug bstan pa'i nyi ma sangs rgyas dpal/ rong ston shes bya kun rig rig pa'i dbang phyug dge ba rgyal mtshan 'dra'o/ /yang srung 'khor tshe sgrub
kyi khrid kyi brgyud pa ni/ lcags mo bkra shis sengge nas/ khams ston bsod nams don grub/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje man 'dra'o/ /glang gi rtags can yod do cog gi
lung gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan nas/ glang bu chos rje 'jam dbyangs chos skyong dbang phyug mkhan chen zhwa lu pa man 'dra'o/ /sa'i rtags yod pa'i
lung gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan nas/ sa skya pa 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen zhwa lu pa man 'dra'o/
/byang chub ma thob kyi bar du chos skyong snying dbus su mi 'bral ba'i nyams khrid zab mo thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan yan gong ltar
las/ de nas glang bu chos rje 'jam dbyangs chos

skyong dbang phyug mkhan chen zhwa lu pa man 'dra'o/ /las bzhi'i rjes gnang la 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i yi ge ltar ram ngag chos pa'i yi ge ltar/ dkar po tshe 'phel gyi
tshe dbang thun mong ma yin pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan yan bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang zhal ngo nang brgyud ltar las/ de nas rnal 'byor dbang phyug
yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ kun spangs
chen po rdo ring pa/ rdo rje 'chang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ rje bod mkhar ba chen po/ spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/
mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ drin chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims
rin chen la'o/ /yang na rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa nas/ mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims
rin chen la'o/ /yang na tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po nas/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug 'dren mchog snying rje bzang po/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/
mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /dkar chag na bzhugs pa'i las bzhi'i mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi yig chung
dngos grub rgya mtsho'am mkhan chen ngag chos kyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi

ge'i steng nas/ dkar po tshe 'phel thun mong ba/ ser po rgyas byed lha dgu/ dmar po dbang sdud/ sngon po bgegs 'joms rnams kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa yan bsnyen
dus kyi rjes gnang tshar lugs ltar las/ de nas lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan sengge/ chos rje dharma kIrti/ chos rje lam 'bras pa blo bzang / nya dbon kun dga'
dpal/ bla ma lung rigs rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen sengge dpal/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ mus chen rnam rgyal 'di mi bzhugs pa'ang
byung / dpal bzang / klu dbang gling pa kun dga' rgyal po/ rje tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho/ rje mai tri   bod mkhar ba/ pa don
grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga chos rgya mtsho/ grub mchog dbang phyug rab brtan/ zhwa lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje
'chang kun dga' lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na dbang phyug rab brtan yan gong ltar las/ de
nas mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ byams pa bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ skyor mda' ba 'phags pa chos kyi rgyal
mtshan/ mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na 'phags pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan nas/ mkhas mchog bkra shis dbang
phyug rdo rje 'chang ba chen po

bkra shis bzang po/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen gyis mnos so/ /yang dkar po tshe 'phel thun mong ba dang ser po rgyas byed lha lnga'i rjes gnang gi brgyud lugs
gcig ni/ rdo rje 'chang dbang rab nas/ glang bu chos rje/ khyab bdag mkhan chen zhwa lu pa/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' lhun grub/ des
bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na rmor chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ mkhas btsun bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen rigs brgya'i
mgon po dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /nor sgrub ser po lha dgu'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ma hA de wa/ paNDi
ta shrI singha/ A tsArYa gnyan chen dpal dbyangs/ rgya gar kA ma rU pa/ gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags/ glang ban ga rod/ rtogs ldan 'tsho dkar ba/ spyan snga bsod nams grags
pa/ rje bsod nams bzang po/ mkhan chen sengge dpal/ grwa thang pa shes rab zla ba/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ grub mchog sbyin pa rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang blo gsal
rgya mtsho/ rje btsun bod mkhar ba/ spyan snga mi pham chos rgya mtsho/ khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen zhwa lu pa/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/
rmor chen rdo rje 'chang man 'dra'o/ /yang na tshar pa rdo rje 'chang nas/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma rnam rgyal bkra shis/ dpal 'byor gling pa dbang
phyug rgyal mtshan/ kun bzang rtse pa dpal ldan tshul khrims/ mkhan chen zhwa lu pa man

'dra'o/ /gdong brnyan can gyi rjes gnang ni bsnyen dus dang 'dra'o/ /yig cha dngos gzhi dang tshar pa rje'i zin tho ltar gnad dbab kyi mgon po'am spogs chog gi mgon po nang
gshin rje ltar sgrub pa'i rjes gnang dang A rtags can gyi lung brgyud ni/ chos rje bla ma dam pa yan bsnyen dus kyi mgon po'i rjes gnang gi zhal ngo nang brgyud ltar las/
de nas gzhi thog pa bdag chen kun dga' rin chen/ gzhi thog pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ grwa thang pa shes rab zla ba/ rje btsun rdo ring pa/
tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ lo pa spyan snga kun dga' don
grub/ lcags zam pa chen po kun dga' bsod nams dbang phyug khyab bdag zhwa lu pa chen po/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang
kun dga' lhun grub/ rigs kun khyab bdag chen po rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul rin la'o/ /'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i zin tho la brten nas/
dpal mgon khyung zhal can nam dmag dpon mgon por grags pa'i rjes gnang 'bum phrag gsum pa nas brgyud pa'i zhar byung du khyung zhal can gser gyi spu gri'i skor dang /
dkar chag gis ma zin pa'i shI rtags can gyi lung dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ma hA de wa/ paNDi ta shI la singha/ A tsArYa gnyan chen dpal dbyangs/ rgya
gar kA ma rU pa/ gnyan lo dar

ma grags/ glang ban ga rod/ rtogs ldan 'tsho dkar ba/ spyan snga bsod nams grags pa/ gnyags phu ba bsod nams bzang po/ sengge dpal ba/ rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med
shes rab zla ba/ rje btsun rdo ring pa kun spangs chen po/ grub mchog sbyin pa rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje man bsnyen dus kyi zhal ngo nang brgyud bzhin
no/ /tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zin tho la brten nas mgon po che chung sogs slob bshad gdams pa phal cher rdzogs mthar bstan pa gtad pa'i tshul gyis bram ze nag
po'i mngag gtad kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni 'phags pa rin po che lan bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang ltar las/ de nas  brgyud lugs 'di lo pa spyan snga'i gsan yig ltar byas/
dam pa kun dga' grags/ bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bdag chen kun rin pa/ gzhi thog pa blo gros pa/ rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ rje shes rab zla
ba/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang / 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse/ sngags 'chang dgon gsar ba chen po/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ zhwa lu
pa mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhas btsun chen
po bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyi zin
bris kyi steng nas rgya gar kA ma rU pa nas brgyud pa'i dpal mgon bram nag bshan pa drug

skor nag po dom mchong gi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags mchog klu sgrub/ dzo ki kA ma rU pa/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ 'jam skya nam mkha' dpal ldan/
bla ma grong mo che ba/ rje btsun red mda' ba/  rje re te zla ba zer ba'ang 'dug grub chen thang stong rgyal po/ ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje
gdan pa/ 'jigs med dpa' bo/ rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog bstan 'dzin ngag dbang nyi zla bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/
mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ byams pa bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ 'phags pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ skyor
mda' ba bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na 'phags pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ mkhas mchog bkra shis dbang phyug
gsan pa 'di nas yin nam brtag mkhas btsun bla ma kun dga' rgya mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /smras pa/ dran pas yid srubs dpung tshogs mthar byed
pa'i/ /zhing skyong dregs pa'i sde dpon yum bzhir bcas/ /rtsa brgyud bla ma'i g.yar dam ma g.yel bar/ /byang chub bar du mi 'bral stong grogs mdzod/ /ces dam pa'i chos thos
pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ stobs 'phrog nag po gdong bzhi pa'i chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste nyer lnga pa'o/ // /gnyan lo tsA
ba dar ma grags kyis rgya

gar 'phags pa'i yul nas bstan srung brgya rtsa tsam gdan drangs pa'i nang nas/ gtso bor gyur pa stobs 'phrog nag po gdong bzhi pa'i bka' sdod bshan pa dmar nag gnyis su grags
pa'i nang nas/ mthu rtsal mchog tu che ba las mkhan dmar po gnod sbyin beg tse lcam dral gyi skor la/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas lcam
sring 'khor mang gi rjes su gnang ba dang / mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas lcam sring gnyis kyi rjes su gnang ba'i bka' srol gnyis
smin rgyas su legs par nos nas/ rgyab brten lung la/ bka' ma'i skor dang gter ma'i skor te gnyis/ dang po la spyi bye brag gnyis/ dang po yongs grags spyi'i chos skor la/
yid ches pa lo rgyus/ nus ldan du bya ba rjes gnang / khungs btsun pa rgyud/ nyams su blang ba sgrub skor/ gong 'og tu nye bar mkho ba gtor mdos bskang ba/ gzungs dang thugs
chen gzugs pa/ bstod bskul/ las tshogs dang brgyad/ dang po la/ gnod sbyin bshan pa lcam sring gi chos skor byung tshul bla ma rnams kyi gsung sgros ltar gnyags kyi
bandes yi ge ra bkod pa/ 'gor bla ma rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /srog gi bshan pa mi reng dmar po zhes yod pa'i brgyud pa'i lo rgyus man ngag la yi ge gcig kyang khyad mi
'dug go'i mtha' can/ 'gor bcom ldan 'das dpal gshin rje gshed la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bshan pa sgrol byed srog bdag dmar po'i lo rgyus ni zhes yod pa'i bshan pa lcam dral gyi
skyes rgyud rgya bod du dar tshul gdams ngag gnyan gyi lugs che

bar gda' 'o'i mtha' can rnams so/ /gnyis pa nus ldan du bya ba rjes gnang la/ 'gor na mo gu ru padma rta mchog dpal la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa bsrung ba'i phyir
zhes yod pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge kun mkhyen dpal ldan sengge'i gsung sgros mjug tu bla ma brgyud pa bkod pa/ 'gor ha ya grI wa la na mo/ beg tse lcam dral gyi gtor dbang
ni zhes yod pa'i sku gsung thugs kyi rjes gnang gi yig rnying gtor dbang yig chung i thi'i mtha' can/ gnod sbyin dregs pa lcam dral gyi rjes gnang gi yi ge kun mkhyen
dpal ldan sengge'i tho yig las cung zad gsal bar rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa phrin las thams cad myur du sgrub par mdzad du gsol gyi mtha' can rnams so/
/gsum pa khungs btsun pa rgyud la/ dmar po khrag gi mda' 'phen ma'i man sngags bshan pa dmar mo'i rgyud le'u drug pa dmar mo 'jig rten za byed ma'i rgyud rdzogs byang gi
mtha' can rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI dha ra kra shu dang bod kyi lo tsA ba mar pas bod yul dbus kyi grwa thang gi gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba/ srog bdag dmar po'i drag sngags
bshan pa sgrol byed kyi rgyud le'u lnga pa shrI dha ra kra shu dang mar pas grwa thang du bsgyur ba'o/ /bzhi pa nyams su blang ba sgrub skor la/ 'gor rgya skad dang
dmar mo khrag gi mda' 'phen ma'i ngan sngags bshan pa dmar mo'i sgrub thabs srid pa gsum gyi yum e ka dza TI la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dur khrod dam chu 'gram mam zhes yod pa
A tsArYa nyi ma grags kyis mdzad pa shrI dha ra kra shus bsgyur ba/ pho'i sgrub pa 'gor

rgya gar skad du dang srog bdag dmar po'i drag sngags bshan pa sgrol byed kyi sgrub thabs dpal gshin rje'i gshed la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dur khrod chu 'gram brag dmar ram zhes
pa A tsArYa nyi ma grags pas mdzad pa shrI dha ra kra shu dang mar pas bsgyur ba/ drag las thams cad pho mo'i sgrub pa 'di gnyis la thug go/ 'gor gnod sbyin 'di ni skyes
bu dbang gi mdog can zhes kyang bya zhes yod pa'i bshan pa dmar po'i sgrub thabs dgra bo dngos su sgrol bar 'gyur gyi mtha' can A tsArYa nyi ma grags kyis mdzad pa shrI
dha ra kra shus bsgyur ba/ 'di'i mjug tu rgya gar bam so dmar po nas nyi 'od grags pas bton tshul dang dgra la mig bltas pa tsam gyis shi ba byung ba'i lo rgyus kyang yod
do/ /dmar po khrag gi mda' 'phen ma dang bshan pa dmar mo'i ngan sngags yab yum sbags te sgrub pa  gnas gsar gyi phyag dper nga yi nor gyi rting la rgyug man 'dri 'phro
lus 'dug A tsArYa nyi ma grags kyis mdzad pa rdzogs byang gi mtha' can shrI dha ra kra shu dang mar pas grwa thang du bsgyur ba/ srog bdag dmar po bshan pa gri thogs kyi
sgrub thabs mu stegs slob dpon rdo rje grags pas mang yul byams sprin mgon po'i thugs kar sbas nas bstan pa'i don du smon lam btab pa gnam lcags thog dmar/ pho rkyang du
sgrub pa gnod sbyin ra zhon yam shud dmar po'i sger sgrub gnyan los mdzad pa bdag gi bran bzhin khol bar shog yam shud srog gi sgrub pa rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ 'gor bcom ldan
'das 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed la phyag 'tshal lo/ /srog bdag dmar po bshan pa gri thogs sgrub par 'dod pas

gnas ni ri gsum 'dus pa'am zhes yod pa'i sgrub thabs mjug tu bstan pa bsrung ba'i las 'di myur du sgrubs kyi mtha' can mang du thos pa'i btsun pa sengge 'bum gyis dpal brag
ram gyi gtsug lag khang du sbyar ba/ 'gor rgya gar skad du dang dur khrod dam brag dmar po'i rtsar bsgrub te zhes yod pa'i gnod sbyin lcam sring gi sgrub thabs drag po gnad
bskul dang bcas pa kun mkhyen dpal ldan sengge mdzad pa dgra bgegs ma lus tshar gcod par shog gi mtha' can/ gnod sbyin beg gdong lcam sring 'khor mang gi sgrub thabs
tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtshos lcags pho 'brug gi lo nag pa zla ba'i yar tshes la sbyar ba'o'i mtha' can/ des mdzad pa'i chos skyong lcam sring gi mngon rtogs mjug tu rkyen
ngan bar chad thams cad zhi ba dang / ci 'dod dngos grub ma lus stsal du gsol zhes yod pa rnams so/ /lnga pa gong 'og tu nye bar mkho ba gtor mdos bskang ba la/ 'gor
chos skyong beg tse can gyi gtor ma gtong bar 'dod pas zhes yod pa'i rta mgrin gyi thugs ka nas lha mo dang de'i smin mtshams nas beg tse spro ba'i gtor chog yig rnying bcol
pa'i phrin las sgrub par mdzod kyi mtha' can/ 'dar phya ru ba rin chen dpal bzang gis brag ram chos grwar mdzad pa'i bskang ba ra dmar khrag chang ma/ mus srad pa rdo
rje rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i bskang ba lha mchog sgrol ging ma/ a mo ghas mdzad pa'i bskang ba dus gsum rgyal ba ma/ gtor chog bsdus pa tshar chen gyi gsung rgyun mthun
rkyen thams cad sgrubs kyi mtha' can/ de'i gsung rgyun gyi

bskang rdzas byin rlabs/ lcang sbe ba sengge 'bum gyis mdzad pa'i bskang ba byang shar dbang ldan ma/ bshags pa bde chen chos sku ma/ buddha bha dras bstod pa'i gnod sbyin
zangs kyi beg tse ma/ buddha warNas mdzad pa'i bstab pa dbang ldan ma ru ma rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i bskang bshags rgyun khyer rol mo drag tu bya'o'i mtha' can/
gnod sbyin lcam dral gyi thugs dam bskang ba'i cho ga rgyas pa byang shar mya ngam ma shar mdo khams pa rdo rje bkra shis kyi ngor rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad
pa/ rje de nyid kyis A tsArYa nyi 'od grags dang gnyan lo sogs gong ma rnams kyi yi ge 'thor ba phyogs gcig tu bsdebs te mdzad pa'i gnod sbyin lcam dral gyi las byang phrin
las lhun grub ma/ gtor mdos la brten nas srog bdag dmar po bshan pa sgrol byed bcos pa'i thabs phyogs phyogs ma gnyan lo tsA bas mdzad pa srog bdag dmar po'i bskang mdos
rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ gnod sbyin bshan pa lcam dral gyi gtor bzlog bos so chos skyong ma dpal ldan 'dar phya ru pa rin chen bzang pos dpal brag ram gyi gtsug lag khang
du mdzad pa rnams so/ /drug pa gzungs dang thugs chen gzugs pa la/ gnod sbyin beg tse lcam  zung 'dzugs dang thugs gso 'di gnyis glegs bam rnams su ma bzhugs pas lung
ma thob/ dral 'khor bcas kyi phyi rten gzugs pa'i lag len gyi rim pa gnyags kyi bande bi dza ya bha dras dpal nyan po'i gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa/ srung ma'i dbang po beg
gdong lcam dral gyi thugs gso ba'i cho ga sbyor dngos rjes gsum gyi sgo nas bstan pa byang shar dbang ldan mar

grags pa/ 'dar gyi bande rig 'dzin rdo rjes sbyar ba/ gnod sbyin beg tse lcam dral gyi phyi rten zung 'dzugs pa'i lag len gyi cho ga 'dod don lhun grub ces bya ba mkhan chen
sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa dang bcas pa'o/ /bdun pa bstod bskul la/ lcang spe ba sengge 'bum gyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa rig pa'i lha mo ma/ kun mkhyen dpal ldan
sengges mus srad dgon par sbyar ba'i bstod pa gang gi thugs rje ma/ rigs 'dzin rtogs ldan blo gros bzang pos bskul ba'i ngor gtsang byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis mus
srad gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa'i bstod bskul gnas mchog rgya gar ma/ gnyags kyi bande rnam rgyal bzang pos bstod pa'i ha ha dgod pa ma/ rgyud las phyung ba'i bskul gnod
sbyin zangs kyi beg tse ma dang rig pa'i lha mo ma/ gnyan los mdzad pa'i skor la/ rgya gar yul gyi dam sri ma/ 'jam dpal thugs kyi pho nya ma/ e ka dza TI ma/ las mkhan
srog bdag ma/ gri thogs brgyad/ bshan pa nyer gcig bka' 'khor spyi/ lha chen brgyad/ klu chen brgyad/ gza' chen brgyad/ rgyu skar nyer brgyad dang bcas pa rnams kyi bskul
gnyan los bsgrigs pa/ gnad nas bskul ba ma hA de wa ma rnams so/ /brgyad pa las tshogs la thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa gnyis/ dang po la/ dam tshig pa  'di be bum
du ngos zin pa zhig med pas lung ma byung ba 'dra snyam ste brtag go/ bskyed bstim/ bsnyen pa/ rtags/ las sbyor/ shi sa/ smyo 'bogaltas ngan/ gcun thabs rnams kyi snying
po'i man ngag A tsArYa nyi ma grags

kyis mdzad pa shrI dha ra kra shus bsgyur ba dam nyams lag tu ma btang zhig gi mtha' can/ 'gor rgya skad dang dmar po khrag gi mda' 'phen ma'i 'khor lo'i man ngag gnad kyis
bsad pa bstan/ e ka dza TI la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rgyud dang mthun pa'i gnas zhes dang 'byung ba rlung la brten nas bskor ba 'khor los smyo 'bog lceb par 'gyur gyi mtha' can/
'di lag tu blangs nas dregs ldan cham la phab pa'i nyams myong yang cung zad bdoga'agor bstan pa bsrung ba'i lha la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sngags dang rdzas dang ting nge
'dzin dang zhes yod pa'i bsad pa'i las sbyor dha ra kra shu'i ngan sngags zhal nas gsungs pa'i bka' rgya ma/ ling ga ming byang 'dri ba'i rdzas dang smyu gu'i ngos 'dzin/
'gor dgra bo lha dang dbye ba la spyir dgra la lha lnga zhes yod pa'i lha dbye'i man ngag lhun bzang bdag la gnang ba lags so'i mtha' can/ 'gor oM AHhU~M yod pa'i sngags
bsnal dkrug bzlog pa sogs kyi zab gnad bsad pa'i sngags i thi'i mtha' can rnams so/ /gnyis pa thun mong ma yin pa la/ phyi nang gsang ba'i bla rdo'i man ngag gnyan lo'i
chig brgyud ma/ bshan pa dmar po'i gsang rten bca' thabs ra ban chos dpal bzang po'i brjed byang / 'gor rang yi dam du gsal ba zhes yod pa'i bzlas pa'i gnad mtho bar byas
nas yab rbad do'i mtha' can/ gnod sbyin lcam dral gyi bsnyen sgrub las gsum lag tu blang ba'i rim pa ha la nag po dug gi spu gri zhes bya ba dbang lung thob pa'i snod ldan
re gnyis la chig brgyud ma gtogs mang por spel na bshan pa dmar po la zas su gtad

pa'i bzhes sgra dang bka' rgya shin tu dam pa rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rjes mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i sgrol gying dmar po'i gnad kyi gdams pa nang gi rnal 'byor la brten
nas bsnyen sgrub las gsum myur du 'grub pa'i zab gnad can rgya mtsho'i nang gi nor bu dang srog bral lto ba'i gser bzhin sba ba'i chig brgyud ma ming tsam yang brjod par
bka' ba'i gdams pa/ yab yum srog 'khor/ sgrub pa'i 'khor lo kha sbyor/ rlung 'khor gyi dpe ris dang bcas pa rnams phyag len dmar khrid nyams su myong bar nos so/ /gnyis
pa bye brag gi skor la/ gnod sbyin dmar po zhal gsum phyag drug par brten pa'i gsang sgrub bka' rgya ma snying khrag thang la pho zhig gi mtha' can/ gnod sbyin gdug pa'i
las sbyor la brten nas dgra la khyi dmag drang ba bai ro tsa nas paNDi ta dha tsaNDa la gser srang gang phul nas zhus pa/ dgra la bya dmag gtong ba sa la sba'o'i mtha' can/
wa thod las kyi rlung dmar la brten nas sngags pa nag po bsgral ba'i gdams pa mantra i thi'i mtha' can rnams so/ /gnyis pa gter ma'i skor la/ gnubs lugs dang nyang lugs
gnyis/ dang po la/ bshan pa dgu skor gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po padmas bsam yas dbu rtse'i ke'u tshang du gter du sbas pa gnubs sangs rgyas ye shes kyis spyan drangs
pa la/ rgyal po gser gyi shugs can dang btsun mo utpa la'i rgyan gnyis kyi sras su gcen grags ldan dang gcung grags skyes gnyis 'khrungs pa'i lo rgyus/ 'gor khrag gis
dmar rjib gtang zhes yod pa'i srog bdag yam shud dmar

po spu gri reg chod ces bya ba yam shud btsan gyi cog brdung bshan pa dgu skor gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon padmas mdzad pa/ slob dpon padmas dur khrod phung lung nag por srog
bdag yam shud dmar po'i srog phrogs nas mdzad pa'i bshan pa dgu skor gyi sgrub thabs ngan sngags kyi rgya bsdebs zhes bya ba/ bsad pa srog las kyi rkyal bu nas phyung ba
ngan sngags kyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ wa thod kyi thun snod la brten pa'i srog bdag yam shud dmar po'i thun gyi sgrub pa/ sngags pa nag po bsgral ba'i man ngag
wa thod las kyi rlung dmar bsad pa'i mantra i thi'i mtha' can/ bya 'ug khra srin bzhi'i sgro sgron pa'i srog bdag yam shud kyi mda' zor/ rdzas la brten nas smyo ba/ mdze/
skrangs 'bur/ bsrung ba/ mtshon srung / las mi byed par 'khu na srog bdag dmar po gzir zhing gcun pa/ mde kha rnam drug ces pa gri srog la brten nas smyo ba/ nal thod
la brten nas bsad pa/ rims thod la brten nas nad rims/ smyo 'bog gi thod par brten nas 'od/ mon thod la brten nas ltas ngan/ phur par brten nas cho 'phrul rnams gtang ba'o/
/'gor srog bdag bshan pa zhes yod pa'i dmod kha brgyad pa i thi'i mtha' can/ 'gor srog bdag chen po'i dus la babs zhes yod pa'i bla 'gugs pho nya'i skabs gtso 'khor
rnams kyi bskul byang bskul zhing rbad do rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ chos skyong dregs pa lcam sring gi bsnyen sgrub bsad pa gcig tu dril ba'i gdams pa 'jigs rung me'i spu gri
zhes bya ba paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa rnams

so/ /gnyis pa nyang lugs skor ni/ drag po btsan gyi rkyal 'bud slob dpon chen pos mnga' bdag la gdams pa spa gro skyer chu dang ru lag grom pa rgyang gnyis su rgod dang / g.yung
mang yul du sbas shing rgod gcig mchims phur sbas pa mnga' bdag nyang gis spyan drangs pa la/ bshan pa srog gcod dmar po'i srog mthu drag po btsan gyi rkyal 'bud bsnyen
sgrub rbad bskul la ma bltos pa'i ngan sngags chig chod ma yid la yang dran du mi rung ngo'i mtha' can/ gsang bskul dur khrod chen po ma phrin las gong ma rnams las
thos pa yi ge ra bkod pa'o'i mtha' can/ bshan pa srog gcod dmar po'i srog mthu'i zhal shes bsad thabs rnam pa lngas bstan pa las 'phro can dang 'phrad shog gi mtha' can/
drag po btsan gyi rkyal 'bud kyi zhal shes yig chung sgrub pa'i zhag grangs spogs pa kha bsgyur rnams bstan pa gsang ba'i zhal shes snying ltar chongs/ las can la 'phrad
shog gi mtha' can/ drag po btsan gyi rkyal 'bud kyi yang yig rgya gar gyi ngan sngags bsad pa'i spu gri ldang ba dgra'i gshed ma bla srog rku ba'i man ngag ma gter nas phyung
ba i thi'i mtha' can dang bcas pa rnams legs par thob cing ngag dbang chos grags pa'i yi ge ltar lcam sring gnyis kyi rjes gnang dang bka' ma phal cher gyi lung man
ngag dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ma hA de ba/ A tsArYa nyi 'od grags pa/ sras zla ba nag po/ paNDi ta gha ya dha ra/  shrI dha ra kra shu'ang zer/ 'di lam
'bras pa'i gha ya dha ra ni min no/ /gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u

pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ ra sa'i shod bu bkra shis 'od zer/ sa bcu'i dbang phyug grub thob 'dar phya ru ba rin chen bzang
po/ chos rgyal bo dong brtson 'grus rdo rje/ jo sras sangs rgyas rin chen/ slob dpon shes rab 'tsho/ bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug lcang spe ba sengge 'bum/ kun mkhyen dpal
ldan sengge bzang po/ chos rje rin chen bkra shis/ rtogs ldan yon tan mgon po/ bla ma gzhon nu dpal ba/ gtsang byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rgyud gsum smra ba shes rab
rin chen/ rdo rje 'chang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug sngags 'chang dgon gsar ba bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhas grub ngag dbang chos
grags/ mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ chos kyi rje ye shes phrin las/ rje btsun
bsod nams chos 'byor/ de las kun dga' chos 'phel yin nam/ de nas mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la shin tu dgyes
bzhin legs par stsal to/ /yang na mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal nas/ byams pa bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ grub dbang bsod nams chos 'byor/
de las dbang bla kun dga' bstan 'dzin nam bkra shis dbang phyug gang rung zhig las/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang pas gsan nam blta/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin
chen gyis so/ /yang

tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i gtor chog dang mkhyen brtse'i tho yig la brten nas 'khor mang gi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po yang
gong ltar las/ de nas 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ mkhan chen ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ byams
pa bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ 'phags pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ skyor mda' ba bsod nams dbang phyug drin chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan chos skyong
/ des bdag la rjes su gnang bas be bum yongs rdzogs kyi lung dang bcas pa stsal to/ /yang na mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan nas/ grub dbang bsod nams chos 'byor/ de
las mkhas mchog bkra shis dbang phyug gis gsan/ de las rje btsun nam mkha' dpal bzang gis gsan/ de las bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen bdag gis 'khor mang gi rjes gnang
be bum gyi lung du bcas pa mnos so/ /rmor chen rdo rje 'chang gi gsan yig tu thugs sras blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas lcam sring gnyis kyi rjes
su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan yan gong ltar las/ de nas mnyam med dkon mchog dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ thugs
sras blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub byams pa bzang po/ sprul sku shAkya rgyal mtshan/ byams pa rin chen chos 'phel/ drin chen rdo rje 'chang padma phrin las/ des bdag
ngag dbang kun

dga' lhun grub la'o zhes 'byung ngo / /yang beg tse lcam dral 'khor mang gi rjes su gnang ba'i brgyud lugs gcig la/ bo dong brtson 'grus rdo rje nas/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan
pa/ mkhan chen chos rgyal dpal bzang / mus srad pa dpal ldan sengge man 'dra'o/ /yang na mus srad pa dpal ldan sengge nas/ gnyags phu ba bsod nams bzang po/ rtogs ldan
yon tan mgon po man 'dra/ yang na kun mkhyen dpal ldan sengge nas/ dpal ldan ratna kIrti/ gu ru dug gsum nad sel/ mtshungs med rin chen bkra shis man 'dra/ yang na rtogs
ldan yon tan mgon po nas/ ston pa chos dpal ba/ dam pa sengge/ be phug pa bde legs rgyal mtshan/ glo bo 'dzar pa chos rgyal bsod nams/ de sras chos skyong bsod nams/ 'jam
dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra'o/ /lung dang gdams skor gyi brgyud pa lugs gcig ni/ rtogs ldan yon tan mgon po nas/ bla chen chos dpal bzang po/ mus srad
pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ mus chen rnam rgyal dpal bzang / 'khrul zhig dkon mchog bzang po/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen po man 'dra'o/ /gnubs lugs gter ma'i lung brgyud
ni/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku padma dbang chen/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ gnubs chen sangs rgyas ye shes/ gnubs pa mtshur ston/ gnubs ston phug pa 'bar/
de nas rim par sngags 'chang sangs rgyas 'phel dang / tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po brgyud par bzhugs pa ltar ro/ /nyang gter gyi brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon chen po

nas/ mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal/ mnga' bdag khri srong lde'u btsan/ lha sras mu tig btsan po/ nyang nyi ma 'od zer nas rim par brgyud de/ tshar chen rdo rje 'chang man
'dra'o/ /nye brgyud ni slob dpon chen po padmas/ grub thob 'dar phyar la dbang dang gdams pa gnang ba yin no/ /'on kyang da dung 'dir dpyad par bya ba rjes gnang gnyis ka'i
brgyud pa'i smad so sor gyes tshul dang / be'u bum gyi lung brgyud kyi smad kyang rjes gnang dang phyogs 'grigs su yod med cung zad brtag par bya'o/ /smras pa/ rnam 'dren
bka' srung bye ba'i 'khor lo sgyur/ /rnam gnyis mgon po 'khor bcas sgrub pa'i skor/ /bla chen mkhyen pa'i drang srong ltor 'khyil ba'i/ /gser chos dag byed skyugs rgyun
de tsam btung / /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las/ gser chos gdong bzhi pa'i bka' sdod las mkhan dmar po gnod sbyin beg tse
lcam dral gyi chos skor thos pa'i brgyud rim gyi sarga ste nyer drug pa'o/ /!/ /yar lung pa'i yi ge dang rje sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi zin bris
kyi steng nas bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa'i bka' srung dpal dur khrod bdag po yab yum gyi rjes gnang legs par nos nas/ rgyab brten lung la/ dpal dur khrod
bdag po'i rgyud gsang ba snying gi 'khor lo le'u brgyad pa paNDi ta bai ro tsa na rakShi ta las brgyud cing 'dzim lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ dur khrod bdag po'i sgrub thabs bai
ro tsa nas mdzad pa/ 'gor he ru ka la phyag

'tshal dang / gang dang rnal 'byor pa rnams kyis/ /zhes yod pa'i sgrub thabs tshigs bcad ma/ mjug tu shin tu gsang nas bsgrubs na yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'byung ngo /
/dpal dur khrod bdag po'i sgrub thabs rdzogs byang dang / bla ma bai ro'i man ngag thun mong ma yin pa'o shin tu zab bo rgyud las phyung nas mdzad pa 'dzim lo'i 'gyur/ yang
jag pa srung ba'i thabs zab mo 'gor rgya skad bod skad dang / srung ba'i lha la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rang gi sngon dang zhes yod pa tshigs bcad ma/ 'di la the tshom spang
ba'o'i mtha' can 'dzim los bsgyur ba/ de'i 'grel pa sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa/ 'gor phyag 'tshal dang / dpal ldan dur khrod bdag po yi/ /gdams pa gzhung dang mi 'gal
ba zhes yod pa/ bdag gzhan bsrung ba'i bsnyen pa/ sgrub pa/ las la sbyar ba rnams kyi lag len gsal bar bkod pa/ 'di la mos shing sgrub pa rnams/ /bar chad med par dngos
grub kun/ /ci 'dod pa ni grub nas su/ /phyag rgya chen po thob par shog/ dpal dur khrod bdag po'i man ngag lag len sa mApta'i mtha' can/ las tshogs dum bu la 'gor yul du
rims nad byung ba la zhes dang des ni mi phyugs nad rnams khegs kyi mtha' can/ bsnyen pa dang sgrub pa'i yig chung / tsakra'i rab gnas/ bsrung ba'i man ngag rnams kyi yig
chung re/ des mdzad pa'i bsnyen sgrub las sbyor gyi man ngag 'gor/ dam tshig ldan pa'i gang zag gis zhes dang / mjug tu las sbyor ni las tshogs so so'i skabs bzhin shes
par bya'o'i mtha' can/ sku rten sba ba'i man ngag kun

gyi gtsug gi nor bur 'gyur ro/ /'di ni rten gyi man ngag go'i mtha' can/ yang sku'i mdun du mchod gtor 'bul ba'i man ngag des dga' mgur 'du ba yin no'i mtha' can/ yang yab
yum gyi sku sba ba'i man ngag rten gyi man ngag logs su bkol ba'o'i mtha' can/ bstod bskul dpal ldan dur khrod bdag po ni zhes dang bstod cing bskul ba rdzogs so'i mtha'
can/ rdzas dang sngags la brten nas smyo ba 'dul ba gzhan zhig 'drir bcug pas kyang 'grub bo'i mtha' can/ de'i las sbyor dam nyams bsgral ba'i las tshogs drag po'i las so'i
mtha' can/ yang dur khrod bdag po yab yum gyi rjes gnang bya ba'i tshul dpal sa skya pa chen pos g.yu mkhar mo sgrol ma lha khang du bris so'i mtha' can/ yar klungs pas
mdzad pa'i mchod gtor 'gor/ 'dir rje btsun sa skya pa nas brgyud pa'i dpal dur khrod bdag po'i bsnyen pa/ mchod gtor bsdus pa bya ba'i tshul ni/ bla ma mtshan nyid dang
ldan pas zhes pa nas/ chom rkun bsrung ba'i mjug tu gzhan las tshogs mang po mchis pa rnams bla ma bai ro tsa na dang bla ma sa skya pa chen po'i gsung rab las shes par
bya'o'i mtha' can/ rjes gnang gtor chog gi yi ge yar klungs pa sengge rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ gzhan yang sa los mdzad pa'i yab yum gyi gtor chog sngags 'chang chen pos
mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge dang bskang ba rnams kyi lung bcas thob pa las/ rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ grub chen padma badzra/
rA hu la badzra/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje/ dznyA na

siddhi/ dpal dam tshig rdo rje/ 'chi med blo gros bzang po/ mkhas pa bai ro tsa na/ khams rgwa lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod
nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bla chen yar sgom se bo/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin can sengge bzang po/  bar
'dir rnal 'byor dbang phyug yar lung pa sengge rgyal mtshan zhes gsan yig 'ga' zhig tu byung / bla ma bsod nams rgyal mchog 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen
rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo tsA ba kun dga' bsod nams/ bla ma dpal ldan bkra shis/ sngags
'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen/ sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ chos rje bsod nams
rab rgyas/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rdo rje 'dzin dbang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/
mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ 'jam mgon bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na rje
sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ sa lo tsA ba/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ shes rab 'byung gnas/ bsod nams rgya mtsho man 'dra'o/
/rje sangs rgyas

rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas thob cing lung yang mnos so/ /yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ lha mchog sengge/ buddha singha/ brang ti paN chen/ snying rje
bzang po/ ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgya mtsho man 'dra/ bai ro tsa na dang sa skya pa chen po dang yar lung pa rnams kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge rnams
kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang yan rjes gnang dang 'dra la/ de nas rje btsun rdo ring pa/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel/ mkhan chen dbang phyug rab brtan/ sngags 'chang thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de nas brgyud dam bla
ma gnyis tsam btsal dgos/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs bkra shis dbang phyug dbang bla kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal bzang / des bdag
tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na bla ma gnyis tsam btsal dgos pa nas/ chos kyi rje bkra shis dpal ldan/ mkhas btsun kun dga' bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun
tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /chos rgyal dbang po'i sdes mdzad pa'i dur khrod bdag
po'i sgrub skor mang du mchis pa rnams kyi lung ni ma thos so/ /!/ /paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i yi ge bklag pas don grub kyi steng nas dpal 'khor lo bde
mchog gi

thugs las sprul pa'i bstan srung chen po rdo rje nag po chen po phyag bzhi pa lha mangs phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang /
ye shes kyi mgon po/ slob dpon chen po 'phags pa klu sgrub/ ArYa de wa/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dus zhabs pa/ rtswa mi sangs rgyas grags/  mi nyag rtswa shing gi rgyal rig
sa/ dpal chen rgwa lo tsA ba/ bde gshegs phag mo grub pa/ 'bri khung 'jig rten mgon po/ skyid shod pa bkra shis 'bum/ skyid shod pa grags pa sengge/ slob dpon sangs rgyas
gzhon nu/ lo tsA ba ma Ni ka shrI/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub
legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa lo tsA ba 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ gnyan lo grags pa blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas sengge/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rje
nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rje dam chos bsam 'grub/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs bral bla ma bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa bkra shis lhun
grub grags pa'i rgyal mtshan/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na ma Ni ka shrI nas/ sprul sku nam mkha' rgyal po/ mkhas btsun nam
mkha' rtse mo/ gu ge paN chen man 'dra/ yang na ArYa de wa nas/ a bha yA ka ra/ rtswa mi sangs rgyas grags man 'dra'o/ /'di mgon po rang gi rgyud nas bshad pa'i lha mangs
mtshan nyid dang ldan pa las sngags gsar rnying gi mgon po

yin no cog bsdus pa ni min no/ /!/ /mgon po gsang ba mngon par 'byung ba'i rgyud le'u lnga bcu pa las/ zhal gsum phyag drug pa lha mo bzhi'i 'khor dang bcas pa zur tsam bstan
pa dang / rtsod dus kyi kun mkhyen gnyis pa bu ston rjes som nyir mdzad kyang phyag bzhi drug gi bla ma brgyud pa phal cher gyis tshad ldan du mdzad pa/ mgon po gsang
ba dngos grub 'byung ba'i rgyud kyi le'u bcu bzhi par/ mgon po kun gyi gnas 'di ni/ /zhal gcig pa la phyag drug pa/ /dang po gri gug thod khrag 'dzin/ /spyan gsum mthing
nag rngam pa yi/ /g.yas g.yon bar pa phreng ba dang / /DA ma ru ni 'dzin cing brdung / /tha ma gnyis kyis kha TwAM ga/ sdigs mdzub zhags pas 'ching bar mdzad/ /ces sogs gsal
bar bstan cing / rgya bod kyi paN grub dang lo tsA ba mkhas grub rnams kyis legs par bkral ba'i ye shes mgon po phyag drug pa'i chos skor la/ mkhas grub khyung po gdub
bu pas ko sa li bikSha'i dur khrod du rje btsun mai tri pa chen po la gser srang bdun phul nas zhus pa'i chos skyong ba'i srung ma 'di nyid kyi rjes su gnang ba'i skor
dang / mkhas grub khyung po 'phan yul 'jog po'i ri la sgrub pa mdzad pa'i tshe grub chen rA hu las chos sgo skyel gyi tshul gnang ba'i rjes gnang gi skor rnams bsdoms pas
mgon po bcu gsum du grags pa/ skyid shod sprul sku ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phrin las kyis mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas legs par thob pa la/ gtor dbang bar gcod kun sel/
rjes gnang bar gcod kun sel/ dbang bzhi

byin rlabs kyi tshul tu bskur ba/ bla ma mgon po dbyer med kyi skor la zhi ba grib sel/ rgyas pa bla ma mgon po dbyer med/ mkha' 'gro dbang sdud dang gnas dbab gcig tu byas
pa/ gsang sgrub mgon po mchin kha/ nang sgrub rgyan can/ mgon po dbang rgyal/ mgon po tshe bdags ra ha'i mgon po khrag 'thung / lha bzhi dril sgrub/ mgon dkar yid bzhin
nor bu ste bka' bcu gsum du grags pa/ de'i khongs su mi the ba tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos mdzad pa'i rjes gnang bya tshul la brten nas mgon po phyag drug pa snying
zhugs kyi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa phyag mtshan chas gos sindhU ra rnams kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi
yi ge'i steng nas bar chad kun sel gyi rjes gnang dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba shangs pa'i phyag len gtsang ma thob pa las/ thog mar gtor dbang bar gcod
kun sel/ rjes gnang bar gcod kun sel/ dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba/ bla ma mgon po dbyer med kyi skor la zhi ba/ rgyas pa/ mkha' 'gro dbang sdud dang gnad
dbab gnyis gcig tu byas pa/ gsang sgrub mgon po mchin kha/ mgon po dbang rgyal/ mgon po snying zhugs thun mong ba rnams kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo
rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mgon po/ grub chen sha ba ri dbang phyug mnga' bdag mai tri pa chen po/ grub chen rA hu la/ shangs pa lo tsA ba khyung po rnal 'byor/ rmog cog
pa rin chen brtson 'grus/ dbon ston skyer sgang pa chos kyi

sengge/ gnyen ston sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/ chos rje sangs rgyas ston pa/ mkhas grub shangs ston chen po/ mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / sngags 'chang rdo rje gzhon nu/ mnyam
med nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang / mtshungs med bzang po rgyal mtshan/ grub chen ngag dbang blo gros/ mar ston tshul khrims rin chen/ rdo rje
'chang sngags rams pa dge 'dun bkra shis/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho/ brag mgon spyan snga gzhon nu chos dpal bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang pha bong kha pa dpal
'byor lhun grub/ rigs kun bdag po chos dbyings rang grol/ pad dkar 'dzin pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ thugs sras 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ spro lung pa grub dbang bsod
nams chos 'phel/ thub bstan mkhan chen tshul khrims bzang po/ khams ston rdo rje 'chang bsod nams dbang phyug drin chen thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong bkra
shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la lhun grub steng gi phan bde gling bla brang du stsal to/ /yang na ngag dbang blo bzang
rgya mtsho nas/ gnas brtan 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des
bdag la stsal to/ /yang na mkhas grub rje nas/ 'brong rtse lha btsun rin chen rgya mtsho blo gros/ paN chen ngo mtshar rgya mtsho/ mar ston tshul khrims rin chen man

'dra/ yang na 'brong rtse chos rje nas/ grub chen ngag dbang blo gros/ mar ston sems dpa' chen po man 'dra/ yang na mkhas grub shangs ston pa nas/ mkhas btsun rgyal mtshan
'bum/ 'jag chen byams pa dpal/ 'jag pa blo gros dpal/ grub chen ngag dbang blo gros man 'dra/ yang na byams pa dpal nas/ kun dga' dpal/ ngag dbang blo gros man 'dra/ yang
na mkhas grub rje nas/ rong ston blo bzang grags pa/ thon pa mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho/ paN chen bsod nams grags pa/ gu ge ba nyi ma bzang po/ khri rin po che rgyal
khang rtse ba dpal 'byor rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang pha bong kha ba man 'dra/ yang rjes gnang bar gcod kun sel gyi brgyud lugs gcig ni/ 'jag chen byams pa dpal nas/ snar
thang lo tsA ba don grub bzang po/ rgyal ba tsong kha pa chen po/ shar ba rin chen rgyal mtshan/ byang gling pa grags pa rin chen/ snar thang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN
chen ye shes rtse mo/ rje chos grags pa/ mar ston sems dpa' chen po/ rdo rje 'chang sngags rams pa man gong ltar ro/ /yang na rgyal ba tsong kha pa chen po nas/ rgyal
sras bzang skyong ba/ rin po che chos dpal ba/ chos rje blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang sngags rams pa man 'dra/ yang na 'jag chen byams
pa dpal nas/ kun mkhyen shes rab dpal bzang / sems dpa' chen po tshul khrims dpal bzang / mkhas grub rin chen bshes gnyen/ chos rje legs pa'i blo gros/ rje phyogs las rnam
rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang sngags rams pa

man 'dra/ dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba bar gcod kun sel gyi brgyud lugs gcig ni/ mkhas grub shangs ston nas/ rje rgyal mtshan 'bum/ 'jag chen byams pa dpal/
rje bsod nams blo gros/ bla ma kun dga' bzang po/ 'dren mchog don yod rgyal mtshan/ yab chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ chos rje
rin po che thub bstan pa/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal man gong bzhin no/ /yang na mtshungs med bzang po rgyal mtshan nas/ rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na mkhas
grub rje nas/ ba so chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ gnas rnying pa kun dga' bde legs/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho man gong ltar ro/ /yang na mtshungs med bzang po rgyal
mtshan nas/ 'jam dbyangs dge 'dun 'phel/ rgyud pa bkra shis 'phags/ rgyud chen brtson 'grus 'phags/ sras khang sngags rams pa bzang po rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang pha bong
kha ba man 'dra/ mgon po rgyan can/ tshe bdag lha bzhi'i dril sgrub/ mgon dkar bzhi'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon dha na saM skr-i ta/ grub
chen rA hu la gupta/ mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor man brgyud tshul gong ma mtha' dag dang 'dra/ sa ra ha'i mgon po khrag 'thung gi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje
'chang / sa ra ha/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon chen po padma thod phreng / grub chen sha ba ri pa/ mnga' bdag mai tri pa/ khyung po rnal 'byor man gong ma rnams dang 'dra/
shangs

lugs gtsang ma'i dbang bzhi byin rlabs kyi tshul du thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhas grub shangs ston chen po yan gong ltar las/ de nas mkhas btsun rgyal mtshan 'bum pa/ khyung
po tshul khrims mgon/ bya btang ri khrod ras chen/ sprul sku sangs rgyas rdo rje/ pha rgod thar pa dpal bzang / drin can sangs rgyas rnam rgyal/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal
po/ gnyan ston rnam sprul gzhon nu blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag zhwa lu pa chen po bsod nams mchog grub/ ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho
man 'dra/ yang na tshar chen nas/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra/ yang na tshar chen nas/ bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal
mtshan/ spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i gtor chog dang rjes gnang gi yi
ge bar chad kun sel gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ gzims shag chos rje ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ 'jam dpal rdo rje bsod nams dbang phyug khyab
bdag zhwa lu pa man 'dra'o/ /yang mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas/ phyag drug nag po 'khor dang bcas pa'i rjes gnang bar gcod kun sel
lung dang bcas pa/ mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang ba las thob pa/ rje des gsan yul bla ma gang yin blta/ de las bdag tshul rin gyis legs par nos so/
/

!/ /mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge la brten nas dpal shangs pa bka' brgyud pa las brgyud pa'i bla ma mgon po dbyer med dam mgon dkar yid
bzhin nor bu'i rjes su gnang ba legs par thob nas/ rgyab brten lung la/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyi 'di skor gyi gdams pa gsar rnying gi yi ge rnams phyogs
gcig tu bsdebs pa be bum du byas pa'i steng nas lung thob pa'i rnam grangs la/ khyung pos mdzad pa'i bcom ldan 'das mgon po yid bzhin nor bu'i sgrub thabs dgos 'dod 'byung
ba'i gdams ngag gi rgyal po dngos grub ma lus pa 'byung ba'i bdag nyid ces bya ba lo rgyus/ sbyor ba/ dngos gzhi/ rjes gsum gyi sgo nas bstan pa/ mjug tu bdag khyung po
rnal 'byor pas zhal gdams snyan brgyud yi ge ra bkod pa'i mtha' can/ des mdzad pa'i bstod pa phyogs bcu dus gsum ma/ yid bzhin nor bu'i lo rgyus 'gor bla ma mai tri pa ko
sa la bikSha'i dur khrod ces dang / zhal dngos su ston no'i mtha' can/ gtor ma'i cho ga 'gro ba'i don la mthu dang ldan par mdzod kyi mtha' can/ mchod 'bul rgyu dang 'bras
bu'i khyad par ma/ bskang ba 'gor/ dad pa dang ni dam tshig ces dang / bsam don ma lus myur 'grub nas/ /longs spyod 'dod dgu'i dpal spyod shog gi mtha' can/ rjes gnang
'gor mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu'i rjes gnang la dkyil 'khor dang gtor ma zhes yod pa/ lte bar hU~M dkar po bris lugs gcig go'i mtha' can/ na mo buddha'i gsol 'debs/ las
tshogs 'gor las kha tshar 'di la zhi ba nor du sgrub

ces dang / tshes brgyad nas gnam stong gi bar la bya'o sa ma ya i thi'i mtha' can/ gter bum bca' ba'i man ngag 'gor bum pa kha yangs shing mchu yongs su grags pa dang ldan
pa zhes dang / ches shin tu gsang bar bya zhing dpe su la'ang mi bstan no'i mtha' can/ 'khor lo'i man ngag 'gor dbang sdud kyi 'khor lo bri ba ni bri ba'i gzhi zhes dang
/ nor bu byed kyi hU~M bri ba ma yin no'i mtha' can/ sbyin sreg gi yi ge 'gor rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg byed na thab khung zhes dang / sbyin sreg byar rung gsung ngo i thi'i
mtha' can/ bum gter bca' ba'i man ngag 'gor chos skyong gi bum pa bca' ba'i thabs ni/ dang po bum pa so ma btang ba zhes dang / zhal shes rnams kyang yi ge ra bkod pa yin
pas dpe gzhan la mi bstan par ches cher dam par bya'o'i mtha' can/ bstod pa chos dbyings spros bral ma/ kun dga' 'od kyis chos skyong zhal mjal dus bstod cing gsol ba btab
pa yin no'i mtha' can/ rab gnas kyi yi ge 'gor rab gnas spyi dang mthun pa'am 'dis sgos kyi rab gnas zhes dang / shangs pa'i zhal gdams yi ge ra bkod pa'o'i mtha' can/
yang bla ma'i sku 'bag rab gnas rdo rje 'dzin pa nam mkha' stobs rgyas kyis mdzad pa ste de rnams yig rnying gi skor ro/ /yi ge phyi ma la tshar chen rdo rje 'chang chen
pos mdzad pa'i mgon dkar gyi sgrub thabs dang bstod pa/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' grol mchog gis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang gi yi ge ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad
pa'i rjes gnang gi phyag len bklag chog tu bkod pa/ mkhas

grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dbang gi rgyal po/ des mdzad pa'i rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg bklag pas don grub dang / yid bzhin nor bu la gnang nas bskul
ba'i tshigs bcad dang brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs rnams dang bcas pa'i lung rnams thob nas/ rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang chen po/ ye shes kyi
mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen sha ba ri dbang phyug rgyal sras mai tri pa chen po/ grub chen rA hu la gupta  jo bo a ti sha'i bla ma ri nag po'i gtsug lag khang du bzhugs pa'i
tshe'i rig 'dzin brnyes pa de yin/ badzra/ mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor/ rmog cog pa rin chen brtson 'grus/ dbon ston skyer sgang pa chos kyi sengge/ gnyen ston sbas
pa'i rnal 'byor/ 'gro mgon sangs rgyas ston pa/ mkhas grub gtsang ma shangs ston/ mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / bla ma rdo rje gzhon nu/ mus chen nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/
sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ ni gu pa sangs rgyas bzang po/ mtsho kha nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug kun dga' bsod nams/ bla ma dkon
mchog legs 'dzin/ mtshungs med e waM pa chen po/ rje dpal ldan don grub/ rje dbon 'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas
phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims
rin chen la lan mang du stsal

to/ /yang na rje sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag bande tshul rin la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ bla ma gcig gnyis btsal/
de nas mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang bkra shis lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu'i sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa khyung pos mdzad pa dang / mkhan
chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mus chen nam mkha'i rnal 'byor yan rjes gnang dang 'dra la/
de nas byang sems sbyin pa bzang po/ grub thob thang stong rgyal po/ mang mkhar ba blo gros rgyal mtshan/ pu rang ba dpal ldan dar po/ zhi dgon pa bsod nams rtse mo/ lo
chen 'gyur med bde chen/ mkhas pa ngag dbang chos grags/ bdag po bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs bkra shis dpal ldan/ chos kyi spyan ldan sangs rgyas dpal bzang /
mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ de las rdo rje 'dzin dbang kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyis gsan/ de las mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas dpal bzang gis gsan/
des snyom las mkhan gyi mthar thug pa bande tshul khrims rin chen bdag la'o/ /!/ /lo pa tshul khrims dar gyis mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge dang gtor chog gi steng nas
jo bo chen po lugs kyi mgon po gri gug lcam dral gyi rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mgon po/ slob dpon bram ze mchog sred/ paN chen
bde ba'i rdo rje/ shraddhA ka

ra warma/ jo bo chen po dpal ldan a ti sha'abrom rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ spyan snga ba tshul khrims 'bar/ bshes gnyen bya yul ba gzhon nu 'od/ mus sman pa/ gro ston bdud rtsi
grags/ zhang chos kyi bla ma/ sangs rgyas sgom pa sengge skyabs/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ skyo smon lam tshul khrims/ snar thang byang chen pa bsod nams 'phel/ bla ma tshul
khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla chen bsod blo/ spyan snga sbyin pa dpal/ mkhan chen grags pa don grub/ gnyug la paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/ lo pa spyan snga rin po che ngag
dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan/ she'u lo tsA ba byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen
rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rdo rje 'chang ba chen po ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen
la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na ye shes kyi mgon po/ bram ze mchog sred/ jo bo a ti sha'abrom ston rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ 'dzeng sgom dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ sne'u

na bla ma dpal ldan pa nas/ gtsang pa blo bzang grags pa/ bka' 'gyur ba shAkya rgyal mtshan/ lo pa spyan snga bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos

grags man 'dra/ yang na rje byams pa phun tshogs nas/ mtshungs med dpal 'byor shes rab/ sgrub khang dpal don man 'dra'o/ /!/ /skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang po khro phu lo tsA
ba byams pa'i dpal gyi man ngag brgya rtsar grags pa la/ thog mar sems nyid ngal gso'i brgyud 'debs/ dge bsnyen zhi ba'i go cha can gyis ri bo po Ta la nas 'phags pa spyan
drangs pa'i lo rgyus phar phyin drug gi nyams len/ skyes bu bzhi'i nyams len/ rten 'brel thabs bzhi'i man ngag stong nyid snying rje'i man ngag zhol spong bzhi'i man ngag
sku bzhi ngo sprod mkhas pa bzhi'i rtsa  rgya gzhung / tshigade'i 'grel pa/ de'i man ngag mdor bsdus/ 'bum skyabs la spring ba'i chos bco brgyad/ thabs mkhas bzhi'i man
ngag kha sarpA Ni'i rgyun gyi nyams len/ smin grol gyi zhal gdams/ 'da' kha ye shes kyi 'chi  kha che paN chen gyi/ kha'i man ngag bla med theg pa'i man ngag bco lnga/
thabs mkhas bzhi'i man ngag bzhi tshan bzhi'i man ngag bla ma bzhi'i man ngag rdo rje gsum gyi ngo sprod/ grub pa'i bcud len gyi man ngag gnad kyi 'pho ba/ 'chi kha'i gdams
pa/ rdo rje bzhi'i rnal 'byor/ bdud rtsi thig le'i gdams pa/ stong nyid dgu phrugs pa/ skyid sdug lam khyer gyi gdams ngag snyan brgyud bdud rtsi'i thigs pa/ gnad kyi
gzer drug gi gdams pa khyad par can/ chab gtor bsdus pa bya tshul/ sgrol ma la brten pa'i 'chi kha'i gdams pa kha che paNDi ta'i gsung khro los bsgyur ba/ zhi byed drug pa
dkar po dang blud kyi sgrib sbyong ba'i

man ngag thugs rje chen po la brten pa/ rang la bskul ba 'ga' zhig chu shul 'pho ba lung du sbyar ba/ gnad kyi ngo sprod gsum pa bdud rtsi'i lta ba'i man ngag bdud rtsi'i nying
khu lta bu'i man ngag dgu pa/ yang zhal gdams 'ga' zhig mtha' bzhi mdud 'grol gyi man ngag mdo khams dga' ston tshul khrims grags la gdams pa/ 'chi kha'i gdams pa/ yang
'chi kha'i gdams pa sgrol ma la brten pa gcig yang 'chi kha'i gdams pa'i gnad/ yang de'i man ngag rgyas 'debs gsum/ rang sems ngo sprod kyi gdams pa/ yang rang sems ngo
sprod gcig skyid sdug lam khyer/ de gsum gyi bsdus  rin po che'i 'bras bu lta bu'i nyams len/ don/ thugs rje chen po la brten pa'i klu'i gdon 'grol/ ngo sprod gsum gyi
zhal gdams/ sgrol ma la brten nas rten mngon shes su 'char ba'i gdams pa/ bdud rtsi bum pa'i man ngag bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ rje btsun ma u rgyan la zhal gdams/ mchog gi gdams
pa rnam gsum/ 'khor lo 'bar ba'i gdams pa/ gnubs lo tsA ba'i skyel ma ring po/ tshe 'dir sgom pa'i ngo sprod gnad gsum pa/ rin ce 'bru gsum gyi man ngag phan med bcu
gnyis pa'i zhal gdams/ tshang bcu gnyis pa'i zhal gdams/ man ngag gnad kyi lde migade'i don 'grel sngon 'gro dngos gzhi rjes kyi gdams pa 'bring po/ snying po don gyi ngo
sprod gsum pa/ gnad drug gi 'pho ba'i gdams pa/ 'gor skad gnyis shan sbyar yod pa'i 'ching ba rnam grol gyi man ngag mi tra dzo kis mdzad pa khro los bsgyur ba/ de'i 'grel

pa khro los mdzad pa/ mi tra dzo ki brgyud bcas la bstod  khro los/ pa/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i sems rnam par sbyong ba'i lam 'bras zhes pa buddhA shrIs mdzad pa khro
los bsgyur ba/ de'i 'grel pa khro los mdzad pa/ buddhA shrI brgyud pa dang bcas pa la bstod pa/  khro los/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i lta spyod rnam dag gi man ngag ces
pa kha che paN chen gyis mdzad pa khro los bsgyur ba/ de'i 'grel pa khro los mdzad pa/ kha che paN chen brgyud par bcas pa'i bstod pa khro los mdzad pa/ 'gor skad shan
sbyar yod pa'i grub pa nges bstan gyi rtsa ba/ snying gtam bzhi gsum bcu gnyis kyi rtsa ba/ de'i 'grel pa shin tu zab pa/ snying po don gsum gyi rtsa tshigade'i bsdus don/
de'i don 'grel shin tu rgyas pa/ lta bsgom spyod pa'i mgur/ yang de'i mgur/ yang sems la gros 'debs kyi mgur shin tu gces pa'i man ngag dwags po rin po che'i zhal gdams/
rje sangs rgyas kyi zhal ngo blta 'dod na zhes yod pa'i zhal gdams/ yid smon bya ba'i man ngag phyi nang gsang gsum gyi bar chad bsrung thabs/ kha sarpA Ni'i snying gi
mun sel gyi man ngag khro los la stod kyi lcim lung du bkod pa/ chos spyi'i lung nod pa'i man ngag zab mo/ gtum mo'i gdams pa zab mo/ 'bral med bzhi'i man ngag thugs rje
chen po'i man ngag mkhan po 'dzad phu ba la gnang ba'i mtha' can/ chos spyod yan lag brgyad pa dge slong byams pa'i dpal gyis bkod pa/ mdo chen bdun gyi man ngag bi ma la
shrI dang khro los bsgyur ba/ chos spyi'i gsung rang

grol gyi man ngag dge rtsa gsum gyi man ngag bogs 'don gsum gyi man ngag zhal nas zhal du brgyud pa/ bar chad sel thabs/ blo las 'das na zhes pa 'gor yod pa'i a cang che'i
zhal gdams phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi 'don thabs/ shAkya shrI'i man ngag sgrol ma'i bstod sgrub tu grags pa/ sgrol ma'i lam gyi rim pa/ man ngag rin chen 'bru dgu'i zhal gdams/
yang zhal gdams tshigs bcad ma/ 'gor sgyu lus kyi chu bur zhes yod pa'i zhal gdams rigs kyi bu bdun ma/ gces pa drug gi zhal gdams/ 'gor nam yang myur du zhes yod pa'i
zhu ba drug gi zhal gdams/ 'gor 'chi ba 'di la zhes yod pa'i zhal gdams lcags kyi brag dmar du bkod pa/ 'gor rang lus 'di la zhes yod pa'i ngo sprod gsum pa/ 'gor sngon
chad ces yod pa'i zhal gdams gsung sgros tshig bskul ma chu shul 'pho ba lung du bkod pa/ bskul 'debs brgyad pa/ dpe don ma'i zhal gdams chu shul 'pho ba lung du bkod
pa mnyam med chos rje'i gsung / 'gor dngos po'i zhes yod pa'i zhal gdams chos rje'i gsung rgyun/ 'gor rje btsun sku drin can zhes yod pa'i zhal gdams chu shul 'pho ba lung
du bkod pa/ yang mnyam med lo tsA ba'i zhal gdams/ bdud rtsi thigs pa'i zhal gdams/ mchog gi gdams pa gsum gyi man ngag shin tu zab pa/ zung 'jug bzhi'i rtsa ba/ de'i man
ngag nyams grib sel ba'i man ngag rang rdo rjer bskyed pa/ shes phyin 'don pa'i man ngag zab mo bla ma paN chen gyi zhal gdams/ rdo rje gug skyed kyi gdams pa mi

tra'i gsung khro los bsgyur ba/ bla ma paN chen gyi man ngag thor bu/ nad gdon lam khyer gyi man ngag g.yung drung ye shes la skyes su bskur ba mjug tu tshigs bcad gcig yod
pa/ nying khu lta bu'i man ngag rtsa ba/ de'i rgyas bshad gnad kyi lde miga'agor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i 'ching ba rnam grol gyi bstan bcos zhes pa niShka langkas mdzad
pa lo chung shes rab kyis bsgyur ba/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i spyan ras gzigs kyi sgrub thabs buddhA shrI'i man ngag tshang bsrung ba'i man ngag de'i bsdus don/ ye
shes g.yung drung la spring pa/ mi tra dzo ki'i man ngag 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i mi tra'i gdams pa i thi'i mtha' can/ sbyin bdag rgyal mo la gdams pa/ jo bo kha sarpA
Ni'i sgrub thabs/ 'gor na mo gu ru zhes yod pa'i zhal gdams rdo rje tshig bzhi'i gdams pa/ tshe sgrub kyi gdams pa zab mo khyad par can/ 'gor brgyud rim dang bcas pa'i
yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs/ 'gor bla ma rdo rje 'dzin pa zhes yod pa'i yan lag bdun pa/ 'gor na mo gu ru zhes yod pa'i 'chi blu gzhan la mi spel ba'i mtha' can/ byams pas
dam bcas pa'i gzungs/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i byams pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon ner tis mdzad pa khro los bsgyur ba/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i byams pa'i bstod
pa khro los mdzad pa/ 'gor thugs rje chen po la phyag 'tshal lo zhes yod pa'i yang snying gsung gi man ngag 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i rmi lam sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs
slob dpon dga' ba'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa khro los

bsgyur ba/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i rtogs pa brjod pa sum cu pa mi tra'i  jo bo'i bka' bzhin mi tras mdzad pa/ spyan sngar khro los bsgyur ba/ rtogs brjod do ha sum cu
pa'i rnam bshad khro los mdzad pa/ rab tu gnas pa'i phyag len khyad par gsum ldan bla ma lo tsA ba'i gsung bzhin khro los mdzad pa/ 'gor na mo gu ru zhes yod pa'i bla ma'i
rnal 'byor shin tu zab pa bka' rgya can/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i rgyal po zla ba'i spring yig mi tras mdzad pa lo chung tshul khrims shes rab kyis bsgyur ba/ lha
sa'i jo bo la bstod pa khro los mdzad pa blo brid drug pa'i zhal gdams/ kha che paN chen gyi thugs dam dzambha la nag po'i chu sbyin sgrub thabs skad shan sbyar yod pa kha
che paN chen gyi gdams pa khro los bsgyur ba 'gor sa brgyad dbang phyug ces yod pa'i bstod pa/ dzambha la'i sgrub thabs kyi gnad sbas pa 'bum 'khyil du grags pa paN chen
gyi gsung sgros khro los bkod pa/ gshin bsngo bya tshul/ rgya gar grub chen brgyad kyi gsol 'debs/ dzambha la nag po'i lo rgyus bla ma paN chen gyi gsung khro los bkod
pa/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i dzam nag gi sgrub thabs gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba sbas pa 'bum 'khyil paNDi ta nor can gyis mdzad pa kha che gser gdugs can yang
zer/ paNDi ta dang khro los bsam yas su bsgyur ba/ de'i bsdus don khro los mdzad pa/ 'gor 'phags pa dzambha la zhes yod pa'i dzam nag sbas pa gsum 'khyil gyi lo rgyus shin
tu ya mtshan pa rdzogs byang gi mtha' rten/ grong khyer shing thag can gyi lo rgyus 'dul lung las btus pa/ dzam nag gi las tshogs

gter bum la brten nas nor sgrub pa/ rta gzugs la brten nas nor sgrub pa/ thod pa la brten nas nor sgrub pa/ rig ma la brten nas nor sgrub pa/ dzam nag gi steng bzhengs thabs/
gzhan gyi ngag mnan thab/ dgra bo rengs pa'i man ngag rigs brgyud bcad pa/ dgra bo bskrad pa/ 'byung po 'dul ba/ klu'i gdon 'grol/ char 'bebs thabs/ nor bdag gnad la gzir
ba'i thabs/ yi ge bcu pa'i phrin las la oM gyis dbang du sdud pa/ dzam gyis nor sgrub pa/ bhas 'jigs pa skyob pa/ la yis rkun po bsrung ba/ dza yis bu ster ba/ len gyis
tshe bsring ba/ tra yis phyugs skyong ba/ ye yis skyed tshal rgyas pa/ swA yis dbang bskur ba/ hA yis nad zhi ba rnams kha che paNDi ta'i gdams pa gzhan la ma gnang ba'i
khyad chos khro los yi ge ra bkod pa/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i dzambha la'i  thun mong gibstod pa/ skad shan sbyar yod pa'i khyad par gyi bstod pa/ phrin las nyi
shu pa paNDi ta nor can gyis mdzad pa kha che paNDi ta dang khro los skyid grong du bsgyur ba/ 'gor 'phags pa rmugs 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes yod pa'i bstod pa rdzogs
byang gi mtha' can/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i bstod pa tsandra go mis mdzad pa/  dzambha la'i/ bstod pa 'dod 'jo'i ba  dzambha la'i/ mo tshigs bcad brgyad pa bla ma
paN chen gyis zhal gzigs dus mdzad pa/ sems kyi bde ba bcu gsum pa'i zhal gdams bla ma paNDi tas gro mo dur khrod phag ri sogs su gsungs pa'i zhal gdams kha thor ba sna
tshogs khro lo byams pa'i

dpal gyis bsgyur ba/ chu bo bzhi 'dor ba la gdams pa khro los mdzad pa/ mkhan chen rin po che'i zhal nas zhes yod pa'i shangs pa blo gros kyis sems la phan par gdams pa/ rin
po che'i zhal nas zhes yod pa'i zhal gdams shangs pa blo gros grags kyis yi ge ra bris pa/ skad shan sbyar yod pa'i lha mo dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta zla bas
byin gzhon nus mdzad pa buddha shrI dang khro los bsgyur ba/ de'i bsdus don khro los mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i sgo nas tshe bsring ba'i man ngag shin tu zab pa/ mjug tu ltas
ngan g.yang len gyi gdams pa dang bcas pa zab po'i mtha' can/ 'gor na mo tA ra zhes yod pa'i lho brag gtam shul du byon pa'i tshe slob ma rnams cung zad 'khrug pa'i tshe
rje btsun ma la smre sngags kyi sgo nas 'bod pa/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor shAkya shrI'i gdams pa/ 'khor byang chub sems dpa' rin chen mang zhes pa'i sgrub thabs gtor ma dang bcas
pa khro los mdzad pa/ rnam sras rta bdag brgyad dang bcas pa'i bstod pa khro los mdzad pa zhus dag pa'i mtha' can/ mjug tu zhal shes phran bu/ gsang 'dus dpa' gcig gi
sgrub thabs khro los bsgyur ba/ skad shan sbyar yod pa'i dus 'khor lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs dus zhabs pas mdzad pa buddha shrI dang khro los bsgyur ba/ 'gor dkon mchog
gsum la zhes yod pa'i smon 'jug sems bskyed kyi cho ga paN chen gyi gsung rgyun rgyas bsdus 'tsham par khro los bkod pa sems bskyed kyi brgyud pa dang bcas pa/ dzambha la
nag po'i chu sbyin pa'i man ngag dzambha la'i chu sbyin gyi lo rgyus smon lam rin chen sil

ma/ de'i bsdus don/ smon lam sil ma tshigs bcad du bsdebs pa rnams khro los mdzad pa/ nor rgyun ma'i sgo nas dbul ba sel ba lo rgyus dang bcas pa/ de'i sngags bzla thabs dang
bcas pa/ 'gor skad shan sbyar yod pa'i rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa paNDi ta buddha shrI dang khro los bsgyur ba/ skad shan sbyar yod
pa'i nor 'dzin chu dbang snying rje can gyi gzungs rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ oM dzambha la zhes yod pa'i nor 'dzin gyi gzungs/ paN chen gsung bskyed rdzogs kyi gnad zab
mo/ khro lo chen po'i gsung mgur 'chi dus ma rang la gdams pa/ yang bla ma rin po che zhes yod pa'i mgur ma blo bde bzhi ma/ na mo gu ru zhes yod pa'i re skyid ma'i mgur
ma/ na mo gu ru zhes yod pa'i ser ba bsrung ba'i man ngag shin tu zab pa hU~M dmar ma khro lo'i phyag bzhes ma/ rang la gros 'debs shlau ka gcig rje btsun sku drin can
la phyag 'tshal lo zhes yod pa'i rang la gros 'debs i thi'i mtha' can/ 'chi ba sems kyi zhes yod pa'i rang la gros 'debs me long bdun pa rnams te chos tshan de rnams kyi
lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khro phu lo tsA ba/ khro phu sems dpa' chen po/ yang rtse ba rin chen sengge/ dgra bcom pa yon tan blo gros/ byang lung pa gzhon nu blo gros/
paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ yig drug pa shes rab dpal 'byor/ rje grol mchog rje karma bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs shAkya bstan 'dzin/ mkhas dbang shAkya nor bu/ sde snod 'dzin
pa kun dag legs pa/ lo chen bshes gnyen rnam

rgyal/ rgyal sras rgyal mtshan bzang po/ smra dbang phyogs las rnam rgyal/ don grub chos gling pa bstan pa rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ ngag dbang
kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'dzin pa kun dga' rgya mtsho/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /rnam 'dren bstan
pa'i mnga' bdag dpag yas rigs kyi khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang chen po dang mi gnyis pa rje btsun sa skya pa gong ma lnga'i gsung rab rin po che rnams kyi lung gi tshogs legs
par nos pa la/ ngor rdzong gong dkar ba gsum la chos tshan gyi grangs la mang nyung dang go rim cung zad mi mthun pa'i khyad par 'ga' zhig mchis par/ 'dir rgyal ba gnyis
pa lta bu rje btsun kun dga' bzang pos glo bo smon thang gi rgyal por dpal sa skya'i rje btsun gong ma yab sras gsum gyi gsung rab rnams rin po che sU warNa las grub par
bzheng bcug skabs mdzad pa'i dkar chag gi sgrig rim dang mthun par rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i dkar chagangor chen thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun
grub/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / shar pa byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ sgrub khang
pa mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rje pa rnams kyi gsan yig la gzhi byas nas gsung rab chos tshan gyi ngos 'dzin zhib tu dpyad nas 'god pa la
lnga ste/ dang por bstan pa'i bdag po chos kyi rje rnal

'byor gyi dbang phyug brtse ba chen po spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug sa skya pa kun dga' snying po'i gsung rab rin po che'i tshogs rnams lung du mnos pa'i rnam grangs la/ dpal
ldan bi rU pa (9)(24)la bstod pa  'dir khyed kyi gzi yis rtog pa kun bral te/ zhes sogs dang mngon sum du bstod pa'i tshig nyams kyi shugs kyis byung ba zhes pa'i tshig
gi zhal gzigs ma yin par gsal lo/ / lhan skyes spros bral ma/ zhang ston la don gyis byin rlabs stsal ba'i bstod (9)(24)pa yon tan mchog mnga' ma/ rgyud (9)(24)sde spyi'i
rnam gzhag chung ngu 'gor/ bla ma rin chen lta bu dang / zhes dang / cha shas kyi bshad pa'i rgyud sampu Ta yin no'i mtha' can/ brtag gnyis kyi sa (9)(24)bcad 'gor/ dpal
kye rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal kye'i rdo rje'i brtag pa gnyis kyi bdag nyid can gyi rgyud ces bya ba dang / mjug tu bdag gis mi shes blo dman phyir/ /rgyud don ji
bzhin ma rtogs pas/ /zhes sogs dang / brtag gnyis kyi bsdus don rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ kye'i rdo rje rtsa ba'i rgyud (9)(24)brtag pa gnyis pa'i tshigs 'grel bla ma mnga'
ris pas mdzad pa 'gor/ bla ma dam pa rnams kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal lo/ /rang bzhin lhan cig skyes pa mkha' ltar zhes pa dang / mi phyed phyag rgya chen po mngon
gyur shog gi mtha' can/ sgyi chu bas (9)(24)mdzad pa'i brtag gnyis kyi dka' 'grel 'gor/ dpal kye'i rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo/ /kye yi rdo rje rnal 'byor che/ /zhes pa
dang man ngag don gsal zhes bya ba rmongs pas rtogs sla ba'i don du bris pa

rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ dkon mchog lhun grub pa'i gsan yig na sgyi chu ba'i dka' 'grel dang TIka chung man (9)ngag don gsal zhes so sor gsungs pa ltar 'dug kyang gcig yin par
'di nyid kyi mjug na gsal/ 'on kyang 'og sa chen nyid kyis mdzad pa 'di gsan yig rnams na mi snang bas dpyad/ brtag gnyis kyi dka' 'grel 'gor/ bcom ldan 'das dpal kye'i
rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo/ /blo gros mtshungs med 'jig rten kun gyi mig/ ces bya ba dang / yang dag rdo rje sems dpa' 'thob ces dang / kye'i rdo rje'i dka' 'grel bla ma
sa chen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so'i mtha' can dang rtsa bshad kyi rgyud du 'jog tshul 'thor bu 'ga' re dang bcas pa/ rdo rje gur (9)(24)gyi tho yig 'gor/ bcom ldan 'das dpal
kye'i rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dges pa rdo rje'i rgyud la 'bum tsho lnga byung ba ni zhes pa dang / nam mkha'i khams kyi dbus gnas par/ /zhes pa la sogs pas bstan
to sa mApta'i mtha' can/ gur gyi (9)(24)bshad pa'i chings 'gor/ oM rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de la thog mar zhes pa dang dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i lam bstan pa'o
rdzogs pa'i mtha' can/ gur rigs bsdus kyi rig pa'i dbang gi bshad pa 'gor 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa la bzhi ste zhes pa dang des lus rtag pa ste rnam snang du 'gyur i
thi'i mtha' can/ gur gyi rgyud kyi dka' (9)(24)gnas bshad pa 'gor/ bla ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /le'u dang po 'khor gyi lha mo'i zhes pa dang lhag ma go sla'o'i
mtha' can/ mchog sgrub pa'i dang las

rgyas pa'i lha'i grangs 'gor 'phags pa mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur 'dis zhes pa dang gong du bstan pa'i gsal bar ston to'i mtha' can/ rdo rje glu'i bshad (9)(24)pa 'gor rdo rje
glu'i bshad pa la don gsum ste zhes pa dang lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes su rtogs par byas shing goms par byas pa'o'i mtha' can/ rtsa'i mngon (9)(24)rtogs 'gor rtsa'i mngon
par rtogs pa'i don bstan pa las zhes pa dang de ni byang sems la brtsis pas phra ba'o/ /sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ rdo rje snying 'grel snga (9)(24)'gyur gyi yig sna
'gor/ 'jig rten spyod pa zhes pa na mar zhes pa dang khyab byed ces bya ste ma lus so/ /sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ gur gyi (9)(24)rgyud kyi zin bris 'gor le'u dang por
rgyal ba rigs lnga zhes pa dang dbang bskur ba'i slob dpon la ji ltar gus par bya ba bstan to/ /sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ 'di la gsan yig dbang gi rgyal por le 'grel
zhes gsung / sampu Ta'i rgyud kyi dka' (9)(24)'grel 'gor/ bla ma dam pa rnams la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal yang dag par sbyor ba zhes pa dang dka' ba'i gnas rnams
bsdus pas nongs par gyur na bla ma mkha' 'gros bzod par mdzod/ sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ kha  rgya mtshor rdzogs rim gyi man ngag gsung / sbyor thig le'i don 'byung (9)(24)ba
'gor dpal yang dag par sbyor ba'i rgyud chen po las kha sbyor thig le'i don zhes pa dang nyams su blang ba'i man ngag sngar bla ma'i zhal las shes par bya'o/ /yang
spyir rang byin gyis brlab pa la zhes pa dang gang rung

por sampuu Ta'i dkyil 'khor cho ga'i tho yig gsungs pa 'di yin nam dpyad/ bde mchog nag po pa'i lo rgyus (9)(24)'gor/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/

nag po pa'i gzhung 'di zhes pa dang / brtsams pa mthar phyin pa'o'i mtha' can/ nag po pa'i dkyil chog gi sa (9)(24)bcad 'gor/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la spyi bos gus pas

phyag 'tshal lo/ /slob dpon spyod pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i zhes pa dang / spyod pa'i rjes su gnang ba'o i thi'i mtha' can/ sgrub thabs sa (9)(24)bcad 'gor slob dpon nag po

/ phur bu dbyung ba la sogs pa mjug gi cho ga bstan pa'o i thi'i mtha' can/ gsang ba'i de kho na nyid gsal (9)ba'i sa bcad 'gor/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs pad spyi bos len/

(9)(24)'gor shrI wAM gu ru bha drA ya na maHdngos grub ma grub pa grub par byed ces pa dang / tshig gi don rnams ni gzhung nyid nas gsal lo sbyin sreg sa mApta mi thi'i mtha'
can/ sbyin sreg gi (9)(24)lag len 'gor kr-iShNa A tsArYas mdzad pa'i zhes pa dang / 'di ni la ma ka la sogs pa'i spyod yul yin gsung ngo i thi'i mtha' can/ ro sreg gi
cho ga (9)(24)'gor bcom ldan 'das bde mchog la phyag 'tshal lo/ /slob dpon spyod pa pa'i zhes pa dang / gzhan dag gi ni bsreg rdzas dang yon bdag tu bya ba'i lugs kyang bzhed
de brgyud pa 'dis mi bzhed do'i mtha' can/ gsang (9)(24)ba'i kho na nyid kyi TI ka 'gor/ bla ma dang dpal he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo/ /slob dpon spyod pa'i rdo rjes
mdzad pa'i zhes pa dang / gsang ba'i de kho na nyid rab tu gsal ba'i gsal byed rdzogs pa'i mtha' can/ de'i tshig don bsdus (9)(24)pa'i go 'byed 'gor/ bcom ldan 'das dpal
'khor lo bde mchog la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gsang ba'i de kho na nyid ces pa dang / tshig don gnyis bsdus pa'i go 'byed cung zad tsam bstan pa'o rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ yang
de'i don gyi cha bla ma'i gsung gnang ba bris pa 'gor/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la spyi bos gus par phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal ldan gsang ba 'dus pa dang / /zhes pa dang / gsang

ra maNDa lA ya/ rje btsun bla ma zhes pa dang o la pa

ti'i rnam par bshad pa i thi/ yang de'i man (9)(24)ngag 'gor/ dbyu gu gcig la sum brgya zhes pa dang / o la pa ti'i man ngag i thi'i mtha' can/ dpyid thig gi TI ka (9)(24)'gor

te de rnams la nag po gzhung drug gi man ngag nag 'bum du grags so/ /de rnams la gsan yig dbang gi rgyal por gzhung drug gi tho yig ces sbas pa tsam las ma gsungs/ rim
pa bzhi'i gdams ngag 'gor/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /srid pa gsum na mtshungs pa med pa'i zhes pa dang / mang ba dang nyung ba khegs gsung ngo i thi'i mtha'
can/ yang de'i lag tu blang ba'i rim pa sogs man ngag thor bu ba 'ga' re/ 'jigs byed rtog (9)(24)bdun gyi TI ka 'gor bcom ldan 'das dpal 'jigs byed la phyag 'tshal lo/

'gor/ rje btsun ma 'phags ma sgrol ma la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dang po mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i bla ma zhes pa dang / dbang gi cho ga'i tho tsam phyogs gcig tu bsdebs nas

ngag gi

rnam grangs bzhi bcu zhe drug lhag tsam phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i gdams pa rnams so/ /'di rnams grub pa'i slob dpon du ma'i man ngag dang rje btsun chen po'i phyag len gces
btus dang sa paN gyi lam sbas bshad sogs nas kyang blangs pa'i slob brgyud cig gis phyis su bsgrigs pa'i lung rgyun mkhan chen sher rdor bas gsan pa 'dir bcug par mngon/
'di nang gi chos tshan mang po'i brgyud pa lam 'bras kyi cha lag glegs bam rnams dang yang gcig go/ gur las gsungs pa'i khro bcu'i srung (9)(24)'khor 'gor/ bla ma dam
pa'i zhabs la spyi bos gus par phyag 'tshal lo/ /'phags pa mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur gyi rgyud las 'byung ba'i uShNI Sha zhes pa dang bla ma'i man ngag gis bsdebs pa yin
no/ /khro bo bcu'i mngon par rtogs pa yongs su rdzogs so'i mtha' can dang / ma hA mA yA'i rgyud stong phrag bco brgyad pa las phyung ba bha ya (9)(24)nA sa'i srung 'khor
'gor/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /bha ya nA sa 'di ni zhes pa dang rang gi lhag pa'i lha'i nga rgyal bya'o bsrung ba'i mchog go rdzogs so'i mtha' can/
skyu ra a (9)(24)skyabs la zhu yig 'gor/ bla ma dam pa rnams kyi zhabs la spyi bos gus par phyag 'tshal lo/ /yon tan rin chen dpag med 'byung ba'i gnas/ /zhes yod pa
