man (9)(24)ngag bstod pa bcas pa'i 'gor/ bla ma

dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /nam mkha' lding bsgom par 'dod pa'i zhes pa dang / rdo rje nam mkha' lding gi bstod pa'o'i mtha' can/ dur khrod bdag po'i sgrub (9)skor tshigs
bcad ma  'on kyang tshigs bcad ma 'di bla ma bai ro tsa nas mdzad pa 'dzim los 'gyur ba de ngos 'dzin dgos te/ sa chen gyis mdzad pa ni de'i 'grel pa tshig lhug pa bsnyen
sgrub las tshogs dang bcas pa 'di yin pa'i shes byed ni/ sngar gyi tshigs bcad ma de la 'dir 'grel par byas pa lag tu blang ba'i rim pa shin tu gsal bar bzhugs pas
shes shing / da ltar dur khrod bdag po'i sgrub skor rgyud gsang ba snying gi 'khor lo rgya gzhung bai ros mdzad pa dang / rje sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa'i sgrub skor las
tshogs thor bur bcas pa dang / yar klungs pas mdzad pa'i yi ge rnams dang bcas pa thams cad kyi lung zur du mdzad pa na'ang bzhugs pas lung rgyun tshang bar yod do/ /'di
bka' 'bum gyi dpe snga ma 'gar bris 'dug pa ltar dang / de'i 'grel pa sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa/ 'gor phyag 'tshal dang / dpal ldan dur khrod bdag po yi/ /gdams pa gzhung
dang mi 'gal ba/ /zhes yod pa/ bdag gzhan bsrung ba'i bsnyen pa/ sgrub pa/ las la sbyar ba rnams kyi lag len gsal bar bkod pa/ 'di la mos shing sgrub pa rnams/ /bar
chad med par dngos grub kun/ /ci 'dod pa ni grub nas su/ /phyag rgya chen po thob par shog/ dpal dur khrod bdag po'i man ngag lag len sa mApta'i mtha' can/ las tshogs dum
bu la 'gor yul du rims nad byung ba la zhes dang des ni mi phyugs nad rnams khegs kyi mtha' can/ bsnyen pa dang sgrub pa'i yig chung / tsakra'i rab gnas/ bsrung ba'i man
ngag rnams kyi yig chung

re/ des mdzad pa'i bsnyen sgrub las sbyor gyi man ngag 'gor/ dam tshig ldan pa'i gang zag gis zhes dang / mjug tu las sbyor ni las tshogs so so'i skabs bzhin shes par bya'o'i
mtha' can/ sku rten sba ba'i man ngag kun gyi gtsug gi nor bur 'gyur ro/ /'di ni rten gyi man ngag go'i mtha' can/ yang sku'i mdun du mchod gtor 'bul ba'i man ngag des
dga' mgur 'du ba yin no'i mtha' can/ yang yab yum gyi sku sba ba'i man ngag rten gyi man ngag logs su bkol ba'o'i mtha' can/ bstod bskul dpal ldan dur khrod bdag po ni zhes
dang bstod cing bskul ba rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ rdzas dang sngags la brten nas smyo ba 'dul ba gzhan zhig 'drir bcug pas kyang 'grub bo'i mtha' can/ de'i las sbyor dam
nyams bsgral ba'i las tshogs drag po'i las so'i mtha' can/ yang dur khrod bdag po yab yum gyi rjes gnang bya ba'i tshul dpal sa skya pa chen pos g.yu mkhar mo sgrol ma
lha khang du bris so'i mtha' can rnams so/ /bde mchog rtsa rgyud le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa'i TI ka (9)(24)mu tig phreng ba 'gor/ sna tshogs padma'i ge sar rdul gyis sku
byug sa pa/ /zhes pa dang / TI ka mu tig phreng ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ 'di bla chen mal dang rje sa chen gnyis char gyi slob ma rje btsun sku mched gnyis kyi
slob dpon bla ma gnyan phul byung bas rje sa chen gyi gsung la zin bris mdzad pas bka' 'bum dngos dang khyad par med cing gsan yig thams cad la'ang yod pas lung rgyun
bzhugs/ slob dpon mtsho skyes (9)(24)kyi lo rgyus 'gor/ bla ma

so i thi'i mtha' can/ sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi (9)(24)bsdus don 'gor/ dpal kye yi rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo/ /slob dpon padma badzras mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs la zhes
bya ba dang / brtsams pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba gzhan don du bsngo ba'o sa mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ mtsho skyes kyi mngon rtogs (9)(24)tshig gi bum pa 'gor/ bla ma rje btsun
sgyi chu ba'i/ /zhes pa dang / des ni bla ma la gus shogs mApta mi thi'i mtha' can/ dkon mchog lhun grub pa'i gsan yig na sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa zhes pa dang mngon

(9)(24)bu jim gyin/ ho (9)(24)kagrags (9)(24)bzang / ston gzhon (9)(24)rnams la spring ba'i 'gor/ 'dir smras pa/ deng sang 'di na zhes pa dang / stobs sogs yon tan zhes
pa dang / mdangs dang dri ro zhes pa dang / blo che rlom che zhes bya ba rnams rim pas yod pa/ gos dar lnga stong dang (9)(24)dgu brgya bzhi bcu phul ba'i dus kyi mchod
brjod dang bsngo ba 'gor/ chos kyi dbyings kyi mkha' las mngon 'phags shing / /zhes yod pa/ tshe dpag med la (9)bstod pa 'gor/ sna tshogs 'dab rgyas chu skyes zhes bya ba

(9)(24)bsngags pa'i rab tu byed pa bdud rtsi'i bum pa 'gor/ khro bo'i rgyal po bdud rtsi 'khyil pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sa yi snying po 'gro ba'i nyer 'tsho dang / /zhes yod
pa/ mchod 'os la bsngags pa 'gor/ bla ma dang dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang las sangs rgyas chos tshogs zhes yod pa/ lnga bsdus sgra gcan gza' (9)(24)lnga dang
bcas pa'i rtsis gzhi rin po che'i 'od zer dri ma med pa 'gor/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs kyi padmor gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /srid dang mya ngan 'das pa'i gtso/ /zhes yod
pa/ nyi khyim 'pho ba'i nges pa (9)'gor/ gsal zhing thogs med myur du 'jug / ces yod pa/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rtsis dus gsal (9)(24)ba'i sgron me 'gor tshig de nyid rgya
skad dang bod skad du yod pa/ de'i don yang dag par bsdus (9)(24)pa 'gor/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rab byung sogs bsdoms bcu gnyis zhes yod pa/ gdod
ma'i dus gsal (9)(24)bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i rtsis 'gor tshig de nyid yod pa/ rtsis kyi gtsug lag (9)(24)dang mthun par nges pa zhes bya ba 'gor/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs la phyag
'tshal lo/ /mkhyen pa'i nyi 'od rab gsal zhing / /zhes yod pa/ dhrU ba gnyis (9)(24)pa'i rtsis 'gor/ na mo gu ru ratna bhaTTA ra kA ya/ gang gi thugs rjes 'gro kun rab
bzung nas/ /zhes yod pa/ lo bdag nyi shu rtsa (9)(24)gnyis kyi rtsis 'gor/ mkhyen pas shes bya kun gzigs nas/ /zhes yod

pa/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i gtsug lag gi de kho na nyid rin po che'i sgron ma (9)(24)'gor tshig de nyid rgya skad dang bod skad du yod pa/ chos 'khor dus kyi bstan
(9)rtsis 'gor sangs rgyas bltams pa'i dus la sogs nas zhes yod pa/ sangs rgyas kyi dus chen bzhi'i ngos 'dzin 'gor/ thams cad mkhyen pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sangs rgyas bcom
ldan 'das dga' ldan nas zhes yod pa/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab 'gyur ro 'tshal bzhengs pa'i/ gsal (9)(24)byed sdeb sbyor gyi rgyan rnam par bkra ba 'gor tshig de
nyid yod pa rgyal po jim gyin gyi don du dpal sa skyar sbyar ba/ yang des rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum bzhengs pa la bsngags pa smar khams sgang du sbyar ba/ yang des dam pa'i
chos rin po che shin tu rgyas pa'i sde snod bzhengs pa'i tshul bstan pa'i rab tu byed pa (9)(24)'gor tshig de nyid yod pa dpal sa skyar sbyar ba/ mangga la yab yum gyis
rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum (9)(24)dang phal po che bzhengs pa la bsngags pa 'gor chos rin po che nye bar bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed kyi rab tu byed pa zhes yod pa tsom mdo gnas
gsar du sbyar ba/ ji big de mur gyis phal po che/ gser 'od dam pa/ stong phrag brgya (9)(24)pa rnams bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed 'gor/ bla ma dang dkon mchog gsum la phyag
'tshal lo/ /thugs rje'i thugs ni kun nas rnam dag cing / /zhes yod pa shing kun du mdzad pa/ rgyal po a rog ches (9)(24)'bum bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed 'gor/ bla ma dang dkon
mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal

lo/ /srid zhi'i bde legs ma lus 'byung ba'i gzhi/ /zhes yod pa/ go pe las rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed 'gor gsung rab rin po che (9)(24)rnam par bkod pa'i
mtshon byed ces yod pa smar khams tsom mdo gnas gsar du sbyar ba/ dge 'dun bzang po sogs kyi yum rgyas 'bring bsdus (9)(24)gsum bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed 'gor/ bla ma dang
dkon mchog gsum la spyi bos gus pas phyag 'tshal zhing skyabs su mchi'o/ /chos kyi dbyings las zhes yod pa/ rin chen dpal gyis 'bum bzhengs pa la bsngags (9)(24)pa 'gor
chos bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed nye bar bkod pa bsod nams rin chen zhes yod pa/ zin shing gi ston pa bcu bdun yang dag pa'i rigs pas pham par byas te rab tu byung ba'i tshe
sbyar ba'i tshigs (9)(24)bcad 'gor/ bla ma dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /yod dang med pa la sogs pa/ /zhes yod pa/ theg pa chen po'i slob dpon dang
slob mas lam nyams su blang ba'i tshul gyi rnam dbye bstan pa (9)(24)'gor/ bla ma dang dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gtsang mkhas rab brtan byams par ldan/ /zhes
yod pa hying hu'i dgon par sbyar ba/ chos rje pa bde bar gshegs dus dbus gtsang gi dge ba'i bshes gnyen (9)(24)rnams la spring pa 'gor/ dus gsum bde bar gshegs pa chos
kyi sku/ /zhes yod pa/ khro phu lo tsA ba la (9)(24)bskur ba dang gdams pa gnyis 'gor/ dpal ldan nyin mor byed pa'i gzi ldan

zhing / /zhes pa dang / mkhyen pa'i dkyil 'khor legs bshad 'od zer gyis/ /zhes yod pa/ las chog rgyas bsdus (9)(24)gnyis kyi 'gor/ thams cad mkhyen pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /mkhan
po dang slob dpon dang dge 'dun rnams zhes yod pa dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du sbyar ba/ bsnyen (9)(24)gnas kyi cho ga 'gor/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal
lo/ /bsnyen gnas kyi sdom pa 'bogs pa'i tshul ni zhes yod pa/ gsan yig dbang gi rgyal por 'di gsal kha med kyang phyi mo thams cad na gong gi las chog dang 'brel nas
'dug pas lung rgyun yod pa 'dra/ rgyal po yab sras kyi mchod rten bzhengs pa la bsngags pa'i sdeb sbyor daNDa ka (9)(24)'gor/ na mo gu ru ratna tra yA ya/ dpal dang ldan
zhing zhes yod pa dpal ldan sa skyar sbyar ba/ gsan yig dbang gi rgyal por rgyal bu jim gyin sogs la bsngags pa gsungs pa 'di yin/ bsngags par 'os pa'i rab tu byed pa (9)(24)'gor
tshig de nyid yod pa smar khams kyi sa'i cha tsom mdor sbyar ba/ gsan yig dbang gi rgyal por hor gyi rgyal rabs lnga po rgyal po go pe la la bsngags par gsungs pa
'di yin/ bod kyi rgyal rabs la bsngags pa'i tshigs bcad 'gor/ gang gi srid gsum rgya mtsho'i zhes yod pa/ gsan yig dbang gi rgyal por jim gyin la bstod pa gsungs pa 'di
yin/ bod kyi rgyal rabs 'gor/ srong btsan sgam po me mo glang la 'khrungs/ zhes yod pa shing mo phag gi lor skyar ka mdor sbyar ba/ lung dang brgyud pa sna tshogs kyi gsan
(9)(24)yig

'gor/ oM swa sti siddhaM/ rdo rje 'chang zhes yod pa/ 'jigs byed skyo lugs kyi brgyud pa nas brtsams te rgyal mtshan rtse mo'i dpung rgyan gyi gzungs sgrub thabs dang bcas
pa'i bar gyi gsan yig rdzogs byang gi mtha' can/ slob dpon bsod nams sengge'i spyan sngar phrin du (9)(24)zhu ba 'gor/ bla ma dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bla
ma dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi zhes yod pa chu pho byi ba'i lor ling chung rtser khab kyi gtsug lag khang du bris pa/ grags pa rin chen gyi zhus (9)(24)lan
'gor/ dpal mchog bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sde snod 'dzin pa grags pa rin chen gyis/ /zhes yod pa 'dam gyi sa cha gang skyar sbyar ba/ rgyal bu byang

pa/ gur mgon gyi rjes gnang 'gor/ bla ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /thog ma kho nar mkha' 'gro dang chos skyong zhes yod pa me mo yos bu'i lor 'dam gyi sa char

(9)(24)bde

ma/ shing phag (9)(24)bla med ma/ me byi dngos (9)(24)grub ma/ me (9)glang don grub ma/ sa stag (9)(24)gang la bkra shis ma/ sa yos (9)(24)gang drin ma/ lcags (9)'brug
thub dbang chos rgyal ma rnams te lo gsar gyi tshe gnang ba'i bkra shis nyer gsum/ rgyal po mangga la (9)(24)yab yum la gnang ba'i bkra shis gcig tu gzhan phan ma/ rgyal
po ji big yab (9)(24)yum la gnang ba'i bkra shis sangs rgyas rnam rgyal ma/ dpon mo chen mo la (9)(24)gnang ba'i bkra shis sangs rgyas kun phrin ma/ yang dpal (9)(24)ldan
khyed sku lhun po ltar brtan zhing / zhes bya ba'i bkra shis shlau ka (9)gcig rnams so/ /'di dag gi go rim bsgrigs pa'i gzhi ni ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi gsan yig rgya
mtsho/ dkon mchog lhun grub pa'i gsan yig thub bstan rgyas pa'i nyin byed/ 'jam mgon sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa'i gsan yig dbang gi rgyal po/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen
pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i gsan yig ganggA'i chu rgyun rnams la zhib tu gtugs tshe/ snga phyi'i go rim 'dra min

dang chos tshan mang nyung sogs kyi khyad par 'ga' re mchis kyang / 'dir sngon gyi bka' 'bum phal cher dkon mchog lhun grub pa'i gsan yig dang mthun shas che ba byung bas 'ga'
zhig de nyid gzhir gzhagad lta'i lung rgyun dpal mchog nas sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas gsan pa 'di nyid khyab che ba snang yang / dkon mchog lhun grub pa'i de dang snga
phyi'i go rim dang chos tshan mang nyung dang / bstan bcos kyi ming gzung yang 'ga' zhig gzhung tshig dang / 'ga' zhig kha byang las dras nas btags pa sogs kyis las dang
po pas ngos zin dka' bar 'dug par/ 'dir gong 'og thams cad kyi khyad par ngos gzung sla ba'i ched du bstan bcos ngos 'dzin dka' ba rnams kyi mgo mjug gi tshig smos pa
dang / bla ma gong ma rnams kyi gsan yig gi mtshan byang thams cad phyogs gcig tu bsdoms nas sgo khyim la anggi dgu pa'i mtshan ma yod pa rnams ded pas ngor chen rdo rje
'chang gi gdan sa dgu pa dkon mchog lhun grub pas gsan ltar rtogs pa dang / anggi nyer bzhi pa'i mtshan ma yod pa rnams ded pas gdan sa nyer bzhi pa sangs rgyas phun tshogs
pas gsan ltar rtogs par 'gyur la/ gzhan paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan

yig na dngos

su ma smos kyang glegs bam gyi gras su sngar yod pa dang phyis rnyed pa gsar 'dzud zhus pa rnams yin pas/ slar 'di dag gi lung rgyun brgyud pa yid ches pa las btsal te rgya
cher spel dgos so zhes shes pa'i ched du bzhag pa yin pas bstan pa rin po che la gces spras byed pa rnams kyis dgongs 'tshal/ ji skad bshad pa'i bstan bcos rin po che de
rnams kyi lung mnos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gong ma yab sras gsum po'i gsung rab rnams kyi lung dang glegs bam dang po nas phyogs gcig tu bsdebs pa ma byung ba la/ dus phyis
bla ma dpal ldan sengge'i thugs dgongs rdzogs pa'i phyir du chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nam rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pas rang nyid la gang bzhugs pa rnams mkhan chen shes
rab rdo rje dang / dbus pa rin chen rgyal mtshan gnyis la gnang / ma bzhugs pa rnams mkhan po shes rab rdo rje dang / dbus pa rin rgyal gnyis la bkas bskul te phyogs kun
tu btang nas lung su yod las zhur bcug cing dpe rnams phyogs gcig glegs bam du bsdebs pa mdzad/ chos rje bla ma dam pas kyang sngar ma gsan pa rnams sher rdor ba las gsan
pas lung thams cad phyogs gcig nas brgyud pa med mod/ 'on kyang mkhan po shes rab rdo rjes bla ma so so las gsan pa'i brgyud pa ni lam 'bras la sogs pa'i lam skor dgu/

mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal

mtshan/ 'gro mgon 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ bla ma dpal ldan sengge/ chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ des mkhan chen shes
rab rdo rje la'o/ /yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ des bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa la'o/ /yang na chos rje
sa skya paNDi ta nas/ tshogs sgom pa kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ bla ma dpal ldan sengge/ de gnyis ka las chos rje bla ma dam pa
bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa la'o/ /'on kyang gsung ngag rin po che'i skor rnams nyams khrid ma gtogs bklag lung byed pa'i srol med do zhes ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis gsan
yig rgya mtsho las gsungs/ rgyud sde spyi'i stong thun/ rnam 'grel dag ldan/ rgyud kyi mngon par rtogs pa ljon shing / gur gyi sa bcad/ rnam bshad/ gur gyi rgyan rnams kyi

tri mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs/ rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma/ lam gyi yan lag pra se na dbab pa/ gnod sbyin mo'i sgrub thabs/ tshangs pa'i bu mo 'gugs pa/ padma pa ti'i man ngag
khol po pa ti'i man

ngag sman chen po'i bcud len/ mai tri mkha' spyod kyi rjes gnang rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ des mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje la'o/
/sgrol ma spyi sgrub/ so so'i sgrub thabs/ bstod pa 'don thabs/ nyi ma sbas pa'i phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi sgrub thabs las tshogs bcas pa'i TIkka/ sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i
sgrol ma lha bcu bdun ma'i dkyil chog rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rin po che bsod nams grags pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ des mkhan po shes rab rdo rje la'o/ /sgrol ma'i bstod
sgrub gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ nyi ma sbas pa/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ nag po pa/ gu rub lo tsA ba/ rong pa/ brang ti dar ma snying po/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ mchims
khu dbon gnyis/ bla ma 'jam gsar ba/ lce mdo sde sengge/ rong pa shes rab sengge/ rin chen bsod nams grags pa/ des chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa la'o/
/sgrol ma'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ klu sgrub/ nyi ma sbas pa/ dA na shrI/ manydzu shrI/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa skya pa chen po/ mchims chos

pa/ des mkhan po shes rab rdo rje la'o/ /sgrol ma maNDal bzhi pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhan po shes rab rgyal mtshan/ grub pa dpal bzang po/ bla ma bzang po pa/ des chos rje
bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan la'o/ /rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa

byab bsrung dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ des chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan la'o/ /dkar mo nyi zla'i brgyud pa ni/ 'gro ba'i mgon
po 'phags pa rin po che/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ bla chen kun blo/ des chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan la'o/ /sa skya pa chen pos mdzad pa'i rgyud sde spyi'i

mtshan/ mkhan

chen shes rab rdo rje/ des chos rje bla ma dam pa la'o/ /rje btsun mi g.yo ba sngon po'i chu srung gi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sku mched gnyis/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta/ zhang

paNDi ta/ 'u yug pa bsod nams sengge/ spru lung pa kun dga' smon lam/ la ru ba yon tan dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen shes

mtsho/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen

pa/ mkhan chen dwangs ma ba/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ des chos bla ma dam pa la'o/ /dril bu pa'i dbang chu/ sgrub thabs gnyis dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa paN yan gong
ltar la/ de nas bo dong rin po che/ khro phu ba rin po che/ yang rtse ba rin chen sengge/ bu ston rin po che nas/ rin chen bsod nams grags pa la'o/ /sdom pa nyi shu pa'i
TI kamatshan brjod 'don thabs bcas kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa paNDi ta/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ bde ba dpal/ bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu/ rin po
che bsod nams grags pa/ mkhan chen gzhon nu mgon/ des mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje la'o/ /kye rdo rje'i dbang gi chu bo chen mo/ dkyil chog nas gling ma/ chos la 'jug pa'i
sgo/ byis pa bde blag tu 'jug pa/ de'i rnam bshad/ mngon rtogs yan lag drug pa/ bdag med ma'i mngon rtogs/ lU hi pa'i mngon rtogs gsum/ phag mo zhal gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs/
sngags kyi byin rlabs/ las bcu/ mchims chos seng la spring yig gzhan phan nyer mkho/ argha'i cho ga kha 'bar ma'i gtor chen rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon rin po
che/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ 'jam skya/ bla ma a mo gha/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje nas/ chos rje bla ma dam
pa la'o/ /dril bu pa'i lo rgyus/ dril bu rim lnga/ tshes bcu'i mchod pa/ nges brjod bla ma'i 'khrul 'khor bri thabs rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ stod lo/ slob

dpon a mo gha/ mkhan po shes rab rdo rje nas/ chos rje bla ma dam pa la'o/ /sgrol ma phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi sa bcad/ TI kanyi ma sbas pa'i lugs kyi sgrol ma nyer gcig ma'i
las tshogs dang sa bcad rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bla ma thub pa mgon/ bla ma a mo gha/ mkhan po shes rab rdo rje nas/ chos rje bla ma dam
pa la'o/ /rigs gsum spyi'i rigs gtad/ a ra pa tsa na'i mngon rtogs/ dkyil chog rnams kyi brgyud pa'ang gong dang 'dra'o/ /dpa' bo grub pa'i rgyud kyi TI ka'i brgyud pa
ni/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ shangs pa bsod nams rin chen/ slob dpon gzungs 'dus/ rin po che bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan po shes rab rdo
rje nas/ chos rje bla ma dam pa la'o/ /brtag pa gnyis pa'i rnam bshad nyi ma'i 'od zer gyi brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun grags pa/ sa paNDi ta/ 'phags pa/
khu dbon gnyis ka las shangs pa bsod nams rin chen/ sras kun rin/ shes rab rdo rje nas/ chos rje bla ma dam pa la'o/ /rab gnas bzang po drug pa/ dus tha ma'i cho ga bstod
pa daNDa kakye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi bkra shis rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi ta/ dbon 'phags pa rin po che/ cog ro ston gzhon/ chos brtson/
sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje nas/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa la'o/ /'dod pa'i rgyal po dmar po'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje myu gus mdzad
pa'i TI ka'i brgyud pa ni/ sa

skya pa chen po/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paNDi ta/ khams pa dbon po/ rje btsun rgwa lo/ A ka ra/ sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan po shes rab rdo rje nas/ chos rje bla ma
dam pa la'o/ /tshogs kyi bdag po'i sgrub thabs che chung gi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paNDi ta/ skyob pa dpal/ gzhon nu bkra shis/ rdo rje dpal/
gu rub shes rab rin chen nas/ sangs rgyas rin chen la'o/ /kye'i rdo rje'i mngon rtogs rgyas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan nas/ mkhan po shes rab
rdo rje la'o/ /klu'i bshad pa la sogs pa mngon rtogs/ bstod pa la sogs pa drug cu rtsa dgu'i brgyud pa ni/ sa skya pa chen po yab sras gsum/ chos rje sa skya paN chen/ dmar
chos kyi rgyal po/ gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ bka' bcu pa gzhon nu sengge/ shes rab rdo rje nas/ chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa la'o/ /gnyen gyi sgrol ma
yan lag drug pa'i brgyud lugs gcig ni/ klu sgrub nas/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal bde ba/ bi ma la gupta/ rin chen rdo rje/ rin chen grags pa/
ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ gnyen lo tsA ba/ gnam kha'u pa/ rje sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ byang chub dpal/ bde ba dpal/
bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu/ rin chen bsod nams grags pa/ rin chen grags tshul ba/ mkhan po shes rdo rje nas/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po pa

la'o/ /de dag rnams las mkhan chen rgyal ba bzang po/ mkhan chen byang chub sengge/ thams cad mkhyen pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal
tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ dpal sa skya pa 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang
pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ mtshungs med nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ rin po che dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ chos kyi rje
rin po che don grub rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun grub pa khams ston nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /yang na yongs 'dzin
dkon mchog 'phel nas/ rje lha mchog sengge/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/
byams pa kun dga' bkra shis man 'dra'o/ /gnyis pa chos rje khu dbon gnyis las/ dang po sa skya paNDi ta'i gsung rab rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs bla ma sa skya
paNDi ta chen po kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po nas/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa bsod nams
dpal/ 'jam dbyangs bla ma don yod rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon 'dul ba 'dzin pa/ chos rje byang chub sengge/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga'
bzang po/ rgyal

tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa skya pa 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje shar khang pa shes
rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ rje nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ chos kyi rje don grub
rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun grub pa khams ston nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams nas/ shar khang
pa shes rab rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /yang na 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel/ rje lha mchog sengge/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang man
'dra'o/ /!/ /gnyis pa 'gro ba'i mgon po 'phags pa rin po che blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i gsung rab rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che
nas/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma don yod rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon 'dul ba 'dzin pa/ chos rje byang chub sengge/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/
rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ sa skya pa 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon
mchog lhun grub/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ rje btsun nam mkha' sangs

rgyas/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ chos rje rin po che don grub rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun grub pa khams ston nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag bande tshul khrims
rin chen la stsal to/ /yang na dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ shar khang ba shes rab rgyal mtshan/ nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra'o/ /yang bka' 'bum gyi brgyud pa lugs gcig
ni/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ bla ma dpal ldan sengge/ bla ma don yod rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /yang na dkon mchog 'phel/
rje lha mchog sengge/ dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /!/ /kun mkhyen g.yag pa dang paN chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas 'jam mgon sa skya
paNDi ta'i bstod pa dang rjes su 'brel ba'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor byin rlabs kyi tshul du nos shing / bstod pa chos rgyal ma/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi yi ge g.yag phrug mi pham
sangs rgyas dpal gyis mdzad pa/ byin rlabs kyi yi ge paN chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa/ sa skya khri chen ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad pa'i 'jam
dbyangs bla sgrub tshigs bcad mchan bu ma rnams kyi lung dang bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya paN chen/ kun mkhyen g.yag mi pham chos kyi bla ma/ rong
ston shes bya kun rig kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel/ kun dga' chos bzang / 'jam dbyangs chos rje/ rab 'byams nor bu phun tshogs/ paN chen lha dbang blo gros/ gnas rab 'byams
pa byams

pa phun tshogs/ nags dgon pa sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ nags dgon pa sbyin pa grags pa/ sa skya pa sngags 'chang thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams
dbang phyug de sras sngags 'chang bla ma ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des bdag bande tshul khrims
rin chen la'o/ /yang na sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ rdo rje 'chang bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ kun mkhyen e waM pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag la'o/ /yang na rong ston
nas/ dge ba rgyal mtshan/ 'bras mo ba bsod nams rgya mtsho/ mdo khams pa yon tan rgya mtsho/ drin chen tshe dbang bkra shis/ rje tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse/ dbang phyug
rab brtan/ ngag dbang chos grags/ sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams man 'dra/ yang na ngag dbang chos grags/ ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis so/ /yang
she'u ris blo gros rgyal mtshan nas/ nags dgon pa sbyin pa grags pa las brgyud pa yang mthong ngo / /ring brgyud ni sa skya paNDi ta/ bla mchod gong ma tog ti shrI grags
pa 'od zer/ sru lung kun dga' smon lam/ byang pa dkon mchog grags pa/ kun mkhyen g.yag pa man 'dra'o/ /!/ /rgyal ba'i sras po 'jig rten dbang phyug thogs med bzang po dpal
ba'i bka' 'bum gyi skor la/ bshes gnyen thar pa dpal gyis bskul ba'i don du mdzad pa'i 'jam dbyangs 'khon ston thugs rje rin chen gyi

bstod pa sngon sbyangs ma/ byang sems rin chen mgon gyi bstod pa rin po che'i cod paN nam spyi gtsug nyi zla ma/ yang de'i bstod pa dad pa skyed byed mkhyen rab ma/ mkhan chen
byang chub rtse mos bskul ba ltar mdzad pa'i snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa dpang lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa'i gsol 'debs sku tshe dpag med ma/ bshes gnyen 'jam
dbyangs dkar pos bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i chos rje bu ston rin po che thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsol 'debs tshogs gnyis ma/ bshes gnyen mi nyag blo ldan dpal dang slob dpon
dpal ldan ye shes gnyis kyis bskul ngor mdzad pa'i dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi gsol 'debs legs rgyu dge tshogs ma/ bya bral ba dpal rin gyis bskul
ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i phyag chen lhan cig skyes sbyor gyi brgyud 'debs gnas spyi gtsug ma/ dmar khrid brgyud pa'i bla ma la phyag 'tshal ba shes bya ma lus ma/ bshes gnyen
shes rab bzang pos bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i theg pa chen po blo sbyong gi brgyud 'debs tshogs gnyis rab rdzogs ma/ rten 'brel snying po'i brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs theg
bde ma/ bcu gcig zhal gyi smyung gnas brgyud pa la phyag 'tshal ba 'gro kun ma/ don yod zhags pa lha lnga brgyud pa dang bcas pa la bstod pa 'gro ba'i skyabs gcig ma/ sems
tsam lugs kyi byang sems sdom pa'i brgyud 'debs mkhyen brtse ma/ bla ma se ston gyis bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i dbu ma lugs kyi smon 'jug sems bskyed kyi brgyud 'debs shes
bya ma lus ma/ byams chos pa byang chub rgyal mtshan gyi ngor mdzad

pa'i bla chen lugs kyi bsnyen rdzogs sdom pa'i brgyud 'debs thams cad mkhyen pa ma/ bshes gnyen shAkya ye shes kyi ngor mdzad pa'i sum pa lo tsA'i snyan brgyud kyi brgyud 'debs
zag med ma/ skyid sdug lam khyer gyi brgyud 'debs rig pa'i gnas lnga ma/ bla ma se ston gyis bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i snying po don gsum gyi brgyud 'debs rab mdzes
ma/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas la bstod pa rgyal ba mnyes byed shar phyogs ma/ mkhan chen bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nus mdzad pa'i chog khrigs ltar sman bla bde gshegs brgyad
kyi lha tshogs rnams kyi bstod pa rgyal ba mnyes par byed pa'i mchod pa bla med gser mdog ma/ de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi sngon gyi smon lam gyi khyad par rgyas pa'i
mdo'i gleng gzhi las byung ba'i byang chub sems dpa' bcu drug gi bstod pa mkhyen rab ma/ sman bla de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi 'khor gyi lha tshogs la phyag 'tshal ba bcom
ldan ma/ jo bo skor ba rnams kyi don du mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das la bstod pa dang po byang chub ma/ bshes gnyen dpal ldan ye shes kyi ngor mdzad pa'i 'jam
dpal dbyangs kyi bstod pa dus gsum rgyal ba ma/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi bstod pa tshig rgyan me tog gi phreng ba mtshan dpe cha shas ma/ yang de nyid la
bstod pa shlau ka nyi shu rtsa lnga pa/ bcom ldan 'das byams pa mgon po la bstod cing gsol ba gdab pa stobs bcu ma/ bcom ldan 'das ma sgrol ma la bstod pa mkhyen brtse ma/
rang gzhan la phan pa'i don du mdzad pa'i rgyal sras

lag len ma/ gnyen po bsten pa'i tshigs su bcad pa tshul bzhin yid byed ma/ sdig spong dge sgrub la bskul ba dge ba dge bshes ma/ chos la bskul ba'i gtam rin po che'i rgyan
gser gyi mchod sdong ma/ rang gi sems la gros 'debs pa gang zhig skyon bral ma/ rang la gros 'debs pa'i gtam ang drug ma/ slob ma rnams la snying gtam du gsungs pa dpag yas
mkhyen brtse ma/ rang la bskul ba mkhyen brtse nus pa ma/ rang la bskul ba sngar spyad bde sdug ma/ rang gi sems la 'dri bar bskul ba nyon mongs dug lnga ma/ sgo yig dang
po bdag la phrad 'dod ma/ sgo yig gnyis pa bdag ni sngon las ma/ smon 'jug gi sems bskyed pa'i cho ga jo bo chen po'i gzhung las ji ltar byung ba bzhin mdzad pa/ jo bo
chen pos mdzad pa'i rjes su 'brangs te bdag nyid kyis byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa'i cho ga 'am sems bskyed dang sdom pa rang gis blang ba'i cho ga dge ba'i bshes
gnyen 'jam dpal rdo rje snying pos bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i slob dpon chen po zhi ba lha lugs kyi smon 'jug byang chub kyi sems bskyed pa'i cho ga smyung bar gnas pa'i
cho ga thugs rje chen po'i sgrub thabs byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lam chen/ las dang po pa 'ga' zhig gi don du gsungs pa'i thugs rje chen po'i sgom bzlas bsdus pa/ rnal
'byor pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i blo sbyong don bdun ma'i khrid yig rten 'brel snying po'i khrid dmigs pa zur 'debs gsum dang bcas pa/ dge
ba'i bshes gnyen kun legs pa'i ngor mdzad pa'i

skyid sdug lam khyer gyi khrid/ ngan song sbyong ba'i mngon rtogs shin tu bsdus pa/ bya bral ba dpal 'byor bzang pos bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i 'od dpag med kyi bla ma'i rnal
'byor/ bya bral ba dpal 'byor bzang po'i ngor gnang ba'i thugs rje chen po'i gtor ma/ bla na med pa'i byang chub thob par 'dod pa'i gang zag rnams kyi chos spyod kyi rim
pa la skyabs 'gro/ zas kyi sgo nas tshogs gsog pa/ yan lag bdun pa/ gtor ma brgya rtsa/ yi dwags kyi chu sbyin/ dbyu gu drug cu rtsa bzhi/ khrul gtor dzam lha'i chu sbyin/
dkar cha bzhi/ sAtstsha gdab pa'i rim pa/ bla ma la gsol ba gdab pa/ yang dag pa'i don spros bral bsgom pa/ rgyal mtshan dpal gyis bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i byang sems
rin chen mgon gyi nang rten dkar chagabasod nams 'od zer gyi don du mdzad pa'i lam rim rgyas pa chos tshul bzhin du nyams su len pa'i man ngag pha jo g.yung drung dpal
gyi don du mdzad pa'i lam rim bsdus pa yang dag sgrub pa/ yang de'i don du mdzad pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa las gsungs pa'i yan lag bdun pa/ la shing
mkhan po shes rab grub kyis bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i zhal gdams tshul gnas ma/ bshes gnyen rab rtse nam mkha' grub la gdams pa'i blo sbyong phar phyin drug ldan ma/ yang
de la gsungs pa'i zhal gdams thugs rje chen po ma/ stag lung pa shAkya dpal bzang po la gsungs pa'i zhal gdams shAkya bstan 'dzin ma/ yang de la gsungs pa'i zhal gdams
chos brgyad lam du slong

ba/ yang de la gdams pa'i sbyor dngos rjes gsum tshang ba'i blo sbyong dal 'byor rnyed dka' ma/ stag lung ka drug pa la gsungs pa'i zhal gdams rgyal ba rgya mtsho ma/ si tu
chen po la nag can zhig skyob pa'i phyir du phul ba'i phrin yig mchod gnod ma/ bla ma rdzogs chen pa chos nyid rgyal mtshan gyi dris lan dkon mchog ma/ bshes gnyen dpal
ldan ye shes kyis bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i gnod byed la phan gdags pa'i dam bca' dang smon lam sngon bcom ma/ lhag bsam zla ba ches pas bskul nas dam chos tshul bzhin sgrub
pa'i thabs yon tan 'od zer ma/ bsod nams dpal gyis bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i lta sgom spyod 'bras gzhi lam 'bras bu'i ngos 'dzin thugs rje chen po ma/ drung nas pa'i
dris lan bsam mi khyab/ rgyal sras kyi spyod pa la bslab pa'i smon lam bdag gam bdag bshes ma/ rigs dang bsod nams thugs dgongs phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pa byams chen
par phul ba'i zhu phrin/ chen po bsod nams bzang po'i thugs dam bskul ba sngon chad bsod nams ma/ byang pa dpon shAkya bzang po zhabs bsnyun pa'i dus gdams pa/ stag lung
sangs rgyas dpal la dam bca' brtan pa'i don du gdams pa gnod byed ma/ slob dpon nam mkha' rin chen dpal bzang po la gdams pa bde lam ma/ des bskul ba'i phar phyin drug
gi ngos 'dzin yon tan dkyil 'khor ma/ rong po chos blo'i don du mdzad pa'i dkon mchog gi ngos 'dzin sgrib gnyis ma/ bon po khyi thul gyi sems la phan pa'i gdams pa/ mkhan
po lo tsA ba byang chub rtse mo'i dris lan rje

mnyam med ma/ sa skyar dge bshes shig gis dris lan nad la sogs pa lam du 'khyer tshul bdag zhen ma/ dge bshes shAkya bsod nams la gdams pa shAka seng ma/ slob dpon nam mkha'
dpal gyi phrin lan/ de la gdams pa dam chos mthar thug rin chen phreng ba phrin las bzang po ma/ gnas rnying pa rgyal dbang la gdams pa blo dkon mchog ma/ slob dpon chen
po grags pa rin chen la gdams pa bslab gsum ma/ slob dpon ldong ston gyis bskul ba la brten nas gdams pa phan bde ma/ slob dpon chos blo dbon po kun dga' rgyal mtshan la
gdams pa shes bya ma lus ma/ de la gdams pa chos kyi blo gros ma/ yang de nyid chos la bskul phyir thogs med ces byas sbyar ba/ mkhan chen gro sa ba la phul ba'i zhu phrin
yang dag ma/ slob dpon chos mchog la phul ba'i zhu phrin/ de nyid shig nad kyis bsnyun dus su phul ba'i zhu phrin/ bla ma spo tog pa'i don du gdams pa dal 'byor rin chen
ma/ sbud skra'i rtogs ldan bsod nams rin chen gyi dam bca' bzhi po brtan pa'i don du mdzad pa dngos grub rtsa ba ma/ 'od zer bzang po la gdams pa nyes pa'i 'byung gnas
ma/ yang mgon gdan sa pa bla ma ri pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan gyi thugs dam gsal 'debs dal 'byor rin chen ma/ rtsibs ri ba slob dpon gzhon nu byang chub kyi dam bca' brtan
pa'i don du mdzad pa gzhan phan ma/ sgom chen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan la gdams pa chos kun ma/ khams pa blo gros dpal la gdams pa dal 'byor mi lus ma/ mi nyag rgyal mtshan
'bum gyi

don du gdams pa dal 'byor rnyed dka' ma/ mi nyag bla ma rab ston 'jam dbyangs grags pa la gdams pa snyigs dus ma/ rin po che skyob pa dpal la gdams pa sems rtog med ma/ rgyal
sras lag len gyi pha yul spong ba'i skabs su blang dor byed pa dang brjed pa'i gti mug mun nag can gnyis po gang yin la 'ga' zhig ma 'cham par rgyal btsugs pa yin zer
nas dris ba'i lan/ nam mkha' bzang pos dris pa'i lan dkon mchog ma/ dge slong chos dbang rin chen grogs mched gnyis kyi phrin lan/ bshad gsar ba rnams kyi don du mdzad pa'i
tshogs kyi mol gtam/ ma Ni ba zla bzang gi drang po'i gtam/ bya bral ba rin chen dpal gyis bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i bsngo ba yon bshad/ dpon rin chen bzang po'i don
du mdzad pa'i smon lam bdag gi skye zhing ma/ khams pa ma Ni pas bskul ba'i ngor mdzad pa'i smon lam bdag ni byang chub ma/ dpon rin gyi yum bar ma gser las bzhengs pa'i
rab gnas kyi don du mdzad pa'i bkra shis thugs dbang ma/ bshes gnyen rgyal mtshan dar ras rkyang ba'i kha chems dris lan gtum mo 'bar ba ma rnams kyi lung legs par thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ 'jig rten dbang phyug thogs med bzang po dpal/ /rnal 'byor dbang phyug lo chen byang chub rtse/ /grub pa'i dbang phyug dpal ldan buddha shrI/ /mkhyen rab
dbang phyug ngor chen kun dga'i mtshan/ /thugs rje'i dbang phyug mus chen dkon rgyal zhabs/ /phrin las dbang phyug sangs rgyas rin chen dpal/ /mkhas pa'i dbang phyug dkon
mchog lhun grub zhabs/ /btsun pa'i dbang

phyug brang ti nam mkha' dpal/ /bzang po'i dbang phyug chos rje dpal grub pa/ /rgyal kun dbang phyug 'dren pa dpal mchog las/ /mkhyen  mkhan chen bkra shis lhun pa'i gsan yig
tu byung / rab dbang phyug sangs rgyas phun tshogs zhabs/ /grub pa'i dbang phyug kun spangs ku sa li/ /lung rtogs dbang phyug bkra shis lhun gyis grub/ /snyom las dbang
phyug tshul khrims rin chen la/ /yang na dbang phyug brgyad ldan dpal mchog zhabs/ /btsun pa'i dbang phyug bsod nams rgyal mtshan las/ /thugs rje'i dbang phyug bkra shis
lhun grub kyis/ /le lo'i dbang phyug tshul rin bdag la'o/ /yang na rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ /rgyal ba lha yi mchog gyur seng ge'i mtshan/ /kun mkhyen dkon mchog
lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /!/ /sgron ma'i bskal pa'i rnam par 'dren pa bcom ldan 'das shAkya seng ge'i lung rtogs kyi rgyal srid chen po skyong ba'i rgyal tshab dam pa mi
'phrogs pa'i mkhyen rab dang thugs rje tshad med pa'i bdag nyid rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po pa'i gsung rab rin po che'i glegs bam bzhi'i lung thob pa'i chos kyi rnam
grangs la/ rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa rnams la bstod pa/ shar chen la bstod pa lnga/ grub chen buddha shrI/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ mkhan chen bkra shis rin chen/ lo chen rin
chen bzang po/ rje sa skya pa chen po rnams la bstod pa re/ sdom gsum bla ma brgyud pa la phyag 'tshal ba/ lam zab brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ lam 'bras phyag mchod kyi kha skong
/ lam 'bras/ bsam mi khyab/ lhan cig

skyes grub/ mchod rten drung thob/ yi ge med pa/ padma pa'i lam/ gtum mo lam rdzogs/ yon po bsrang pa/ indra bhU ti'i lam ste lam skor dgu'i brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ bde mchog
rim lnga/ rtsa dbu ma'i ring brgyud/ rtsa dbu ma'i nye brgyud/ bde mchog dkar po/ ma hA mA yA/ spros med/ gsang 'dus rim lnga 'gos lugs/ rwa rtse sems 'dzin/ shin tu spros
med/ spyod 'jug zhen pa bzhi bral rnams kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje lha bcu dgu'i dkyil chog rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ shes phyin dkar mo/ 'dod
rgyal/ tshogs bdaga'achi bdag 'joms pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal lha dgu/ nor rgyun ma lha bcu dgu'i bstod pa smon lam dang bcas pa/ sa skya pa'i
bka' srung rnams te de rnams la bstod pa le tshan re/ yan lag bdun pa'i cho gas skya paNDi ta'i rnam thar gsung sgros ma/ grub chen buddha shrI'i rnam thar/ sa bzang 'phags
pa'i rnam thar/ rje nyid kyi gsan yig rgya mtsho/ lam 'bras chos 'byung rtsom 'phro/ bshad thabs gsang ba'i sgo 'byed/ zhus lan gsal ba'i sa bcad/ dbang bzhi'i rtogs
bskyed/ mngon rtogs tshul bzhi'i sdom tshigaphyi nang gi bskyed rim dbang dang bcas pa'i sdom tshiganang gi bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bir srung bar chad kun sel/ sku'i rnam 'gyur
drug gi zin bris/ bir srung thun mong ma yin pa'i byin rlabs bya tshul/ de'i nyams len/ de dang lam 'bras mtshan mtshon sbyar ba/ bir srung gsar ma/ lus dkyil/ rtsod
spong che

chung / rgyud gsum gnod 'joms rtsa 'grel/ zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang gi sa mtshams rnam par bshad pa/ kye rdo rje'i rgyud kyi byung tshul dang bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar ngo
mtshar rgya mtsho/ brtag gnyis kyi 'gyur chad bsabs pa shlau ka gnyis/ brtag gnyis kyi 'grel pa'i dkar chagakye rdor Dombi lugs kyi sgrub thabs/ phrin yig dbang po rdo
rje/ gzhal yas khang gi tshad rnam par gzhag pa/ 'phar ma gnyis kyi don bshad pa/ dpal kye rdo rje'i sgrub pa'i thabs kyi rgya cher bshad pa bskyed rim gnad kyi zla zer/
gtor chog gi 'grel pa/ mtsho skyes lugs dang Dombi lugs kyi sgrub thabs dang dkyil chog gi tho yig sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi bsdus don/ bstod pa nyi shu pa'i 'grel pa/
mtsho skyes lugs kyi maNDal mchod chog 'dod rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ shes phyin dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ gur rigs bsdus kyi sbyin sreg gar gyi shan 'byed/ sangs rgyas kyi gar/
phyogs bzhi gtor ma'i gtang thabs/ chos skyong gi man ngag rnams kyi dkar chagamagon rkyang gi sgrub thabs rgyud 'grel las phyung ba/ lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / gtor chog
dgra las rnam rgyal/ gtor sgrub kyi man ngag g.yul las rnam rgyal/ bka' srung rnams kyi thugs dam bskang ba'i cho ga kye rdo rje lha bcu bdun ma'i sgrub thabs/ sampu
Ta rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sgrub thabs/ yang dag sbyor ba'i rgyud las 'byung ba'i 'byung po thams cad pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga rdo rje dbyings kyi mchod pa'i cho
ga dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga sbyin sreg bkra shis dge

legs nyi ma rnams dang / tshogs kyi 'khor lo gsang ba kun rgyan/ yang tshogs kyi 'khor lo kun bzang rnam rol/ bde mchog bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga bsod nams rab rgyas/ bde mchog
'khor lo'i pho brang gi rnam gzhaganA ro mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs/ mkha' spyod kyi man ngag zab mo/ bde mchog dkar po'i sgrub thabs byin rlabs cho ga dang bcas pa/
rdo rje lha mo'i tshe sgrub/ lwa wa pa'i lugs kyi bde mchog sbyangs pa'i yon tan lha bcu gsum pa'i cho ga la dgos pa'i zin bris/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sgrub thabs dang /
nag po pa'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba'i khyad par/ za byed rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi sgrub thabs dngos grub rin po
che'i mdzod/ gtso bo yab yum gyi sgrub thabs/ de'i sngags phreng gsang sngags rin po che'i mdzod mtshan ma/ de'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dbang gi snye ma/ mchod phreng bsod
nam rin po che'i mdzod/ gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi sgrub thabs dngos grub rgya mtsho/ de'i gtor chog mchod phreng / rdo rje sems dpa'i mchod chog
dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga sbyin sreg rab gnas/ bkra shis dge legs rgya mtsho/ gsang 'dus kyi bskyed rim shin tu rnal 'byor gyi khyad par/ gsang 'dus rim lnga'i khrid yig zung
'jug gsal ba/ rdo rje phreng bar gsungs pa'i sa chog dgra nag gi rgyud nas gsungs pa'i char 'bebs/ 'jigs byed kyi gtor chog 'jigs byed kyi rdzogs rim/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i
sgrub thabs/ de'i dag pa/ sgrub

thabs kyi lung sbyor/ dkyil chog spros med mdzes rgyan/ kun rig gi dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi sgrub thabs sgrib pa rnam sel/ kun rig gi cho ga gzhan phan mtha' yas/ de la
nye bar mkho ba'i cho ga cha gsum gtor ma/ dkyil 'khor sgo sbrags kyi bshad pa/ spyod rgyud spyi'i rnam gzhagabya rgyud spyi'i rnam gzhagami 'khrugs pa'i sgo nas gshin po
rjes su gzung ba'i cho ga 'phags pa 'od zer dri med kyi dkyil chog dri med lha nyi shu rtsa lnga'i sgrub thabs/ a ra pa tsa na'i rjes gnang / 'od dpag med kyi tshe sgrub/
sengge sgra/ sna tshogs yum/ rma bya chen mo/ so sor 'brang ma/ 'byung po 'dul byed/ rta mgrin rnams kyi sgrub thabs/ bde gshegs brgyad kyi mchod pa'i chog sgrigasems
bskyed rang gis blang ba'i cho ga dbu ma lugs/ gso sbyong rang gis blang ba'i cho ga mchod sbyin chen po'i zin bris/ gtor chen gyi dbang gzugs/ gser sku rdo rje 'chang bzhengs
tshul/ gnod sbyin 'khor lo'i sngags la zhus dag mdzad pa/ dge tshul gyi rags sdom bcu'i bslab bya/ bka' 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chagabastan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag
mdor bsdus gcig rdo rje theg pa'i bstan 'gyur gyi dkar chagamatshan nyid bstan 'gyur gyi dkar chagarje btsun gong ma gsum gyi bka' 'bum gyi dkar chagaslob ma rnams la
spring ba'i yi ge sa bzang pa bsod nams dpal/ lo tsA ba rdo rje dpal/ dge 'dun mgon/ a mo gha/ bla chen chos rin pa/ gling 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ bla ma

bsam grub rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon bsam bzang / dbu ma pa shes rab rgya mtsho/ mdo stod pa bshes gnyen dge bzang rnams kyis dris lan re/ sde snod 'dzin pa ratna shrI la gdams
pa/ gsang sngags pa kun dga' gzhon nu la gdams pa/ bla ma sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la gdams pa dang bsngags pa gnyis/ byang chub sems dpa' bsod nams rin chen la gdams pa
shlau ka gcig rgya rong pa bkra shis dpal la gdams pa/ sgrub pa po blo bzang la gdams pa/ nyag re sangs grags la gdams pa/ paNDi ta nags kyi rin chen la springs pa/ bal
yul ye rang gi paNDi ta shrI ma no bo dhi yab sras la springs pa/ dpon po rgyal mtshan dpal yab yum sras bcas la gdams pa/ ya tshe rgyal po hasti rA dza yab yum sras bcas
la gdams pa/ de'i blon po la gdams pa shlau ka gcig a ya dbang phyug bkra shis la gdams pa/ dpon rgan thar pa ye shes la gdams pa/ slob dpon bzod chen la gdams pa/ phyi
nang gi yas gtam/ theg pa chen po'i smon lam/ gser 'od dam pa las btus pa'i smon lam/ der ma thus pa chos rje shar pa'i rnam thar/ 'di man gsan yig dbang gi rgyal por ma
bzhugs pas lung rgyun yod med brtag mngon byang gi bshad pa/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i rnam bshad/ rnal 'byor rgyud kyi spyi rnam rtsom 'phro/ kye rdo rje'i mngon rtogs bsdus
pa/ bka' shog thor bu ba kha yar rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog
'phel/ rgyal ba lha mchog

sengge/ rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas sengge/ brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / mun chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' sangs rgyas/
mtshungs med bsod nams rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ bstan pa'i sgron me sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ kun mkhyen dpal ldan
chos skyong / de dbon mtshungs med rin chen mchog grub/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la bka' drin du stsal to/ /!/ /zab cing rgya che'i chos kyi 'dren byed rnam
par  'di de sngon ma thob kyang thob 'gyur gyi dbang gi bris/ yangs pa mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i bka' 'bum gyi lung thob pa'i chos
kyi rnam grangs la/ bka' 'bum gyi dkar chag rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po (ba)la bstod pa sde snod ma/ yang de la bstod
pa (ra)gnyis/ sdom gsum brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs kyi kha skong snga phyi gnyis/ gsung ngag brgyud 'debs sogs tshan pa lnga'i kha skong / sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal
mchog la bstod pa gnyis/ dkon mchog gsum la bstod pa/ bstan srung rnams la bstod pa/ mkhan po bo dhi satwa/ chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan/ jo bo dI paM ka ra gsum
la bstod pa re/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims ()kyi rnam thar/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun ()dga' bzang po'i rnam thar kha skong dang bcas pa/ gsan yig mthong ba dad 
'di ngor pa'i gsan yig

rnams su ma byung / 'jug sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang rgya mtsho'i gsan tho/ 'dul ba'i brgyud yig dpal kye rdo rje'i mngon rtogs ()yan lag drug pa/ 'byung po thams cad ()pa'i
gtor ma'i cho ga bar chad kun sel/ lus dkyil gyi nyams len ()lam dus kyi dbang dang bcas pa/ dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi dbang chu ()gsal ba'i me long / kye rdo
rje'i sta gon gyi skabs ()kyi swa shing sogs kyi dgos pa nyung ngu / kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi dbang gi chu bo chen ()mo'i sa chog gi skabs kyi lhan thabs/ lam 'bras
bu dang bcas pa'i gnad kyi gsung sgros zin bris/ gsung ngag rin po che'i dmigs rim gyi yi ge bde mchog nag po pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i lhan thabs/ dpal 'khor lo bde
mchog gi bskyed rim nyams su len pa'i gnad zab mo/ rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i bshad srol las dril bu pa'i zhabs kyi dgongs pa'i lus dkyil bshad pa'i zin bris/ lo nag dril gsum
gang  'di rmor gyi gsan yig na ma byung / zag gcig gis nyams su len tshul/ dril bu pa'i dbang gi chu bo'i skabs kyi bum bskyed gsal bar bya ba'i lhan thabs/ nag po dkyil
chog la dgos pa'i lhan thabs/ bde gshegs sa gzung gi lag  'di rmor pa'i gsan yig na ma byung / len/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i
gsal byed kha skong / bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bskyed rim gyi bshad pa/ zin bris 'di'i nang du 'jigs byed la dngos yum med pa'i sgrub byed mang du snang ngo
/ /thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor gyi sgrub

thabs/ bcom ldan 'das kun rig gi cho ga gzhan la phan pa'i 'od zer gyi dgongs pa'i lag len 'di'i nang du sngags spel tshig can zhes pa tshe 'das sam chai mo sarba karma a wa
ra Na bi shuddhe swA hA zhes brjod par bshad de/ jo bo chen po'i phyag na shog dril zhig 'dug pa bstan par zhus pa'i nang du gtsug tor dri med/ mi 'khrugs pa/ kun rig gi
rtsa sngags rnams 'dug par bikShu dI paM ka ra sarba karma a wa ra Na zhes sogs snang zhes khungs 'dren par mdzad snang ngo / /phyag na rdo rje 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i bsnyen
pa dang tshe sgrub kyi man ngag zab mo/ sAtstsha'i rab gnas bsdus pa/ mkhan po boddhi sa twa'i dgongs don gsal byed gtsug tor dri med kyi cho ga'i lag len gyi rim pa/
gcod skor gsum gyi nyams  'di ngor pa'i gsan yig rnams na ma byung / len/ skyabs 'gro yan lag brgyad pa/ smon lam lnga pa/ rnal 'byor bla med nas gsungs pa'i bskyed pa'i

sbyong gi sngon 'gro'i rim pa/  'di gnyis ngor pa'i gsan yig rnams su ma byung / dngos gzhi byang chub kyi sems sbyang pa'i gdams ngag gdams pa phran bu'i skor la/ rje
rang la bskul ba'i gdams pa/ gso sbyong rang gi blang ba'i cho ga gro sa mkhan po shes rab bzang po'i dris lan/  ngor pa'i gsan yig rnams su 'di gnyis ma byung / bdag chen
rgya gar ba'i dris lan/ dgon pa bde ba can pa la spring pa'i yi ge dge bshes nam mkha' dpal

bzang la gdams pa/ yang dge bshes nam mkha' dpal bzang la gdams pa snying gtam rin chen ma/ bla ma nam mkha' dpal bzang la gdams pa gnyis/ bla ma blo rin la gdams pa/ bla ma
chos rin la springs pa/ pa nam nang so kun dga' chos skyong la gdams pa/ slob dpon chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyi snyan du phul ba/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po rab 'byams sangs

kyi brgyud pa ni/ mus chen nas/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ de dbon kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba kun dga' chos grags/ rdo rje
