rgyal po bsod nams sengge'i zab mo sngags kyi phyogs gtso bor gyur pa'i gsung rab kyi lung thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ bla ma rin 'byung la gsol ba 'debs pa (mai)bsod
nams rab rgyas/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang la bstod pa (mai)bstod dbyangs rgya mtsho rnam par rol pa/ yang de la bstod pa lha bcas ma/ rje mus pa la bstod pa rnam thar
(mai)dang mthun pa ngo mtshar chu rgyun/ yang de'i kha skong gang la yon tan ma/ yang de la bstod pa rin chen dkon mchog ma/ blo gros dbang phyug la bstod pa zab yangs blo

gros ma/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug la bstod pa dpal ldan kun dga' ma/ gung ru shes rab bzang po la bstod pa (mai)rgya chen shes bya ma'am phrin las char 'bebs ma/ kun
mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel la bstod pa kA li la spel ba/ yang de la bstod pa dpal ldan lha dbang ma/ chos rje gung ru la (mai)bstod pa shes bya ma/ 'phags pas mdzad pa'i
kye rdo rje'i 'grel (mai)pa lugs kyi brgyud 'debs kha skong / sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i bde mchog brgyud 'debs kha skong / sher phyin brgyud 'debs 'gro bla ma/ tshad ma'i brgyud
'debs mtha' dag ma/ byams mgon la bstod pa theg mchog gnad kyi sgo byed/ sgrol ma la bstod pa dngos grub rgya mtsho ma/ gur mgon lha brgyad la bstod pa rnam par rgyal
ba'i rnga chen/ rnal 'byor chen po'i sdom pa'i gnad bye brag tu bshad pa zab mo bdud rtsi'i nying khu 'chi ba med pa'i go 'phang sbyin pa/ zab don bdud rtsi'i nying khu'i
rnam bshad bdud rtsi spel ba/ phar phyin gyi mchod yar/ rnam 'grel gyi mchod yar/ brda 'grol nges pa'i dpal gter/ rje mus pa'i rnam thar rgyas pa (mai)ngo mtshar rgya
mtsho/ de'i kha (mai)skong dang bcas pa/ lam 'bras brgyud pa'i bris thang gi dkar chagagazhal yas khang gi chag tshad sgo sbrags sogs kyi bshad pa le tshan gnyis/ gur rigs
(mai)bsdus kyi sgrub thabs dngos grub rgya mtsho/ dkyil chog bde chen rgya mtsho/ sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi drwa migabade mchog chos 'byung (mai)/ sgrub thabs (mai)mngal
sgong sbyong byed/ nag po rim bzhi'i gsung sgros ma'i khrid yig rnal

'byor ma'i sgrub (mai)thabs/ sbyin (mai)sreg tshes bcu'i (mai)mchod pa/ mar me'i sbyin (mai)sreg bde mchog lU hi pa'i rnam bshad 'dod dgu sbyin pa'i dpag bsam ljon pa/ gsang
'dus 'jam rdor gyi sgrub thabs kun tu bzang po'i nyi 'od/ de'i dkyil chog ye shes rnam rol/ de'i phyi rol tshogs bsags kyi cho ga gtor chog phrin las rnam rol/ 'jig rten
dbang phyug gi khyad par sgrub thabs kun tu bzang po'i nyi 'od kyi 'grel pa lam bzang gsal ba'i snang ba/ gsang 'dus rim lnga'i khrid yig zung 'jug gsal ba'i sgron me/
rdo rje theg pa la log smra tshar gcod pa rig pa'i mtshon cha/ spros med rgyun gyi rnal 'byor/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub dkyil/ mngon par byang chub pa'i tshul la grangs
nges phye ba/ ngan song sbyong rgyud kyi TI ka (wa)gzhan phan kun khyab/ kun rig rtsod spong (wa)gzhan phan gnod 'joms/ kun rig gi zhi ba'i sbyin sreg (wa)'jig rten dbang
phyug gi gzhung bzhi nyams su len tshul/ sdom gsum (sa)rab dbye'i bsdus don/ sdom pa (sa)gsum gyi rab tu dbye ba'i rnam bshad gsung rab dgongs gsal/ sdom gsum gyi rab
(sa)tu dbye ba'i spyi don legs bshad 'od stong 'phro ba/ sdom pa gsum gyi rab (sa)tu dbye ba'i dris lan sdom gsum 'khrul spong / sdom pa gsum gyi rab tu dbye ba'i (sa)kha
skong legs bshad 'od kyi snang ba/ de'i bsdus (sa)don/ nyi zla sengge'i dris lan/ mdo khams pa dbang phyug rgyal mtshan gyi dris lan/ sngags 'chang ratna shrI'i dris lan/
ga zi rin chen dpal

gyi dris lan/ mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi dris lan/ ldan ma shes rab sengge'i dris lan/ sgrub pa ba tshul khrims bzang po'i dris lan/ dris lan (sa)padmo bzhad pa/
bka' bcu pa rin chen byang chub kyi dris lan/ blo sbyong zhen pa bzhi bral/ mdo khams la 'bul sdud gnang ba'i bka' shogagyad gnyer dger gsum la bskur ba/ sa skya pa chen
po'i nang rten dkar chagakarma mi pham mgon po'i bstod pa/ slob dpon kun dga' 'bum gyi bstod pa/ slob dpon sbyin bzang la bstod pa/ gling smad shes rab dpal ldan la bstod
pa/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi bstod pa/ paNDi ta grags pa rdo rje'i bstod pa/ rje rin po che sku skye ba'i bstod pa/ bde chen mkhan po'i bstod pa/ chu 'dus mkhas btsun
pa'i bstod pa/ sog po bka' bcu pa la bstod pa/ drung chen kun spangs pa la gdams pa/ go bo sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la gdams pa/ rtags 'jug gi TI kasmon lam bcu pa/ smon
lam bdun cu pa/ bsngo ba mdor bsdus pa/ dpon drung g.yung pa la gnang ba'i bka' shogagasung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i chos 'byung gsung ngag bstan pa (mai)rgyas
pa'i nyi 'od kyi kha skong dang bcas pa/ snang ba (mai)gsum gyi skabs su nye bar mkho ba'i gsal byed/ dpal kye rdo rje'i (mai)lus kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rnam bshad
bde chen bcud kyi snying po/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba'i lam spyi'i rnam gzhagalam dus (mai)kyi dbang bskur tshul/ lam dus kyi dbang (mai)chog gso byed tshul/ bi srung
thun mong (mai)ma yin pa'i byin rlabs byed

tshul/ rnam 'joms bir lugs (mai)kyi byin rlabs byed tshul/ gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gzhung bshad a seng ma'i rnam bshad/ bdag med ma'i sgrub dkyil
gyi tho yig kye rdo rje'i rnal 'byor la (mai)brten pa'i rab gnas dge legs rgya mtsho/ dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi mngon rtogs man ngag snang ba/ kye rdo rje'i mchod
gtor gyi rnal 'byor/ kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi bskyed rim gyi bshad (mai)pa man ngag gi gsal byed/ dpal kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs kyi rgya cher bshad pa bskyed rim
gnad kyi zla zer la rtsod pa (wa)spong ba gnad kyi gsal byed/ brda 'grol nges pa'i dpal ster/ dbang chu chen mo'i sa chog gi gsal byed dang / rgyud kyi tshig don la (mai)dogs
gcod/ sampu Ta'i bsdus don tshigs bcad ma/ dpal kye rdo rje'i dbang gi chu bo chen po'i rnam par (mai)bshad pa bde chen rgya mtsho/ lam 'bras bla ma brgyud pa la gsol
ba gdab pa'i rim pa/ a seng rdo rje brtan pas sku brnyen phul ba'i mtshon byed/ thub bstan na bzhugs pa'i gsung ngag brgyud pa'i bris sku'i ngos nas bshus pa'i gsung ngag
brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ rnam 'joms bir lugs (mai)kyi byin rlabs/ rje sa skya pa chen po'i bris sku'i nang rten gyi dkar chagarten rnying pa la bya (wa)ba'i argha'i cho
ga kye rdo rje'i rgyud dang mthun pa'i smon lam/ gsung ngag rin po che'i dmigs rim dang mthun pa'i smon lam phun (wa)tshogs dge legs ma/ bde ba can gyi smon lam (mai)mi
mjed ma ste chos tshan de rnams kyi lung thob pa

las mai'i rtags can ma gtogs pa'i yongs rdzogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ kun mkhyen chos kyi spyan ldan bsod nams sengge/ 'dren mchog dkon mchog 'phel ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon
mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / brtse chen smra ba'i nyi ma kun dga' bsod nams/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags/ dpal sa skya
pa chen po sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ mus pa grub pa'i dbang phyug bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa bzang
po rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ tshul khrims rin chen la'o/
/sa'i rtags can rnams kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ spro lung pa/ dkon mchog grags/ g.yag pa sangs rgyas dpal/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
/ mkhas pa gzhon nu sengge/ mun chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ gung ru shes rab bzang po/ kun mkhyen chos kyi rgyal po bsod nams sengge/ rje ratna wardha/ sangs rgyas
sengge/ ri khrod pa kun dga' mchog ldan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / brtse chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ mus chen
bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa bzang po rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ wa'i rtags can rnams kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ ngag dbang chos grags yan gong ltar

las/ de nas grub mchog ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mus chen bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen bha dra dhwa dza man 'dra/ rtse'i rtags can gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ kun dga' bsod nams
lhun grub nas/ mkhan chen ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rje/ 'khon bsod nams bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ maM g.yung drung can gyi rtags
can gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ mus chen bkra shis lhun grub yan gong yongs rdzogs ltar las/ de nas mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ gnyis ka las ngag dbang kun dga' lhun
grub/ grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho man 'dra/ mai'i rtags can rnams kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ thar rtse pa yan gong ltar las/ de las khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun
grub dang / ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka las mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/
grub dbang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ gnas gsar ba ngag dbang kun dga' legs 'byung / tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na dkon mchog lhun grub yan gong ltar las/ de nas dkon
mchog rgya mtsho/ she'u lo tsA ba/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po man 'dra'o/ /!/ /dus gsum rgyal ba'i gdung 'tshob byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mus pa sangs
rgyas rin chen gyi gsung 'bum yongs rdzogs kyi lung thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ thog mar rnam rgyal bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ mus chen dkon mchog

rgyal mtshan gyi bstod pa shlau ka gnyis/ kun mkhyen bsod nams sengge'i bstod pa shlau ka gnyis/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros la bstod pa shlau ka gsum/ shes rab blo gros
la bstod pa shlau ka gcig ri khrod pa kun dga' mchog ldan la bstod pa shlau ka gcig byams pa chos legs la bstod pa shlau ka gcig ngor chen lha mchog sengge dang mus chen
nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis la bstod pa shlau ka re re/ kun mkhyen bsod nams sengge'i rnam thar/ grub chen dkon mchog blo gros pa'i rnam thar bstod pa dang de'i 'grel pa gnyis
ka'i 'gor mkhyen pa'i ye shes zhes yod pa/ rje rin po che dkon mchog 'phel ba'i rnam thar yon tan mtha' yas/ lam zab bsdus pa'i  'di dpe ma 'byor nas lung ma thob/ nyams
len/ lam 'bras khrid yig dngos grub 'byung ba'i gter/ de'i kha skong shes rab ye shes kyi dbang gi lam phyag rgya'i rnal 'byor zhes sogs yod pa bcas/ rtsa ba'i ltung
ba 'khrul pa spong ba'i gnad kyi gsal byed/ rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi rnam par bshad pa'i zin bris/ dpal kye rdo rje'i rnam bshad snying po don gsal/ bcom ldan 'das kyi rtsa
ba'i sngags kyi bshad pa'i zin bris/ bdud rtsi ril bu bsgrub pa'i phyag len/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug lU hi pas mdzad pa'i dpal mngon par rtogs pa'i gsal byed 'gor/ tshad
med bzhi yi ngo bo zhal bzhis legs par mdzes byas shing zhes yod pa/ 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i sgrub thabs ma nor gsal ba'i sgron me/ bde mchog lU hi pa'i sgrub mchod
kyi ngag 'don zur 'debs/ bde mchog dkar po'i tshe sgrub/ dpal

gsang ba 'dus pa 'phags lugs kyi phyag len/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub dkyil gyi lhan thabs dang de'i bkra shis 'gor/ rje btsun 'jam rdor mi bskyod cod paN can zhes yod pa dang
shlau ka gsum/ sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor phyi ma bcu gcig gi bdag mdun bsgrub tshul/ sbyong rgyud nas gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang bskur ba'i phyag len/
de'i sta gon gyi zur 'debs/ dpal 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i ras bris la brten pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga phrin las kun khyab/ tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du slob ma dbang
bskur ba'i cho ga rin po che'i phreng ba/ rong ston chen po nas brgyud pa'i tshe sgrub khyad par can 'gor phyag 'tshal gyi tshig dang / 'dir tshe sgrub byed par 'dod
pas zhes dang / dkar gsum la brten te bsgrub par byas na tshe dang bsod nams dpag tu med pa 'phel bar 'gyur ro'i mtha' can/ tshe dpag med grub rgyal ma'i dbang chog 'gor
tshe sgrub khyad par 'di'i lo rgyus ni zhes yod pa/ sgrol ma dkar mo'i mngon rtogs dang / de'i rjes gnang bya tshul gnyis ka la kun mkhyen bsod nams sengge'i gsung la zin
bris su bris pa'i mtha' can/ 'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i mngon rtogs dang de'i bsnyen sgrub byed tshul dang bcas pa/ 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes  mngon rtogs sa paN
de yin/ gnang bya tshul/ phyag rdor u tsArYa'i rjes gnang byed tshul rjes spyi dang 'dra'o zab zab kyi mtha' can/ 'byung po 'dul byed kyi rjes gnang bya tshul/ mgon po lcam
dral gyi rjes gnang bya tshul 'gor bla ma yi dam chos skyong

la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po lcam dral gyi sogs dang bsrung ba dang bkra shis bya'o'i mtha' can/ dpal nag po chen po'i man ngag rtsa gsum la brten pa bsnyen
sgrub las gsum 'jam par bsgrub pa/ mgon po 'khor bcas kyi bsnyen sgrub las gsum rtsub par bsgrub pa/ mgon po 'khor rkyang gi rjes gnang bya tshul bsrung ba rnams bya'o'i
mtha' can/ gtor ma la brten nas dgra bsad pa til 'bru tsam yang med par byas par bsam mo'i mtha' can/ mgon po'i gzi brjid bskyed pa btsan po'i mkhar du 'jug pa thod
pa kha sprod kyi man ngag go'i mtha' can/ rmi lam ngan pa dang mtshan ma ngan pa zlog par byed pa dus tho rangs kyi dus su bya'o'i mtha' can/ brag rdzong  'khon nag zas su
za ba'i man ngag ma'i zhal shes zab mo 'di ni zab pas te srod thun gyi mjug tu ma chag par bsgom mo'i mtha' can/ dur khrod bdag po'i rjes gnang byed tshul gtor chog lam
srung dang bcas pa/ dpal ldan dud sol lha mo'i rjes gnang gtor chog dang bcas pa/ dud sol lha mo'i thugs dam bskang ba'i cho ga gnod sbyin pho mo'i sgrub yig rje btsun bla
ma dam pa rnams kyi drung du dam pa'i chos thos pa'i tho yig nyin zhag  'di ma byung / phrugs re'i nyams len gyi tho/ gcod khrid gdan thog gcig tu nyams su len tshul le
tshan gnyis kyi dang po la/ rmi lam sgyu ma lta bur spyod lam bya'o'i mtha' can dang / gnyis pa'i 'gor skyabs 'gro yan lag brgyad pa ni zhes dang / byang chub thob kyang
gnas gyur cig dang brgyud rim gyi mtha' can/ gcod skor gsum gyi khrid chung gcod skor gsum gyi

nyams su len tshul mdor bsdus te bris so'i mtha' can/ gling kha bde ba can na bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun rnams kyis kun spyod mdzad dgos tshul gyi bca' yig mdo khams kyi 'bul sdud
yi ge dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa 'bogs pa'i cho ga dang bcas pa de rnams kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ rgyal ba lha mchog sengge/ rdo rje 'chang
sangs rgyas sengge/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang nas bla ma gnyis tsam btsal/ de nas mus chen kun dga' rgya mtsho/  'di yod pa rgyus ldan gyi gsung las thos so/ /khams ston
bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ bla chen kun dga' tshe brtan/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la lhun grub steng gi phan bde gling bla
brang du stsal to/ /!/ /kun mkhyen nyi ma'i gnyen gyi lung rtogs chos kyi snang byed chen po/ ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum gyi lung thos
pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ 'dren mchog chos kyi rgyal po la bstod pa sgra rgyan me tog dkar po'i phreng ba/ yang de la bstod pa dngos grub kun 'byung / de la gsol ba
'debs pa bla ma rgyang 'bod/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen la bstod pa dad pa'i pho nya/ de la gsol ba 'debs pa bla ma rgyang 'bod/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub
la bstod pa ngo mtshar me tog gi phreng ba/ dpal sa skya lo tsA ba la bstod pa dad pa'i snye ma/ de la gsol ba 'debs pa bla ma rgyang 'bod/ rtsa ba'i bla ma ngor mus sa
gsum la gdung dbyangs kyi sgo nas gsol ba 'debs pa

snying gi thig le/ yang de gsum la gdung dbyangs kyi sgo nas gsol ba 'debs pa dad pa'i gsal 'debs/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa la phul ba'i zhu yig bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs
la phul ba'i zhu yig yul khyad par can la mchod brjod kyi tshig ngag gi 'dod 'jo/ phud mchod dgos 'dod kun 'byung / rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi sku yi rnam 'gyur drug
la nang gi rnam dag dang mthun par bstod pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang la snyan ngag 'khor lo'i sgo nas bstod pa bdud rtsi'i 'od can/ ri khrod pa kun dga' mchog ldan la bstod
pa byin rlabs myur 'jug rje lha mchog sengge la bstod pa mtshan rin po che'i phreng ba/ mkhas pa lha dbang blo gros la bstod pa rin po che'i mgul rgyan/ dpal sa skya pa'i
yab chos rgyud gsum man ngag dang bcas pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs byin rlabs myur du 'jug pa'i pho nya/ de'i kha skong shlau ka gcig lam zab brgyud 'debs kyi kha
skong / 'khor lo bde mchog gi bla ma brgyud pa la gsol ba 'debs pa byin rlabs char 'bebs/ shin tu spros med kyi brgyud 'debs 'od gsal snye ma/ tshe dpag med kyi bla ma brgyud
pa la gsol ba 'debs pa/ mgon po'i chos skor gyi brgyud 'debs phrin las myur 'grub/ byams pa'i rnam thar bstod pa byams chos kyi lam rim gyi sgo nas gsol ba 'debs pa
mi pham dgongs rgyan/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs la bstod pa yon tan me tog gi phur ma/ dbyangs can ma la bstod pa don rgyan rnam par bkod pa'i phreng ba/ sgrol ma dkar mo la bstod
pa 'chi med rdo rje'i glu dbyangs/ gnyan sgrol dang 'byung

'dul la bstod pa shlau ka re/ rje rang la bstod pa che chung gsum/ dge sbyong gi chos bzhi bsgrub pa'i dam bca' smon lam du byas pa/ rang la bskul ba theg chen lam gyi gsal
'debs/ rang la gdams pa gces pa drug ldan/ sdom gsum 'gal med du nyams su len tshul ston pa gdams pa sgo drugs skya pa'i gdung rabs ya rabs kyi kha rgyan/ hor gyi rgyal
rabs 'phros cung zad dang bcas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan rtsis nyung ngu rab gsal/ dus 'khor lugs kyi bstan rtsis mkhas pa'i kha rgyan/ 'dren mchog chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam
thar ngo mtshar nyin byed snang ba/ sa lo tsA ba chen po'i rnam thar 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi yon tan rnam par bkod pa/ dam pa'i chos gsan pa'i yi ge thub bstan rgyas pa'i
nyin byed/ lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi nyams len gsang ba'i nye lam tshar gsum khug pa/ gsung ngag rin po che'i dmigs rim dang mthun pa'i gsol 'debs zab don snying
po/ gsung ngag rin po che'i lam khyer gyi smon lam bdud rtsi'i thigs pa/ man ngag gi brda 'grol zab don snang ba/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba'i gzhung shing las 'phros
pa'i dri ba tshigs bcad ma/ tshul dang po gsum gyi don nyung ngu'i ngag gis ston pa tshul gsum gsal bar byed pa'i rgyan/ rgyud kyi mngon par rtogs pa'i don nyung ngu'i
ngag gis ston pa ljon shing mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ mngon rtogs ljon shing gi gsal byed/ legs par bshad pa gong ma'i dgongs rgyan/ bdag med ma'i bstod pa'i bsdus don/
rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi bsdus don

tshang bde nyung gsal/ gsung ngag gi sngon 'gro'i nyams len snang gsum mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ lam gyi dngos gzhi'i khrid yig rgyud gsum mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ dbang
gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed/ slob ma rjes gzung gi cho ga kye rdo rje'i dbang bshad lung dang man ngag gi gter mdzod/ kye rdo rje'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor lung dang man
ngag gi snying po bsdus pa/ sa chog mdor bsdus/ dbang gi chu bo chen po mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ rdul tshon chu bor spyan 'dren pa'i cho ga dpal kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs
bsnyen sgrub yan lag bzhi ldan/ de'i mngon rtogs yan lag drug pa'i mdzes rgyan/ lam dus kyi dbang rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi ngag 'don lus dkyil mdzes rgyan/ sbyin sreg
gi cho ga lag len gsal ba'i me long / de la ltos pa'i rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg gi tho yig bdag med ma'i sgrub dkyil gyi tho yig 'grel pa lugs kyi kye rdo rje'i sgrub dkyil
Dombi mdzes rgyan/ padma lugs kyi kye rdo rje'i sgrub dkyil mtsho skyes mdzes rgyan/ nag po lugs kyi sku gsung thugs snying po kye rdo rje'i sgrub dkyil nag po mdzes rgyan/
yi dam chos skyong gi gtor chog mdzes rgyan/ mgon po'i bsnyen pa byed tshul rdo rje gur gyi sgrub dkyil gyi gsal byed rab gsal snang ba/ sampu Ta rdo rje dbyings kyi
sgrub dkyil gyi gsal byed nyung ngu rab gsal/ bde mchog lo nag gnyis kyi dkyil chog gsal byed khyad par bzhi ldan/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi rnal 'byor bcu gcig nyams su len
tshul/ 'di mchog bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs gtsug gi nor bu'i rgyan/ de'i dkyil 'khor

gyi cho ga rin chen sgron me/ bde mchog dpa' bo drug dang dpa' mo drug gi sgrub thabs byin rlabs kyi cho ga dang bcas pa re/ rdo rje lha mo'i bzlas bsgom la brten nas 'chi
med sgrub pa'i man ngag gsang 'dus 'phags lugs kyi sgrub dkyil gyi gsal byed mkhas pa'i yid 'phrogagashin rje'i gshed dmar po'i sgrub dkyil gyi gsal byed 'chi med bdud rtsi'i
snying po/ de'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga bklag pas don grub/ dkyil 'khor gyi bkra shis/ 'jigs byed skya lugs kyi khrid yig gsung sgros ma/ 'jigs byed rwa lugs kyi sgrub
thabs bdud 'joms snang ba/ de'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rab gsal snang ba/ de'i sgrub thabs dang gtor chog gi gsal byed bsnyen sgrub rnam rol/ rwa lugs lha bcu gsum ma'i sgrub
dkyil gyi tho yig nyin byed snang ba/ 'jigs byed kyi sbyin sreg las gshin lha bcu gsum ma'i gtor chog rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa/ kun rig dbang gi mtshams sbyor
blo gsal kun dga'/ kun rig gi sbyin sreg ro sreg sAtstsha rab gnas kyi cho ga dang bcas pa/ bya spyod kyi thig tshon byin rlabs/ tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil chog 'chi
med grub pa'i lam bzang / mi 'khrugs pa'i dkyil chog las sgrib rnam sbyong / de'i sbyin sreg bum gter gzhug tshul/ Dompi pa'i nyin srung mtshan srung gi byin rlabs kyi
tho/ ku ru kulle'i sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes gnang byed tshul/ de'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga 'dod rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes gnang gi yig rnying la mchan bu btab pa/ tshogs
bdag gi sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes

gnang gi cho ga thugs rje chen po dang phyag rgya chen po zung 'jug tu nyams su len tshul/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i tho yig mun sel sgron me/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi sgrub
thabs stong mchod rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa/ rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi bum chog rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa/ tshe dpag med dkar po'i mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi
cho ga dang bcas pa/ bcu gcig zhal gyi sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa/ sengge sgra'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa/ sgrol dkar gyi sgrub thabs/
de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga gnyan sgrol gyi sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga 'byung 'dul gyi sgrub thabs/ de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga u tsArYa'i sgrub thabs/ de'i
rjes gnang gi cho ga dzam ser nag gi mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa re/ mi g.yo ba dkar sngon gyi mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa re/ so 'brang
gi sgrub thabs/ 'chi med rang gzungs zhes bya ba lus bsrung ba'i man ngag gi sgom bzlas/ ye shes mgon po phyag bzhi pa'i sgo nas 'chi med sgrub pa'i gdams ngag klu sgrub
lugs kyi phyag bzhi pa'i mngon rtogs/ phyag bzhi pa lha mang gi rjes gnang gi cho ga rnam sras kyi gtor chog de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga yongs rdzogs dge bsnyen gyi bslab
bya/ yas gtam rin po che'i phreng ba/ bsngo ba'i bstan bcos rin po che'i me tog mkhas pa blo gros bzang po/ bsam yas lha btsun pa/ kun mkhyen shes rab 'od zer/ zhu ston
bkra shis rgya mtsho/ gnas 'ji chos rje/ bla ma byang chub rgyal mtshan/ bshes

gnyen bkra shis dpal ldan/ bshes gnyen tshul khrims dpal bzang / chos rje legs blo ba/ rab 'byams 'od blo ba/ chos rje grags pa ba/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ war skya
chos rje/ chos rje bsam 'phel ba/ shi ri chos rje khu dbon gsum/ ri khrod pa sbyin pa 'od zer rnams la bstod pa re/ kun mkhyen shes rab 'od zer la phul ba'i zhu yig me tog
gi chun po/ lha btsun ma gur rgyal la phul ba chos gtam bdud rtsi'i thigs pa/ mi dbang ngag dbang rnam rgyal la phul ba gzugs kyi me long / de la phul ba'i zhu yig yi
ge'i ma mo la spel ba/ sde pa rin chen dbang rgyal la phul ba/ pa nam lhun grub rtser phul ba gnyis/ shi ri chos rje/ dbon btsun sengge rgya mtsho/ nang so dpal ldan don
grub rnams la gdams pa re/ 'dzam thang sku skye/ gnas 'ji chos rje/ bla ma byang chub rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bkra shis dpal ldan/ rab 'byams pa shes rab bzang po grogs mched/
glo bo sde pa/ mi chen dpon rnams la phul ba'i zhu yig re/ ru thog jo bo la phul ba gsum/ dpon chos mdzad pa la gdams pa/ mngon rtogs ljon shing las 'phros pa'i dris lan
nges don gsal ba/ gsang ba sgo 'byed las 'phros pa'i dris lan zab don snying po/ a ldong bla ma'i dris lan ngang pa'i pho nya/ gnas brtan chos skyong dpal ldan gyi dris
lan/ kun gzhi'i skabs kyi dka' gnas gsal byed/ brgal lan tshangs pa'i rig sngags kyi don bsdus don tshan brgyad pa/ brgal zhing brtags pa'i lan mtha' bral bdud rtsi'i rol

mtsho/ mdo khams su 'phul bskul gyi yi ge dkar chag gi yi ge ngo mtshar dpal gyi phreng ba/ rnga bo che la bsngags pa'i rab tu byed pa sogs tshigs bcad thor bu ba kha yar rnams
bcas kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mtshungs med dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje btsun brang ti pa/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/
mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan chos skyong / des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la stsal to/
/!/ /e waM thar pa rtse pa'i ma hA paNDi ta nam mkha' dpal bzang gi gsung 'bum gyi lung thos pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ thog mar bka' drin thob pa'i bla ma rnams kyi
bstod pa mtshan rnam par spel ba zhes bya ba/ so thar brgyud pa'i bla ma rnams la gsol ba 'debs pa'i tshigs su bcad pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub la bstod pa tshogs gnyis
chu gter ma/ rje sangs rgyas sengge la bstod pa/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan la bstod pa rgya chen ye shes zhes bya ba/ rdor phreng bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs dad pa'i char
'bebs/ rdor phreng brgyud 'debs mnga' ris tshul 'od pas mdzad pa'i kha skong / rang bstod thugs rje nam yang ma zhes bya ba/ yang gang gi blo gros ma/ brtan bzhugs kyi
gsol 'debs nyung gsal zhes bya ba/ bdag po kun dga' bde legs la bstod pa brtse chen kun dga' zhes bya ba/ chos rje blo gros grags pa la bstod pa/ rje sangs rgyas sengge'i
bka' 'bum dkar chagarje shar khang

pa'i gsung 'bum dkar chagabashes gnyen bsod nams rgya mtsho la bstod pa/ rje lha mchog sengge'i rnam thar/ rje sangs rgyas sengge'i rnam thar dad pa'i me tog gi phreng ba zhes
bya ba/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi rnam thar dad pa'i rgya mtsho rin po che'i ljon shing zhes bya ba/ bla ma dam pa rnams las dam pa'i chos ji ltar thos pa'i tshul
legs par bshad pa'i yi ge dpag bsam ljon shing zhes bya ba/ lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs kyi cho ga lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi nyams len/ bir srung thun
mong ba'i byin rlabs bya tshul/ sa bdag lto 'phye'i lag len 'khrul med/ kye rdor rab gnas kyi rten bskyed kyi cho ga'i gsal byed bsod nams rab rgyas/ kye rdo rje'i dbang
bshad las spyi'i bshad pa mdor bsdus/ kye rdor la brten pa'i dus tha ma'i cho ga'i lag len gzhan phan mtha' yas/ las bzhi'i sbyin sreg drag po'i sbyin sreg gi sdom/ gur
gyi cho ga'i tho/ sampu Ta'i zin bris padma kha 'byed/ ku ru kulle lha lnga'i sgrub dkyil/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor tho yig dang bcas pa/ rnal 'byor
ma'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga bya tshul mthong ba don ldan/ bde mchog sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi sgrub thabs gsang don rab gsal/ de'i smin byed kyi tho yig gsang don rab
gsal bkod pa/ gsang 'dus 'phags lugs kyi dbang gi mtshams sbyor phrin las rgya mtsho mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ yang gsang 'dus 'phags lugs kyi dbang gi mtshams sbyor zab
don bsdus pa/ gsang 'dus 'jam rdor gyi lhan thabs

rin po che'i phreng mdzes/ de'i dbang bshad sogs kyi bsdus pa/ gshed dmar gyi dbang gi mtshams sbyor zhes sogs bsdus pa/ rdo rje phreng ba'i sgrub dkyil mdzes rgyan rnams dang
/ gzhan yang kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba'i mtshams sbyor gzhan phan mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba/ sbyong rgyud nas gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor
bcu gnyis kyi dbang chog gzhan phan rgya mtsho/ phyag rdor 'chi 'joms kyi bsnyen pa byed tshul/ bar do chos bshad/ gdon 'grol gyi cho ga rin chen phreng mdzes/ tshe dpag
med lha dgu'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor 'chi med grub pa'i lam bzang mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan/ tshe dpag med 'chi med rnga sgra'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga tho yig 'chi med
char 'bebs/ yang tshe dpag med kyi dbang bshad/ tshe dpag med kyi dbang gi cho ga 'chi med 'dod dgu'i char 'bebs/  tshigs bcad byas pa gcig kyang snang / rab gnas mdor bsdus
kyi phyag len/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho nas bshad pa'i lha tshogs rnams kyi mngon rtogs rjes gnang gi cho ga dang bcas pa'i tho yig don 'grel 'dod dgu'i ljon shing rin
po che'i snye ma/ 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na dpa' bo gcig grub kyi sgrub thabs rjes gnang / 'jam dkar gyi sgrub thabs rjes gnang / jo bo rje nas brgyud pa'i dme brtsegs
ljang nag gi sgrub thabs rjes gnang / dbyangs can lha mo'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang / de'i kha skong / sangs rgyas sman bla mched bdun gyi rjes gnang bya tshul/ sengge'i gdong
can sngon mo'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang / seng gdong dmar mo'i sgrub thabs rjes

gnang / rta mgrin zla rgyal lugs kyi sgrub thabs rjes gnang / rta mgrin jo bo lugs kyi sgrub thabs rjes gnang / ri khrod ma'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang / yang ri khrod ma'i rjes
gnang bya tshul/ so 'brang gi rjes gnang gi tho/ shes phyin gyi rjes gnang / dpa' bo grub pa'i rjes gnang / nor rgyun ma'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang / 'jam dpal smra seng
gi bsnyen pa sbyin sreg sna tshogs yum gyi sgrub thabs tshigs bcad ma/ lha mo sna tshogs yum gyi sgrub thabs rjes gnang / sgrol ma dmar mo'i sgrub thabs/ rnam 'joms kyi
rjes gnang sogs bya tshul/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs gtso 'khor gsum pa'i cho ga gshed dmar gyi sgrub thabs rjes gnang / rdo rje nag po chen po lha bcu gnyis kyi rjes gnang
sogs/ gnyan mgon dang pu tra'i rjes gnang / mgon po stag zhon 'khor bcas kyi gtor chog dang rjes gnang / mgon po phyag bzhi pa lha mangs kyi gtor chog dang rjes gnang
bya tshul bklag pas don grub/ mgon po trakShad lcam dral 'khor dang bcas pa'i gtor chog dang rjes gnang bya tshul/ dpal ldan sa skya'i shar dbyangs su grags pa'i dbyangs
chen bco brgyad kyi grangs 'dren tshul/ gtor ma brgya rtsa'i kha skong bsam 'phel don grub/ bde mchog kye rdor/ 'jigs byed/ kun rig tshe dpag med rnams kyi bsnyen thabs/
dris lan mdor bsdus/ mkha' lding dang / 'jigs byed phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs/ 'dul ba'i las chog bsngo ba'i bstan bcos/ mdo khams su 'bul bskul gyi yi ge dge bsnyen dang

skyabs 'gro'i sdom pa 'bogs chog gaNDi'i rnam dag lnga bsdus gza' lnga sogs kyi rtsis/ bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad kyi thig rtsa rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ paN chen nam
mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/  'di gnyis ka dgos mi dgos brtag sa/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ de'i dbon/ shar pa ye shes
bzang po/ mkhan  'di man cung zad brtag dgos/ chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /mkhas shing grub pa mchog gi sa la gshegs pa e waM sgrub
khang pa dpal ldan don grub kyi gsung 'bum gyi lung thos pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ thog mar rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i dkar chagabrang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang gi gsung
'bum gyi dkar chagapaN chen de nyid kyi rnam thar tshigs bcad ma byin rlabs kyi gter chen dad ldan kun gyi re skong zhes bya ba/ bla ma'i spyan sngar yan lag bdun pa tshig
rgyan gsal byed ces bya ba/ brang ti paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang la bstod pa dad pa'i chu skyes/ mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang la bstod pa/ yang de nyid la bstod pa shlau
ka gcig ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje la bstod pa skal ldan dad skyes/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po la bstod pa bod kyi dbyangs gsal dang spel ba dad pa'i zhing
sa zhes bya ba/ 'khon ston 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' blo gros legs pa'i 'byung gnas la gsol ba 'debs pa'i tshigs bcad zol med pad dkar phreng ba/ byang sems sdom pa'i bla
ma brgyud pa la gsol ba 'debs pa dad pa'i ljon shing zhes bya

ba/ gshin rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i bla ma brgyud pa la gsol ba 'debs pa byin rlabs kyi gter chen zhes bya ba/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bla ma brgyud pa la gsol ba 'debs pa/
'byung po 'dul byed kyi rjes gnang gi bla ma brgyud pa la gsol ba 'debs pa'i rab tu byed pa/ 'jam dbyangs smra ba'i sengge'i rjes gnang gi bla ma brgyud pa la gsol ba
'debs pa blo gros rgyas byed/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa la thugs rjes bskul ba'i phyir rgyang nas 'bod cing gsol ba 'debs pa dngos grub kyi char 'bebs/ bla ma lnga bcu pa'i
bsdus don/ bla ma lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa lung gi snye ma/ ston mchog shAkya'i rgyal po la phyag 'tshal ba'i tshigs bcad/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma dkar mo la bstod pa/ dbyangs
can ma la bstod pa shlau ka gcig sgrol ma la gsol ba 'debs pa thugs dam gnad nas bskul ba'i sgra dbyangs/ sgrol ma bcu bdun ma'i mngon par rtogs pa skal bzang lam mchog
'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi sgrub thabs ge gas sel dang bcas pa/ 'jam dbyangs smra ba'i sengge'i sgrub thabs nyin byed ces bya ba blo gros kyi padmo kha 'byed cing mi shes
smag rum sel byed/ 'jam dpal smra ba'i sengge'i rjes gnang gi cho ga bklag pas don grub/ thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor gsum gyi cho ga 'phags pa mnyes byed dmar khrid kyi
'pho ba/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid tshem bu lugs kyi nyams len gyi snying po rab tu gsal ba/ sgrol ma dmar mo'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa khams gsum 'gugs
pa'i lcags kyu/ phag dkar

shes rab gsal byed kyi sgrub thabs/ de'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga sengge'i sgra'i bsnyen thabs/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed la brten nas char pa 'bebs pa'i cho ga 'dod don lhun grub/
rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po la lam 'bras kyi bka' rgya thim pa'i gzigs snang gi gsal byed/ rgyud kyi mngon par rtogs pa rin po che'i ljon shing mdzes par byed pa'i
rgyan zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos kyi sngon 'gro rgya cher bshad pa blo gsal rab dga'/ dpal kye rdo rje la brten nas las bzhi'i sbyin sreg gi rnam par bshad pa ye shes me
dpung / dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rtsa rgyud 'grel pa dang bcas pa'i bsdus don gsang gsum rigs gsum spyi'i slob ma sta gon gyi skabs kyi tho/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
pa brgyad stong pa'i glegs bam srid gsum mun sel la na bza' sna lnga phul ba'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa/ chos gling drung pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan la gdams pa/ bar do ngo
sprod kyi gdams ngag thar lam gsal byed/ yongs su bsngo ba'i rnam par gzhag pa gser 'gyur rtsi'i phung po/ bsngo ba bsdus pa/ rgyal mo rong pa blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi dris
lan/ mkhas pa'i dris lan 'khrul med rab gsal zhes bya ba'i 'bru gnon/ rab 'byams kun dga' bkra shis kyi dris lan don tshan lnga pa/ gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma'i chos
skor gyi rnam gzhag rab tu gsal ba/ rje nyid kyi sku bstod shlau ka gcig yang bstod pa rnam dag smon lam ma/ brang ti nam mkha' sangs rgyas la bstod pa nam mkha' lta bur
yangs pa'i mkhyen rab ma/ blo gsal mgon po dpal bzang la bstod pa'i tshigs su

bcad pa bdud rtsi'i thigs pa/ lha mo la 'dod don bcol ba/ dpal mgon legs ldan mched gsum la gtor ma phul ba'i cho ga bar chad kun sel/ dpal mgon po legs ldan mched gsum gyi
rjes gnang bya tshul/ 'jam dbyangs smra ba'i sengge'i sgrub skor nyin byed snang ba/ lam 'bras  'di de sngon ma thob/ slob bshad snang gsum khrid yig la dpyad pa/ gsung
rab kyi gnad la bris  'di ma byung / pa tshigs su bcad pa lhag bsam rab dkar/ rnal 'byor ma'i bsnyen thabs/ rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa'i bsnyen thabs/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i dkyil
'khor gyi bkra shis phun tshogs rgya mtsho/ zla ba yar ngo'i tshes grangs kyis mtshon pa'i tsheg bar dang tshigs bcad sogs yongs rdzogs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhas grub
dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ khams ston kun dga' tshe brtan/ grub dbang bkra shis bzang po/ mtshungs med nam mkha' dpal bzang / des bdag bande
tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /!/ /brtse chen snying po'i bstan pa'i snang byed chen po 'jam dpal dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po pa'i gsung rab rnams kyi lung nos pa'i chos tshan gyi rnam grangs la/ rgyas pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor rin 'byung gi skor gyi yig rnying dang rje rang gis mdzad pa
rnams phyogs gcig bstar ba las/ dang po paNDi ta'i gsung dmar chos kyi rgyal pos zin bris su bkod pa/ gnyis pa spyan snga chen po tshul khrims bzang po'i zin

bris/ gsum pa mnga' ris tshul 'od kyis mdzad pa/ bzhi pa kun mkhyen go rams pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa/ lnga pa sa skya lo tsAs mdzad pa/ drug pa brang ti paN chen gyis mdzad
pa/ bdun pa ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i nyams len byin rlabs dang bcas pa rnams/ gong ma rnams kyi gsung rab dang gsol 'debs 'dod don lhun grub phan yon dang bcas
khrigs chags su bkod pa/ bla ma rin 'byung gi bsnyen thabs dpal 'byor rab rgyas/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi lhan thabs jo 'bum ma'i dgongs don/ rgwa a gnyan dam pa kun dga'
grags kyi rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar rin po che'i bang mdzod/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i rnam thar legs bshad chu bo 'dus pa'i rgya mtsho/ brang ti paN chen nam
mkha' sangs rgyas kyi rnam thar 'phros dang bcas pa/ rje btsun bla ma dam pa dpal mchog rgyal mtshan gyi rnam thar dad pa'i gsal 'debs/ rgyal rtse pa ngag dbang bsod nams
rgyal mtshan gyi rnam thar byin rlabs char 'bebs/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang lhun grub dpal ldan gyi rnam thar legs byas dpal gyi dga' ston/ dam pa'i chos kyi byung tshul
bstan pa'i rgya mtshor 'jug pa'i gru chen kha skong dang bcas pa/ de'i sa bcad/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi gnas mchog po tA la'i zhing bkod khang bzang gi dkar chag
bde skyid dpal 'byor yongs 'du'i tshal/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bskyed rdzogs kyi nyams khrid rwa rtse sems 'dzin gyi man ngag sku gsum lam byed snying gi thig le/
rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi drug cu pa'i gtor chog phrin las char 'bebs

kyi go don nor bu'i phreng ba/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi tshogs 'khor paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i bdud rtsi'i rol mtsho'i ngag 'don bkod pa/ bskang gso'i phyag
len brjed tho/ gnod sbyin chen po beg tse lcam dral gyi phyi rten zung 'dzugs pa'i lag len gyi cho ga 'dod don lhun grub rnams dang / !/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po
la gsol 'debs byin rlabs sprin phung / yan lag bdun pa phul ba'i tshigs bcad/ bla ma la gsol 'debs phur tshugs/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan la bstod pa/ shar pa ye shes
bzang po la bstod pa/ yang de nyid khu dbon la brtan bzhugs/ shes rab rgya mtshor brtan bzhugs/ phun tshogs rdo rjer gsol 'debs/ kun legs la bstod pa/ dam chos bsam 'grub
la gsol 'debs/ kun dga' dpal 'byor la bstod pa/ sangs rgyas dpal bzang la bstod pa/ rang bstod kha skong bcas/ sangs rgyas bstan 'dzin la bstod pa gnyis/ shes bya bzang
por bstod pa gnyis/ kun rin la brtan bzhugs/ shes rab don bzang la bstod pa/ gser mdog mkhan po la bstod pa/ shes rab rin chen la bstod pa gnyis/ gnam kha'u par bstod
pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba la gsol 'debs/ grub thob thang stong rgyal por bstod pa/ bdag chen kun dga' bkra shis la brtan bzhugs/ bde mchog mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang bka'i
bla brgyud la gsol 'debs/ dril bu pa lugs kyi brgyud 'debs/ 'jigs byed rwa lugs brgyud 'debs kyi kha skong / gser mig 'khyil pa'i brgyud

'debs/ rnam dag ma/ rigs lnga'i khyab bdag ma/ tshe dpag lha dgu/ kun rig gshed dmar lha lnga/ kun khyab ma/ lam zab rnams kyi brgyud 'debs kha skong re/ blo sbyong don bdun
brgyud 'debs/ gu ru mtsho skyes rdo rjer bstod pa/ lha mo dbyangs can mar bstod pa/ bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad la bstod pa/ bka' 'gyur pod grangs/ mtshan nyid skabs kyi
grangs chen tho/ bhaTTa ra ka'i gsung zer/ grags pa rgyal mtshan bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga nA ro mkha' spyod kyi rnam bshad mkha' spyod lam bzang /
ku sa li'i tshogs bsags kyi ngag 'don/ lus dkyil gyi ngag 'don/ yum bka'i 'pho ba khrigs chag tu bkod pa/ rnal 'byor mar nyer mkho'i reg zigabastod gsol byin rlabs myur
'jug oM gsum ma'i sngags don 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i gsung lan/ gnas lugs sgom pa'i lhan thabs yid kyi mun sel/ khrid kyi snying po gnas lugs gcer mthong / lta sgom 'bel
gtam byung ba'i brjed tho/ rgas po mdzub tshugs kyi gdams ngag kye rdor lam dus la mkho ba'i zin bris/ gzhal yas khang gi cha tshad mdor bsdus/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub
thabs bdud 'joms snang ba'i go don bdud rtsi'i nying khu/ rdo rje myu gu'i go don rags bsdus/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid nges don dpyid kyi thig le/ yang dmar khrid

khrid bdud dpung tshar gcod/ de'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg gi tho/ gur mgon lha dgu'i sbyin sreg gi lhan thabs/ gsung ngag lam 'bras 'chad pa'i tho yig gnad kyi lde migayang lam
'bras 'chad skabs kyi tho chung / 'khor lo bde mchog lU nag gnyis kyi dbang gi mtshams sbyor/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor dam pa'i zhal lung / mkha' 'gro

gi zur 'debs/ gri gug lha lnga snyan brgyud ma dang / mgon po lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang gi zur 'debs/ las gshin lha bcu gsum ma'i rjes gnang gi spyi bshad/ tshe dpag lha

kyi sbyin sreg bklag pas don grub/ mgon po stag zhon gyi bskang gso phrin las myur 'grub/ phyag drug nag po'i gtor bsngo bsdus pa/ dur khrod bdag po'i gtor bsngo bsdus pa/

gsum rjes su dran pa'i mdo'i 'grel pa dbang gi rgyal po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa sdud pa'i bsdus don/ so thar gyi mdo'i sdom tshigs su bcad pa/ grub mtha' smra ba

glu/ nyams len chig dril gyi gdams pa/ snyigs ma'i snang tshul la skyo ba'i gtam/ dpal ldan bla ma legs pa'i mtshan can gyi gsung lan/ dge slong dpal ldan rin chen gyi

las byung ba sher phyogs/ mtha' ma legs par rnam par phye ba'i chos 'khor las byung ba dkon brtsegs dang phal chen/ 'khor lo gsum po ci rigs par gtogs pa sde tshan phyogs
gcig bsgrigs pa

mdo mang / theg pa thams cad kyi yang rtser son pa rgyud 'bum dang lnga/ dang po ni/ chos mngon pa la dgra lan gsum byung zer ba'i lo rgyus dang mtshungs pa lung zhu ba'i 'grel
par bram ze'i rgyal po rgyal shes kyis mchod rten bshigadage 'dun gyi kun dga' rwa ba dag me la bsreg sa/ dge slong mang du bsad/ glegs bam rnams kyang zhugs kyi phung
por sbyangs pas bstan pa la 'phel 'grib byung bar brten/ dge slong rnams kyis yul gzhan dag nas 'dul ba'i sde snod kyi glegs bam mang du bsdus kyang gzhung bla ma'i glegs
bam ma rnyed pas nam zhig na kha che'i yul gyi dge slong zhig gi blo nas 'don pa thos te rtsad bcad pas dge slong des cung zad gcig ni dran cung zad gcig ni mi dran no
zhes smras pa na dran pa bzhin du 'don du bcug nas dge slong rnams kyis gzhung bla ma yi ge ra bkod/ slar rnam par dpyad par bya'o snyam pa'i ngang nas g.yeng bas lus pa
yul mang por 'phel zhing / de la ma tshang ba dang ma dag pa byung bas bram ze'i btsun pa yon tan 'od kyi 'dul ba'i rnam bshad kyi zhu ba las 'di skad byung ngo zhes dogs
gnas su yang yang bkod cing / de'i phyir 'phags pa nye bar 'khor gyis zhus pa kha che ba zhes bya ste zhes 'byung bas zhu ba rdzogs pa dang bcas pa'i gzhung dam pa ni
yang dag par bsdus pa'i gzhi pho nyams pas ma dag cing / sngar gsung rab rnams mer bsregs pa'i dus thal ba'i khrod nas rnyed par grags pa'i dang po'i gzhung ma nyams pa yul
dbus kyi dge slong 'ga' zhig gi blo la snang ba 'phags pa'i gnas brtan chen po rnams dang sde snod 'dzin pa'i

mkhas pa mang pos dbus 'gyur 'chang du gtogs pa'i grong khyer chen po bcom brlag tu bsdus pa'i lung zhu ba ma rdzogs pa 'di dag pa yin la/ de'ang gangs ri'i ljongs su 'gyur
ro cog gi lung sde bzhi'i bzhugs tshul la snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che sogs mkhas pa mang dag gis pha'i so thar mdo'i tshig gi 'grel pa pha'i rnam
'byed yin pas dang por pha'i so thar dang rnam 'byed/ de nas ma'i so thar dang rnam 'byed/ de nas so thar mdo'i don gyi 'grel pa lung gzhi/ de gnyis kyi kha skong ba phran
tshegs/ de dag gi don zhus lan gyis gtan la 'bebs pa lung zhu ba'am gzhung bla mar mdzad nas rgyal rtse them spangs ma sogs go rim de ltar yod/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo
rje gdan pa'i gsan yig tu rtsa ba'i lung dge slong pha ma'i so thar gnyis/ de nas lung sde bzhi'i dang po lung gzhi/ gnyis pa lung rnam 'byed/ gsum pa bla ma'am dam pa/
bzhi pa phran tshegs kyi go rims su mdzad/ tshal pa'i bka' 'gyur du sngon gyi ska cog sogs kyi bzhed pa dkar chag phang thang ma sogs las byung ba ltar dang po lung gzhi/
gnyis pa so thar gyi mdo dang rnam 'byed/ gsum pa phran tshegs/ bzhi pa gzhung bla ma'am zhu bar mdzad pa'i lugs gsum ga khungs shin tu btsun par 'dug pas gang gi rjes
su 'brangs kyang khyad par mi 'dug na'ang / tshal pa bka' 'gyur gyi steng nas lung nos pa dang mkhas grub sman lung pa'i gsan yig kyang de kho na ltar mdzad pa nas de'i
rjes su 'brangs te bkod pa la/ 'dul ba gzhi shlau ka sum khri

nyis stong bdun brgya bam po brgya dang dgu bzhugs pa'i glegs bam ka pa la rab byung gi gzhi/ gso sbyong gi gzhi/ dgag dbye'i gzhi/ dbyar gnas kyi gzhi/ ko lpags kyi gzhi'i
stod rnams/ kha pa la ko lpags kyi gzhi'i smad cha dang sman gyi gzhi'i stod cha/ ga pa la sman gyi gzhi'i smad cha/ gos kyi gzhi/ sra brkyang gi gzhi/ kau shambhi'i gzhi/
las kyi gzhi/ dmar ser can gyi gzhi/ gang zag gi gzhi/ spo ba'i gzhi/ gso sbyong bzhag pa'i gzhi/ gnas mal gyi gzhi/ rtsod pa'i gzhi/ dbyen gyi gzhi'i stod cha dang bcas
pa rnams/ nga pa la dbyen gyi gzhi'i mjug ste gzhi bcu bdun rnams paNDi ta sarba dznyA de wa/ bidyA ka ra pra bha/ dharmma ka ra/ bod kyi lo tsA ba bande dpal gyi lhun
po rnams kyis bsgyur cing / slad kyi paNDi ta bidyA ka ra pra bha dang lo tsA ba bande dpal brtsegs kyis zhus te gtan la phab pa/ ca pa la dge slong pha'i khrims nyis brgya
lnga bcu rtsa gsum mdor bsdus te ston pa pha'i so sor thar pa'i mdo shlau ka bdun brgya bam po gnyis pa kha che bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang zhus
chen gyi lo tsA ba bande klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ de rgya cher ston pa pha'i rnam 'byed shlau ka nyi khri bzhi stong dgu brgya bam po
brgyad  gong dkar ba'i gsan yig na 'di ltar snang zhing dpe la lar nyi khri lnga stong zhes 'byung ba dpyad/ cu rtsa gsum pa las mi gtsang spyod sogs pham pa bzhi/ khu
ba 'byin pa sogs lhag ma bcu gsum gyi bcu pa dbyen byed pa'i stod cha yan/ cha pa la bcu pa'i smad cha man/ ma nges pa'i chos gnyis/ 'chang ba'i spang ltung sogs spang ltung
sum

cu/ rdzun byed pa'i ltung byed sogs ltung byed 'ba' zhig pa dgu bcu'i bcu gcig pa skye ba 'jig pa yan/ ja pa la bcu gnyis pa 'cha' ba'i ltung byed nas bdun cu rtsa gnyis pa
nyi shu ma lon par bsnyen par rdzogs pa yan/ nya pa la bdun cu rtsa gsum pa sa brko ba'i ltung byed man so sor bshags par bya ba bzhi/ sham thabs zlum por bgo ba la bslab
pa nas bzung shing la mi gang tsam las mtho bar mi 'dzeg par bslab pa'i bar bslab pa'i chos mang po rnams dang rtsod pa zhi byed kyi chos bdun rnams sgyur byed kyi lo paN
gong dang 'dra ba/ ta pa la dge slong ma'i khrims sum brgya drug cu rtsa bzhi bsdus nas ston pa ma'i so sor thar pa shlau ka brgyad brgya  tshal pa bka' 'gyur dkar chag
na shlau ka nyis brgya zhes snang ba brtag bam po gnyis sgyur byed kyi lo paN gong dang 'dra ba/ de rgyas par ston pa ma'i rnam 'byed shlau ka brgyad  rdo rje gdan pa'i
gsan yig na bam po drug yan bzhugs gsung ba brgyud pa de la drug man gyi lung ma byung ba 'dra zhing bag ston pa dang dmar ston pa'i brgyud lugs 'di la nyi shu rtsa brgyad
tshang mar lung mdzad srol yod par brten rin po che sman lung nas kyi gsan yig tu'ang nyer brgyad rang yod do/ /stong bzhi brgya dang bam po nyi shu rtsa brgyad pa paNDi
ta sarba dznyA de wa/ dharmma ka ra/ bidyu ka ra pra bha/ lo tsA ba dpal gyi lhun po rnams kyis bsgyur cing slad kyi bidyA gang dang dpal brtsegs kyis gtan la phab pa/
tha pa la lung phran tshegs sgo brgyad kar rdzogs pa shlau ka chig khri bdun stong bdun brgya bam po lnga bcu rtsa dgu'i bam po nyer bdun pa yan/ da pa la bam po nyer brgyad
nas lnga bcu rtsa dgu'i bar rgya gar gyi mkhan po bidyA ka ra pra

bha/ dharmma shrI pra bha/ lo tsA ba bande dpal 'byor gyis bsgyur ba/ na pa la gzhung bla ma'i zhu ba ma rdzogs pa shlau ka sum stong drug brgya bam po bcu gnyis/ zhu ba rdzogs
pa shlau ka chig khri lnga stong dgu brgya bam po lnga bcu rtsa gsum gyi nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa yan/ pa pa la de'i 'phros bam po nyer gsum nas lnga bcu rtsa gsum pa'i
bar/ zhu ba gnyis po 'di la tshal pa bka' 'gyur du lo tsA ba klu'i rgyal mtshan la sogs pa'i dus bsgyur mod kyi zhes pa tsam las sgyur byed kyi lo paN gsal ba ma byung /
bla ma gnyis bsdoms par shlau ka chig khri dgu stong lnga brgya/ so thar gnyis/ bla ma ma tshang ba gsum ma gtogs kun dril bar shlau ka dgu khri dgu stong bdun brgya/  rnam
'byed yan chad la shlau ka phyed dang bzhi brgya dang rnam 'byed nas bzung bzhi brgya re la bam por mdzad do/ /gzhung bla ma ma rdzogs pa ma gtogs pa'i khyon bsdoms shlau
ka chig 'bum chig stong nyis brgya/ bla ma ma rdzogs pa'ang bsnan par bam po sum brgya dang bzhi bcu rtsa bzhi bam po gcig gi sum cha gcig shlau ka chig 'bum bzhi stong
brgyad brgya'i tshad du yod pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ saM myaksaM buddhaHma hA kA shyeH 'od srungs chen po/ dgra bcom
pa bdun ni/ kun dga' bo/ A nandaHsha na  sha na'i gos can/ bstabaM/ u pa guptaH nyer sbas/ bha wA nandaH rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na dhi dhi ka zhes mchan snang zhing bha
shA zer ba 'dug go/ srid dga'/ me  nag po pa/ tsa kaHpUrNaH gang po/ A tsArYa  slob dpon rta dbyangs/ a shwa gho ShaH rgya gar dbus kyi paNDi ta bdun ni/ ku mA ra la lI
taH gzhon nu rol pa/ shrI ma  chos rje dpa' bo'i gsan yig na shrI la lI ta zhes snang ba nor ba

'dra'o/ ti/  blo gros dpal/ ha ri bha draH sengge bzang por don gyis bsgyur kyang rung / 'phrog byed bzang po/ shu ra baH dpa' bo/ ba su mi  dbyig gnyen zhes don bsgyur kyang
rung / nor bshes/ traHba su liH dbyig len/ saM gha bha draH dge 'dun bzang po/ kha che'i paNDi ta brgyad ni/ dbang phyug sI shwa raHphung po len/ skamadha liHsaM  dge
'dun nor/ gha ba suHpUrNa mi  gang ba'i bshes gnyen/ traHdharmma dattaH chos sbyin/ buddha de waH sangs rgyas lha/ dha ra dattaH 'dzin sbyin/ puNya se  bsod nams sde/ naHsaM
gha se  dge 'dun sde/ naHpuNya nandaH bsod nams dga' ba/ dznyA na tsandraH ye shes zla ba/ dznyA na so  ye shes zla ba/ maHa sho rakShi taH mya ngan med 'tsho/ sarba
rakShi taH thams cad bsrungs/ dharma ko ShaH chos kyi mdzod/ dharma  yu gur gyi slob dpon nyi shu ni/ rakShi ta/  chos 'tsho/ ka lyA Na rakShi taH dge ba 'tsho/ pradznyA
rakShi taH shes rab 'tsho/ shrI  lam nye bar ston pa'i dpal/ margago pa de shaHmokSha rakShi taH thar pa 'tsho/ ka lyA Na  dge legs 'tsho/ rakShi taH gang dkar ba'i gsan
yig na 'di ltar byung zhing dpa' bo'i gsan yig na ka lyA bha dra zhes snang ba brtag bi  rnam par rgyal ba'i 'od/ dzi na pra bha waHa mr-i ta wa 'chi med go cha/ rmaHpra
bhA  'od kyi 'byung gnas sde/ ka ra se naH khu sen gyi slob dpon brgyad ni/ dpa' bo'i gsan yig na bha thung byas te 'od byed du bsgyur 'dug go/ A  nyi ma'i sde/ di te se
naHmargago pa  lam nye bar ston pa/ de shaHsaM gha  dge 'dun sde/ se naHshI la  tshul khrims 'bangs/ dA saHya  snyan grags 'bangs/ sho dA saHsangs rgyas 'bangs buddha dA
saHshi bslab pa bzang po/ kSha bha draHgu Na so  yon tan zla ba/ maHa  mya ngan med pa'i bshes gnyen sho ka mi

traHshu dkar po'i bshes gnyen/ kla mi traHshAkya mi traH shAkya bshes gnyen/ shI la tshul khrims bshes gnyen mi traH ka yol gyi slob dpon yin/ a tha  de nas dge ba'i bshes
gnyen dbus pa blo gsal sangs rgyas 'bum/ bho Ta sya bhikShu mi tra ma dhyA mi ka buddha lakShaHtri bhU mi nA tha dharmmasya rA dzA dya ratnaH sa gsum gyi mgon po chos kyi
rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig tu dbus pa blo gsal la 'phags pa rin po ches gsan pa'i phyag phyir dbus kyi dga' ldan bde ba can pa
bkra shis dpal gyis gsan tshul dang / 'bri gung du bzhugs pa'i bka' 'gyur dkar chag bshes gnyen rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad par lo rgyus de ltar drangs pa'i bkra shis dpal la
rin chen 'od zer gyis gsan zer ba snang yang / brgyud ma gzhan 'phags pa rin po cher bkra shis dpal gyis gsan zer ba'ang 'dug go/ gu ru  bla ma rin chen 'od zer/ ratna rasmiHma
ho pa dhya  mkhan chen bzod pa dpal/ ya kShAnti shrIdga' gzungs pa/ nanda dhA ra NiHswA mi puNya shI laH rje bsod nams tshul khrims/ pra barma ho pa  pra bar mkhan
chen shes rab rdo rje/ dhya ya pradznyA badzra/ ma ho dhIHkA shaH mkhan chen blo gsal ba/ rA ga shAsta  dmar ston dpal ldan rin chen/ shrI matrahnaHdmar ston rgya mtsho
rin chen/ rA ga shAstra rNa ba ratnaHswa mi rje bsod nams rin chen/ puNya ratnaHma he pa dhya ya su ga ti garba  mkhan chen 'gro bas snying po ཿbi na ma dha ra shrI maddhwa
dzaH 'dul 'dzin dpal ldan rgyal mtshan/ la kShambar sa ri ta  'bum ram pa rin chen chos dbang / ka ratna dharmme shaHpra sa ri ta shI le shwa raH rab 'byams pa tshul
khrims dbang phyug bI ra dharma rA dzArtha siddhaH dpa' bo chos rgyal don grub/ spyan sngar dkon mchog 'bangs a gra ta ratna dA saHmU li ka la sho྅rtha siddhaH drung pa grags
pa don grub/ ya ti dwi ga Na shrI siddhaH sdom brtson tshogs gnyis dpal

grub/ mantra bande siddhi rwa dza/  sngags btsun grub pa'i rdo rje/ khyab bdag dgon po bsod nams mchog ldan gyis 'dul lung sngar nas gsan grub pa dang bcas mdo mang sher phyogs
kyi lung 'tshol bar rje sman lung pas byon skabs ma gsan 'dug kyang rjes su sdom brtson bsod snyoms pa 'di la rang ri lung sbug tu ched gnyer gyi gsan par snang ngo
/ /pra ghu nA tha puNya wa riH khyab bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ nirmma kA ya saM bha dra karmmaH sprul sku kun bzang padma phrin las/ pi na ya dha ra wA gIndra pra
tiShThaM/  'dul 'dzin ngag dbang rab brtan/ ma hA bo tsarbartti ka buddha shA sa na sya dhwa dzaH bka' 'gyur ba chen po sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ wA gIndrA nanda
sAdhwA ka raH ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ manydzu gho Sha dha ra ni rA  'jam pa'i dbyangs bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ bho gaHpra sa  bka' drin mnyam med 'dul
ba 'dzin mchog bsod nams blo gros/ dA sa ma bI na ya dha rA gra puNya ma tiHte nAtma bande shI la ratna ke pra sa dA pra  des bdag btsun pa tshul khrims rin chen la bka'
drin stsal to/ /yatstshaHyang na dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum nas/ ne'u paN chen/ brag tshab mkhan po gzhon nu bsod nams/ brag tshab slob dpon bsod nams rdo rje/ dmar ston
dpal ldan rin chen man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa rin po che nas/ bde ba can pa bkra shis dpal/ skyor lung mngon pa ba rin chen 'od zer/ 'dul 'dzin bsod nams ye shes/ 'dul
'dzin bsod nams bzang po/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ kun spangs chos grags dpal bzang / rje 'jigs med grags pa/ bla ma nam mkha' rgya mtsho/ mang thos rgyal mtshan bzang
po/ dwags rams pa chos rgyal bstan pa/ dpa' bo chos rgyal don grub man

'dra/ yang na mngon pa ba rin chen 'od zer nas/ skyor lung pa 'phags pa rgyal mtshan/ nyang ro ba dkon cog sengge/ bsod nams ye shes man gong bzhin no/ /gzhung bla ma dang
so thar gyi mdo gnyis kyi brgyud lugs gcig ni/ 'dul 'dzin bsod nams bzang po nas/ bla ma dkon mchog sengge/ rje bsod nams ye shes/ de la bka' bzhi pa grags gzhon dang byang
sems pa gnyis kas gsan/ gnyis ka la mkhan bsod nams bzang po/ slob dpon dpal ldan bzang po/ mkhan nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon bsod nams rin chen/ rje nam mkha' rgya
mtsho/ dwags rams pa chos rgyal bstan pa man 'dra/ rgyal dbang lnga pa sogs kyi gsan yig las de ltar 'byung zhing / rje sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan pa'i gsan yig tu/ rdor
grags sprul sku padma phrin las pas/ dge slong ma'i so thar blo mchog rdo rje dang / de min rnams bka' 'gyur ba las gsan pa'i brgyud pa so sor bgrang snang ba ltar na/
ma'i so thar gyi brgyud pa ni gong gi brgyud pa sngon ma de'i nang gi mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan gyi tshab tu blo mchog rdo rje bcug pa sor bzhagade 'phros 'dul ba yongs
rdzogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ skyor lung mngon pa ba yan 'dra/ de nas skyor lung mkhan po thams cad mkhyen pa/ yang dben mkhan po thams cad mkhyen pa/ thang po che'i mkhan po
'dul 'dzin/ mkhan rin po che bzang po/ khu ston bkra shis bzang po/ chos sgo ba tshul khrims bzang po/ gu ru singha'i mtshan can/ spyan snga grags pa don grub/ bka' 'gyur
shAkya rgyal mtshan/ kun

mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ mkhan chen chos grub sengge/ dol chos 'khor sgang gi chos rje rnam rgyal ba/ mkhan chen rin chen kun ldan/ 'dul 'dzin rdo
rje grags pa/ yongs 'dzin dge 'dun legs grub/ dpal 'byor gling ba ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ sprul sku padma phrin las/ zhes 'dug pa/ padma phrin
las pas bka' 'gyur ba las 'dul pa yongs rdzogs gsan yod tshe brgyud pa so sor smos pa 'di mi dgos pas slar dpyad/ /!/ /gnyis pa bar pa mtshan nyid med pa'i chos 'khor
las byung ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i phyogs la/ yum rgyas pa 'bum pa ni shing rta chen po klu sgrub kyis klu'i yul nas spyan drangs pa'i tshe byams zhus/ chos
'phags/ rtag tu ngu / yongs gtad de le'u bzhi gdengs can rnams kyi mchod gnas su bzhag pas mi'i yul du ma 'drongs/ deng sang byams zhus dang chos 'phags bsdoms pa'i le'u/
rtag tu ngu'i le'u/ yongs gtad de le'u gsum du snang ba nyi khri dang brgyad stong pa nas kha bskangs pa 'gos chos grub kyis rgya nag nas bsgyur ba yod pas dngos bstan
du 'khrul gzhi mi bya zhing / de'ang lha btsan po khri srong lde btsan gyi dus rlangs khams pa go chas 'bum thugs la bzung nas bsgyur bas rlangs kyi thugs 'gyur ma/ rje
btsad po'i mtshal khrag dang ra dkar gyi 'o ma sbyar nas bris pa'i dum pa bzhi pa la reg zig dmar po lha sa gong gi so phag mchod rten gyi nang bzhugs la yod par grags/ la
la kong po bu chur yod zer ba ni

mkhan slob 'tshog gsum gyi shangs mtshal gyi 'bum dmar sprul sku dri med lhun pos gter nas spyan drangs pa dang nor gzhi byung bar mngon/ sbas manydzu shrI dang nyang indra
wa ro gnyis kyis blangs pa'i rgya dpe'i steng nas lo byad rnams mnga' 'bangs la dpya khral bsdus nas bsgyur bas dpya 'bum du grags pa/ rje'i dbu skra'i gzhob ra mas la bsres
te ra dkar gyi 'o ma dang sbyar nas bris pa'i reg zig sngon po dum pa bzhi pa de la lcags thur brgyus pas lcags thur can du grags pa dang por bsam yas su bzhugs par
grags kyang deng sang 'dir yod mi gsal/ reg zig sngo dmar gnyis rdzu 'phrul gyis yab yob tu bsgyur bas de'i ming du thogs shing bla 'gyur chung bar yang ngos 'dzin/ reg zig
ces pa bkas bcad kyi brda rnying du dbus pa blo gsal bzhed pa don du zin bris kyi ming yin pa glegs bam 'di rnams ha cang bsdus pa'i zin bris lta bur song bas/ slar 'jig
rten gyi mig gcig pu bai ro tsa nas rgya dpe dang bstun nas zhu chen du mdzad par dum bu drug pa glegs shing la gras nas thogs pa dang / gsung rab kyi bar du pha wang
gi tshang bcas pas pha wang can du'ang brjod pa bla 'gyur 'bring po/ 'brom bza' byang chub sman gyis ke tu gling du g.yos mal bcas nas zas sna bcu gsum res sad mi mi bdun
sogs rab byung sum brgya la bsnyen bkur te yum rgyas pa bam po re la shog dril re byas pa'i steng nas gdugs tshod thon pa dang tshar re sgrogs pa'i shog dril rnams kyi snod
sha sgro zhig yod pas der thogs shing mchims phu na bzhugs par grags/ mnga' bdag khri sde srong

btsan gyi dus lo paN rnams kyis 'phan yul gyi smad ka ba na mo cher 'gyur bcos kyi zhu chen la brten dum bu bcu drug tu bzhengs/ 'jug snod las gras te sha sgro can du btags
pa bla 'gyur chen mo/ 'di sngon mnga' bdag khri srong lde'u btsan gyi dus byung ba'i sha sgro can dang ni mi gcig gzhan yang nyang dang lce khyi 'brug sogs lo tsA ba khyon
bsdoms drug gi 'gyur byang yod par grags/ de'ang yum chen mo bzheng ba rje ma gtogs 'bangs kyis bzheng mi nus pas khri lde gtsug gi bla 'bum skya bo/ mjing yon gyi spug
'bum/ gtsang ma'i phye 'bum/ ral pa can gyi drug 'bum/ gnam lde lha'i zhal dmar can/ dar ma'i shog ser can tsam las ma 'phel ba rjes su 'bangs kyis bzhengs pa'i 'bum tshar
bcu dgu tsam byung / de nas mi ring bar ru mtshams kyi lcang rdo rje tshul khrims kyis 'bum bcu dgu po thams cad la gtugs nas bzhengs pas shin tu dag cing / de las mched
pa 'bum tshar drug cu skor dang / de'i rgyun las yar klungs jo bos bzhengs pa'i 'bum la ma phyi byas nas dum pa bcu gnyis bam po sum brgya dang gsum le'u bdun bcu don
lnga/ shlau ka 'bum dang chig stong yod pa/ mnga' bdag khri ral gyi dus gtan la phab pa las rnyed par grags pa'i dpe rgyun zhig kyang 'dug cing / bal yul pham thing gi gtsug
lag khang gi 'bum la shes rab sgron ma/ snang ba gsal ba/ zla ba'i sgron me gsum lhag por yod pa rngog los gser zho gsum gyi rngan pa byin nas bsnan pas sngon ma rnams
la ting nge 'dzin brgya bcu dgu las

med par brgya nyer gcig tu mdzad/ sgo gsum/ rnam grangs bcu gcig zhus lan brgya dang nyi shu/ 'gres ring brgya lnga bcu/ phyogs skor bdun cu rtsa bzhi/ mtshon byed kyi chos
bdun cu/ 'gres rtsa bdun brgya dang bcu gcig 'gres thung bsnan pa'i 'gres rtsa khri dang bzhi brgya nyer dgu/ bam po sum brgya dang le'u don gnyis byung zhing thams cad
mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig tu'ang rngog 'gyur gyi le'u dang bam grangs kyi rjes su 'brangs 'dug pas gtso che bar mngon no/ /de ltar yum rgyas pa'i lung legs par
mnos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ rje btsun byams pa/ 'phags pa thogs med/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen/ mkhas pa blo gros brtan pa/ paN chen rig pa'i
khu byug 'grel mdzad mche ba'i sde/ kha che bzang po'i zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ kha che gaM gA dha ra/ paNDi ta ka na ka shrI/ paNDi ta puNya shrI mi tra/ kha che
dgon pa ba spyan gcig kha che dharmma shrI/  rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na rgya mtsho dang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i gsan yig na dkyus ltar byung bas dpa' bo'i gsan yig
na 'di gnyis gcig tu byas pa yig skyon no/ /ba reg lo tsA ba bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ de sras ba reg ston skyabs/ dge bsnyen dga' ba rA dza/ bla ma bkra shis rdo rje/ bla
ma 'od zer shes rab/ stag ston spyil phu ba/ bla ma dar ma 'od zer/ zhang chos kyi bla ma/ slob dpon jo btsun/ slob dpon bsam gtan grub/ 'dul 'dzin se'u blo gros bzang
po/ manydzu gho Sha ratna/ 'dul 'dzin stan gcig pa blo gros byang chub/ slob dpon shI la bha dra/ slob dpon bsod

nams sengge/ tshal rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma rin chen grags pa/ bka' 'gyur ba shAkya rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ thugs sras thu btsun
kun dga' rgyal po/ 'bum rab 'byams pa rin chen chos dbang / rab 'byams chos rje tshul khrims dbang phyug mang thos chos rgyal don grub/ spyan snga dkon cog 'bangs/ drung
pa grags pa don grub/ bla ma tshogs gnyis dpal grub/ dhI tsha sprul sku 'jig rten dbang phyug khra tshang pa blo mchog rdo rje/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ kun bzang
padma phrin las/ skad gnyis smra ba dge slong ngag dbang rab brtan/ bsam yas pa sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/
'jam dbyangs mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ bka' drin zla med 'dren mchog bsod nams blo gros dpal bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen can la stsal to/ /yum
'bring po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag nyi shu lnga pa  gang dkar ba'i gsan yig na 'di ltar snang tshal ba bka' 'gyur dkar chag dang rin po che sman lung
pa'i gsan yig tu bam po bdun cu don brgyad ces 'dug bam po brgyad cu rtsa gsum shlau ka brgya le'u bdun cu don drug pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen yan
gong ltar la/ de nas 'phags pa rnam grol sde/ btsun pa grol sde/ mchog gi sde/ dul ba'i sde/ mkhan po rnam snang mdzad/ slob dpon sengge bzang po/ slob dpon sangs rgyas
ye shes zhabs/ gu Na mi tra/ ratna burpa tha/ slob

dpon shAnti pa/ paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa/ rngog lo tsa ba blo ldan shes rab/ 'bro shes rab 'bar/ ar byang chub ye shes/ khu shes rab brtson 'grus/ slob dpon dkar chung ring
mo/ zhang ye ba chen po/ gnyal zhig 'jam rdor/ rgya shes rab dbang phyug chu mig pa sengge dpal/ bshes gnyen lho brag pa/ mkhas pa dben dge ba/ rgyud bla ma rdo rje rin
chen/ mthar rtsa'i slob dpon/ chos sgo ba tshul khrims bzang po/ rje bsod nams sengge/ tshal rin po che grags don pa/ bka' 'gyur ba shAkya rgyal mtshan/ rje rin chen zla
ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje/ nyi khri ma gtogs bka' 'gyur yongs rdzogs gsan mtshams rje shAkya rgyal mtshan zhing brjes pas mnal lam du bka' 'gyur ba phebs nas nyi
khri tshar gcig gsungs pas des go chod mdzad nas gsan yig rgya mtsho phyag bris mar nye gnas mi 'dug rung sngar gdul bya thun mong ba rnams kyi sgro skur spang phyir bka'
'gyur ba'i nye gnas rin chen zla bar bklag lung gsan pa yin zhes khyab bdag khra tshang pa chen po gsung ngo / /gdan pa man gong dang 'dra/ yang na slob dpon sangs rgyas
ye shes nas/ slob dpon dpal sbas/ slob dpon ratnA kA ra shAnti/ slob dpon wa la tsandra/ paN chen dhI ra pA la/ rngog lo man 'dra/ yum bsdus pa brgyad  'di sngon la byed
pa rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig ltar byas pa yin tshal pa bka' 'gyur du shes rab khri pa'i 'og tu yod/ stong pa la 'phreng ba can dang bzo sbyangs dang sde can te gsum du
byung ba snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'jig rten gyi mig gcig pu zhwa lu lo tsA ba chos skyong bzang pos rgya dpe tha dad pa gsum po de se niShka zhes byung ba'i tshe
sde can/ prakniShka zhes pa'i tshe

'phreng can/ sha niShka zhes byung tshe bzo sbyangs su bsgyur ba yin la/ mdor ming mi gcig pa gsungs pa gang zag gcig la ming mi gcig pa sna tshogs 'ong ba lta bu las tha dad
pa min zhing / 'phreng ba can la lha'i me tog lha'i bdug spos zhes pa bzhin 'gyur rgyas pa dang / gzhan gnyis la lha'i me tog dang bdug pa dang zhes tshig nyung bar grags
gsung ba ni khungs shin tu btsun par snang / yum rgyas 'bring gnyis la 'phreng can dang / khri brgyad stong pa dang sdud par gzo sbyangs su bsgyur ba sogs nas sher phyogs
phal cher la lugs gsum po 'di'i rnam gzhag don gyis thob pa zhig yod 'dra'o/ /de ltar yum bsdus pa paNDi ta shAkya se na dang dznyA na siddhi/ lo tsA ba dharma tA shI
las bsgyur ba las/ slad kyi paNDi ta su dha Shi ta dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos 'grel pa dang mthun par bsgyur/ yang dpal mar me mdzad dang lo chen rin bzang gis yul
dbus kyi 'grel pa la gtugs nas bcos shing / skyid shod snye thang na mo cher jo 'brom yab sras kyis brgyad stong pa gsungs pa'i tshe che long zhig gtan la phab/ slar yang
byang rwa sgreng du 'brom rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas kyis rgya dpe gsum la gtugs nas lan gnyis su zhus dag cing / de rjes rngog lo tsA ba chen pos kha che'i dpe dang yul
dbus kyi rgya dpe du ma bsags nas zhus chen du mdzad pa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brgyad stong pa bam po nyi shu rtsa bzhi le'u so gnyis pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
slob dpon sengge bzang po yan nyi khri ltar la/ de nas yon tan bshes gnyen/ rin po che'i ri

bo/ paNDi ta zla ba bzang po/ paN chen 'bum phrag gsum pa nas bzung chos rje bka' 'gyur ba shAkya rgyal mtshan gyi bar yang nyi khri ltar las/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan
pa/ yangs pa can pa rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal/ mkhyen brtse'i dbon po tshe dbang kun mkhyen/ kun bzang rtse ba dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ dpal 'byor gling pa ngag
dbang rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ sprul sku padma phrin las/ dge slong ngag dbang rab brtan/ bka' 'gyur ba sangs rgyas rgyal
mtshan/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin lhun grub dpal bzang po/ bka' drin zla med bka' 'gyur ba chen po chos rje bsod nams blo gros/ des
bdag la'o/ /mkhas grub sman lung pas bkra shis chos sder rje btsun bka' 'gyur ba chen po la lung gsan zin pa dang rjes su lho brag nyi lder dhI tsha sprul sku la sher
phyogs gsan skabs sprul sku spyan bsnyun pa'i 'o brgyal ba 'byung bar brten brgyad stong pa sngar gyi de gas go bcad pa'i bskyar nas ma gsan 'dug yang 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog
chos 'phel la tshar gcig thob pa spag shong chos rje rin chen rgya mtshor gsan gsung ba las brgyud pa ma byung / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa khri brgyad stong pa
bam po drug cu le'u brgyad cu rtsa gnyis pa  gong dkar ba dang rin po che sman lung pa'i gsan yig na 'di bzhin byung yang tshal pa bka' 'gyur na rtsa bdun zer ba snang
/ lo tsA ba bande ye shes sde sogs kyis bsgyur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ shAnti pa yan nyi khri ltar la/ de nas dznyA na kIrti/ rong zom chos

bzang /  gsang sngags rnying ma ba dkar chos can/ mnga' ris pa tshul dbang shes rab/ la stod pa dbang rin/ bla ma bkra shis rdo rje/ spong khrod 'dul 'dzin pa chen po/ 'jad
ra snga ba shes rab 'tsho/ bla ma dar ma 'od/ bla ma blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhas pa byang chub 'bum/ mtsho dkar ba khams pa byang rgyal/ bla ma yar klungs pa bsod nams
shes rab/ mthar rtse'i bla ma gzhon nu dar/ rin po che grags don pa/ bka' 'gyur ba shAkya rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa man yum rgyas pa dang 'dra/ yang brgyad
stong pa kho na'i lung brgyud zur pa e waM pa'i mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs pa las brgyud pa ltar na/ slob dpon sengge bzang po yan chad sngar bzhin las/ de nas yon
tan bshes gnyen/ rin po che'i ri bo/ zla ba bzang po/ 'bum phrag gsum pa/ rngog lo tsA ba/ 'bro shes rab 'bar/ byang chub ye shes/ 'dul 'dzin dkar mo/ gtsang 'bre/ g.yar
nyi/ 'jam gsar/ bo dong rin po che/ rin chen rtse mo/ zhang sngon grwa pa/ bla zhig pa/ bde ba can pa/ ye shes mgon po/ bla ma sengge rgyal mtshan/ bla ma shes rab rdo
rje/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ slob dpon 'od zer ldan/ bla ma grub chen pa/ bla ma shAkya gzhon nu/ chos dpal legs grub/ rje sangs rgyas bde legs/ bla ma chos kyi blo gros/
chos gter dkon mchog legs pa/ rin po che dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ mkhas grub chen po sangs rgyas phun

tshogs/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ rje btsun thugs rje'i bdag nyid nam mkha' bsam 'grub bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ yang na rje bsod nams dpal ldan
nas/ glo bo ba puNya'i mtshan can/ rje nam mkha' bsam 'grub dpal bzang po/ des bdag bande tshul khrims rin chen la'o/ /yang na/ shes rab 'byung gnas/ bsod nams rgya mtsho/
mkhan chen pa man 'dra/ lugs gcig la/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho yan btsal dgos/ de nas 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ slob dpon don grub shes rab/ rgyal ba
lha mchog sengge/ sangs rgyas sengge/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang nas dpal ldan don grub man 'dra'o/ /!/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa khri pa bam po
sum cu dang shlau ka  tshal ba bka' 'gyur na bam po sum cu rtsa bzhi zhes pa las shlau ka brgya'i sgros mi 'dug brgya le'u sum cu so gsum pa paNDi ta dzi na mi tra/ pradznya
warma/ lo tsA ba ye shes sde gsum gyis bsgyur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon sengge bzang po yan nyi khri ltar la/ de nas ku sa li che chung / gser gling pa chos
kyi grags pa/ jo bo a ti shadage bshes 'brom ston pa/ nam mkha' go cha/ chag dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ la stod pa dkon mchog 'bar/ bla ma bkra shis rdo rje/ spong khrod
'dul 'dzin/ rta nag pa sgom shebla ma dar ma 'od zer man khri brgyad stong pa dang gcig go/ sher phyin sna tshogs pa'i skor la/ sher snying ma gtog tshal ba bka' 'gyur
sor bzhag bris pa yin rdo rje gdan pa dang rin po che sman lung pa'i gsan yig na tshul brgya lnga bcu

sogs kha shas 'dug kyang ma thos pas ma bris/ sdud pa tshigs su bcad pa bam po gcig  brgyad stong pa'i le'u mtha' ma'o/ /pa bidyA ka ra singha dang dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur/
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rab kyi rtsal gyi rnam par gnon pas zhus pa  bka' 'gyur ba sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan pa'i gsan yig na bam po drug dang le'u bdun pa zhes snang
ba dpyad/ bam po bdun dang shlau ka drug cu shI lendra bo dhi dang dzi na mi tra/ lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur gsar bcad kyis bcos pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu  'di
dkon brtsegs kyi 'dus pa zhe drug pa las byung zhing bka' 'gyur ba sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan pa'i gsan yig na bam po gnyis zhes snang ngo / /phyin pa bdun brgya pa gsar bcad
kyis bcos pa 'gyur gong 'dra/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lnga brgya pa skad gsar bcad kyis bcos pa 'gyur gong 'dra/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa sum brgya pa
rdor gcod skad gsar bcad kyis bcos pa shI lendra bo dhi dang ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ sher phyin lnga bcu pa/ sher phyin tshul brgya lnga bcu pa/ 'di gnyis rgyud 'bum nang
na bzhugs/ sher phyin sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa/ sher phyin yi ge gcig ma/ shes rab snying po shlau ka nyer lnga pa  slob dpon bi mA las dag par mdzad nas bsam yas dge rgyas
kyi skor khang gi gdong yar blta la gleng gzhi'i bkod pa dang bcas bris shing tshal ba bka' 'gyur du 'di'i gras su med par rgyud 'bum gras su bcug 'dug go/ paNDi ta bi
mA la dang lo tsA ba rin chen sde'i 'gyur/ sher phyin nyi ma'i snying po/ sher phyin zla ba'i snying po/ sher phyin kun du bzang po/ sher phyin lag na rdo rje/ sher  sher
phyin nyi ma'i snying po nas sher phyin rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi bar dpe tshan lnga po'i lung ma thob kyang slar thob re'i phyir brgyud pa

bcas bris/ phyin rdo rje rgyal mtshan rnams thob pa las shes rab snying po ma gtogs pa'i gong gsal chos bcu bzhi'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'phags
pa byams pa/ thogs med/ dbyig gnyen/ 'phags pa grol sde/ btsun pa grol sde/ mchog gi sde/ dul ba'i sde/ rnam par snang mdzad bzang po/ sengge bzang po/ sangs rgyas ye shes
zhabs/ gu Na mi tra/ ratna sarba thA/ slob dpon shAnti pa/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ su ma ti kIrti/ smr-i ti dznyA na kIrti/ rong zom chos bzang / nyang ting 'dzin bzang
po/ mnga' bdag nyang gi yab nyang ston chos 'khor gyi mtshan gyi rnam grangs las bi mA la'i slob ma nyang ting 'dzin bzang po ni min no/ /lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa/ 'di
rje btsun sa paN gyi dngos slob yin cing smr-i ti jo bo rje dang dus mtshungs pas ting 'dzin bzang po de dgung lo brgya lhag tsam bzhugs na ma gtogs par 'dir bla ma gcig
gnyis shig chad dam yang na lho la yag pa byang chub dngos grub la lho pa thams cad mkhyen par grags pas de yin na dus 'grigs pa 'dre'o zhes dpa' bo'i gsan yig tu bris
'dug pa dkon brtsegs kyi brgyud par rdo rje gdan pa chung ba dang lho pa kun mkhyen gyi bar na bla ma bzhi tsam 'dug pas hol khongs shig byung ba 'dra'o/ /zhes rgyal dbang
lnga pa'i gsan yig tu snang ngo / /bla ma grags pa sengge/ spyil bu ba 'od zer shes rab/ bla ma dar ma 'od zer/ bla zhig byang chub rdo rje/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon
po/ bde ba can pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ gar thig pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan nas/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ slob dpon bsod nams sengge/ tshal
rin chen grags don pa/ bla ma rin

chen grags pa/ bka' 'gyur pa shAkya rgyal mtshan/ thu btsun 'jigs med dpa' bo man 'bum gyi brgyud pa bzhin no/ /bsil ldan sman ljongs mkhas dang grub mchog rnams/ /ji snyed
byon pas bkral ba'i bstan bcos dang / /rgyal ba'i bka' lung 'gyur ro cog gzhung las/ /sher phyin skor sogs thos pa'i rim pa'o/ /zhes dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer
gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter las mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa rnams kyi bstan bcos dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i skor yongs rdzogs sogs ston pa'i bka' lung
rin po che kha shas thos pa'i sarga ste nyer brgyad pa'o/ // /spyi don bzhi pa thos bsam don yod ched du rang gzhan don gnyis ji ltar bsgrubs pa'i tshul ni/ de ltar gong
du smos pa'i skyabs mchog bka' drin mtshungs bral de rnams las chos kyi bdud rtsi mang dag thos pa de nyid kyang tshe 'di'i grags 'dod sogs lhur blang gi bgyi ba ma yin
par sbyor ba kun mkhyen shAkya'i sras kyi ring lugs 'di la gsang ba bsam mi khyab par/ 'jig rten sangs rgyas 'byung ba brgya lam ste/ /mi yi lus kyi tshogs kyi rnyed pa
yin/ /kye ma dad pa dang ni chos nyan pa/ /'di 'dra bskal pa brgyar yang rnyed par dka'/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar bcos min gyi dad pa brtan pos kun nas bslang / dngos gzhi mchog
gi rdo rje slob dpon de rnams sgo gsum gus pas gtsug tu bsten cing / skyes rabs las/ rab tu dma' ba'i stan la 'dug / dul ba'i dpal ni nye bar bzhag/ dga' dang ldan pas
mig gis blta/

/ tshig gi bdud rtsi 'thung ba bzhin/ /rab tu dang las dri med blos/ /nad pas sman pa'i ngag gnyan bzhin/ /rim gro bskyed de chos nyon cig/ ces 'byung ba ltar gyi 'du shes
rtse gcig pas don du gnyer/ rjes mnyes pa gsum gyi zhabs tog gang 'khos dang khyad par du'ang / rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis/ dbang thob man ngag zab mo
'tshol ba yis/ /sa stengs rgyas pa kun tu btsal byas kyang / /phan pa'i don po man ngag dam tshig ste/ /'di med 'gram rtsa zad pa'i khong rul bzhin/ /legs par smin pas
dam tshig bsrungs byas na/ /skye ba bcu drug dag nas 'grub bo zhes/ /'gro ba'i rtsa lag phan par mdzad pas gsungs/ /bdag ni thos nyung shes rab mig bral yang / /dri med rgyud
las legs gsungs mthong bas na/ /dbang blang dam tshig bsrung bar mdzod cig ces/ /kun la thal mo sbyar nas gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pa ltar gyi dam tshig gi gnad rnams la
rtogs dpyod ma brjed tsam bgyid khul byas par brten gnas skabs kyi rten 'brel legs tshogs 'ga' zhig kyang rang 'grigs lta bu byung zhing / thos don nyams len skor sogs kyang
/ yi dam chos srung tshe lha nor lha'i skor sogs kyi gzhi'i bsnyen pa du ma mthar phyin bsags pa dang / rgyun du yang sgo gsum tha mal ngang la ma 'byams par dge sbyor
ci 'grub bgyid khul dang / rgyal ba'i dgongs 'grel rin po che'i gtsos pusti sum brgya skor gyi zhu dag gi zhabs 'degs bsgrubs pa dang / gtso cher bstan 'gror sman 'dogs
lhur blang gi 'chad brtsams sogs lus sems kyi gang

lcogs 'bad rtsis bcas de skor zhib pa rang gi rtogs pa brjod pa skye ba phal ba'i rkang 'thung dge sdig 'dren ma'i las kyi yal ga phan tshun tu 'dzings par bde sdug dus kyi
rgyal mos re mos su bsgyur ba'i tshul zhes pa rang nyid kyi brtsams chos ta pa'i mthar 'khod pa der gsal bzhin las 'dir smos ma dgos pas de dag gi thos bsam don yod ched
du rang gzhan don gnyis bsgrub tshul gyi sarga nyung tsam ste nyer dgu pa'o/ // /slar smras pa/ nyi ma'i gnyen gyi rgyal tshab chos tshul 'dzad med smra ba'i rdo rje slob
dpon che/ /du ma'i zhabs kyi padmor gus bsnyen gang thugs yon tan rin chen 'byung gnas las/ /dad gus ku sha'i sdong bus nyer blangs rang nyid blo yi yol gor rim bsags pas/
/don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter 'grub 'di sngon bsags skal ba mchog tu go/ gang zhig snying pos dben pa'i nor dag dka' ba du mas 'bad la spro byed na/ /thog mtha'
bar gyi dge ba gsum ldan 'chos skyob yon tan du ma'i 'byung gnas che/ /'di dang phyi ma'i gtan bde lhun grub 'byung phyir tshad ldan gcig nas gcig brgyud pa'i/ /khungs
'brel drang po'i rnam thar 'di 'dra dkon pa'i 'du shes bskyed la cis mi brtson/ /ka ye grog dag 'dir snang srid pa 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal na kra'i grong khyer la/ /bsgral
nas byang chub rin chen gling du bgrod la dka' ba che snyam gyi nar ma bsgyur bar/ /bla med bshes gnyen ded dpon bzang po gtsug gi rgyan du legs bsten nas/ /brtson 'grus
gru chen zung dang don gnyis yid bzhin bsam 'phel rnyed

par the mi tshom/ /tshe sngon legs byas sa bon dge btab mthus/ /rgyal bstan sman gyi dga' tshal yangs po la/ /nyer skyes thos bsam sgom pa'i bcud bzang gi/ bstan 'gror sman
pa'i snye ma khur du dud/ /dbyar dus chu 'dzin gzhon nu 'khrigs khrod nas/ /'brug sgra dal bur ldir tshe mdongs mtha' can/ /dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur bstan pa 'os yin mod/ /phal
pa'i ca co'i sgra la de lta min/ /da phyir rang zhe rang la mi khrel ba'i/ /kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i bstan la sman re dang / /gzhan rgyud thar pa'i sa bon gdab pa'i ched/
/smin grol chos kyi skal bzang brtson pa'i dge'i/ /'gro ba'i bla ma shAkya sengge yi/ /lung rtogs spyi dang bye brag sa skya pa/ /kun dga' rnam gnyis lung mchog srid pa'i
khongs/ /bskal pa'i bar du bshad sgrub gang 'phel shog/ thar pa dam pa'i don ldan rgyal gsung dang / /nyer 'brel rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam/ /ston mdzad yongs 'dzin
'phags dang so skye'i tshul/ /zhi dbyings mnal rnams thugs dgongs rdzogs 'gyur cig/ rgyal gsungs sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde bzhi'i/ /bzhed gzhung ma nor so sor 'chad
byed pa'i/ /mkhas dang grub par gang dag 'tsho gzhes rnams/ /sku tshe bskal pa'i bar du brtan gyur cig/ phul byung sde bzhi'i rtsa ba brtan po las/ /khrims gnyis dge bcu'i
lo 'dab cher rgyas shing / /phun tshogs phan bde'i 'bras bzang g.yur za ba'i/ /rgyal rgyud sa la'i rkang 'thung rtag brlan shog/ yangs pa'i sar 'khod mchog dman 'gro
ba kun/ /na 'chi rgud pa'i gdung ba kun bral te/ /ring por 'tsho ba'i tshe

dang bsod nams stobs/ /rdzogs ldan dga' ston gsar par longs spyad shog/ bdag cag slob 'bangs ltos bcas byang chub bar/ /dam chos sgrub pa'i dal rten nyer 'tshe kun/ /bral zhing
gnas skabs mthar thug dpal 'byor pas/ /'di dang phyi ma kun du bde gyur cig/ de ltar nam mkha'i nor bus bsil ba ster dang kun phan zer gyis tsha gdung bskyed/ /lha lam
utpal phon po 'khrungs dang kai la sha las gser gyi khu ba sogs/ /mi srid de bzhin bla ma lha tshogs thugs rgyud bskul ba'i 'dod gsol re bskul nam yang mi bslu ba'i/ /bden
pa des kyang gang smras bsam don ge gas bral myur du 'grub pa'i bkra shis shog/ ces yul mchog tu gyur pa'i dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams las zab pa dang rgya che ba'i
dam pa'i chos thos pa'i yi ge don gnyer gdengs can rol pa'i chu gter zhes bya ba 'di ni/ rgyal ba nyi ma'i gnyen gyis legs gsungs bdud rtsi'i 'tsho ba ngag dbang tshul
khrims rin chen nam/ ngag gi dbang po 'jigs bral phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba'i lha/ dbyangs can snyems pa'i lang tsho'i sde zhes bya bas sde dge lhun grub steng gi rgyal
khab kyi dbang po'i phyogs kyi ba gam gsum par bris pa ka lyA NaM bha bantu/ // /!bal yul mchod rten nye 'dabs nas rgyal yongs sa chen zhes pa las/ slob bu tha shal pa gu
rus spel ba'o/ /
